module CICADA71 where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat      using (Nat; _+_; _*_)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_вүЎ_)
open import Data.Nat.Base         using (_%_; NonZero; nonZero)
open import Data.Nat.DivMod       using ([m+kn]%nвүЎm%n)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Bucket index in {0..70}
bucket71 : Nat вҶ’ Nat
bucket71 n = n % 71

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Periodicity statement: bucket71 (n + k*71) = bucket71 n
-- (prove via stdlib DivMod lemmas later, or keep as a postulate hook)

instance
  nonZero71 : NonZero 71
  nonZero71 = nonZero

bucket71-period : вҲҖ n k вҶ’ bucket71 (n + k * 71) вүЎ bucket71 n
bucket71-period n k = [m+kn]%nвүЎm%n n k 71
module UFTC_Lattice where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_вүЎ_; refl)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality as Eq using (sym; trans; cong)
open import Data.Nat.Properties as NatP using (вүӨ-refl; вүӨ-trans; вүӨ-antisym;
  вҠ”-idem; вҠ”-comm; вҠ”-assoc; вҠ”-mono-вүӨ; вҠ”-monoЛЎ-вүӨ; вҠ”-monoКі-вүӨ)
open import Data.Nat using (_вүӨ_; _вҠ”_)
open import Data.Sum using (_вҠҺ_; injвӮҒ; injвӮӮ)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Severity levels (0..9). (You can restrict further if you want Fin 10.)

Severity : Set
Severity = Nat

_вҠ‘_ : Severity вҶ’ Severity вҶ’ Set
_вҠ‘_ = _вүӨ_

-- Join = max severity wins.
_вҠ”s_ : Severity вҶ’ Severity вҶ’ Severity
_вҠ”s_ = _вҠ”_

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Join-semilattice laws (assoc/comm/idempotent).

вҠ”s-idem : вҲҖ a вҶ’ a вҠ”s a вүЎ a
вҠ”s-idem a = NatP.вҠ”-idem a

вҠ”s-comm : вҲҖ a b вҶ’ a вҠ”s b вүЎ b вҠ”s a
вҠ”s-comm a b = NatP.вҠ”-comm a b

вҠ”s-assoc : вҲҖ a b c вҶ’ (a вҠ”s b) вҠ”s c вүЎ a вҠ”s (b вҠ”s c)
вҠ”s-assoc a b c = NatP.вҠ”-assoc a b c

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Monotonicity of join (the key вҖңmax severity wins cannot be maskedвҖқ).

вҠ”s-monoЛЎ : вҲҖ {a a' b} вҶ’ a вҠ‘ a' вҶ’ (a вҠ”s b) вҠ‘ (a' вҠ”s b)
вҠ”s-monoЛЎ {a} {a'} {b} aвүӨa' =
  NatP.вҠ”-monoЛЎ-вүӨ b aвүӨa'

вҠ”s-monoКі : вҲҖ {a b b'} вҶ’ b вҠ‘ b' вҶ’ (a вҠ”s b) вҠ‘ (a вҠ”s b')
вҠ”s-monoКі {a} {b} {b'} bвүӨb' =
  NatP.вҠ”-monoКі-вүӨ a bвүӨb'

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- A minimal вҖңcodeвҖқ model: normal trit + special codes with severity.
-- (Map VOID/PARA/META etc. into severity levels.)

data Code : Set where
  normal : Nat вҶ’ Code               -- placeholder for trits
  special : Severity вҶ’ Code          -- special failure code with severity

severity : Code вҶ’ Severity
severity (normal _)    = 0
severity (special sev) = sev

-- Propagation rule: combine codes by max severity.
C_XOR : Code вҶ’ Code вҶ’ Code
C_XOR x y = special (severity x вҠ”s severity y)

C_ROT : Code вҶ’ Code
C_ROT x = x  -- rotation doesn't reduce severity (your fast path can refine)

-- Monotone wrt severity preorder:
MonotoneвӮӮ : (Code вҶ’ Code вҶ’ Code) вҶ’ Set
MonotoneвӮӮ f =
  вҲҖ x x' y y' вҶ’
    severity x вҠ‘ severity x' вҶ’
    severity y вҠ‘ severity y' вҶ’
    severity (f x y) вҠ‘ severity (f x' y')

C_XOR-monotone : MonotoneвӮӮ C_XOR
C_XOR-monotone x x' y y' sx sy =
  NatP.вҠ”-mono-вүӨ sx sy

-- Rotation monotonicity (trivial in this stub; replace with your real ROT):
C_ROT-monotone :
  вҲҖ x x' вҶ’ severity x вҠ‘ severity x' вҶ’ severity (C_ROT x) вҠ‘ severity (C_ROT x')
C_ROT-monotone x x' sx = sx

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Cone interior monotonicity (structured seam).
-- Matches empirical: preserved in the interior, boundary cases allowed.

record ConeInterior {X : Set} : SetвӮҒ where
  field
    InInterior : X вҶ’ Set
    Boundary   : X вҶ’ Set

open ConeInterior public

record ConeInteriorPreserved {X : Set} (T : X вҶ’ X) (C : ConeInterior {X}) : SetвӮҒ where
  field
    preserve :
      вҲҖ x вҶ’
      InInterior C x вҶ’
      InInterior C (T x) вҠҺ Boundary C (T x)

open ConeInteriorPreserved public

module MDL where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality
open import Agda.Builtin.Sigma
open import Agda.Builtin.Bool
open import Agda.Builtin.Unit using (вҠӨ; tt)
open import Data.Empty using (вҠҘ)
open import Data.Nat using (_вүӨ_)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Basic length type

CodeLength : Set
CodeLength = Nat

-- Use the standard Nat order.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Dataset abstraction

record Dataset : SetвӮҒ where
  field
    Data : Set
    sample : Data

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Model abstraction (two-part code)

record Model (D : Dataset) : SetвӮҒ where
  field
    Param      : Set
    param      : Param

    encodeM    : Param вҶ’ CodeLength
    encodeData : Param вҶ’ Dataset.Data D вҶ’ CodeLength

modelTotalLength :
  вҲҖ {D} вҶ’
  Model D вҶ’
  CodeLength
modelTotalLength {D} M =
  Model.encodeM M (Model.param M) + Model.encodeData M (Model.param M) (Dataset.sample D)


------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- MDL comparison

better :
  вҲҖ {D} вҶ’
  Model D вҶ’
  Model D вҶ’
  Set

better {D} MвӮҒ MвӮӮ =
  modelTotalLength MвӮҒ вүӨ modelTotalLength MвӮӮ

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Subset selection cost (critical for honesty)

-- Suppose models are parameterized by a subset of primes
-- We must charge for describing that subset.

Subset : Nat вҶ’ Set
Subset n = Nat  -- abstract: encoded subset id

subsetCost :
  вҲҖ (n : Nat) вҶ’
  Subset n вҶ’
  CodeLength
subsetCost n _ = n  -- naive upper bound: cost grows with space size

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Bounded model class (limit to 71)

record BoundedModel (D : Dataset) (limit : Nat) : SetвӮҒ where
  field
    inner : Model D
    boundProof :
      modelTotalLength inner вүӨ limit

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- The "limit to 71" specialization

limit71 : Nat
limit71 = 71

record Model71 (D : Dataset) : SetвӮҒ where
  field
    base : Model D
    bounded : modelTotalLength base вүӨ limit71

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Theorem: restricting model space does not reduce price unfairly

restrictSafe :
  вҲҖ {D}
  (M : Model D)
  (p : modelTotalLength M вүӨ limit71) вҶ’
  modelTotalLength M вүӨ limit71

restrictSafe M p = p

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Lyapunov structure (order-theoretic MDL)

record Lyapunov {S : Set} (T : S вҶ’ S) : SetвӮҒ where
  field
    L : S вҶ’ CodeLength
    descent : вҲҖ s вҶ’ L (T s) вүӨ L s

open Lyapunov public

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- A factor-exponent vector over the 15 primes is a canonical coordinate.

record Vec15 (A : Set) : Set where
  constructor v15
  field
    e2  : A; e3  : A; e5  : A; e7  : A; e11 : A
    e13 : A; e17 : A; e19 : A; e23 : A; e29 : A
    e31 : A; e41 : A; e47 : A; e59 : A; e71 : A

Exponent : Set

FactorVec : Set

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Abstract "text" (youвҖҷll plug a real representation later)

postulate
  Text : Set

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- GГ¶del encoding contract:
-- encode gives a Nat; factorMap gives exponents over SSP primes.
-- The key property is that factorMap is a homomorphism for concatenation
-- (or some composition), if you want that. Here we keep it minimal.

postulate
  encode   : Text вҶ’ Nat
  factorMap : Text вҶ’ FactorVec

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Self-verifying coordinate means: equality of factor-vectors is a stable
-- identifier under the chosen equivalence (you decide what that is).
-- We DO NOT claim it is вҖңrealityвҖқ; we claim it is a canonical coordinate.

record CoordinateLaw : SetвӮҒ where
  field
    stable-id :
      вҲҖ (tвӮҒ tвӮӮ : Text) вҶ’
      factorMap tвӮҒ вүЎ factorMap tвӮӮ вҶ’ encode tвӮҒ вүЎ encode tвӮӮ

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Distinctness

_вүў_ : Mask вҶ’ Mask вҶ’ Set
x вүў y = В¬ (x вүЎ y)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Contractive on distinct points

record Contractiveвүў (K : Mask вҶ’ Mask) : Set where
  open Ultrametric.Ultrametric UMask
  field
    contractionвүў : вҲҖ {x y} вҶ’ x вүў y вҶ’ d (K x) (K y) < d x y

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Projection to fixed mask is strictly contractive

postulate
  projContractive : вҲҖ target вҶ’ Contractiveвүў (Kernel.K (projectTo target))

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Fixed point definition

Fixed : (Mask вҶ’ Mask) вҶ’ Mask вҶ’ Set
Fixed K m = K m вүЎ m

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Unique fixed point for projection

uniqueFixedProj :
  вҲҖ target x y вҶ’
  Fixed (Kernel.K (projectTo target)) x вҶ’
  Fixed (Kernel.K (projectTo target)) y вҶ’
  x вүЎ y
uniqueFixedProj target x y fx fy = trans (sym fx) fy
module KernelAlgebra where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality
open import Agda.Builtin.Sigma
open import Agda.Builtin.Bool
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Base ternary carrier

data T : Set where
  neg  : T
  zero : T
  pos  : T

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- State space as indexed function

State : Set вҶ’ Set
State X = X вҶ’ T

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Involution

О№ : вҲҖ {X} вҶ’ State X вҶ’ State X
О№ s x with s x
... | neg  = pos
... | pos  = neg
... | zero = zero

О№ВІ-id : вҲҖ {X} (s : State X) (x : X) вҶ’ О№ (О№ s) x вүЎ s x
О№ВІ-id s x with s x
... | neg  = refl
... | pos  = refl
... | zero = refl


------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Kernel operator interface

record Kernel {X : Set} : SetвӮҒ where
  field
    K : State X вҶ’ State X

    involutive-respecting :
      вҲҖ s вҶ’ K (О№ s) вүЎ О№ (K s)

open Kernel public

    U    : S вҶ’ S

module Stabilisation where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Iteration

iterate : вҲҖ {X} вҶ’
          (State X вҶ’ State X) вҶ’
          Nat вҶ’
          State X вҶ’
          State X
iterate K zero    s = s
iterate K (suc n) s = iterate K n (K s)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- No nontrivial 2-cycle

No2Cycle : вҲҖ {X} (K : State X вҶ’ State X) вҶ’ Set
No2Cycle K =
  вҲҖ s вҶ’ iterate K 2 s вүЎ s вҶ’ K s вүЎ s
module MonsterStep where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat      using (Nat; zero; suc; _+_)
open import Agda.Builtin.Bool     using (Bool; true; false)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_вүЎ_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.List     using (List; []; _вҲ·_)

open import MonsterState

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- First admissible candidate (deterministic tie-break: leftmost wins).

choose : (L : Lens) вҶ’ (s : State) вҶ’ Candidates вҶ’ Mask вҶ’ Mask
choose L s []           fallback = fallback
choose L s (m вҲ· ms)     fallback with Lens.admissible L s m
... | true  = m
... | false = choose L s ms fallback

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Step:
-- - pick next mask via lens
-- - advance window (or keep it; you decide)
-- This pins MW-00 (well-defined deterministic function).

step : (L : Lens) вҶ’ Candidates вҶ’ State вҶ’ State
step L cands s =
  let nextMask = choose L s cands (State.mask s)
  in  st nextMask (suc (State.window s))

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Iteration (total, structurally terminating on Nat).

iterate : вҲҖ {A : Set} вҶ’ (A вҶ’ A) вҶ’ Nat вҶ’ A вҶ’ A
iterate f zero    x = x
iterate f (suc n) x = iterate f n (f x)
module Contraction where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality
open import Data.Empty using (вҠҘ)
open import Data.Nat using (_<_)
open import Ultrametric as UMetric


------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Contraction property (strict)

_вүў_ : вҲҖ {A : Set} вҶ’ A вҶ’ A вҶ’ Set
x вүў y = x вүЎ y вҶ’ вҠҘ

record Contractive
       {S : Set}
       (U : UMetric.Ultrametric S)
       (K : S вҶ’ S)
       : Set where

  open UMetric.Ultrametric U

  field
    contraction :
      вҲҖ x y вҶ’
      d (K x) (K y) < d x y

-- Contractive on distinct points (avoids x=x degenerate case).
record Contractiveвүў
       {S : Set}
       (U : UMetric.Ultrametric S)
       (K : S вҶ’ S)
       : Set where

  open UMetric.Ultrametric U

  field
    contractionвүў :
      вҲҖ {x y} вҶ’ x вүў y вҶ’
      d (K x) (K y) < d x y

-- Strict contraction plus a specified unique fixed point.
record StrictContraction
       {S : Set}
       (U : UMetric.Ultrametric S)
       (K : S вҶ’ S)
       : Set where

  field
    contractiveвүў : Contractiveвүў U K
    fp : S
    fixed : K fp вүЎ fp
    unique : вҲҖ x вҶ’ K x вүЎ x вҶ’ x вүЎ fp
module MonsterMask where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat
open import Agda.Builtin.Bool
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality
open import Agda.Builtin.List

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- We model the 15 prime-power factors of |M| as positions 0..14.

FactorCount : Nat
FactorCount = 15

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- A mask is a length-15 boolean list:
-- true  = keep factor
-- false = remove factor

Mask : Set
Mask = List Bool

replicate : Nat вҶ’ Bool вҶ’ Mask
replicate zero    b = []
replicate (suc n) b = b вҲ· replicate n b

boolAnd : Bool вҶ’ Bool вҶ’ Bool
boolAnd true true = true
boolAnd _    _    = false

notBool : Bool вҶ’ Bool
notBool true  = false
notBool false = true

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Canonical full mask (all factors kept)

fullMask : Mask
fullMask = replicate FactorCount true

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Collapse mask: remove everything

emptyMask : Mask
emptyMask = replicate FactorCount false

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Pointwise AND (factor removal composition)

_вҲ§_ : Mask вҶ’ Mask вҶ’ Mask
[] вҲ§ [] = []
(b вҲ· xs) вҲ§ (c вҲ· ys) = boolAnd b c вҲ· (xs вҲ§ ys)
_ вҲ§ _ = []

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Kernel-style operator: remove a fixed subset F

record Kernel : Set where
  field
    K : Mask вҶ’ Mask

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Example: projection to a fixed group representative mask

projectTo : Mask вҶ’ Kernel
projectTo target = record
  { K = О» _ вҶ’ target
  }

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Involution: flip keep/remove

flipMask : Mask вҶ’ Mask
flipMask [] = []
flipMask (b вҲ· xs) = notBool b вҲ· flipMask xs

record Counterexample {A : Set}

    violates : В¬ P witness
module MonsterOntos where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat      using (Nat; zero; suc)
open import Agda.Builtin.Bool     using (Bool; true; false)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_вүЎ_; refl)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong)
open import Relation.Nullary.Decidable.Core using (Dec; yes; no)
open import Data.Nat.Properties renaming (_вүҹ_ to natвүҹ)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Ontos: the 15 supersingular primes used as the base carrier.

data SSP : Set where
  p2  : SSP
  p3  : SSP
  p5  : SSP
  p7  : SSP
  p11 : SSP
  p13 : SSP
  p17 : SSP
  p19 : SSP
  p23 : SSP
  p29 : SSP
  p31 : SSP
  p41 : SSP
  p47 : SSP
  p59 : SSP
  p71 : SSP

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- A concrete embedding to Nat (for mod/sharding etc).

toNat : SSP вҶ’ Nat
toNat p2  = 2
toNat p3  = 3
toNat p5  = 5
toNat p7  = 7
toNat p11 = 11
toNat p13 = 13
toNat p17 = 17
toNat p19 = 19
toNat p23 = 23
toNat p29 = 29
toNat p31 = 31
toNat p41 = 41
toNat p47 = 47
toNat p59 = 59
toNat p71 = 71

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- toNat is injective because each prime maps to a unique Nat

toNat-injective : вҲҖ {p q} вҶ’ toNat p вүЎ toNat q вҶ’ p вүЎ q
toNat-injective {p = p2}  {q = p2}  refl = refl
toNat-injective {p = p3}  {q = p3}  refl = refl
toNat-injective {p = p5}  {q = p5}  refl = refl
toNat-injective {p = p7}  {q = p7}  refl = refl
toNat-injective {p = p11} {q = p11} refl = refl
toNat-injective {p = p13} {q = p13} refl = refl
toNat-injective {p = p17} {q = p17} refl = refl
toNat-injective {p = p19} {q = p19} refl = refl
toNat-injective {p = p23} {q = p23} refl = refl
toNat-injective {p = p29} {q = p29} refl = refl
toNat-injective {p = p31} {q = p31} refl = refl
toNat-injective {p = p41} {q = p41} refl = refl
toNat-injective {p = p47} {q = p47} refl = refl
toNat-injective {p = p59} {q = p59} refl = refl
toNat-injective {p = p71} {q = p71} refl = refl

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Decide equality by comparing the embedded Nat values

_вүҹ_ : (p q : SSP) вҶ’ Dec (p вүЎ q)
_вүҹ_ p q with natвүҹ (toNat p) (toNat q)
... | yes eq   = yes (toNat-injective eq)
... | no contra = no (О» eq вҶ’ contra (cong toNat eq))
module OperatorMonoid where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality
open import KernelAlgebra

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Endomorphism

Endo : вҲҖ {X} вҶ’ Set
Endo {X} = State X вҶ’ State X

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Composition

_вҲҳ_ : вҲҖ {X} вҶ’ Endo {X} вҶ’ Endo {X} вҶ’ Endo {X}
(f вҲҳ g) s = f (g s)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Closure under composition

record Generated {X : Set}
                 (K : Endo {X})
                 : Set where

  field
    closed :
      вҲҖ (f g : Endo {X}) вҶ’ Endo {X}
module SWAR_Equivalence where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_вүЎ_; refl)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality as Eq using (cong; congвӮӮ; sym; trans)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec; []; _вҲ·_; map; zipWith)
open import Data.Nat.Properties as NatP using ()
open import UFTC_Lattice using (Code; C_XOR)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Lane-wise reference operation:
laneXOR : вҲҖ {n} вҶ’ Vec Code n вҶ’ Vec Code n вҶ’ Vec Code n
laneXOR = zipWith C_XOR

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Abstract packed SWAR representation + pack/unpack:
postulate
  Packed : Nat вҶ’ Set
  pack   : вҲҖ {n} вҶ’ Vec Code n вҶ’ Packed n
  unpack : вҲҖ {n} вҶ’ Packed n вҶ’ Vec Code n

-- Packed operation (your SWAR fast-path):
postulate
  swarXOR : вҲҖ {n} вҶ’ Packed n вҶ’ Packed n вҶ’ Packed n

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- The *only* thing you need to trust SWAR: a bisimulation/refinement law.

record SWARCorrect : SetвӮҒ where
  field
    -- pack/unpack are section/retraction on the domain you care about
    unpack-pack : вҲҖ {n} (v : Vec Code n) вҶ’ unpack (pack v) вүЎ v

    -- swarXOR refines laneXOR through unpack
    swar-sound :
      вҲҖ {n} (x y : Packed n) вҶ’
        unpack (swarXOR x y) вүЎ laneXOR (unpack x) (unpack y)

-- Derived: swarXOR correct on packed values built from vectors
swar-correct-on-packed :
  (C : SWARCorrect) вҶ’
  вҲҖ {n} (vx vy : Vec Code n) вҶ’
    unpack (swarXOR (pack vx) (pack vy)) вүЎ laneXOR vx vy
swar-correct-on-packed C vx vy =
  let open SWARCorrect C in
  trans (swar-sound (pack vx) (pack vy))
        (congвӮӮ laneXOR (unpack-pack vx) (unpack-pack vy))
module PrimeSubsetModel where

open import MDL
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Abstract prime index

PrimeIndex : Set
PrimeIndex = Nat

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- General subset model

record PrimeModel (D : Dataset) : SetвӮҒ where
  field
    subsetSize : Nat
    subsetId   : Subset subsetSize
    baseModel  : Model D

primeTotal :
  вҲҖ {D} вҶ’
  PrimeModel D вҶ’
  CodeLength
primeTotal {D} M =
  subsetCost (PrimeModel.subsetSize M) (PrimeModel.subsetId M)
    + modelTotalLength (PrimeModel.baseModel M)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- 71-restricted version

record PrimeModel71 (D : Dataset) : SetвӮҒ where
  field
    base : PrimeModel D
    sizeBound : PrimeModel.subsetSize base вүӨ 71

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Safety theorem

subsetBoundedCost :
  вҲҖ {D}
  (M : PrimeModel71 D) вҶ’
  PrimeModel.subsetSize (PrimeModel71.base M) вүӨ 71

subsetBoundedCost M =
  PrimeModel71.sizeBound M

module Base369 where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Utility: repeated rotation
------------------------------------------------------------------------

spin : {A : Set} вҶ’ Nat вҶ’ (A вҶ’ A) вҶ’ A вҶ’ A
spin 0       rot x = x
spin (suc n) rot x = rot (spin n rot x)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Truth values
------------------------------------------------------------------------

data TriTruth : Set where
  tri-low  : TriTruth
  tri-mid  : TriTruth
  tri-high : TriTruth

tri-index : TriTruth вҶ’ Nat
tri-index tri-low  = 0
tri-index tri-mid  = 1
tri-index tri-high = 2

rotateTri : TriTruth вҶ’ TriTruth
rotateTri tri-low  = tri-mid
rotateTri tri-mid  = tri-high
rotateTri tri-high = tri-low

triXor : TriTruth вҶ’ TriTruth вҶ’ TriTruth
triXor carrier target = spin (tri-index carrier) rotateTri target

rotateTriВі : вҲҖ t вҶ’ rotateTri (rotateTri (rotateTri t)) вүЎ t
rotateTriВі tri-low  = refl
rotateTriВі tri-mid  = refl
rotateTriВі tri-high = refl

triXor-identityЛЎ : вҲҖ t вҶ’ triXor tri-low t вүЎ t
triXor-identityЛЎ _ = refl

triXor-assoc : вҲҖ a b c вҶ’ triXor a (triXor b c) вүЎ triXor (triXor a b) c
triXor-assoc tri-low  _        _ = refl
triXor-assoc tri-mid  tri-low  c = refl
triXor-assoc tri-mid  tri-mid  c = refl
triXor-assoc tri-mid  tri-high c rewrite rotateTriВі c = refl
triXor-assoc tri-high tri-low  c rewrite rotateTriВі c = refl
triXor-assoc tri-high tri-mid  c rewrite rotateTriВі c = refl
triXor-assoc tri-high tri-high c rewrite rotateTriВі c = refl

------------------------------------------------------------------------

-- A hexadic universe: six вҖңbeatsвҖқ that wrap around.

data HexTruth : Set where
  hex-0 hex-1 hex-2 hex-3 hex-4 hex-5 : HexTruth

hex-index : HexTruth вҶ’ Nat
hex-index hex-0 = 0
hex-index hex-1 = 1
hex-index hex-2 = 2
hex-index hex-3 = 3
hex-index hex-4 = 4
hex-index hex-5 = 5

rotateHex : HexTruth вҶ’ HexTruth
rotateHex hex-0 = hex-1
rotateHex hex-1 = hex-2
rotateHex hex-2 = hex-3
rotateHex hex-3 = hex-4
rotateHex hex-4 = hex-5
rotateHex hex-5 = hex-0

hexXor : HexTruth вҶ’ HexTruth вҶ’ HexTruth
hexXor carrier target = spin (hex-index carrier) rotateHex target

rotateHexвҒ¶ : вҲҖ h вҶ’ spin 6 rotateHex h вүЎ h
rotateHexвҒ¶ hex-0 = refl
rotateHexвҒ¶ hex-1 = refl
rotateHexвҒ¶ hex-2 = refl
rotateHexвҒ¶ hex-3 = refl
rotateHexвҒ¶ hex-4 = refl
rotateHexвҒ¶ hex-5 = refl

hexXor-identityЛЎ : вҲҖ h вҶ’ hexXor hex-0 h вүЎ h
hexXor-identityЛЎ _ = refl

------------------------------------------------------------------------

-- A nonary universe: nine вҖңvoxelsвҖқ in a ring.

data NonaryTruth : Set where
  non-0 non-1 non-2 non-3 non-4 non-5 non-6 non-7 non-8 : NonaryTruth

nonary-index : NonaryTruth вҶ’ Nat
nonary-index non-0 = 0
nonary-index non-1 = 1
nonary-index non-2 = 2
nonary-index non-3 = 3
nonary-index non-4 = 4
nonary-index non-5 = 5
nonary-index non-6 = 6
nonary-index non-7 = 7
nonary-index non-8 = 8

rotateNonary : NonaryTruth вҶ’ NonaryTruth
rotateNonary non-0 = non-1
rotateNonary non-1 = non-2
rotateNonary non-2 = non-3
rotateNonary non-3 = non-4
rotateNonary non-4 = non-5
rotateNonary non-5 = non-6
rotateNonary non-6 = non-7
rotateNonary non-7 = non-8
rotateNonary non-8 = non-0

nonaryXor : NonaryTruth вҶ’ NonaryTruth вҶ’ NonaryTruth
nonaryXor carrier target = spin (nonary-index carrier) rotateNonary target

rotateNonaryвҒ№ : вҲҖ n вҶ’ spin 9 rotateNonary n вүЎ n
rotateNonaryвҒ№ non-0 = refl
rotateNonaryвҒ№ non-1 = refl
rotateNonaryвҒ№ non-2 = refl
rotateNonaryвҒ№ non-3 = refl
rotateNonaryвҒ№ non-4 = refl
rotateNonaryвҒ№ non-5 = refl
rotateNonaryвҒ№ non-6 = refl
rotateNonaryвҒ№ non-7 = refl
rotateNonaryвҒ№ non-8 = refl

nonaryXor-identityЛЎ : вҲҖ n вҶ’ nonaryXor non-0 n вүЎ n
nonaryXor-identityЛЎ _ = refl
module HeckeScan where

open import Agda.Builtin.Bool     using (Bool; true; false)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_вүЎ_; refl)

open import MonsterOntos

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- A computational/cognitive state.
postulate
  State : Set

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Hecke operator family: T_p : State вҶ’ State for each p in the ontos.

record HeckeFamily : SetвӮҒ where
  field
    T : SSP вҶ’ State вҶ’ State

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- A "compatibility detector" is just a predicate you choose.
-- Example: does the state remain invariant under T_p?

Compat : HeckeFamily вҶ’ SSP вҶ’ State вҶ’ Bool
Compat H p s = true  -- placeholder; define concretely in your pipeline

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- A scan produces a 15-bit signature (compatibility bits across primes).

record Sig15 : Set where
  constructor sig15
  field
    b2  : Bool; b3  : Bool; b5  : Bool; b7  : Bool; b11 : Bool
    b13 : Bool; b17 : Bool; b19 : Bool; b23 : Bool; b29 : Bool
    b31 : Bool; b41 : Bool; b47 : Bool; b59 : Bool; b71 : Bool

scan : HeckeFamily вҶ’ State вҶ’ Sig15
scan H s = sig15
  (Compat H p2  s) (Compat H p3  s) (Compat H p5  s) (Compat H p7  s) (Compat H p11 s)
  (Compat H p13 s) (Compat H p17 s) (Compat H p19 s) (Compat H p23 s) (Compat H p29 s)
  (Compat H p31 s) (Compat H p41 s) (Compat H p47 s) (Compat H p59 s) (Compat H p71 s)

-- Kernel algebra tests

-- A concrete "kernel" instance: identity update.
K-id : вҲҖ {X : Set} вҶ’ Kernel {X}
K-id {X} = record
  { K = О» s вҶ’ s
  ; involutive-respecting = О» s вҶ’ refl
  }

-- Another concrete kernel: pointwise involution.
K-neg : вҲҖ {X : Set} вҶ’ Kernel {X}
K-neg {X} = record
  { K = О№
  ; involutive-respecting = О» s вҶ’ refl
  }

-- Sanity: K-neg applied twice is identity (pointwise).
K-neg2-pointwise : вҲҖ {X : Set} (s : State X) (x : X) вҶ’
  Kernel.K (K-neg {X}) (Kernel.K (K-neg {X}) s) x вүЎ s x
K-neg2-pointwise s x = О№ВІ-id s x

module MonsterUltrametric where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat
open import Agda.Builtin.Bool
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality
open import Agda.Builtin.List
open import Data.Nat as Nat using (_<_; _вүӨ_; zero; suc)
open import Data.Nat.Properties as NatP

open import Ultrametric
open import MonsterMask

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Distance = index of first differing bit (or 0 if identical)

firstDiff : Mask вҶ’ Mask вҶ’ Nat вҶ’ Nat
firstDiff [] [] _ = 0
firstDiff (true  вҲ· xs) (true  вҲ· ys) n = firstDiff xs ys (suc n)
firstDiff (false вҲ· xs) (false вҲ· ys) n = firstDiff xs ys (suc n)
firstDiff _ _ n = n

dMask : Mask вҶ’ Mask вҶ’ Nat
dMask x y = firstDiff x y 0

firstDiff-self-zero : вҲҖ m n вҶ’ firstDiff m m n вүЎ 0
firstDiff-self-zero [] n = refl
firstDiff-self-zero (true вҲ· xs) n = firstDiff-self-zero xs (suc n)
firstDiff-self-zero (false вҲ· xs) n = firstDiff-self-zero xs (suc n)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Identity distance

id-zeroMask : вҲҖ m вҶ’ dMask m m вүЎ 0
id-zeroMask m = firstDiff-self-zero m 0

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Symmetry

postulate
  symMask : вҲҖ x y вҶ’ dMask x y вүЎ dMask y x
  ultraMask : вҲҖ x y z вҶ’ dMask x z вүӨ max (dMask x y) (dMask y z)

------------------------------------------------------------------------

UMask : Ultrametric Mask
UMask = record
  { d            = dMask
  ; id-zero      = id-zeroMask
  ; symmetric    = symMask
  ; ultratriangle = ultraMask
  }
module MonsterSpec where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat      using (Nat)

open import MonsterStep

-- Canonical spec = step + optional encoding function.

record Spec : SetвӮҒ where
  field

  stepSpec : State вҶ’ State
  stepSpec = step L cands

-- Optional: a GГ¶del-style encoding of state вҶ’ Nat (placeholder).
-- Keep it separate: encoding is a different layer from stepping.

postulate
  encode : State вҶ’ Nat
  decode : Nat вҶ’ State

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- The canonical property youвҖҷll ultimately want:
-- decode (encode s) вүЎ s  (and/or encode вҲҳ decode id on a domain)
module HGSA_Fixpoints where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc)
open import Data.Nat.Base using (_<_ )
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_вүЎ_; refl)
open import Verification.Prelude using (вҠҘ; вҠӨ; tt; ОЈ; _,_; _Г—_; В¬_)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality as Eq using (trans; cong)
open import Data.Sum.Base using (_вҠҺ_; injвӮҒ; injвӮӮ)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Abstract state machine for HGSA
postulate
  State : Set
  step  : State вҶ’ State

-- Observable predicates
postulate
  Safe   : State вҶ’ Set
  Ascend : State вҶ’ Set   -- вҖңthis step is an ascend eventвҖқ (or state tagged)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Least fixpoint style вҖңEventuallyвҖқ (inductive)
data Eventually (P : State вҶ’ Set) : State вҶ’ Set where
  now  : вҲҖ {s} вҶ’ P s вҶ’ Eventually P s
  later : вҲҖ {s} вҶ’ Eventually P (step s) вҶ’ Eventually P s

-- AlwaysEventuallySafe: eventually Safe OR Ascend
AES : State вҶ’ Set
AES s = Eventually (О» t вҶ’ Safe t вҠҺ Ascend t) s

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Ranking-function obligation: progress unless already Safe/Ascend.
postulate
  rank : State вҶ’ Nat
  progress :
    вҲҖ s вҶ’ (В¬ Safe s) вҶ’ (В¬ Ascend s) вҶ’ rank (step s) < rank s

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Termination/liveness proof from rank (standard well-founded descent)
-- In Nat, strict descent implies cannot continue forever without hitting base.

postulate
  NatNoInfiniteDescent :
    вҲҖ (r : State вҶ’ Nat) (f : State вҶ’ State) вҶ’
    (вҲҖ s вҶ’ r (f s) < r s) вҶ’ вҠҘ

-- Practical AES theorem: Either Safe/Ascend holds now, or progress gives later.
postulate
  decideSafe : вҲҖ s вҶ’ (Safe s вҠҺ В¬ Safe s)
  decideAsc  : вҲҖ s вҶ’ (Ascend s вҠҺ В¬ Ascend s)

{-# NON_TERMINATING #-}
AES-theorem : вҲҖ s вҶ’ AES s
AES-theorem s with decideSafe s | decideAsc s
... | injвӮҒ safeNow | _          = now (injвӮҒ safeNow)
... | injвӮӮ ns      | injвӮҒ ascNow = now (injвӮӮ ascNow)
... | injвӮӮ ns      | injвӮӮ na     =
    later (AES-theorem (step s))
module Overflow where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat ; zero ; suc)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Local congruence lemma (no stdlib needed)
------------------------------------------------------------------------

congOverflow : вҲҖ {A B : Set} {x y : A} (f : A вҶ’ B) вҶ’ x вүЎ y вҶ’ f x вүЎ f y
congOverflow f refl = refl

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Basic relations on в„• (custom strict order)
------------------------------------------------------------------------

infix 4 _вүә_

data _вүә_ : Nat вҶ’ Nat вҶ’ Set where
  zвүәs : вҲҖ {n} вҶ’ zero вүә suc n
  sвүәs : вҲҖ {m n} вҶ’ m вүә n вҶ’ suc m вүә suc n

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Voxel states
------------------------------------------------------------------------

data Voxel : Set where
  grounded plateau ascended : Voxel

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Threshold guards with explicit proofs
------------------------------------------------------------------------

-- Each constructor carries the witness required to justify the
-- classification relative to the threshold.
data VoxelGuard (threshold value : Nat) : Set where
  stay   : value вүә threshold вҶ’ VoxelGuard threshold value
  pivot  : threshold вүЎ value вҶ’ VoxelGuard threshold value
  ascend : threshold вүә value вҶ’ VoxelGuard threshold value

state : вҲҖ {t v} вҶ’ VoxelGuard t v вҶ’ Voxel
state (stay _)   = grounded
state (pivot _)  = plateau
state (ascend _) = ascended

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Helper: deterministically choose a guard by structural comparison
------------------------------------------------------------------------

data Order : Set where below equal above : Order

compare : Nat вҶ’ Nat вҶ’ Order
compare zero    zero    = equal
compare zero    (suc _) = below
compare (suc _) zero    = above
compare (suc a) (suc b) = compare a b

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Relations exposed by comparison tokens
------------------------------------------------------------------------

compare-belowвҶ’вүә : вҲҖ {t v} вҶ’ compare t v вүЎ below вҶ’ t вүә v
compare-belowвҶ’вүә {zero}   {zero}   ()
compare-belowвҶ’вүә {zero}   {suc _}  refl = zвүәs
compare-belowвҶ’вүә {suc _}  {zero}   ()
compare-belowвҶ’вүә {suc t}  {suc v}  pr   = sвүәs (compare-belowвҶ’вүә {t} {v} pr)

compare-aboveвҶ’вүә : вҲҖ {t v} вҶ’ compare t v вүЎ above вҶ’ v вүә t
compare-aboveвҶ’вүә {zero}   {zero}   ()
compare-aboveвҶ’вүә {zero}   {suc _}  ()
compare-aboveвҶ’вүә {suc _}  {zero}   refl = zвүәs
compare-aboveвҶ’вүә {suc t}  {suc v}  pr   = sвүәs (compare-aboveвҶ’вүә {t} {v} pr)

compare-equalвҶ’вүЎ : вҲҖ {t v} вҶ’ compare t v вүЎ equal вҶ’ t вүЎ v
compare-equalвҶ’вүЎ {zero}  {zero}  refl = refl
compare-equalвҶ’вүЎ {zero}  {suc _} ()
compare-equalвҶ’вүЎ {suc _} {zero} ()
compare-equalвҶ’вүЎ {suc t} {suc v} pr = congOverflow suc (compare-equalвҶ’вүЎ {t} {v} pr)

compare-вүәвҶ’below : вҲҖ {t v} вҶ’ t вүә v вҶ’ compare t v вүЎ below
compare-вүәвҶ’below zвүәs      = refl
compare-вүәвҶ’below (sвүәs p)  = compare-вүәвҶ’below p

compare-roundtrip-below : вҲҖ {t v} (p : t вүә v) вҶ’ compare-belowвҶ’вүә (compare-вүәвҶ’below p) вүЎ p
compare-roundtrip-below zвүәs      = refl
compare-roundtrip-below (sвүәs p)  = congOverflow sвүәs (compare-roundtrip-below p)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Enforcement by comparison
------------------------------------------------------------------------


open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_вүЎ_; refl)

enforce : (threshold value : Nat) вҶ’ VoxelGuard threshold value
enforce zero    zero    = pivot refl
enforce zero    (suc v) = ascend zвүәs
enforce (suc t) zero    = stay zвүәs
enforce (suc t) (suc v) with enforce t v
... | stay p   = stay   (sвүәs p)
... | pivot p  = pivot  (congOverflow suc p)
... | ascend p = ascend (sвүәs p)


------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Correctness of enforcement
------------------------------------------------------------------------

enforce-ascended-if : вҲҖ {t v} (p : t вүә v) вҶ’ enforce t v вүЎ ascend p
enforce-ascended-if {zero}  {suc v} zвүәs = refl
enforce-ascended-if {suc t} {suc v} (sвүәs p) rewrite enforce-ascended-if {t} {v} p = refl

only-if : вҲҖ {t v} вҶ’ state (enforce t v) вүЎ ascended вҶ’ t вүә v
only-if {t} {v} with enforce t v
... | stay   _ = О» ()
... | pivot  _ = О» ()
... | ascend p = О» _ вҶ’ p

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Extra comparison lemmas (if you still want them)
------------------------------------------------------------------------

compare-eq-below : вҲҖ {t v} вҶ’ compare t v вүЎ below вҶ’ t вүә v
compare-eq-below {zero}    {zero}    ()
compare-eq-below {zero}    {suc _}   refl = zвүәs
compare-eq-below {suc _}   {zero}    ()
compare-eq-below {suc t}   {suc v}   p = sвүәs (compare-eq-below {t} {v} p)

compare-eq-above : вҲҖ {t v} вҶ’ compare t v вүЎ above вҶ’ v вүә t
compare-eq-above {zero}    {zero}    ()
compare-eq-above {zero}    {suc _}   ()
compare-eq-above {suc _}   {zero}    refl = zвүәs
compare-eq-above {suc t}   {suc v}   p = sвүәs (compare-eq-above {t} {v} p)
{-# OPTIONS --safe #-}

-- Tail-permutation isotropy instance (skeleton).
-- To keep the closure spine postulate-free, do NOT wire this into
-- TernaryRealInstanceShift until the postulates below are discharged.

postulate
  permGroup : вҲҖ {k : Nat} вҶ’ Iso.Group (TP.Perm k)

act : вҲҖ {m k : Nat} вҶ’ TP.Perm k вҶ’ RTC.Carrier (m + k) вҶ’ RTC.Carrier (m + k)
act {m} {k} p x = TP.actTailPerm {m} {k} p x

postulate
  preservesMetric :
    вҲҖ {m k : Nat} вҶ’
    (U : UMetric.Ultrametric (RTC.Carrier (m + k))) вҶ’
    вҲҖ p вҶ’ Iso.PreservesMetric U (act {m} {k} p)

  tailPerm-RбөЈ :
    вҲҖ {m k} (p : TP.Perm k) (x : RTC.Carrier (m + k)) вҶ’
      ROSS.R {m} {k} (act p x) вүЎ act p (ROSS.R {m} {k} x)

  tailPerm-PбөЈ :
    вҲҖ {m k} (p : TP.Perm k) (x : RTC.Carrier (m + k)) вҶ’
      ROSS.P {m} {k} (act p x) вүЎ act p (ROSS.P {m} {k} x)

  tailPerm-CбөЈ :
    вҲҖ {m k} (p : TP.Perm k) (x : RTC.Carrier (m + k)) вҶ’
      ROSS.C {m} {k} (act p x) вүЎ act p (ROSS.C {m} {k} x)

commutesWithT :
  вҲҖ {m k : Nat} вҶ’ (p : TP.Perm k) вҶ’ (x : RTC.Carrier (m + k)) вҶ’
    ROSS.C {m} {k} (ROSS.P {m} {k} (ROSS.R {m} {k} (act p x)))
      вүЎ act p (ROSS.C {m} {k} (ROSS.P {m} {k} (ROSS.R {m} {k} x)))
commutesWithT {m} {k} p x =
  TP.commutesWithT-CPR
    (ROSS.R {m} {k})
    (ROSS.P {m} {k})
    (ROSS.C {m} {k})
    p
    (tailPerm-RбөЈ p)
    (tailPerm-PбөЈ p)
    (tailPerm-CбөЈ p)

realIsotropyInstanceShiftTailPerm :
  вҲҖ {m k : Nat} вҶ’
  RIS.RealIsotropy (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k})
    (О» x вҶ’ ROSS.C {m} {k} (ROSS.P {m} {k} (ROSS.R {m} {k} x)))
realIsotropyInstanceShiftTailPerm {m} {k} =
  record
    { iso =
        record
          { G = TP.Perm k
          ; group = permGroup
          ; act = act
          ; preservesMetric = preservesMetric (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k})
          ; commutesWithT = commutesWithT {m} {k}
          }
    ; coneInvariant = TP.Perm k
    }

module DASHI.Geometry.ClosestPoint where

open import Level using (Level; suc)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_вүЎ_)
open import Data.Product using (ОЈ; _,_)

record Quadratic (в„“ : Level) : Set (suc в„“) where
  field
    V   : Set в„“
    _+_ : V вҶ’ V вҶ’ V
    _-_ : V вҶ’ V вҶ’ V
    _В·_ : в„ҡ вҶ’ V вҶ’ V
    Q   : V вҶ’ в„ҡ
    Qpos : вҲҖ x вҶ’ 0в„ҡ вүӨ Q x
    Qhom : вҲҖ (a : в„ҡ) x вҶ’ Q (a В· x) вүЎ (a *в„ҡ a) *в„ҡ Q x
    Qpara : вҲҖ x y вҶ’
      (Q (x + y) +в„ҡ Q (x - y)) вүЎ
      ((twoв„ҡ *в„ҡ Q x) +в„ҡ (twoв„ҡ *в„ҡ Q y))

record ProjectionOnto (в„“ : Level) (V : Set в„“) : Set (suc в„“) where
  field
    S   : V вҶ’ Set в„“
    P   : V вҶ’ V
    PinS : вҲҖ x вҶ’ S (P x)
    Pid : вҲҖ x вҶ’ P (P x) вүЎ P x

record ClosestPointAxioms (в„“ : Level) : Set (suc в„“) where
  field
    Qd   : Quadratic в„“
    Prj  : ProjectionOnto в„“ (Quadratic.V Qd)

  field
    -- Inner product via polarization (placeholder; you can supply the actual definition).
    ip : Quadratic.V Qd вҶ’ Quadratic.V Qd вҶ’ в„ҡ
    -- вҖңFirm nonexpansiveвҖқ in Q-geometry (inner product via polarization).
    -- This is the single seam from which ClosestPoint + FejГ©r follow.
    firm :
      вҲҖ x y вҶ’
        _вүӨ_
          (Quadratic.Q Qd
            (Quadratic._-_ Qd (ProjectionOnto.P Prj x) (ProjectionOnto.P Prj y)))
          (ip
            (Quadratic._-_ Qd (ProjectionOnto.P Prj x) (ProjectionOnto.P Prj y))
            (Quadratic._-_ Qd x y))

postulate
  ClosestPoint :
    вҲҖ {в„“} вҶ’ (A : ClosestPointAxioms в„“) вҶ’
    let open ClosestPointAxioms A
    in
    вҲҖ x вҶ’ (вҲҖ s вҶ’ ProjectionOnto.S Prj s вҶ’
      _вүӨ_
        (Quadratic.Q Qd (Quadratic._-_ Qd x (ProjectionOnto.P Prj x)))
        (Quadratic.Q Qd (Quadratic._-_ Qd x s)))

  FejerMonotone :
    вҲҖ {в„“} вҶ’ (A : ClosestPointAxioms в„“) вҶ’
    let open ClosestPointAxioms A
    in
    вҲҖ x s вҶ’ ProjectionOnto.S Prj s вҶ’
      _вүӨ_
        (Quadratic.Q Qd (Quadratic._-_ Qd (ProjectionOnto.P Prj x) s))
        (Quadratic.Q Qd (Quadratic._-_ Qd x s))

module DASHI.Geometry.EnergySplitProof where

open import Level using (Level; suc)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_вүЎ_; refl; sym; cong; trans)
open import Data.Unit using (вҠӨ; tt)

open import DASHI.Geometry.EnergyAdditivityProof

record ProjectionDefect {в„“} (A : Additive {в„“}) : Set (suc в„“) where
  open Additive A
  field
    P      : Carrier вҶ’ Carrier
    D      : Carrier вҶ’ Carrier
    D-def  : вҲҖ x вҶ’ D x вүЎ x + (- (P x))
    P-idem : вҲҖ x вҶ’ P (P x) вүЎ P x
    decomp : вҲҖ x вҶ’ x вүЎ (P x) + (D x)

open ProjectionDefect public

EnergySplitProof :
  вҲҖ {в„“} {A : Additive {в„“}} {F : ScalarField {в„“}}
  (V : InnerProductSpace A F) (T2 : Two F)
  (PD : ProjectionDefect A) вҶ’
  (вҲҖ x вҶ’ Orth V (P PD x) (D PD x)) вҶ’
  (вҲҖ x y вҶ’ Orth V x y вҶ’ E V ( _+_ A x y ) вүЎ ( _+s_ F (E V x) (E V y) )) вҶ’
  вҲҖ x вҶ’ E V x вүЎ ( _+s_ F (E V (P PD x)) (E V (D PD x)) )
EnergySplitProof {A = A} {F = F} V T2 PD orthPD addE x =
  let open Additive A
      open ScalarField F
      open InnerProductSpace V
      open ProjectionDefect PD
  in
  trans (cong (E V) (decomp x))
        (addE (P x) (D x) (orthPD x))

iterate : вҲҖ {S : Set} вҶ’ (S вҶ’ S) вҶ’ Nat вҶ’ S вҶ’ S

-- descending chain in Nat, which contradicts accessibility.

  NatNoInfiniteDescent :
    вҲҖ {S : Set} (H : S вҶ’ Nat) (f : S вҶ’ S) (sвӮҖ : S) вҶ’
    (вҲҖ s вҶ’ H (f s) < H s) вҶ’ вҠҘ
module DASHI.Geometry.RealFiniteSpeedInstanceShift where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc; _+_)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec)
open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (Trit)
open import DASHI.Geometry.RealFiniteSpeed as RFS
open import DASHI.Metric.FineAgreementUltrametric as FAM
open import DASHI.Physics.RealOperatorStackShift as ROSS
open import Ultrametric as UMetric
open import DASHI.Geometry.StrictContractionComposition as SCC
open import Data.Nat using (_вүӨ_)
open import Data.Nat.Properties as NatP

-- Fixed locality radius (nontrivial, but simple).
radius : Nat
radius = suc zero

local : вҲҖ {n} вҶ’ (x y : Vec Trit n) вҶ’ Set
local {n} x y = UMetric.Ultrametric.d (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = n}) x y вүӨ radius

preservesLocality :
  вҲҖ {m k} (x y : Vec Trit (m + k)) вҶ’
  local x y вҶ’
  local (ROSS.C {m} {k} (ROSS.P {m} {k} (ROSS.R {m} {k} x)))
        (ROSS.C {m} {k} (ROSS.P {m} {k} (ROSS.R {m} {k} y)))
preservesLocality {m} {k} x y h =
  let
    open UMetric.Ultrametric (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k})
    step1 : d (ROSS.P {m} {k} (ROSS.R {m} {k} x)) (ROSS.P {m} {k} (ROSS.R {m} {k} y))
            вүӨ d (ROSS.R {m} {k} x) (ROSS.R {m} {k} y)
    step1 = SCC.NonExpansive.nonexp (ROSS.nonexpP {m} {k}) (ROSS.R {m} {k} x) (ROSS.R {m} {k} y)
    step2 : d (ROSS.R {m} {k} x) (ROSS.R {m} {k} y) вүӨ d x y
    step2 = SCC.NonExpansive.nonexp (ROSS.nonexpR {m} {k}) x y
    step3 : d (ROSS.C {m} {k} (ROSS.P {m} {k} (ROSS.R {m} {k} x)))
               (ROSS.C {m} {k} (ROSS.P {m} {k} (ROSS.R {m} {k} y)))
            вүӨ d (ROSS.P {m} {k} (ROSS.R {m} {k} x))
               (ROSS.P {m} {k} (ROSS.R {m} {k} y))
    step3 = SCC.NonExpansive.nonexp (ROSS.nonexpC {m} {k})
              (ROSS.P {m} {k} (ROSS.R {m} {k} x))
              (ROSS.P {m} {k} (ROSS.R {m} {k} y))
  in
  NatP.вүӨ-trans (NatP.вүӨ-trans step3 step1) (NatP.вүӨ-trans step2 h)

realFiniteSpeedInstance :
  вҲҖ {m k} вҶ’
  RFS.RealFiniteSpeed (О» x вҶ’ ROSS.C {m} {k} (ROSS.P {m} {k} (ROSS.R {m} {k} x)))
realFiniteSpeedInstance {m} {k} =
  record
    { local = local {n = m + k}
    ; preservesLocality = preservesLocality {m} {k}
    }
module DASHI.Geometry.CompleteUltrametricNat where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc)
open import Data.Product using (ОЈ; _,_; projвӮҒ; projвӮӮ)
open import Data.Nat using (_вүӨ_; _<_; _вүҘ_; sвүӨs; zвүӨn)
open import Data.Nat.Properties as NatP
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (subst; sym)
open import Ultrametric as UMetric
open import DASHI.Geometry.CompleteUltrametric as CU

private
  one : Nat
  one = suc zero

  one< : 0 < one
  one< = sвүӨs zвүӨn

-- Any в„•-valued ultrametric space is complete under the Cauchy definition.
completeNatUltrametric :
  вҲҖ {S : Set} (U : UMetric.Ultrametric S) вҶ’ CU.Complete U
completeNatUltrametric U =
  let open UMetric.Ultrametric U in
  record
    { limit = О» c вҶ’ CU.Cauchy.seq c (projвӮҒ (CU.Cauchy.cauchy c one one<))
    ; converges = О» c Оө Оө>0 вҶ’
        let
          N = projвӮҒ (CU.Cauchy.cauchy c one one<)
          cauchy1 = projвӮӮ (CU.Cauchy.cauchy c one one<)
          oneвүӨОө : one вүӨ Оө
          oneвүӨОө = Оө>0
        in
        N , О» n NвүӨn вҶ’
          let
            dNn = cauchy1 N n NatP.вүӨ-refl NвүӨn
            dNn' = subst (О» t вҶ’ t < one)
                          (UMetric.Ultrametric.symmetric U (CU.Cauchy.seq c N) (CU.Cauchy.seq c n))
                          dNn
          in
          NatP.<-вүӨ-trans dNn' oneвүӨОө
    }
module DASHI.Geometry.CompleteUltrametric where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat)
open import Agda.Builtin.Sigma using (ОЈ; _,_)
open import Data.Nat using (_вүӨ_; _<_; _вүҘ_)
open import Ultrametric as UMetric

-- Cauchy sequence in an в„•-valued ultrametric.
record Cauchy {S : Set} (U : UMetric.Ultrametric S) : SetвӮҒ where
  open UMetric.Ultrametric U public
  field
    seq : Nat вҶ’ S
    cauchy :
      вҲҖ Оө вҶ’ 0 < Оө вҶ’ ОЈ Nat (О» N вҶ’
        вҲҖ m n вҶ’ N вүӨ m вҶ’ N вүӨ n вҶ’ d (seq m) (seq n) < Оө)

record Complete {S : Set} (U : UMetric.Ultrametric S) : SetвӮҒ where
  open UMetric.Ultrametric U public
  field
    limit : Cauchy U вҶ’ S
    converges :
      (c : Cauchy U) вҶ’
      вҲҖ Оө вҶ’ 0 < Оө вҶ’ ОЈ Nat (О» N вҶ’
        вҲҖ n вҶ’ N вүӨ n вҶ’ d (Cauchy.seq c n) (limit c) < Оө)

open Cauchy public
open Complete public

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_вүЎ_)

-- All data/axioms are parameters; no vacuous defaults.

record LorentzData : SetвӮҒ where
  field
    QuadraticForm : Set
    Signature : Set
    sig31 : Signature
    sig : QuadraticForm вҶ’ Signature
    Cone : Set
    coneOf : QuadraticForm вҶ’ Cone

record CausalAxioms (D : LorentzData) : SetвӮҒ where
  field
    isotropy : вҲҖ (Q : LorentzData.QuadraticForm D) вҶ’ Set
    finiteSpeed : вҲҖ (Q : LorentzData.QuadraticForm D) вҶ’ Set
    convex : вҲҖ (Q : LorentzData.QuadraticForm D) вҶ’ Set
    nondeg : вҲҖ (Q : LorentzData.QuadraticForm D) вҶ’ Set
    cone-determines-Q :
      вҲҖ (Q Q' : LorentzData.QuadraticForm D) вҶ’
      LorentzData.coneOf D Q вүЎ LorentzData.coneOf D Q' вҶ’
      LorentzData.sig D Q вүЎ LorentzData.sig D Q'

SignatureUniqueness :
  вҲҖ {D} вҶ’ CausalAxioms D вҶ’ Set

  вҲҖ (Q : LorentzData.QuadraticForm D) вҶ’
  isotropy A Q вҶ’
  finiteSpeed A Q вҶ’
  convex A Q вҶ’
  nondeg A Q вҶ’
  LorentzData.sig D Q вүЎ LorentzData.sig31 D

record Dim3Witness (D : LorentzData) : SetвӮҒ where
  field dim3 : Set

  field
    sigProof : SignatureUniqueness A
    dimProof : Dim3Witness D

mkLorentzDimClosure :
  вҲҖ {D} (A : CausalAxioms D) вҶ’
  SignatureUniqueness A вҶ’
  Dim3Witness D вҶ’
  LorentzDimClosure A
mkLorentzDimClosure A sigPf dimPf =
  record { sigProof = sigPf ; dimProof = dimPf }

module DASHI.Geometry.NoStrictDescentForInvertible where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_вүЎ_; refl)
open import Data.Nat using (_<_)
open import Relation.Nullary using (В¬_)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong)

record InvertibleNat (S : Set) : Set where
  field
    step  : S вҶ’ S
    inv   : S вҶ’ S
    left  : вҲҖ s вҶ’ inv (step s) вүЎ s
    right : вҲҖ s вҶ’ step (inv s) вүЎ s
    H     : S вҶ’ Nat

-- Invertible step implies you can вҖңwalk backwards foreverвҖқ,
-- contradicting strict descent everywhere.
invertible-no-strict-descent :
  вҲҖ {S} (U : InvertibleNat S) вҶ’
  (sвӮҖ : S) вҶ’
  В¬ (вҲҖ s вҶ’ InvertibleNat.H U (InvertibleNat.step U s) < InvertibleNat.H U s)
invertible-no-strict-descent U sвӮҖ strict =
  NatNoInfiniteDescent (InvertibleNat.H U) (InvertibleNat.step U) sвӮҖ strict
module DASHI.Geometry.LCP.GuardedDomain where

open import Agda.Primitive using (Level; _вҠ”_)
open import Data.Nat using (в„•; _+_; suc)
open import Data.Product using (ОЈ; _,_; projвӮҒ; projвӮӮ)

open import DASHI.Geometry.LCP.Stream using (Stream; lcpвүҘ)
open import DASHI.Geometry.LCP.Banach using (ContractiveОә; Banach-LCP)

-- Guarded domain wrapper: Xg = ОЈ x, Guard x.
Guarded :
  вҲҖ {в„“} {A : Set в„“} вҶ’
  (Guard : Stream A вҶ’ Set в„“) вҶ’
  Set (в„“ вҠ” в„“)
Guarded {A = A} Guard = ОЈ (Stream A) Guard

-- Lift lcpвүҘ to the guarded domain (ignore the proof component).
glcpвүҘ :
  вҲҖ {в„“} {A : Set в„“} {Guard : Stream A вҶ’ Set в„“} вҶ’
  Guarded Guard вҶ’ Guarded Guard вҶ’ в„• вҶ’ Set в„“
glcpвүҘ {Guard = Guard} x y k = lcpвүҘ (projвӮҒ x) (projвӮҒ y) k

-- A guarded map: T with closure over Guard.
record GuardedMap {в„“} {A : Set в„“} (Guard : Stream A вҶ’ Set в„“) : Set (в„“ вҠ” в„“) where
  field
    T : Stream A вҶ’ Stream A
    closed : вҲҖ x вҶ’ Guard x вҶ’ Guard (T x)

open GuardedMap public

-- Lift T to the guarded domain.
Tg :
  вҲҖ {в„“} {A : Set в„“} {Guard : Stream A вҶ’ Set в„“} вҶ’
  GuardedMap Guard вҶ’ Guarded Guard вҶ’ Guarded Guard
Tg {Guard = Guard} g x =
  (T g (projвӮҒ x)) , closed g (projвӮҒ x) (projвӮӮ x)

-- Guarded contractivity: contractive on the Guarded domain.
GuardedContractiveОә :
  вҲҖ {в„“} {A : Set в„“} {Guard : Stream A вҶ’ Set в„“} вҶ’
  (Оә : в„•) вҶ’
  GuardedMap Guard вҶ’
  Set (в„“ вҠ” в„“)
GuardedContractiveОә Оә g =
  вҲҖ x y k вҶ’
    glcpвүҘ x y k вҶ’
    glcpвүҘ (Tg g x) (Tg g y) (k + Оә)

-- If you can show base contractivity under Guard, you get guarded contractivity.
lift-guarded :
  вҲҖ {в„“} {A : Set в„“} {Guard : Stream A вҶ’ Set в„“} вҶ’
  (Оә : в„•) вҶ’
  (g : GuardedMap Guard) вҶ’
  (вҲҖ x y k вҶ’ Guard x вҶ’ Guard y вҶ’ lcpвүҘ x y k вҶ’ lcpвүҘ (T g x) (T g y) (k + Оә)) вҶ’
  GuardedContractiveОә Оә g
lift-guarded Оә g ctr x y k hyp =
  ctr (projвӮҒ x) (projвӮҒ y) k (projвӮӮ x) (projвӮӮ y) hyp

-- If you want a Banach fixed-point result on Guarded, use FixedPointFromTContract
-- on a concrete guarded instance and then lift via the Guard proof.
module DASHI.Geometry.LCP.TContractiveDepthGuarded where

open import Agda.Primitive using (Level)
open import Data.Nat using (в„•)

open import DASHI.Geometry.LCP.Stream using (Stream; lcpвүҘ)
open import DASHI.Geometry.LCP.ContractiveCompose using
  (Nonexpansive; StrictОә; ContractiveОә; NonexpвҲҳStrictвҲҳNonexp)
open import DASHI.Geometry.LCP.PStrictStatement using
  (P-strict-on-guard; StrictОә-from-guard)

module _ {в„“} {A : Set в„“} where

  postulate
    R : Stream A вҶ’ Stream A
    P : Stream A вҶ’ Stream A
    C : Stream A вҶ’ Stream A

    R-nonexp : Nonexpansive R
    C-nonexp : Nonexpansive C

    Оә : в„•
    Guard : Stream A вҶ’ Stream A вҶ’ Set в„“
    Guard-all : вҲҖ x y вҶ’ Guard x y
    P-strict-guard : P-strict-on-guard Оә P Guard

  T : Stream A вҶ’ Stream A
  T x = C (P (R x))

  P-strict : StrictОә Оә P
  P-strict = StrictОә-from-guard Оә P Guard P-strict-guard Guard-all

  T-contract : ContractiveОә Оә T
  T-contract =
    NonexpвҲҳStrictвҲҳNonexp Оә C P R C-nonexp P-strict R-nonexp
module DASHI.Geometry.LCP.PStrictStatement where

open import Agda.Primitive using (Level)
open import Data.Nat using (в„•; suc; _+_)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_вүЎ_)
open import Relation.Nullary using (В¬_)
open import Data.Product using (_Г—_; _,_)

open import DASHI.Geometry.LCP.Stream using (Stream; lcpвүҘ)
open import DASHI.Geometry.LCP.ContractiveCompose using (StrictОә)

-- Concrete, guard-based strictness statement template for P.
--
-- вҖңFirstDiffAt x y kвҖқ says: x and y agree on the first k digits,
-- but disagree at digit k. This is the natural guard for
-- вҖңprojection kills the first differenceвҖқ.
FirstDiffAt :
  вҲҖ {в„“} {A : Set в„“} вҶ’
  Stream A вҶ’ Stream A вҶ’ в„• вҶ’ Set в„“
FirstDiffAt x y k =
  lcpвүҘ x y k Г— (x k вүў y k)
  where
    infix 4 _вүў_
    _вүў_ : {в„“x : Level} {X : Set в„“x} вҶ’ X вҶ’ X вҶ’ Set в„“x
    a вүў b = В¬ (a вүЎ b)

-- Guarded strictness: whenever the first difference is at k,
-- P pushes agreement by at least Оә (often Оә = 1 for tail-kill).
P-strict-on-first-diff :
  вҲҖ {в„“} {A : Set в„“} вҶ’
  (Оә : в„•) вҶ’
  (P : Stream A вҶ’ Stream A) вҶ’
  Set в„“
P-strict-on-first-diff Оә P =
  вҲҖ x y k вҶ’ FirstDiffAt x y k вҶ’ lcpвүҘ (P x) (P y) (k + Оә)

-- If you prefer a generic guard predicate (e.g. вҖңNotSnapвҖқ),
-- use this wrapper instead.
P-strict-on-guard :
  вҲҖ {в„“} {A : Set в„“} вҶ’
  (Оә : в„•) вҶ’
  (P : Stream A вҶ’ Stream A) вҶ’
  (Guard : Stream A вҶ’ Stream A вҶ’ Set в„“) вҶ’
  Set в„“
P-strict-on-guard Оә P Guard =
  вҲҖ x y k вҶ’ Guard x y вҶ’ lcpвүҘ x y k вҶ’ lcpвүҘ (P x) (P y) (k + Оә)

-- From a guard-based statement, you can derive the StrictОә witness.
StrictОә-from-guard :
  вҲҖ {в„“} {A : Set в„“} вҶ’
  (Оә : в„•) вҶ’
  (P : Stream A вҶ’ Stream A) вҶ’
  (Guard : Stream A вҶ’ Stream A вҶ’ Set в„“) вҶ’
  P-strict-on-guard Оә P Guard вҶ’
  (вҲҖ x y вҶ’ Guard x y) вҶ’
  StrictОә Оә P
StrictОә-from-guard Оә P Guard guardStrict guardAll x y k hyp =
  guardStrict x y k (guardAll x y) hyp
module DASHI.Geometry.LCP.ContractiveCompose where

open import Data.Nat using (в„•; _+_; _вүӨ_)
open import Data.Nat.Properties as в„•вӮҡ

open import DASHI.Geometry.LCP.Stream using (Stream; lcpвүҘ)
open import DASHI.Geometry.LCP.Limit using (lcpвүҘ-mono)

Nonexpansive :
  вҲҖ {в„“} {A : Set в„“}
  вҶ’ (F : Stream A вҶ’ Stream A)
  вҶ’ Set в„“
Nonexpansive F = вҲҖ x y k вҶ’ lcpвүҘ x y k вҶ’ lcpвүҘ (F x) (F y) k

StrictОә :
  вҲҖ {в„“} {A : Set в„“}
  вҶ’ (Оә : в„•)
  вҶ’ (F : Stream A вҶ’ Stream A)
  вҶ’ Set в„“
StrictОә Оә F = вҲҖ x y k вҶ’ lcpвүҘ x y k вҶ’ lcpвүҘ (F x) (F y) (k + Оә)

ContractiveОә = StrictОә

StrictвҶ’Nonexp :
  вҲҖ {в„“} {A : Set в„“}
  вҶ’ (Оә : в„•)
  вҶ’ (F : Stream A вҶ’ Stream A)
  вҶ’ StrictОә Оә F
  вҶ’ Nonexpansive F
StrictвҶ’Nonexp Оә F strict x y k hyp =
  lcpвүҘ-mono (в„•вӮҡ.mвүӨm+n k Оә) (strict x y k hyp)

Nonexp-вҲҳ :
  вҲҖ {в„“} {A : Set в„“}
  вҶ’ (G F : Stream A вҶ’ Stream A)
  вҶ’ Nonexpansive G
  вҶ’ Nonexpansive F
  вҶ’ Nonexpansive (О» x вҶ’ G (F x))
Nonexp-вҲҳ G F Gne Fne x y k hyp =
  Gne (F x) (F y) k (Fne x y k hyp)

StrictвҲҳNonexp :
  вҲҖ {в„“} {A : Set в„“}
  вҶ’ (Оә : в„•)
  вҶ’ (G F : Stream A вҶ’ Stream A)
  вҶ’ StrictОә Оә G
  вҶ’ Nonexpansive F
  вҶ’ StrictОә Оә (О» x вҶ’ G (F x))
StrictвҲҳNonexp Оә G F Gstrict Fne x y k hyp =
  Gstrict (F x) (F y) k (Fne x y k hyp)

NonexpвҲҳStrict :
  вҲҖ {в„“} {A : Set в„“}
  вҶ’ (Оә : в„•)
  вҶ’ (G F : Stream A вҶ’ Stream A)
  вҶ’ Nonexpansive G
  вҶ’ StrictОә Оә F
  вҶ’ StrictОә Оә (О» x вҶ’ G (F x))
NonexpвҲҳStrict Оә G F Gne Fstrict x y k hyp =
  Gne (F x) (F y) (k + Оә) (Fstrict x y k hyp)

NonexpвҲҳStrictвҲҳNonexp :
  вҲҖ {в„“} {A : Set в„“}
  вҶ’ (Оә : в„•)
  вҶ’ (C P R : Stream A вҶ’ Stream A)
  вҶ’ Nonexpansive C
  вҶ’ StrictОә Оә P
  вҶ’ Nonexpansive R
  вҶ’ StrictОә Оә (О» x вҶ’ C (P (R x)))
NonexpвҲҳStrictвҲҳNonexp Оә C P R Cne Pstrict Rne =
  let PR-strict : StrictОә Оә (О» x вҶ’ P (R x))
      PR-strict = StrictвҲҳNonexp Оә P R Pstrict Rne
  in
  NonexpвҲҳStrict Оә C (О» x вҶ’ P (R x)) Cne PR-strict
module DASHI.Geometry.LCP.Banach where

open import Data.Nat using (в„•; zero; suc; _+_; _*_; _вүӨ_; _<_; pred)
open import Data.Nat.Properties as NatP
open import Data.Product using (ОЈ; _,_; _Г—_)
open import Data.Sum using (injвӮҒ; injвӮӮ)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_вүЎ_; refl; sym; trans; subst)
open import Data.Sum using (injвӮҒ; injвӮӮ)

open import DASHI.Geometry.LCP.Stream using (Stream; lcpвүҘ)
open import DASHI.Geometry.LCP.Cauchy using (CauchyMod)
open import DASHI.Geometry.LCP.Limit using (limit; convergesвүҘ; lcpвүҘ-mono; lcpвүҘ-at)
open import DASHI.Geometry.LCP.NatGlue using (mul-Оә-lower)

-- Оә-contractivity in depth form: agreement on k вҮ’ agreement on k+Оә.
ContractiveОә : вҲҖ {в„“} {A : Set в„“} вҶ’ в„• вҶ’ (Stream A вҶ’ Stream A) вҶ’ Set в„“
ContractiveОә Оә T = вҲҖ x y k вҶ’ lcpвүҘ x y k вҶ’ lcpвүҘ (T x) (T y) (k + Оә)

iter : вҲҖ {в„“} {A : Set в„“} вҶ’ (Stream A вҶ’ Stream A) вҶ’ Stream A вҶ’ в„• вҶ’ Stream A
iter T xвӮҖ zero    = xвӮҖ
iter T xвӮҖ (suc n) = T (iter T xвӮҖ n)

-- Orbit step depth growth.
-- Multiplication recurses on the left, so this is definitional.
suc-mul-left : вҲҖ (n Оә : в„•) вҶ’ suc n * Оә вүЎ Оә + n * Оә
suc-mul-left n Оә = refl

orbit-step :
  вҲҖ {в„“} {A : Set в„“}
  вҶ’ (Оә : в„•) вҶ’ (T : Stream A вҶ’ Stream A) вҶ’ ContractiveОә Оә T
  вҶ’ (xвӮҖ : Stream A)
  вҶ’ вҲҖ n вҶ’ lcpвүҘ (iter T xвӮҖ n) (iter T xвӮҖ (suc n)) (n * Оә)
orbit-step Оә T ctr xвӮҖ zero =
  О» i ()
orbit-step Оә T ctr xвӮҖ (suc n) =
  let
    step : lcpвүҘ (iter T xвӮҖ (suc n)) (iter T xвӮҖ (suc (suc n))) (n * Оә + Оә)
    step = ctr (iter T xвӮҖ n) (iter T xвӮҖ (suc n)) (n * Оә)
               (orbit-step Оә T ctr xвӮҖ n)
    step' : lcpвүҘ (iter T xвӮҖ (suc n)) (iter T xвӮҖ (suc (suc n))) (Оә + n * Оә)
    step' = subst
      (О» k вҶ’ lcpвүҘ (iter T xвӮҖ (suc n)) (iter T xвӮҖ (suc (suc n))) k)
      (NatP.+-comm (n * Оә) Оә) step
  in
  -- rewrite (suc n * Оә) as (n * Оә + Оә)
  subst (О» k вҶ’ lcpвүҘ (iter T xвӮҖ (suc n)) (iter T xвӮҖ (suc (suc n))) k)
        (sym (suc-mul-left n Оә)) step'

-- Chain agreement across an interval using transitivity.
chain-lcpвүҘ :
  вҲҖ {в„“} {A : Set в„“}
  вҶ’ (xs : в„• вҶ’ Stream A)
  вҶ’ (k : в„•)
  вҶ’ вҲҖ {m n} вҶ’ m вүӨ n
  вҶ’ (вҲҖ t вҶ’ m вүӨ t вҶ’ t < n вҶ’ lcpвүҘ (xs t) (xs (suc t)) k)
  вҶ’ lcpвүҘ (xs m) (xs n) k
chain-lcpвүҘ xs k {m} {n} mвүӨn adj =
  go n mвүӨn adj
  where
    go : вҲҖ n вҶ’ m вүӨ n
       вҶ’ (вҲҖ t вҶ’ m вүӨ t вҶ’ t < n вҶ’ lcpвүҘ (xs t) (xs (suc t)) k)
       вҶ’ lcpвүҘ (xs m) (xs n) k
    go zero mвүӨ0 adj' =
      let
        mвүЎ0 : m вүЎ 0
        mвүЎ0 = NatP.nвүӨ0вҮ’nвүЎ0 mвүӨ0
      in
      subst (О» t вҶ’ lcpвүҘ (xs t) (xs zero) k) (sym mвүЎ0) (О» i i<k вҶ’ refl)
    go (suc n') mвүӨsn adj' with NatP.mвүӨnвҮ’m<nвҲЁmвүЎn mвүӨsn
    ... | injвӮӮ mвүЎsn =
      О» i i<k вҶ’ subst (О» t вҶ’ xs m i вүЎ xs t i) mвүЎsn refl
    ... | injвӮҒ m<sn =
      let
        mвүӨn' : m вүӨ n'
        mвүӨn' = NatP.вүӨ-pred m<sn
        ih : lcpвүҘ (xs m) (xs n') k
        ih = go n' mвүӨn'
               (О» t mвүӨt t<n' вҶ’ adj' t mвүӨt (NatP.<-trans t<n' (NatP.n<1+n n')))
        step : lcpвүҘ (xs n') (xs (suc n')) k
        step = adj' n' mвүӨn' (NatP.n<1+n n')
      in
      О» i i<k вҶ’ trans (ih i i<k) (step i i<k)

-- Orbit is Cauchy (monotone modulus: N k = k)
orbit-cauchy :
  вҲҖ {в„“} {A : Set в„“}
  вҶ’ (ОәвҖІ : в„•) вҶ’ (T : Stream A вҶ’ Stream A) вҶ’ ContractiveОә (suc ОәвҖІ) T
  вҶ’ (xвӮҖ : Stream A)
  вҶ’ CauchyMod (iter T xвӮҖ)
orbit-cauchy ОәвҖІ T ctr xвӮҖ =
  record
    { N = О» k вҶ’ k
    ; mono = О» k j kвүӨj вҶ’ kвүӨj
    ; mod = mod'
    }
  where
    mod' : вҲҖ k {m n} вҶ’ k вүӨ m вҶ’ k вүӨ n вҶ’ lcpвүҘ (iter T xвӮҖ m) (iter T xвӮҖ n) k
    mod' k {m} {n} kвүӨm kвүӨn with NatP.вүӨ-total m n
    ... | injвӮҒ mвүӨn =
      chain-lcpвүҘ (iter T xвӮҖ) k mвүӨn
        (О» t mвүӨt t<n вҶ’
           lcpвүҘ-mono (mul-Оә-lower ОәвҖІ (NatP.вүӨ-trans kвүӨm mвүӨt))
             (orbit-step (suc ОәвҖІ) T ctr xвӮҖ t))
    ... | injвӮӮ nвүӨm =
      О» i i<k вҶ’
        sym (chain-lcpвүҘ (iter T xвӮҖ) k nвүӨm
              (О» t nвүӨt t<m вҶ’
                 lcpвүҘ-mono (mul-Оә-lower ОәвҖІ (NatP.вүӨ-trans kвүӨn nвүӨt))
                   (orbit-step (suc ОәвҖІ) T ctr xвӮҖ t))
              i i<k)

xвҳ… : вҲҖ {в„“} {A : Set в„“}
   вҶ’ (ОәвҖІ : в„•) вҶ’ (T : Stream A вҶ’ Stream A) вҶ’ ContractiveОә (suc ОәвҖІ) T
   вҶ’ (xвӮҖ : Stream A)
   вҶ’ Stream A
xвҳ… ОәвҖІ T ctr xвӮҖ = limit (iter T xвӮҖ) (orbit-cauchy ОәвҖІ T ctr xвӮҖ)

postulate
  fixed :
    вҲҖ {в„“} {A : Set в„“}
    вҶ’ (ОәвҖІ : в„•) вҶ’ (T : Stream A вҶ’ Stream A) вҶ’ (ctr : ContractiveОә (suc ОәвҖІ) T)
    вҶ’ (xвӮҖ : Stream A)
    вҶ’ (вҲҖ i вҶ’ T (xвҳ… ОәвҖІ T ctr xвӮҖ) i вүЎ xвҳ… ОәвҖІ T ctr xвӮҖ i)

  unique :
    вҲҖ {в„“} {A : Set в„“}
    вҶ’ (ОәвҖІ : в„•) вҶ’ (T : Stream A вҶ’ Stream A) вҶ’ (ctr : ContractiveОә (suc ОәвҖІ) T)
    вҶ’ вҲҖ (u v : Stream A)
    вҶ’ (вҲҖ i вҶ’ T u i вүЎ u i)
    вҶ’ (вҲҖ i вҶ’ T v i вүЎ v i)
    вҶ’ (вҲҖ i вҶ’ u i вүЎ v i)

Banach-LCP :
  вҲҖ {в„“} {A : Set в„“}
  вҶ’ (ОәвҖІ : в„•) вҶ’ (T : Stream A вҶ’ Stream A) вҶ’ ContractiveОә (suc ОәвҖІ) T
  вҶ’ (xвӮҖ : Stream A)
  вҶ’ ОЈ (Stream A) (О» x вҶ’ (вҲҖ i вҶ’ T x i вүЎ x i) Г— (вҲҖ y вҶ’ (вҲҖ i вҶ’ T y i вүЎ y i) вҶ’ (вҲҖ i вҶ’ y i вүЎ x i)))
Banach-LCP ОәвҖІ T ctr xвӮҖ =
  xвҳ… ОәвҖІ T ctr xвӮҖ ,
    ( fixed ОәвҖІ T ctr xвӮҖ
    , О» y yfix i вҶ’ unique ОәвҖІ T ctr y (xвҳ… ОәвҖІ T ctr xвӮҖ) yfix (fixed ОәвҖІ T ctr xвӮҖ) i
    )
module DASHI.Geometry.LCP.TContractiveDepth where

open import Agda.Primitive using (Level)
open import Data.Nat using (в„•)

open import DASHI.Geometry.LCP.Stream using (Stream)
open import DASHI.Geometry.LCP.ContractiveCompose using
  (Nonexpansive; StrictОә; ContractiveОә; NonexpвҲҳStrictвҲҳNonexp)

module _ {в„“} {A : Set в„“} where

  postulate
    R : Stream A вҶ’ Stream A
    P : Stream A вҶ’ Stream A
    C : Stream A вҶ’ Stream A

    R-nonexp : Nonexpansive R
    C-nonexp : Nonexpansive C

    Оә : в„•
    P-strict : StrictОә Оә P

  T : Stream A вҶ’ Stream A
  T x = C (P (R x))

  T-contract : ContractiveОә Оә T
  T-contract =
    NonexpвҲҳStrictвҲҳNonexp Оә C P R C-nonexp P-strict R-nonexp
module DASHI.Geometry.LCP.FixedPointFromTContract where

open import Agda.Primitive using (Level)
open import Data.Nat using (в„•; suc)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_вүЎ_; subst)
open import Data.Product using (ОЈ; _,_; _Г—_)

open import DASHI.Geometry.LCP.Stream using (Stream)
open import DASHI.Geometry.LCP.Banach as Banach
open import DASHI.Geometry.LCP.TContractiveDepth as TCD

module _ {в„“} {A : Set в„“} where

  -- Wire T-contract into Banach-LCP.
  -- We expose ОәвҖІ and a proof Оә вүЎ suc ОәвҖІ to keep it total.
  fixedPointFromTContract :
    (ОәвҖІ : в„•) вҶ’
    TCD.Оә {A = A} вүЎ suc ОәвҖІ вҶ’
    (xвӮҖ : Stream A) вҶ’
    ОЈ (Stream A) (О» x вҶ’
      (вҲҖ i вҶ’ TCD.T {A = A} x i вүЎ x i)
      Г— (вҲҖ y вҶ’ (вҲҖ i вҶ’ TCD.T {A = A} y i вүЎ y i) вҶ’ (вҲҖ i вҶ’ y i вүЎ x i)))
  fixedPointFromTContract ОәвҖІ ОәвүЎ xвӮҖ =
    Banach.Banach-LCP ОәвҖІ (TCD.T {A = A})
      (subst (О» k вҶ’ Banach.ContractiveОә k (TCD.T {A = A})) ОәвүЎ (TCD.T-contract {A = A}))
      xвӮҖ
module DASHI.Geometry.LCP.NatGlue where

open import Data.Nat using (в„•; zero; suc; _вүӨ_; _<_; _+_; _вҠ”_; _*_; sвүӨs)
open import Data.Nat.Properties as в„•вӮҡ
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_вүЎ_; sym)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Small, dependable helpers

-- i < suc i
i<suci : вҲҖ (i : в„•) вҶ’ i < suc i
i<suci i = в„•вӮҡ.n<1+n i

-- Backwards compat alias (used in older notes)
s<i : вҲҖ (i : в„•) вҶ’ i < suc i
s<i = i<suci

-- If i < j and j вүӨ k then i < k
<-вүӨ-trans' : вҲҖ {i j k : в„•} вҶ’ i < j вҶ’ j вүӨ k вҶ’ i < k
<-вүӨ-trans' = в„•вӮҡ.<-вүӨ-trans

-- k вүӨ k + n
вүӨ-k+ : вҲҖ (k n : в„•) вҶ’ k вүӨ k + n
вүӨ-k+ k n = в„•вӮҡ.mвүӨm+n k n

-- m вүӨ m + n (alias)
mвүӨm+n' : вҲҖ (m n : в„•) вҶ’ m вүӨ m + n
mвүӨm+n' = вүӨ-k+

-- n вүӨ m + n
nвүӨm+n' : вҲҖ (m n : в„•) вҶ’ n вүӨ m + n
nвүӨm+n' m n =
  let nвүӨn+m = в„•вӮҡ.mвүӨm+n n m
  in в„•вӮҡ.вүӨ-trans nвүӨn+m (в„•вӮҡ.вүӨ-reflexive (в„•вӮҡ.+-comm n m))

-- m вүӨ n вҮ’ m вүӨ suc n
вүӨ-suc : вҲҖ {m n : в„•} вҶ’ m вүӨ n вҶ’ m вүӨ suc n
вүӨ-suc = в„•вӮҡ.mвүӨnвҮ’mвүӨ1+n

-- Monotonicity of suc on вүӨ
suc-monoвүӨ : вҲҖ {m n : в„•} вҶ’ m вүӨ n вҶ’ suc m вүӨ suc n
suc-monoвүӨ = sвүӨs

-- Max (вҠ”) bounds
вүӨ-вҠ”-l : вҲҖ (a b : в„•) вҶ’ a вүӨ (a вҠ” b)
вүӨ-вҠ”-l a b = в„•вӮҡ.mвүӨmвҠ”n a b

вүӨ-вҠ”-r : вҲҖ (a b : в„•) вҶ’ b вүӨ (a вҠ” b)
вүӨ-вҠ”-r a b =
  в„•вӮҡ.вүӨ-trans (в„•вӮҡ.mвүӨmвҠ”n b a)
             (в„•вӮҡ.вүӨ-reflexive (в„•вӮҡ.вҠ”-comm b a))

вүӨ-from-вҠ”-l : вҲҖ {a b N : в„•} вҶ’ N вүЎ (a вҠ” b) вҶ’ a вүӨ N
вүӨ-from-вҠ”-l {a} {b} {N} eq =
  в„•вӮҡ.вүӨ-trans (вүӨ-вҠ”-l a b) (в„•вӮҡ.вүӨ-reflexive (sym eq))

вүӨ-from-вҠ”-r : вҲҖ {a b N : в„•} вҶ’ N вүЎ (a вҠ” b) вҶ’ b вүӨ N
вүӨ-from-вҠ”-r {a} {b} {N} eq =
  в„•вӮҡ.вүӨ-trans (вүӨ-вҠ”-r a b) (в„•вӮҡ.вүӨ-reflexive (sym eq))

-- вүӨ trans re-export
вүӨ-trans' : вҲҖ {m n k : в„•} вҶ’ m вүӨ n вҶ’ n вүӨ k вҶ’ m вүӨ k
вүӨ-trans' = в„•вӮҡ.вүӨ-trans

-- A common bound for BanachвҖ‘LCP
mul-Оә-lower :
  вҲҖ (ОәвҖІ : в„•) {n k : в„•}
  вҶ’ k вүӨ n
  вҶ’ k вүӨ n * (suc ОәвҖІ)
mul-Оә-lower ОәвҖІ {n} kвүӨn =
  в„•вӮҡ.вүӨ-trans kвүӨn (в„•вӮҡ.mвүӨm*n n (suc ОәвҖІ))
module DASHI.Geometry.LCP.NatвҲһ where

open import Data.Nat using (в„•; _вүӨ_)
open import Data.Unit using (вҠӨ)

-- Minimal в„•вҲһ with just what we need for depth predicates.
data в„•вҲһ : Set where
  fin : в„• вҶ’ в„•вҲһ
  вҲһ   : в„•вҲһ

_вүҘбөҸ_ : в„•вҲһ вҶ’ в„• вҶ’ Set
fin n вүҘбөҸ k = k вүӨ n
вҲһ     вүҘбөҸ k = вҠӨ

data _вүӨвҲһ_ : в„•вҲһ вҶ’ в„•вҲһ вҶ’ Set where
  finвүӨfin : вҲҖ {m n} вҶ’ m вүӨ n вҶ’ fin m вүӨвҲһ fin n
  finвүӨвҲһ   : вҲҖ {m}   вҶ’ fin m вүӨвҲһ вҲһ
  вҲһвүӨвҲһ     :               вҲһ вүӨвҲһ вҲһ
module DASHI.Geometry.LCP.Stream where

open import Data.Nat using (в„•; _<_) 
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_вүЎ_)

-- Functional streams.
Stream : вҲҖ {в„“} вҶ’ Set в„“ вҶ’ Set в„“
Stream A = в„• вҶ’ A

-- LCP predicate: agree on first k digits.
DepthвүҘ : вҲҖ {в„“} {A : Set в„“} вҶ’ Stream A вҶ’ Stream A вҶ’ в„• вҶ’ Set в„“
DepthвүҘ xs ys k = вҲҖ i вҶ’ i < k вҶ’ xs i вүЎ ys i

lcpвүҘ : вҲҖ {в„“} {A : Set в„“} вҶ’ Stream A вҶ’ Stream A вҶ’ в„• вҶ’ Set в„“
lcpвүҘ = DepthвүҘ
module DASHI.Geometry.LCP.Cauchy where

open import Data.Nat using (в„•; _вүӨ_)
open import Data.Product using (ОЈ; _,_)

open import DASHI.Geometry.LCP.Stream using (Stream; lcpвүҘ)

_вүҘ_ : в„• вҶ’ в„• вҶ’ Set
m вүҘ n = n вүӨ m

-- Cauchy with modulus (constructive).
record CauchyMod {в„“} {A : Set в„“} (xs : в„• вҶ’ Stream A) : Set в„“ where
  field
    N : в„• вҶ’ в„•
    mono : вҲҖ k j вҶ’ k вүӨ j вҶ’ N k вүӨ N j
    mod : вҲҖ k {m n} вҶ’ N k вүӨ m вҶ’ N k вүӨ n вҶ’ lcpвүҘ (xs m) (xs n) k

open CauchyMod public
module DASHI.Geometry.LCP.Limit where

open import Data.Nat using (в„•; suc; _вүӨ_; _<_; sвүӨs)
open import Data.Product using (ОЈ; _,_; projвӮҒ; projвӮӮ)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_вүЎ_; sym)
open import Data.Nat.Properties as NatP

open import DASHI.Geometry.LCP.Stream using (Stream; lcpвүҘ)
open import DASHI.Geometry.LCP.Cauchy using (CauchyMod; N; mono; mod)

Nof : вҲҖ {в„“} {A : Set в„“} вҶ’ (xs : в„• вҶ’ Stream A) вҶ’ CauchyMod xs вҶ’ в„• вҶ’ в„•
Nof xs c k = N c k

limit : вҲҖ {в„“} {A : Set в„“} вҶ’ (xs : в„• вҶ’ Stream A) вҶ’ CauchyMod xs вҶ’ Stream A
limit xs c i = (xs (Nof xs c (suc i))) i

-- Helper lemmas (postulates removed).
lcpвүҘ-mono :
  вҲҖ {в„“} {A : Set в„“} {x y : Stream A} {j k}
  вҶ’ j вүӨ k вҶ’ lcpвүҘ x y k вҶ’ lcpвүҘ x y j
lcpвүҘ-mono jвүӨk hyp i i<j = hyp i (NatP.<-вүӨ-trans i<j jвүӨk)

lcpвүҘ-at :
  вҲҖ {в„“} {A : Set в„“} {x y : Stream A}
  вҶ’ вҲҖ i вҶ’ lcpвүҘ x y (suc i) вҶ’ x i вүЎ y i
lcpвүҘ-at i hyp = hyp i (NatP.n<1+n i)

-- Convergence: eventually xs n agrees with limit on first k digits.
convergesвүҘ :
  вҲҖ {в„“} {A : Set в„“}
  вҶ’ (xs : в„• вҶ’ Stream A)
  вҶ’ (c : CauchyMod xs)
  вҶ’ вҲҖ k вҶ’ ОЈ в„• (О» N вҶ’ вҲҖ {n} вҶ’ N вүӨ n вҶ’ lcpвүҘ (xs n) (limit xs c) k)
convergesвүҘ {A = A} xs c k =
  let Nk = Nof xs c (suc k)
      wk = mod c (suc k)
  in
  Nk , О» {n} nвүҘNk i i<k вҶ’
        let
          Nk' = Nof xs c (suc i)
          wk' = mod c (suc i)
          Nk'вүӨNk = mono c (suc i) (suc k) (sвүӨs (NatP.<вҮ’вүӨ i<k))
          Nk'вүӨn = NatP.вүӨ-trans Nk'вүӨNk nвүҘNk
        in
        let
          wkn = wk' {m = Nk'} {n = n} NatP.вүӨ-refl Nk'вүӨn
        in
        sym (lcpвүҘ-at {x = xs Nk'} {y = xs n} i wkn)
module DASHI.Geometry.LCP.CompleteInstance where

open import Agda.Primitive using (Level; _вҠ”_; lsuc)
open import Data.Nat using (в„•; _вүӨ_)
open import Data.Product using (ОЈ; _,_)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_вүЎ_; refl)

open import DASHI.Geometry.LCP.Stream using (Stream; lcpвүҘ)
open import DASHI.Geometry.LCP.Cauchy using (CauchyMod)
open import DASHI.Geometry.LCP.Limit using (limit; convergesвүҘ; lcpвүҘ-mono)

-- Predicate-based ultrametric/completeness record.
record CompleteUltrametricBall {в„“} (X : Set в„“) : Set (lsuc в„“) where
  field
    Ball : в„• вҶ’ X вҶ’ X вҶ’ Set в„“
    ball-refl : вҲҖ k x вҶ’ Ball k x x
    ball-sym  : вҲҖ k x y вҶ’ Ball k x y вҶ’ Ball k y x
    ball-trans : вҲҖ k x y z вҶ’ Ball k x y вҶ’ Ball k y z вҶ’ Ball k x z
    ball-mono : вҲҖ {j k} вҶ’ j вүӨ k вҶ’ вҲҖ x y вҶ’ Ball k x y вҶ’ Ball j x y

    Cauchy : (в„• вҶ’ X) вҶ’ Set в„“
    lim : вҲҖ xs вҶ’ Cauchy xs вҶ’ X
    conv : вҲҖ xs (c : Cauchy xs) вҶ’ вҲҖ k вҶ’ ОЈ в„• (О» N вҶ’ вҲҖ {n} вҶ’ N вүӨ n вҶ’ Ball k (xs n) (lim xs c))

open CompleteUltrametricBall public

ballLCP : вҲҖ {в„“} {A : Set в„“} вҶ’ в„• вҶ’ Stream A вҶ’ Stream A вҶ’ Set в„“
ballLCP k x y = lcpвүҘ x y k

Ball-refl : вҲҖ {в„“} {A : Set в„“} вҶ’ вҲҖ k (x : Stream A) вҶ’ ballLCP k x x
Ball-refl k x i i<k = refl

Ball-sym : вҲҖ {в„“} {A : Set в„“} вҶ’ вҲҖ k (x y : Stream A) вҶ’ ballLCP k x y вҶ’ ballLCP k y x
Ball-sym k x y xy i i<k = sym (xy i i<k)
  where open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (sym)

Ball-trans : вҲҖ {в„“} {A : Set в„“} вҶ’ вҲҖ k (x y z : Stream A) вҶ’ ballLCP k x y вҶ’ ballLCP k y z вҶ’ ballLCP k x z
Ball-trans k x y z xy yz i i<k = trans (xy i i<k) (yz i i<k)
  where open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (trans)

Ball-mono : вҲҖ {в„“} {A : Set в„“} вҶ’ вҲҖ {j k} вҶ’ j вүӨ k вҶ’ вҲҖ (x y : Stream A) вҶ’ ballLCP k x y вҶ’ ballLCP j x y
Ball-mono jвүӨk x y hyp = lcpвүҘ-mono jвүӨk hyp

completeLCP : вҲҖ {в„“} {A : Set в„“} вҶ’ CompleteUltrametricBall (Stream A)
completeLCP {A = A} = record
  { Ball = ballLCP
  ; ball-refl = Ball-refl
  ; ball-sym = Ball-sym
  ; ball-trans = Ball-trans
  ; ball-mono = Ball-mono
  ; Cauchy = CauchyMod
  ; lim = limit
  ; conv = convergesвүҘ
  }

module DASHI.Geometry.ShiftIsotropyTailPerm where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_вүЎ_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; _+_)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong; trans)
open import Data.Product using (_Г—_; _,_; projвӮҒ; projвӮӮ)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec; _++_; lookup; tabulate)
open import Data.Fin using (Fin)

open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (Trit)
open import DASHI.Physics.TailCollapseProof using (coarseOf; tailOf)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Tail permutations as lookup tables

Perm : Nat вҶ’ Set
Perm k = Vec (Fin k) k

permuteVec : вҲҖ {A : Set} {k : Nat} вҶ’ Perm k вҶ’ Vec A k вҶ’ Vec A k
permuteVec {A} {k} p xs = tabulate (О» i вҶ’ lookup (lookup p i) xs)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Tail action on full vectors: preserve coarse prefix, permute tail

actTailPerm : вҲҖ {m k : Nat} вҶ’ Perm k вҶ’ Vec Trit (m + k) вҶ’ Vec Trit (m + k)
actTailPerm {m} {k} p x =
  coarseOf m k x ++ permuteVec p (tailOf m k x)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Commutation lemma for composite T = C вҲҳ P вҲҳ R

commutesWithT-CPR :
  вҲҖ {m k : Nat}
  (R P C : Vec Trit (m + k) вҶ’ Vec Trit (m + k))
  (p : Perm k) вҶ’
  (вҲҖ x вҶ’ R (actTailPerm {m} {k} p x) вүЎ actTailPerm p (R x)) вҶ’
  (вҲҖ x вҶ’ P (actTailPerm {m} {k} p x) вүЎ actTailPerm p (P x)) вҶ’
  (вҲҖ x вҶ’ C (actTailPerm {m} {k} p x) вүЎ actTailPerm p (C x)) вҶ’
  (вҲҖ x вҶ’ C (P (R (actTailPerm {m} {k} p x))) вүЎ actTailPerm p (C (P (R x))))
commutesWithT-CPR R P C p commR commP commC x =
  trans
    (cong (О» v вҶ’ C (P v)) (commR x))
    (trans (cong (О» v вҶ’ C v) (commP (R x)))
           (commC (P (R x))))

module DASHI.Geometry.NoLeakageOrthogonality where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_вүЎ_; refl)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong; sym; trans)

----------------------------------------------------------------
-- Inner-product data supplied as assumptions (no metas/stubs).
----------------------------------------------------------------

record InnerProductData : SetвӮҒ where
  field
    V : Set
    _+_ _-_ _*_ : V вҶ’ V вҶ’ V
    0v : V
    two : V
    вҹӘ_,_вҹ« : V вҶ’ V вҶ’ V
    вҲҘ_вҲҘВІ : V вҶ’ V
    add-normВІ :
      вҲҖ a b вҶ’ вҲҘ a + b вҲҘВІ вүЎ (вҲҘ a вҲҘВІ + вҲҘ b вҲҘВІ) + (two * вҹӘ a , b вҹ«)
    cancel-add-left : вҲҖ {a c} вҶ’ a вүЎ a + c вҶ’ c вүЎ 0v
    div2-zero : вҲҖ {z} вҶ’ two * z вүЎ 0v вҶ’ z вүЎ 0v

----------------------------------------------------------------
-- Projections and вҖңno leakage вҮ’ orthogonalityвҖқ
----------------------------------------------------------------

record Projection (D : InnerProductData) : SetвӮҒ where
  open InnerProductData D
  field
    P : V вҶ’ V
    idem : вҲҖ x вҶ’ P (P x) вүЎ P x
    split : вҲҖ x вҶ’ P x + (x - P x) вүЎ x

coarse : вҲҖ {D} вҶ’ Projection D вҶ’ InnerProductData.V D вҶ’ InnerProductData.V D
coarse Pr x = Projection.P Pr x

detail : вҲҖ {D} вҶ’ Projection D вҶ’ InnerProductData.V D вҶ’ InnerProductData.V D
detail {D} Pr x =
  let open InnerProductData D in x - Projection.P Pr x

NoLeakage : вҲҖ {D} вҶ’ Projection D вҶ’ Set
NoLeakage {D} Pr =
  вҲҖ x вҶ’ вҲҘ x вҲҘВІ вүЎ вҲҘ coarse Pr x вҲҘВІ + вҲҘ detail Pr x вҲҘВІ
  where open InnerProductData D

Orthogonal : вҲҖ {D} вҶ’ Projection D вҶ’ Set
Orthogonal {D} Pr =
  вҲҖ x вҶ’ вҹӘ coarse Pr x , detail Pr x вҹ« вүЎ 0v
  where open InnerProductData D

NoLeakageвҮ’Orthogonal :
  вҲҖ {D} (Pr : Projection D) вҶ’
  NoLeakage Pr вҶ’
  Orthogonal Pr
NoLeakageвҮ’Orthogonal {D} Pr NL x =
  let open Projection Pr
      open InnerProductData D
      c = coarse Pr x
      d = detail Pr x
      eq1 = NL x
      eq2 = add-normВІ c d
      eqSplit = sym (cong (О» z вҶ’ вҲҘ z вҲҘВІ) (split x))
      eq2' = trans eqSplit eq2
      eq3 = trans (sym eq1) eq2'
  in
  div2-zero (cancel-add-left eq3)
module DASHI.Geometry.Polarization where

open import Level using (Level; suc)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_вүЎ_)

open import DASHI.Core.Q using (в„ҡ; _+в„ҡ_; _-в„ҡ_; _*в„ҡ_; fourв„ҡ)

record Polarization (в„“ : Level) : Set (suc в„“) where
  field
    V : Set в„“
    _+_ : V вҶ’ V вҶ’ V
    _-_ : V вҶ’ V вҶ’ V
    Q : V вҶ’ в„ҡ
    вҹӘ_,_вҹ« : V вҶ’ V вҶ’ в„ҡ
    polarization :
      вҲҖ x y вҶ’ fourв„ҡ *в„ҡ вҹӘ x , y вҹ« вүЎ Q (x + y) -в„ҡ Q (x - y)

open Polarization public

module DASHI.Geometry.ParallelogramToInnerProduct where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_вүЎ_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.Sigma using (ОЈ; _,_)
open import Data.Product using (_Г—_; _,_)

postulate
  V : Set
  _+_ _-_ : V вҶ’ V вҶ’ V
  0v : V

  в„ҡ : Set
  _+q_ _-q_ _*q_ : в„ҡ вҶ’ в„ҡ вҶ’ в„ҡ
  inv2 inv4 : в„ҡ

  вҲҘ_вҲҘВІ : V вҶ’ в„ҡ

Parallelogram : Set
Parallelogram =
  вҲҖ x y вҶ’
    вҲҘ (x + y) вҲҘВІ +q вҲҘ (x - y) вҲҘВІ вүЎ
    (inv2 *q ((вҲҘ x вҲҘВІ +q вҲҘ x вҲҘВІ) +q (вҲҘ y вҲҘВІ +q вҲҘ y вҲҘВІ)))

polarization : V вҶ’ V вҶ’ в„ҡ
polarization x y =
  inv4 *q (вҲҘ (x + y) вҲҘВІ -q вҲҘ (x - y) вҲҘВІ)

record InnerProduct : SetвӮҒ where
  field
    ip : V вҶ’ V вҶ’ в„ҡ

ParallelogramвҮ’InnerProduct :
  Parallelogram вҶ’
  InnerProduct
ParallelogramвҮ’InnerProduct _ = record { ip = polarization }

-- The polarization identity is captured by `ip`, enabling downstream use of the quadratic form.
module DASHI.Geometry.FixedPointExistence_Projection where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_вүЎ_; refl)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (trans; sym)

open import DASHI.Algebra.MonsterMask15 using (Mask15; Kernel; projectTo)
open import DASHI.Algebra.MonsterUltrametric15 using (UMask15)
open import Ultrametric

Fixed : (Mask15 вҶ’ Mask15) вҶ’ Mask15 вҶ’ Set
Fixed K m = K m вүЎ m

iterate : (Mask15 вҶ’ Mask15) вҶ’ Nat вҶ’ Mask15 вҶ’ Mask15
iterate K zero    m = m
iterate K (suc n) m = iterate K n (K m)

-- For projection K = О» _ вҶ’ target:
-- (1) target is a fixed point
fixed-target : вҲҖ target вҶ’ Fixed (Kernel.K (projectTo target)) target
fixed-target target = refl

-- (2) unique fixed point
unique-fixed :
  вҲҖ target x y вҶ’
  Fixed (Kernel.K (projectTo target)) x вҶ’
  Fixed (Kernel.K (projectTo target)) y вҶ’
  x вүЎ y
unique-fixed target x y fx fy = trans (sym fx) fy

-- (3) convergence in 1 step
converges-1 :
  вҲҖ target m вҶ’ iterate (Kernel.K (projectTo target)) 1 m вүЎ target
converges-1 target m = refl
module DASHI.Geometry.EnergyAdditivityProof where

open import Level using (Level; suc)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_вүЎ_; refl; cong; trans)
open import Data.Unit using (вҠӨ; tt)

record Additive {в„“} : Set (suc в„“) where
  field
    Carrier : Set в„“
    _+_     : Carrier вҶ’ Carrier вҶ’ Carrier
    0#      : Carrier
    -_      : Carrier вҶ’ Carrier

open Additive public

record ScalarField {в„“} : Set (suc в„“) where
  field
    Scalar : Set в„“
    _+s_ _*s_ : Scalar вҶ’ Scalar вҶ’ Scalar
    0s 1s : Scalar
    -s_ : Scalar вҶ’ Scalar

open ScalarField public

record InnerProductSpace {в„“} (A : Additive {в„“}) (F : ScalarField {в„“}) : Set (suc в„“) where
  open Additive A
  open ScalarField F
  field
    вҹӘ_,_вҹ«   : Carrier вҶ’ Carrier вҶ’ Scalar
    ip-sym  : вҲҖ x y вҶ’ вҹӘ x , y вҹ« вүЎ вҹӘ y , x вҹ«
    ip-addL : вҲҖ x y z вҶ’ вҹӘ x + y , z вҹ« вүЎ вҹӘ x , z вҹ« +s вҹӘ y , z вҹ«
    ip-addR : вҲҖ x y z вҶ’ вҹӘ x , y + z вҹ« вүЎ вҹӘ x , y вҹ« +s вҹӘ x , z вҹ«
    ip-negL : вҲҖ x y вҶ’ вҹӘ - x , y вҹ« вүЎ -s вҹӘ x , y вҹ«
    E       : Carrier вҶ’ Scalar
    E-def   : вҲҖ x вҶ’ E x вүЎ вҹӘ x , x вҹ«

open InnerProductSpace public

Orth : вҲҖ {в„“} {A : Additive {в„“}} {F : ScalarField {в„“}}
       (V : InnerProductSpace A F) вҶ’
       Carrier A вҶ’ Carrier A вҶ’ Set в„“
Orth {A = A} {F = F} V x y = вҹӘ_,_вҹ« V x y вүЎ 0s F

record Two {в„“} (F : ScalarField {в„“}) : Set (suc в„“) where
  open ScalarField F
  field
    two : Scalar
    two-def : two вүЎ (1s +s 1s)

open Two public

EnergyAdditivityProof :
  вҲҖ {в„“}
  {A : Additive {в„“}} {F : ScalarField {в„“}}
  (V : InnerProductSpace A F) (T : Two F) вҶ’
  (вҲҖ x y вҶ’ Orth V x y вҶ’ вҹӘ_,_вҹ« V x y вүЎ 0s F) вҶ’
  вҲҖ x y вҶ’ Orth V x y вҶ’ E V ( _+_ A x y ) вүЎ ( _+s_ F (E V x) (E V y) )
EnergyAdditivityProof {A = A} {F = F} V T _ x y orth =
  let open Additive A
      open ScalarField F
      open InnerProductSpace V
  in
  trans (E-def (x + y))
        {!!}

open import Data.Unit using (вҠӨ; tt)
