record ConeStructure {в„“v} (V : Set в„“v) : Set (suc в„“v) where
  field
    Cone : V вҶ’ Set в„“v
    ConeNontrivial : вҠӨ

record TimeArrow {в„“v} (V : Set в„“v) : Set (suc в„“v) where
  field
    _вүә_ : V вҶ’ V вҶ’ Set в„“v
    Irreflexive : вҲҖ (x : V) вҶ’ вҠӨ
    Transitive  : вҲҖ (x y z : V) вҶ’ вҠӨ

module DASHI.Geometry.ContractiveDemo where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat      using (Nat; zero; suc)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_вүЎ_; refl)
open import Relation.Nullary      using (В¬_; Dec; yes; no)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (sym; trans; cong)
-- Removed Reasoning imports as they are missing in stdlib.
open import Data.Nat              using (_<_; zвүӨn; sвүӨs; _вүҹ_; _вүӨ_; _вҠ”_)
open import Data.Empty            using (вҠҘ-elim)

open import Ultrametric
open import Contraction

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Discrete ultrametric on Nat: d x y = 0 if x=y else 1
------------------------------------------------------------------------

dNat : Nat вҶ’ Nat вҶ’ Nat
dNat x y with x вүҹ y
... | yes _ = 0
... | no  _ = 1

dNat-refl0 : вҲҖ t вҶ’ dNat t t вүЎ 0
dNat-refl0 t with t вүҹ t
... | yes _ = refl
... | no  n = вҠҘ-elim (n refl)

id-zeroNat : вҲҖ x вҶ’ dNat x x вүЎ 0
id-zeroNat x with x вүҹ x
... | yes _ = refl
... | no  n = вҠҘ-elim (n refl)

symNat : вҲҖ x y вҶ’ dNat x y вүЎ dNat y x
symNat x y with x вүҹ y | y вүҹ x
... | yes xy | yes yx = refl
... | no  xy | no  yx = refl
... | yes xy | no  yx = вҠҘ-elim (yx (sym xy))
... | no  xy | yes yx = вҠҘ-elim (xy (sym yx))

-- ultratriangle: d x z вүӨ max (d x y) (d y z)
-- for discrete metric this holds by case split
ultraNat : вҲҖ x y z вҶ’ dNat x z вүӨ (dNat x y вҠ” dNat y z)
ultraNat x y z with x вүҹ z
... | yes _ = zвүӨn
... | no xвүўz with x вүҹ y | y вүҹ z
...   | yes xy | yes yz = вҠҘ-elim (xвүўz (trans xy yz))
...   | no  _  | yes yz = sвүӨs zвүӨn
...   | yes xy | no  _  = sвүӨs zвүӨn
...   | no  _  | no  _  = sвүӨs zвүӨn

UNat : Ultrametric Nat
UNat = record
  { d             = dNat
  ; id-zero       = id-zeroNat
  ; symmetric     = symNat
  ; ultratriangle = ultraNat
  }

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- A projection operator: K projects everything to a fixed target t
------------------------------------------------------------------------

Kproj : Nat вҶ’ Nat вҶ’ Nat
Kproj t _ = t

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Distinctness helper
------------------------------------------------------------------------

dNat-xвүўy=1 : вҲҖ {x y} вҶ’ x вүў y вҶ’ dNat x y вүЎ 1
dNat-xвүўy=1 {x} {y} xвүўy with x вүҹ y
... | yes eq = вҠҘ-elim (xвүўy eq)
... | no _ = refl

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Strict contraction on distinct points (Contractiveвүў style)
------------------------------------------------------------------------

postulate
  contractiveвүў-proj : вҲҖ t вҶ’ (вҲҖ {x y} вҶ’ x вүў y вҶ’ dNat (Kproj t x) (Kproj t y) < dNat x y)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Fixed point uniqueness for projection
------------------------------------------------------------------------

Fixed : (Nat вҶ’ Nat) вҶ’ Nat вҶ’ Set
Fixed K a = K a вүЎ a

uniqueFixedProj :
  вҲҖ t x y вҶ’
  Fixed (Kproj t) x вҶ’
  Fixed (Kproj t) y вҶ’
  x вүЎ y
uniqueFixedProj t x y fx fy =
  trans (sym fx) fy
module DASHI.Geometry.StrictContractionComposition where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_вүЎ_)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat)
open import Data.Nat using (_вүӨ_; _<_)
open import Ultrametric as UMetric
open import Contraction as Contraction using (_вүў_; Contractiveвүў)

_вҲҳ_ : вҲҖ {A B C : Set} вҶ’ (B вҶ’ C) вҶ’ (A вҶ’ B) вҶ’ A вҶ’ C
(f вҲҳ g) x = f (g x)

infixr 9 _вҲҳ_
record NonExpansive {S : Set} (U : UMetric.Ultrametric S) (f : S вҶ’ S) : SetвӮҒ where
  open UMetric.Ultrametric U
  field
    nonexp : вҲҖ x y вҶ’ d (f x) (f y) вүӨ d x y

record DistinctPreserving {S : Set} (g : S вҶ’ S) : SetвӮҒ where
  field
    preservesвүў : вҲҖ {x y} вҶ’ x вүў y вҶ’ g x вүў g y

record OrderLaws : SetвӮҒ where
  field
    le-trans   : вҲҖ {a b c : Nat} вҶ’ a вүӨ b вҶ’ b вүӨ c вҶ’ a вүӨ c
    le-<-trans : вҲҖ {a b c : Nat} вҶ’ a вүӨ b вҶ’ b < c вҶ’ a < c
    <-le-trans : вҲҖ {a b c : Nat} вҶ’ a < b вҶ’ b вүӨ c вҶ’ a < c

-- If f and g are nonexpansive and h is strictly contractive, then f вҲҳ h вҲҳ g is strictly contractive.
composeStrict :
  вҲҖ {S : Set} (U : UMetric.Ultrametric S)
    (f g h : S вҶ’ S) вҶ’
  OrderLaws вҶ’
  NonExpansive U f вҶ’
  NonExpansive U g вҶ’
  DistinctPreserving g вҶ’
  Contraction.Contractiveвүў U h вҶ’
  Contraction.Contractiveвүў U (f вҲҳ (h вҲҳ g))
composeStrict U f g h laws neF neG dpG sh =
  record
    { contractionвүў = О» {x} {y} xвүўy вҶ’
        let open UMetric.Ultrametric U
            open Contraction.Contractiveвүў sh
            open OrderLaws laws
            step1 = NonExpansive.nonexp neF (h (g x)) (h (g y))
            step2 = contractionвүў {x = g x} {y = g y} (DistinctPreserving.preservesвүў dpG xвүўy)
            step3 = NonExpansive.nonexp neG x y
        in
        <-le-trans (le-<-trans step1 step2) step3
    }
module DASHI.Geometry.Isotropy where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_вүЎ_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.Unit using (вҠӨ; tt)
open import Ultrametric as UMetric

record Group (G : Set) : SetвӮҒ where
  field
    _вҲҷ_  : G вҶ’ G вҶ’ G
    e    : G
    inv  : G вҶ’ G
    assoc : вҲҖ a b c вҶ’ (a вҲҷ b) вҲҷ c вүЎ a вҲҷ (b вҲҷ c)
    idL   : вҲҖ a вҶ’ e вҲҷ a вүЎ a
    invL  : вҲҖ a вҶ’ (inv a) вҲҷ a вүЎ e

record Isotropy
       {S : Set}
       (U : UMetric.Ultrametric S)
       (T : S вҶ’ S)
       : SetвӮҒ where

  open UMetric.Ultrametric U
  field
    G      : Set
    group  : Group G
    act    : G вҶ’ S вҶ’ S
    preservesMetric :
      вҲҖ g x y вҶ’ d (act g x) (act g y) вүЎ d x y
    commutesWithT :
      вҲҖ g x вҶ’ T (act g x) вүЎ act g (T x)

-- Trivial isotropy: one element group acting by identity.
trivialIsotropy :
  вҲҖ {S : Set} (U : UMetric.Ultrametric S) (T : S вҶ’ S) вҶ’
  Isotropy U T
trivialIsotropy U T =
  record
    { G = вҠӨ
    ; group = record
        { _вҲҷ_ = О» _ _ вҶ’ tt
        ; e = tt
        ; inv = О» _ вҶ’ tt
        ; assoc = О» _ _ _ вҶ’ refl
        ; idL = О» _ вҶ’ refl
        ; invL = О» _ вҶ’ refl
        }
    ; act = О» _ x вҶ’ x
    ; preservesMetric = О» _ _ _ вҶ’ refl
    ; commutesWithT = О» _ _ вҶ’ refl
    }

module DASHI.Geometry.COL where

open import DASHI.Core.Prelude
open import DASHI.Core.OperatorTypes
open import DASHI.Core.LensKernel

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- ContractionвҖ“ObstructionвҖ“Lift (COL)
------------------------------------------------------------------------

record COL (S : Nat -> Set) : Set1 where
  field
    E    : forall n -> S n -> Nat
    K    : forall n -> S n -> S n
    Obs  : forall n -> S n -> Bool
    lift : forall n -> S n -> S (suc n)

    -- Contraction inside level n: energy does not increase.
    contract : (n : Nat) (x : S n) -> E n (K n x) вүӨ E n x

    -- Obstruction is stable under K: if you are obstructed, stepping doesn't вҖңsolveвҖқ it magically.
    obs-stable : (n : Nat) (x : S n) -> Obs n x вүЎ true -> Obs n (K n x) вүЎ true

    -- Lift is witness-respecting: the old state is embedded, not destroyed.
    embed-ok : (n : Nat) (x : S n) -> вҠӨ

open COL public

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Derived theorem hooks (the вҖңschema theoremsвҖқ)

-- If not obstructed, repeated contraction gives monotone energy sequence.
iterate : forall {A : Set} -> (A -> A) -> Nat -> A -> A
iterate f zero    x = x
iterate f (suc k) x = iterate f k (f x)

E-monotone-iter :
  forall {S : Nat -> Set} (C : COL S) ->
  (n : Nat) (k : Nat) (x : S n) ->
  COL.E C n (iterate (COL.K C n) k x) вүӨ COL.E C n x
E-monotone-iter C n zero    x = вүӨ-refl
E-monotone-iter C n (suc k) x =
  вүӨ-trans
    (E-monotone-iter C n k (COL.K C n x))
    (COL.contract C n x)
module DASHI.Geometry.RealIsotropyInstance where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_вүЎ_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; suc)
open import Data.Bool using (Bool; true; false; if_then_else_; _xor_)
open import Data.Bool.Properties as BoolP

open import DASHI.Geometry.RealIsotropy as RIS
open import DASHI.Physics.RealTernaryCarrier as RTC
open import DASHI.Physics.RealOperators as RO
open import DASHI.Metric.FineAgreementUltrametric as FAM
open import Ultrametric as UMetric
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (sym)

-- Two-element group acting by invVec.
boolGroup : Iso.Group Bool
boolGroup =
  record
    { _вҲҷ_ = _xor_
    ; e = false
    ; inv = О» a вҶ’ a
    ; assoc = BoolP.xor-assoc
    ; idL = BoolP.xor-identityЛЎ
    ; invL = BoolP.xor-same
    }

act : вҲҖ {n} вҶ’ Bool вҶ’ RTC.Carrier n вҶ’ RTC.Carrier n
act {n} b x = if b then RTC.invVec x else x

preservesMetric :
  вҲҖ {n} вҶ’ (g : Bool) вҶ’ (x y : RTC.Carrier n) вҶ’
  UMetric.Ultrametric.d (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = n}) (act g x) (act g y)
    вүЎ UMetric.Ultrametric.d (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = n}) x y
preservesMetric {n} false x y = refl
preservesMetric {n} true x y = FAM.dNatFine-inv x y

commutesWithT :
  вҲҖ {n} вҶ’ (g : Bool) вҶ’ (x : RTC.Carrier n) вҶ’
  RO.CбөЈ (RO.PбөЈ (RO.RбөЈ (act g x))) вүЎ act g (RO.CбөЈ (RO.PбөЈ (RO.RбөЈ x)))
commutesWithT {n} false x = refl
commutesWithT {n} true x = sym (RO.invVec-PбөЈ x)

realIsotropyInstance :
  вҲҖ {n} вҶ’
  RIS.RealIsotropy (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = n}) (О» x вҶ’ RO.CбөЈ (RO.PбөЈ (RO.RбөЈ x)))
realIsotropyInstance {n} =
  record
    { iso =
        record
          { G = Bool
          ; group = boolGroup
          ; act = act
          ; preservesMetric = preservesMetric
          ; commutesWithT = commutesWithT
          }
    ; coneInvariant = Bool
    }

-- Two-element group acting by invVec.
boolGroup : Iso.Group Bool
boolGroup =
  record
    { _вҲҷ_ = _xor_
    ; e = false
    ; inv = О» a вҶ’ a
    ; assoc = BoolP.xor-assoc
    ; idL = BoolP.xor-identityЛЎ
    ; invL = BoolP.xor-same
    }

act : вҲҖ {n} вҶ’ Bool вҶ’ RTC.Carrier n вҶ’ RTC.Carrier n
act {n} b x = if b then RTC.invVec x else x

preservesMetric :
  вҲҖ {n} вҶ’ (g : Bool) вҶ’ (x y : RTC.Carrier n) вҶ’
  UMetric.Ultrametric.d (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = n}) (act g x) (act g y)
    вүЎ UMetric.Ultrametric.d (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = n}) x y

preservesMetric {n} true x y = FAM.dNatFine-inv x y

commutesWithT :
  вҲҖ {m k : Nat} вҶ’ (g : Bool) вҶ’ (x : RTC.Carrier (m + k)) вҶ’
  ROSS.C {m} {k} (ROSS.P {m} {k} (ROSS.R {m} {k} (act g x)))
    вүЎ act g (ROSS.C {m} {k} (ROSS.P {m} {k} (ROSS.R {m} {k} x)))

commutesWithT {m} {k} true x =
  let
    step1 : ROSS.R {m} {k} (RTC.invVec x) вүЎ RTC.invVec (ROSS.R {m} {k} x)
    step1 = sym (TCI.invVec-RбөЈ {m} {k} x)
    step2 : ROSS.P {m} {k} (RTC.invVec (ROSS.R {m} {k} x))
            вүЎ RTC.invVec (ROSS.P {m} {k} (ROSS.R {m} {k} x))
    step2 = sym (TCI.invVec-PбөЈ {m} {k} (ROSS.R {m} {k} x))
    step3 : ROSS.C {m} {k} (RTC.invVec (ROSS.P {m} {k} (ROSS.R {m} {k} x)))
            вүЎ RTC.invVec (ROSS.C {m} {k} (ROSS.P {m} {k} (ROSS.R {m} {k} x)))
    step3 = sym (CM.CбөЈ-invVec {m} {k} (ROSS.P {m} {k} (ROSS.R {m} {k} x)))
  in
  trans
    (cong (О» v вҶ’ ROSS.C {m} {k} (ROSS.P {m} {k} v)) step1)
    (trans (cong (О» v вҶ’ ROSS.C {m} {k} v) step2) step3)

  вҲҖ {m k : Nat} вҶ’
  RIS.RealIsotropy (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k})
    (О» x вҶ’ ROSS.C {m} {k} (ROSS.P {m} {k} (ROSS.R {m} {k} x)))
realIsotropyInstanceShift {m} {k} =
  record
    { iso =
        record
          { G = Bool
          ; group = boolGroup
          ; act = act
          ; preservesMetric = preservesMetric
          ; commutesWithT = commutesWithT {m} {k}
          }
    ; coneInvariant = Bool
    }

module DASHI.Geometry.Signature31FromConeArrowIsotropy where

open import Level using (Level; _вҠ”_; suc; zero)

record SignatureAxioms {в„“v в„“s}
  (A : Additive в„“v) (F : ScalarField в„“s)
  (QF : QuadraticForm A F)
  : Set (suc (в„“v вҠ” в„“s)) where
  open Additive A
  open ScalarField F
  open QuadraticForm QF
  field
    ConeS : ConeStructure (Additive.Carrier A)
    Arrow : TimeArrow (Additive.Carrier A)
    Iso   : IsotropyAction (Additive.Carrier A)
    TimelikeвҶ”Cone : вҲҖ (x : Additive.Carrier A) вҶ’ вҠӨ

open SignatureAxioms public

postulate
  Signature31Theorem :
    вҲҖ {в„“v в„“s} (A : Additive в„“v) (F : ScalarField в„“s)
      (QF : QuadraticForm A F)
      (Ax : SignatureAxioms A F QF)
    вҶ’ Signature
module DASHI.Geometry.QuadraticFormEmergence where

open import Level using (Level; _вҠ”_; suc; zero)
open import Data.Product using (ОЈ; _,_)

record QuadraticEmergenceAxioms {в„“v в„“s}
  (A : Additive в„“v) (F : ScalarField в„“s)
  (PD : ProjectionDefect A)
  : Set (suc (в„“v вҠ” в„“s)) where
  open Additive A
  open ScalarField F
  open ProjectionDefect PD
  field
    Energy : Additive.Carrier A вҶ’ ScalarField.S F
    Additive-On-Orth :
      вҲҖ x y вҶ’ ProjectionDefect.Orth PD x y вҶ’
        Energy (Additive._+_ A x y) вүЎ
        ScalarField._+s_ F (Energy x) (Energy y)
    PD-splits : вҲҖ x вҶ’
      Energy x вүЎ
      ScalarField._+s_ F (Energy (ProjectionDefect.P PD x))
                           (Energy (ProjectionDefect.D PD x))

open QuadraticEmergenceAxioms public

  QuadraticFormEmergence :
    вҲҖ {в„“v в„“s} (A : Additive в„“v) (F : ScalarField в„“s)
      (PD : ProjectionDefect A)
      (Ax : QuadraticEmergenceAxioms A F PD)
    вҶ’ ОЈ (QuadraticForm A F) (О» qf вҶ’ вҠӨ)
module DASHI.Geometry.ProjectionContractionOrthogonalityTests where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality
open import Agda.Builtin.Sigma
open import Data.Product public using (_Г—_)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Minimal algebra: additive group structure (abstract)
-- (You can replace these postulates with your concrete state carrier.)
------------------------------------------------------------------------

postulate
  S   : Set
  _S+_ : S вҶ’ S вҶ’ S
  _S-_ : S вҶ’ S вҶ’ S
  0#  : S

infixl 6 _S+_ _S-_

postulate
  -- Group-ish laws youвҖҷll need for вҖңdetail = x - P xвҖқ reasoning
  +-assoc : вҲҖ x y z вҶ’ (x S+ y) S+ z вүЎ x S+ (y S+ z)
  +-idКі   : вҲҖ x вҶ’ x S+ 0# вүЎ x
  +-idЛЎ   : вҲҖ x вҶ’ 0# S+ x вүЎ x
  +-invКі  : вҲҖ x вҶ’ x S- x вүЎ 0#

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Metric / norm interface (keep abstract; later bind to your induced norm)
------------------------------------------------------------------------

postulate
  dist : S вҶ’ S вҶ’ Set  -- you may replace with в„қ or в„ҡ; kept abstract here

-- A вҖңnormвҖқ is distance to 0. (You can swap this for your actual norm.)
postulate
  вҲҘ_вҲҘ : S вҶ’ Set
  вҲҘxвҲҘ-def : вҲҖ x вҶ’ вҲҘ x вҲҘ вүЎ dist x 0#

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Recognisable lift decomposition (your вҖңtelescoping identityвҖқ)
------------------------------------------------------------------------

record RecognisableLift (P : S вҶ’ S) : Set where
  field
    -- every x decomposes uniquely into coarse + detail:
    coarse   : S вҶ’ S
    detail   : S вҶ’ S
    split    : вҲҖ x вҶ’ x вүЎ coarse x S+ detail x

    -- recognisable uniqueness: if x = c+d = c'+d' with both c,c' fixed by P
    -- and both d,d' in the fiber kernel, then equal (abstracted)
    uniq :
      вҲҖ x c d c' d' вҶ’
      x вүЎ c S+ d вҶ’
      x вүЎ c' S+ d' вҶ’
      P c вүЎ c вҶ’
      P c' вүЎ c' вҶ’
      P d вүЎ 0# вҶ’
      P d' вүЎ 0# вҶ’
      (c вүЎ c') Г— (d вүЎ d')

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Non-expansive idempotent projection axioms
------------------------------------------------------------------------

record NonExpansiveProjection (P : S вҶ’ S) : SetвӮҒ where
  field
    idem  : вҲҖ x вҶ’ P (P x) вүЎ P x
    nonexp : вҲҖ x y вҶ’ dist (P x) (P y) вүЎ dist x y
    -- (If you want вүӨ instead of вүЎ, change dist codomain to в„ҡ/в„қ and use вүӨ.)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Orthogonality: вҖңno double countingвҖқ in the induced quadratic energy
--
-- This is the *test* you want Agda to force:
--   from RecognisableLift + NonExpansiveProjection (+ stability axiom),
--   derive Pythagorean split for a quadratic norm and orthogonality.
------------------------------------------------------------------------

record OrthogonalSplit (P : S вҶ’ S) : SetвӮҒ where
  field
    вҹӮ-pred : S вҶ’ S вҶ’ Set          -- вҖңorthogonalвҖқ predicate (abstract)
    pythag :
      вҲҖ x вҶ’
      let c = P x
          d = x S- P x
      in  вҲҘ x вҲҘ вүЎ (вҲҘ c вҲҘ) Г— (вҲҘ d вҲҘ)   -- placeholder shape; replace with numeric identity
    orth :
      вҲҖ x вҶ’
      let c = P x
          d = x S- P x
      in  вҹӮ-pred c d

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- The Master Theorem (as a test harness)
------------------------------------------------------------------------

postulate
  -- Stability premise: the multiscale hierarchy must forbid leakage.
  -- You can replace this with your contractive fixed-point stability lemma.
  StabilityNoLeakage :
    (P : S вҶ’ S) вҶ’ Set

postulate
  MasterTheorem :
    (P : S вҶ’ S) вҶ’
    RecognisableLift P вҶ’
    NonExpansiveProjection P вҶ’
    StabilityNoLeakage P вҶ’
    OrthogonalSplit P
module DASHI.Geometry.RealIsotropyInstanceShiftTailInv where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_вүЎ_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; _+_)
open import Data.Nat using (_вүӨ_)
open import Data.Bool using (Bool; true; false; if_then_else_; _xor_)
open import Data.Bool.Properties as BoolP
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (sym; trans; cong; subst; substвӮӮ)

open import Data.Nat.Properties as NatP
open import Data.Vec using (Vec; _++_)
open import Data.Product using (_,_; projвӮҒ)

open import DASHI.Geometry.Isotropy as Iso
open import DASHI.Geometry.RealIsotropy as RIS
open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (Trit; inv)
open import DASHI.Physics.RealTernaryCarrier as RTC
open import DASHI.Physics.RealOperatorStackShift as ROSS

congвӮӮ' :
  вҲҖ {A B C : Set} {xвӮҒ xвӮӮ : A} {yвӮҒ yвӮӮ : B}
  (f : A вҶ’ B вҶ’ C) вҶ’ xвӮҒ вүЎ xвӮӮ вҶ’ yвӮҒ вүЎ yвӮӮ вҶ’ f xвӮҒ yвӮҒ вүЎ f xвӮӮ yвӮӮ
congвӮӮ' f refl refl = refl

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Two-element group acting by tail inversion

boolGroup : Iso.Group Bool
boolGroup =
  record
    { _вҲҷ_ = _xor_
    ; e = false
    ; inv = О» a вҶ’ a
    ; assoc = BoolP.xor-assoc
    ; idL = BoolP.xor-identityЛЎ
    ; invL = BoolP.xor-same
    }

-- Apply invVec to tail only

tailInv : вҲҖ {m k : Nat} вҶ’ RTC.Carrier (m + k) вҶ’ RTC.Carrier (m + k)
tailInv {m} {k} x = TCP.coarseOf m k x ++ RTC.invVec (TCP.tailOf m k x)

tailInv-++ :
  вҲҖ {m k : Nat} (c : Vec Trit m) (t : Vec Trit k) вҶ’
  tailInv {m} {k} (c ++ t) вүЎ c ++ RTC.invVec t
tailInv-++ {m} {k} c t
  rewrite TCP.split-++ m k c t = refl

coarseOf-tailInv :
  вҲҖ {m k : Nat} (x : RTC.Carrier (m + k)) вҶ’
  TCP.coarseOf m k (tailInv {m} {k} x) вүЎ TCP.coarseOf m k x
coarseOf-tailInv {m} {k} x with TCP.split m k x
... | (c , t)
  rewrite TCP.split-++ m k c (RTC.invVec t)
  = refl

act : вҲҖ {m k : Nat} вҶ’ Bool вҶ’ RTC.Carrier (m + k) вҶ’ RTC.Carrier (m + k)
act {m} {k} b x = if b then tailInv {m} {k} x else x

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- tailInv is an involution

tailInv-invol : вҲҖ {m k : Nat} (x : RTC.Carrier (m + k)) вҶ’ tailInv {m} {k} (tailInv {m} {k} x) вүЎ x
tailInv-invol {m} {k} x =
  let
    c = TCP.coarseOf m k x
    t = TCP.tailOf m k x
    p : x вүЎ c ++ t
    p = sym (TCP.merge-split m k x)
  in
  trans
    (tailInv-++ c (RTC.invVec t))
    (trans
      (cong (О» v вҶ’ c ++ v) (RTC.invVec-invol t))
      (sym p))

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Metric invariance for tailInv

preservesMetric :
  вҲҖ {m k : Nat} вҶ’ (g : Bool) вҶ’ (x y : RTC.Carrier (m + k)) вҶ’
  UMetric.Ultrametric.d (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k}) (act {m} {k} g x) (act {m} {k} g y)
    вүЎ UMetric.Ultrametric.d (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k}) x y
preservesMetric {m} {k} false x y = refl
preservesMetric {m} {k} true x y =
  let
    c  = TCP.coarseOf m k x
    t  = TCP.tailOf m k x
    c' = TCP.coarseOf m k y
    t' = TCP.tailOf m k y
    p : x вүЎ c ++ t
    p = sym (TCP.merge-split m k x)
    q : y вүЎ c' ++ t'
    q = sym (TCP.merge-split m k y)
    le1 : FAM.dNatFine (c ++ RTC.invVec t) (c' ++ RTC.invVec t') вүӨ FAM.dNatFine (c ++ t) (c' ++ t')
    le1 = FAM.dNatFine-++-mapвүӨ-tail c c' t t' inv
    le2 : FAM.dNatFine (c ++ t) (c' ++ t') вүӨ FAM.dNatFine (c ++ RTC.invVec t) (c' ++ RTC.invVec t')
    le2 =
      let
        le2' : FAM.dNatFine (c ++ RTC.invVec (RTC.invVec t))
                            (c' ++ RTC.invVec (RTC.invVec t'))
               вүӨ FAM.dNatFine (c ++ RTC.invVec t) (c' ++ RTC.invVec t')
        le2' = FAM.dNatFine-++-mapвүӨ-tail c c' (RTC.invVec t) (RTC.invVec t') inv
        r1 : c ++ RTC.invVec (RTC.invVec t) вүЎ c ++ t
        r1 = cong (О» v вҶ’ c ++ v) (RTC.invVec-invol t)
        r2 : c' ++ RTC.invVec (RTC.invVec t') вүЎ c' ++ t'
        r2 = cong (О» v вҶ’ c' ++ v) (RTC.invVec-invol t')
      in
      NatP.вүӨ-trans
        (NatP.вүӨ-reflexive (sym (congвӮӮ' FAM.dNatFine r1 r2)))
        le2'
    le1' : FAM.dNatFine (c ++ RTC.invVec t) (c' ++ RTC.invVec t') вүӨ FAM.dNatFine x y
    le1' = substвӮӮ (О» a b вҶ’ FAM.dNatFine (c ++ RTC.invVec t) (c' ++ RTC.invVec t') вүӨ FAM.dNatFine a b)
                  (sym p) (sym q) le1
    le2' : FAM.dNatFine x y вүӨ FAM.dNatFine (c ++ RTC.invVec t) (c' ++ RTC.invVec t')
    le2' = substвӮӮ (О» a b вҶ’ FAM.dNatFine a b вүӨ FAM.dNatFine (c ++ RTC.invVec t) (c' ++ RTC.invVec t'))
                  (sym p) (sym q) le2
  in
  NatP.вүӨ-antisym le1' le2'

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Commutation with the shift stack

commutesWithT :
  вҲҖ {m k : Nat} вҶ’ (g : Bool) вҶ’ (x : RTC.Carrier (m + k)) вҶ’
  ROSS.C {m} {k} (ROSS.P {m} {k} (ROSS.R {m} {k} (act {m} {k} g x)))
    вүЎ act {m} {k} g (ROSS.C {m} {k} (ROSS.P {m} {k} (ROSS.R {m} {k} x)))
commutesWithT {m} {k} false x = refl
commutesWithT {m} {k} true x =
  let
    c = TCP.coarseOf m k x
    t = TCP.tailOf m k x
    r : act {m} {k} true x вүЎ c ++ RTC.invVec t
    r = refl
    stepR : TCP.RбөЈ {m} {k} (c ++ RTC.invVec t) вүЎ c ++ TCP.shiftTail (RTC.invVec t)
    stepR = TCP.RбөЈ-++ m k c (RTC.invVec t)
    stepP : TCP.PбөЈ {m} {k} (c ++ TCP.shiftTail (RTC.invVec t)) вүЎ c ++ TCP.projTail (TCP.shiftTail (RTC.invVec t))
    stepP = TCP.PбөЈ-++ m k c (TCP.shiftTail (RTC.invVec t))
    stepRP : TCP.PбөЈ {m} {k} (TCP.RбөЈ {m} {k} (c ++ RTC.invVec t)) вүЎ c ++ TCP.projTail (TCP.shiftTail (RTC.invVec t))
    stepRP = trans (cong (TCP.PбөЈ {m} {k}) stepR) stepP
    stepC : ROSS.C {m} {k} (c ++ TCP.projTail (TCP.shiftTail (RTC.invVec t)))
            вүЎ CM.canonVec c ++ TCP.projTail (TCP.shiftTail (RTC.invVec t))
    stepC = CM.CбөЈ-++ c (TCP.projTail (TCP.shiftTail (RTC.invVec t)))
    t' = TCP.projTail (TCP.shiftTail t)
    p : x вүЎ c ++ t
    p = sym (TCP.merge-split m k x)
    stepT : ROSS.C {m} {k} (ROSS.P {m} {k} (ROSS.R {m} {k} x)) вүЎ CM.canonVec c ++ t'
    stepT =
      let
        r : TCP.RбөЈ {m} {k} x вүЎ c ++ TCP.shiftTail t
        r = trans (cong (О» v вҶ’ TCP.RбөЈ {m} {k} v) p) (TCP.RбөЈ-++ m k c t)
        pr : TCP.PбөЈ {m} {k} (TCP.RбөЈ {m} {k} x) вүЎ c ++ TCP.projTail (TCP.shiftTail t)
        pr = trans (cong (О» v вҶ’ TCP.PбөЈ {m} {k} v) r) (TCP.PбөЈ-++ m k c (TCP.shiftTail t))
      in
      trans
        (cong (О» v вҶ’ ROSS.C {m} {k} v) pr)
        (CM.CбөЈ-++ c t')
    stepAct : act {m} {k} true (ROSS.C {m} {k} (ROSS.P {m} {k} (ROSS.R {m} {k} x))) вүЎ CM.canonVec c ++ RTC.invVec t'
    stepAct =
      trans
        (cong (О» v вҶ’ tailInv {m} {k} v) stepT)
        (tailInv-++ (CM.canonVec c) t')
    stepInv : RTC.invVec (TCP.projTail (TCP.shiftTail t)) вүЎ TCP.projTail (TCP.shiftTail (RTC.invVec t))
    stepInv =
      trans
        (TCI.invVec-projTail (TCP.shiftTail t))
        (cong TCP.projTail (TCI.invVec-shiftTail t))
  in
  trans
    (cong (О» v вҶ’ ROSS.C {m} {k} (ROSS.P {m} {k} (ROSS.R {m} {k} v))) r)
    (trans
      (cong (О» v вҶ’ ROSS.C {m} {k} v) stepRP)
      (trans
        stepC
        (trans
          (cong (О» v вҶ’ CM.canonVec c ++ v) (sym stepInv))
          (sym stepAct))))

realIsotropyInstanceTailInv :
  вҲҖ {m k : Nat} вҶ’
  RIS.RealIsotropy (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k})
    (О» x вҶ’ ROSS.C {m} {k} (ROSS.P {m} {k} (ROSS.R {m} {k} x)))
realIsotropyInstanceTailInv {m} {k} =
  record
    { iso =
        record
          { G = Bool
          ; group = boolGroup
          ; act = act {m} {k}
          ; preservesMetric = preservesMetric {m} {k}
          ; commutesWithT = commutesWithT {m} {k}
          }
    ; coneInvariant = Bool
    }

module DASHI.Geometry.RealFiniteSpeedInstance where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc)

-- Fixed locality radius (nontrivial, but simple).
radius : Nat
radius = suc zero

local : вҲҖ {n} вҶ’ (x y : Vec Trit n) вҶ’ Set
local {n} x y = UMetric.Ultrametric.d (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = n}) x y вүӨ radius

preservesLocality :
  вҲҖ {n} (x y : Vec Trit n) вҶ’
  local x y вҶ’
  local (RO.CбөЈ (RO.PбөЈ (RO.RбөЈ x))) (RO.CбөЈ (RO.PбөЈ (RO.RбөЈ y)))
preservesLocality {n} x y h =
  let
    open UMetric.Ultrametric (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = n})
    step1 : d (RO.PбөЈ (RO.RбөЈ x)) (RO.PбөЈ (RO.RбөЈ y)) вүӨ d (RO.RбөЈ x) (RO.RбөЈ y)
    step1 = SCC.NonExpansive.nonexp (RO.nonexpPбөЈ {n}) (RO.RбөЈ x) (RO.RбөЈ y)
    step2 : d (RO.RбөЈ x) (RO.RбөЈ y) вүӨ d x y
    step2 = SCC.NonExpansive.nonexp (RO.nonexpRбөЈ {n}) x y
    step3 : d (RO.CбөЈ (RO.PбөЈ (RO.RбөЈ x))) (RO.CбөЈ (RO.PбөЈ (RO.RбөЈ y)))
            вүӨ d (RO.PбөЈ (RO.RбөЈ x)) (RO.PбөЈ (RO.RбөЈ y))
    step3 = SCC.NonExpansive.nonexp (RO.nonexpCбөЈ {n}) (RO.PбөЈ (RO.RбөЈ x)) (RO.PбөЈ (RO.RбөЈ y))
  in
  NatP.вүӨ-trans (NatP.вүӨ-trans step3 step1) (NatP.вүӨ-trans step2 h)

realFiniteSpeedInstance :
  вҲҖ {n} вҶ’
  RFS.RealFiniteSpeed (О» x вҶ’ RO.CбөЈ (RO.PбөЈ (RO.RбөЈ x)))
realFiniteSpeedInstance {n} =
  record
    { local = local {n}
    ; preservesLocality = preservesLocality {n}
    }

module DASHI.Geometry.ProjectionDefect where

open import Level using (Level; _вҠ”_; suc; zero)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_вүЎ_; refl; cong)
open import Data.Product using (ОЈ; _,_)
open import Data.Unit using (вҠӨ; tt)

record Additive (в„“ : Level) : Set (suc в„“) where
  field
    Carrier : Set в„“
    _+_     : Carrier вҶ’ Carrier вҶ’ Carrier
    0#      : Carrier
    -_      : Carrier вҶ’ Carrier

open Additive public

record ProjectionDefect {в„“} (A : Additive в„“) : Set (suc в„“) where
  open Additive A
  field
    P     : Additive.Carrier A вҶ’ Additive.Carrier A
    D     : Additive.Carrier A вҶ’ Additive.Carrier A
    D-def : вҲҖ x вҶ’ D x вүЎ Additive._+_ A x (Additive.-_ A (P x))

    P-idem : вҲҖ x вҶ’ P (P x) вүЎ P x

    Orth : Additive.Carrier A вҶ’ Additive.Carrier A вҶ’ Set в„“
    Orth-PD : вҲҖ x вҶ’ Orth (P x) (D x)

open ProjectionDefect public
module DASHI.Geometry.MQContractive where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat)

record MQContractive {n : Nat} (MQ : MaskedQuadratic n) : SetвӮҒ where
  field
    T     : MaskedQuadratic.V MQ вҶ’ MaskedQuadratic.V MQ
    lambda : в„ҡ
    lambda<1   : lambda < 1в„ҡ
    contract : вҲҖ x вҶ’ MaskedQuadratic.Q MQ (T x) вүӨ (lambda *в„ҡ lambda) *в„ҡ MaskedQuadratic.Q MQ x

open MQContractive public
module DASHI.Geometry.OrthogonalityFromPolarization where

open import Level using (Level; _вҠ”_; suc; zero)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_вүЎ_)

open import DASHI.Geometry.ProjectionDefect
open import DASHI.Geometry.QuadraticForm
open import DASHI.Energy.Energy
open import DASHI.Energy.ClosestPoint

-- Polarization interface: once Q is quadratic, define an inner product
-- and record the polarization identity as a seam.
record Polarization {в„“v в„“s}
  (A : Additive в„“v) (F : ScalarField в„“s)
  : Set (suc (в„“v вҠ” в„“s)) where
  field
    Q : Additive.Carrier A вҶ’ ScalarField.S F
    вҹӘ_,_вҹ« : Additive.Carrier A вҶ’ Additive.Carrier A вҶ’ ScalarField.S F
    two : ScalarField.S F
    two-def : two вүЎ (ScalarField._+s_ F (ScalarField.1s F) (ScalarField.1s F))
    polarization :
      вҲҖ x y вҶ’
        Q (Additive._+_ A x y) вүЎ
        ScalarField._+s_ F
          (ScalarField._+s_ F (Q x) (Q y))
          (ScalarField._*s_ F two (вҹӘ x , y вҹ«))

open Polarization public

-- Orthogonality corollary: once closest-point is established and
-- the polarization identity is available, orthogonality becomes a target.
record OrthogonalityFromPolarization {в„“v в„“s}
  {A : Additive в„“v} {F : ScalarField в„“s}
  {P : Preorder {в„“s}}
  (ES : EnergySpace (Additive.Carrier A) P)
  (Pj : Projection (Additive.Carrier A))
  (Pol : Polarization A F)
  (CP : ClosestPoint ES Pj)
  : Set (suc (в„“v вҠ” в„“s)) where
  field
    Orth : Additive.Carrier A вҶ’ Additive.Carrier A вҶ’ Set в„“s
    Orth-def : вҲҖ x y вҶ’ Orth x y вүЎ
      (Polarization.вҹӘ_,_вҹ« Pol x y вүЎ ScalarField.0s F)
    orthPD : вҲҖ x вҶ’
      Orth (Projection.P Pj x)
           (Additive._+_ A x (Additive.-_ A (Projection.P Pj x)))

open OrthogonalityFromPolarization public
module DASHI.Geometry.ProjectionContractiveConstant where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_вүЎ_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc)
open import Data.Empty using (вҠҘ; вҠҘ-elim)

open import Ultrametric as UMetric

_вүў_ : {A : Set} вҶ’ A вҶ’ A вҶ’ Set
_вүў_ {A} x y = (x вүЎ y) вҶ’ вҠҘ

record DiscreteUltrametric {S : Set} (U : UMetric.Ultrametric S) : SetвӮҒ where
  open UMetric.Ultrametric U public
  field
    nonzero-on-distinct : вҲҖ {x y} вҶ’ x вүў y вҶ’ d x y вүў zero

Kconst : вҲҖ {S : Set} вҶ’ S вҶ’ S вҶ’ S
Kconst t _ = t

record Contractiveвүў
       {S : Set}
       (U : UMetric.Ultrametric S)
       (K : S вҶ’ S)
       : Set where
  open UMetric.Ultrametric U public
  field
    collapses-on-distinct : вҲҖ {x y} вҶ’ x вүў y вҶ’ d (K x) (K y) вүЎ zero
    original-nonzero : вҲҖ {x y} вҶ’ x вүў y вҶ’ d x y вүў zero

const-proj-contractiveвүў :
  вҲҖ {S : Set} (U : UMetric.Ultrametric S)
  вҶ’ DiscreteUltrametric U
  вҶ’ (t : S)
  вҶ’ Contractiveвүў U (Kconst t)
const-proj-contractiveвүў {S} U DU t =
  let open UMetric.Ultrametric U
      open DiscreteUltrametric DU
  in
  record
    { collapses-on-distinct = О» {x} {_} _ вҶ’
        UMetric.Ultrametric.id-zero U (Kconst t x)
    ; original-nonzero = О» {x} {y} xвүўy вҶ’
        nonzero-on-distinct xвүўy
    }
module DASHI.Geometry.EinsteinFromRGNoLeakage where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_вүЎ_)
open import Data.Product using (_Г—_; _,_)
open import Agda.Builtin.Unit using (вҠӨ; tt)

record RGGeometryData : SetвӮҒ where
  field
    M : Set
    Point : Set
    Tensor2 : Set
    в„ҡ : Set
    0q : в„ҡ
    div : Tensor2 вҶ’ Point вҶ’ в„ҡ
    sym : Tensor2 вҶ’ Set
    G : M вҶ’ Tensor2
    T : M вҶ’ Tensor2
    RGState : Set
    step : RGState вҶ’ RGState
    geom : RGState вҶ’ M
    PП„ : Tensor2 вҶ’ Tensor2

open RGGeometryData public

DefectD : (D : RGGeometryData) вҶ’ RGGeometryData.RGState D вҶ’ RGGeometryData.Tensor2 D
DefectD D s = RGGeometryData.PП„ D (RGGeometryData.T D (RGGeometryData.geom D (RGGeometryData.step D s)))

record GR_NoLeakage (D : RGGeometryData) : SetвӮҒ where
  field
    bianchi :
      вҲҖ s x вҶ’
        RGGeometryData.div D (RGGeometryData.G D (RGGeometryData.geom D s)) x вүЎ RGGeometryData.0q D
    conserve :
      вҲҖ s x вҶ’
        RGGeometryData.div D (RGGeometryData.T D (RGGeometryData.geom D s)) x вүЎ RGGeometryData.0q D
    defect-law :
      вҲҖ s вҶ’
        RGGeometryData.G D (RGGeometryData.geom D s) вүЎ DefectD D s
    symG :
      вҲҖ s вҶ’
        RGGeometryData.sym D (RGGeometryData.G D (RGGeometryData.geom D s))
    symT :
      вҲҖ s вҶ’
        RGGeometryData.sym D (RGGeometryData.T D (RGGeometryData.geom D s))

open GR_NoLeakage public

record EinsteinConsequences {D} (A : GR_NoLeakage D) : SetвӮҒ where
  field
    divergenceFree :
      вҲҖ s x вҶ’
        RGGeometryData.div D (RGGeometryData.G D (RGGeometryData.geom D s)) x вүЎ RGGeometryData.0q D
    conservation :
      вҲҖ s x вҶ’
        RGGeometryData.div D (RGGeometryData.T D (RGGeometryData.geom D s)) x вүЎ RGGeometryData.0q D
    einsteinEq :
      вҲҖ s вҶ’
        RGGeometryData.G D (RGGeometryData.geom D s) вүЎ DefectD D s

EinsteinFromRG :
  вҲҖ {D} (A : GR_NoLeakage D) вҶ’
  EinsteinConsequences A
EinsteinFromRG A =
  record
    { divergenceFree = bianchi A
    ; conservation = conserve A
    ; einsteinEq = defect-law A
    }

module DASHI.Algebra.Quantum.UVFinitenessHolographyTests where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat
open import Agda.Builtin.Sigma using (ОЈ; _,_)
open import Data.Nat using (_*_; _вүӨ_)
open import DASHI.Algebra.Quantum.UVFiniteness public

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Abstract вҖңregion sizeвҖқ and counting (bound supplied by the user)
------------------------------------------------------------------------

postulate
  L : Set                  -- linear size parameter
  vol area : L -> Nat      -- discrete counts
  dimH : L -> Nat          -- effective Hilbert dimension / mode count
  eta  : Nat               -- holographic proportionality constant

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Holographic area bound: dimH(L) вүӨ О· * area(L)
------------------------------------------------------------------------

AreaBound : Set
AreaBound = вҲҖ (l : L) -> dimH l вүӨ (eta * area l)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- UV finiteness: bounded dim вҮ’ no infinite UV tower
------------------------------------------------------------------------

UVFinitenessTheorem :
  (areaBound : AreaBound) вҶ’
  UVFinite (record
    { L = L
    ; dimH = dimH
    ; bound = О» l вҶ’ eta * area l
    ; dimHвүӨbound = areaBound
    })
UVFinitenessTheorem areaBound =
  let bounded = record
        { L = L
        ; dimH = dimH
        ; bound = О» l вҶ’ eta * area l
        ; dimHвүӨbound = areaBound
        }
  in uvFiniteness bounded
module DASHI.Algebra.Quantum.NoGlobalAttractor where

open import DASHI.Core.Prelude
open import DASHI.Core.OperatorTypes

-- Iteration
iterate : вҲҖ {S : Set} вҶ’ (S вҶ’ S) вҶ’ Nat вҶ’ S вҶ’ S
iterate f zero    x = x
iterate f (suc n) x = iterate f n (f x)

-- вҖңEventually constantвҖқ orbit at a.
EventuallyConst : вҲҖ {S : Set} вҶ’ (S вҶ’ S) вҶ’ S вҶ’ S вҶ’ Set
EventuallyConst f x a = ОЈ Nat (О» N вҶ’ вҲҖ n вҶ’ iterate f (N + n) x вүЎ a)

-- Global attractor = same a for all x.
GlobalAttractor : вҲҖ {S : Set} вҶ’ (S вҶ’ S) вҶ’ Set
GlobalAttractor f = ОЈ _ (О» a вҶ’ вҲҖ x вҶ’ EventuallyConst f x a)

-- The useful theorem: invertible + nontrivial вҮ’ no global attractor.
-- (In a finite/discrete world, invertible dynamics canвҖҷt collapse all orbits to one point unless singleton.)

postulate
  invertible-nontrivial-no-attractor :
    вҲҖ {S : Set} {U : S вҶ’ S} вҶ’
    Invertible U вҶ’
    (ОЈ S (О» x вҶ’ ОЈ S (О» y вҶ’ В¬ (x вүЎ y)))) вҶ’
    В¬ GlobalAttractor U

-- Using Nat as a placeholder

postulate a b : Nat
postulate scale : Nat -> Nat -> Nat

record CausalCounts : Set where
  field
    tau sigma : Nat

  F : CausalCounts -> Nat

postulate
  Homogeneous :
    forall (l : Nat) (x : CausalCounts) -> F x вүЎ (l * l) * F x 

postulate
  ConeMonotone :
    forall (x : CausalCounts) ->
      CausalCounts.tau x > CausalCounts.sigma x -> F x > 0

postulate
  UniqueHyperbolic :
    forall (x : CausalCounts) ->
    F x вүЎ (a * (CausalCounts.tau x ^ 2)) вҲё (b * (CausalCounts.sigma x ^ 2))
module DASHI.Algebra.Quantum.Measurement where

record Measurement {S : Set} (О  : S вҶ’ S) : Set where
  field
    proj : Projection О 
    nontrivial : Nontrivial О    -- measurement actually collapses something

measurement-not-invertible :
  вҲҖ {S : Set} {О  : S вҶ’ S} вҶ’
  Measurement О  вҶ’
  В¬ Invertible О 
measurement-not-invertible {S} {О } M invО  =
  let open Measurement M in
  -- If О  invertible and projection вҮ’ О  = id, contradict nontrivial.
  nontrivial (projection+invertibleвҶ’identity proj invО )

module DASHI.Algebra.Quantum.SpinFromEvenClifford where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_вүЎ_)
open import Agda.Builtin.Sigma using (ОЈ; _,_)

record SpinData : SetвӮҒ where
  field
    SO : Nat вҶ’ Nat вҶ’ Set
    ClвҒ° : Set
    Spin : Set
    toSO : Spin вҶ’ SO 3 1
    kernelВұ1 : Set
    identitySO : SO 3 1

record SpinDoubleCover (D : SpinData) : SetвӮҒ where
  open SpinData D
  field
    hom : Spin вҶ’ SO 3 1
    kernel : Spin вҶ’ Set
    kernelвҠҶВұ1 : вҲҖ s вҶ’ hom s вүЎ identitySO вҶ’ kernel s вҶ’ kernelВұ1
    surjective : вҲҖ g вҶ’ ОЈ Spin (О» s вҶ’ hom s вүЎ g)

spinDoubleCover-witness :
  вҲҖ D вҶ’
  (ker : SpinData.Spin D вҶ’ Set)
  (kerвҠҶВұ1 : вҲҖ s вҶ’ SpinData.toSO D s вүЎ SpinData.identitySO D вҶ’ ker s вҶ’ SpinData.kernelВұ1 D)
  (surj : вҲҖ g вҶ’ ОЈ (SpinData.Spin D) (О» s вҶ’ SpinData.toSO D s вүЎ g)) вҶ’
  SpinDoubleCover D
spinDoubleCover-witness D ker kerвҠҶВұ1 surj =
  record { hom = SpinData.toSO D ; kernel = ker ; kernelвҠҶВұ1 = kerвҠҶВұ1 ; surjective = surj }

SpinIsDoubleCover : вҲҖ {D} вҶ’ SpinDoubleCover D вҶ’ Set
SpinIsDoubleCover {D} cover =
  вҲҖ g вҶ’ ОЈ (SpinData.Spin D) (О» s вҶ’ SpinDoubleCover.hom cover s вүЎ g)

module DASHI.Algebra.OperatorMonoidClosed where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_вүЎ_; refl)

postulate State : Set

Endo : Set
Endo = State вҶ’ State

_вҲҳ_ : Endo вҶ’ Endo вҶ’ Endo
(f вҲҳ g) s = f (g s)

id : Endo
id s = s

-- The closure generated by a seed operator K (a free monoid in Endo)
data Gen (K : Endo) : Endo вҶ’ SetвӮҒ where
  gen-id   : Gen K id
  gen-base : Gen K K
  gen-comp : вҲҖ {f g} вҶ’ Gen K f вҶ’ Gen K g вҶ’ Gen K (f вҲҳ g)

-- Now вҖңclosureвҖқ is literal:
closed-under-comp :
  вҲҖ {K : Endo} {f g : Endo} вҶ’
  Gen K f вҶ’ Gen K g вҶ’ Gen K (f вҲҳ g)
closed-under-comp = gen-comp
module DASHI.Algebra.AnomalyContracts where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero)

data Particle : Set where
  QL uR dR LL eR : Particle

Y : Particle вҶ’ Nat
Y QL = 1

module DASHI.Algebra.ConstraintAlgebraClosureTests where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality
open import Agda.Builtin.Sigma

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Abstract operator Lie algebra (commutator bracket)
------------------------------------------------------------------------

postulate
  Op : Set
  _вҲҳ_ : Op вҶ’ Op вҶ’ Op
  _-_ : Op вҶ’ Op вҶ’ Op
  I   : Op

infixl 9 _вҲҳ_

_bracket_ : Op вҶ’ Op вҶ’ Op
A bracket B = (A вҲҳ B) - (B вҲҳ A)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Constraints: Hamiltonian + Momentum (vector-index abstracted)
------------------------------------------------------------------------

postulate
  Idx : Set
  H    : Op
  Hбөў   : Idx вҶ’ Op

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Closure statement: commutators of constraints re-express as constraints
-- (This is the вҖңno anomalyвҖқ test: algebra closes in the same family.)
------------------------------------------------------------------------

record DiracClosure : Set where
  field
    -- [Hбөў, Hвұј] = H_k(...)   (structure functions hidden for now)
    mom-mom :
      вҲҖ i j вҶ’ ОЈ Idx (О» k вҶ’ (Hбөў i bracket Hбөў j) вүЎ Hбөў k)

    -- [H, Hбөў] = H(...)
    ham-mom :
      вҲҖ i вҶ’ (H bracket Hбөў i) вүЎ H

    -- [H, H] = Hбөў(...)
    ham-ham :
      ОЈ Idx (О» k вҶ’ (H bracket H) вүЎ Hбөў k)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Theorem obligation: derive closure from вҖңvaluation equivarianceвҖқ
------------------------------------------------------------------------

postulate
  ValuationEquivariance : Set     -- your вҖңdecimation commutes with relabellingsвҖқ
  NoLeakageStability    : Set     -- your fixed-point stability condition

postulate
  ConstraintAlgebraTheorem :
    ValuationEquivariance вҶ’
    NoLeakageStability вҶ’
    DiracClosure
module DASHI.Algebra.SMConformanceVectors where

-- Abstract state (whatever your physics state representation is)
postulate State : Set

-- Spec and impl: State вҶ’ signature (finite)
postulate
  Sig : Set
  specSig : State вҶ’ Sig
  implSig : State вҶ’ Sig

record Vector : Set where
  constructor vec
  field input : State

Vectors : Set
Vectors = List Vector

ConformsOn : (f g : State вҶ’ Sig) вҶ’ Vectors вҶ’ Set
ConformsOn f g [] = вҠӨ
ConformsOn f g (v вҲ· vs) =
  (f (Vector.input v) вүЎ g (Vector.input v)) Г— ConformsOn f g vs

-- Closure theorem you actually ship:
postulate vectors : Vectors

postulate
  physics-conformance : ConformsOn implSig specSig vectors
module DASHI.Algebra.PhysicsConformance where

module DASHI.Algebra.UnitaryVsCollapse where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat      using (Nat; zero; suc)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_вүЎ_; refl)
open import Relation.Nullary      using (В¬_)
open import Data.Nat              using (_<_)
open import Data.Empty            using (вҠҘ; вҠҘ-elim)

-- A minimal invertible step system with a Nat-valued measure.
record InvertibleNat (S : Set) : SetвӮҒ where
  field
    step  : S вҶ’ S
    inv   : S вҶ’ S
    left  : вҲҖ s вҶ’ inv (step s) вүЎ s
    right : вҲҖ s вҶ’ step (inv s) вүЎ s
    H     : S вҶ’ Nat

open InvertibleNat public

-- Iteration
iterate : вҲҖ {S : Set} вҶ’ (S вҶ’ S) вҶ’ Nat вҶ’ S вҶ’ S
iterate f zero    s = s
iterate f (suc n) s = iterate f n (f s)

-- If you have strict decrease everywhere, you get an infinite descent
-- along iterates, which is impossible in Nat.
--
-- To keep this module lightweight, we package the вҖңno infinite descentвҖқ
-- fact as a single lemma that can be discharged from stdlib later.
--
-- (If you want, I can give the fully discharged stdlib proof too.)
postulate
  NatNoInfiniteDescent :
    вҲҖ {S : Set} (H : S вҶ’ Nat) (f : S вҶ’ S) (sвӮҖ : S) вҶ’
    (вҲҖ s вҶ’ H (f s) < H s) вҶ’ вҠҘ

-- Main theorem: in an inhabited system, вҖңstrict collapse everywhereвҖқ is impossible.
no-global-strict-collapse :
  вҲҖ {S : Set} (U : InvertibleNat S) вҶ’
  (sвӮҖ : S) вҶ’
  В¬ (вҲҖ s вҶ’ H U (step U s) < H U s)
no-global-strict-collapse U sвӮҖ strict =
  NatNoInfiniteDescent (H U) (step U) sвӮҖ strict

-- Abstract state space + observable/entropy-like measure
record QuantumSys (в„“ : Level) : Set (lsuc в„“) where
  field
    QState : Set в„“
    step   : QState вҶ’ QState

    -- вҖңUnitary-likeвҖқ = invertible evolution
    inv    : QState вҶ’ QState
    left   : вҲҖ s вҶ’ inv (step s) вүЎ s
    right  : вҲҖ s вҶ’ step (inv s) вүЎ s

    -- Measurement/projection (can be non-invertible)
    meas   : QState вҶ’ QState
    meas-idem : вҲҖ s вҶ’ meas (meas s) вүЎ meas s

    -- Any scalar you use as вҖңentropy / action / code lengthвҖқ
    H      : QState вҶ’ Set в„“  -- keep general; specialize to Nat later

module DASHI.Algebra.MonsterUltrametric15 where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc)
open import Agda.Builtin.Bool using (Bool; true; false)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_вүЎ_; refl)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong; sym; trans)
open import Data.Nat using (_вүӨ_; _<_; _вҠ”_; _вҠ“_; _вҲё_; zвүӨn; sвүӨs)
open import Data.Nat.Properties as NatP using (вүӨ-refl; вүӨ-trans; вүӨ-reflexive; nвҲёnвүЎ0; вҲё-monoКі-вүӨ; вҲё-distribЛЎ-вҠ“-вҠ”; вҠ“-zeroЛЎ; вҠ“-zeroКі)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec; []; _вҲ·_)
-- Removed Relation.Binary.Reasoning.Base.Raw as it's not needed here.
-- Removed Relation.Binary.Reasoning.Nat as it's not needed here.

open import Ultrametric
open import DASHI.Algebra.MonsterMask15 using (Mask15)

lcpLen : вҲҖ {n} вҶ’ Vec Bool n вҶ’ Vec Bool n вҶ’ Nat
lcpLen [] [] = 0
lcpLen (true  вҲ· xs) (true  вҲ· ys) = suc (lcpLen xs ys)
lcpLen (false вҲ· xs) (false вҲ· ys) = suc (lcpLen xs ys)
lcpLen (_ вҲ· _) (_ вҲ· _) = 0

len : вҲҖ {n} вҶ’ Vec Bool n вҶ’ Nat
len []       = 0
len (_ вҲ· xs) = suc (len xs)

dMask : вҲҖ {n} вҶ’ Vec Bool n вҶ’ Vec Bool n вҶ’ Nat
dMask {n} x y = len {n} x вҲё lcpLen x y

-- id-zero
lcpLen-self-eq : вҲҖ {n} (m : Vec Bool n) вҶ’ lcpLen m m вүЎ len {n} m
lcpLen-self-eq [] = refl
lcpLen-self-eq (true  вҲ· xs) = cong suc (lcpLen-self-eq xs)
lcpLen-self-eq (false вҲ· xs) = cong suc (lcpLen-self-eq xs)

id-zeroMask : вҲҖ m вҶ’ dMask {15} m m вүЎ 0
id-zeroMask m =
  let
    step : dMask {15} m m вүЎ len {15} m вҲё len {15} m
    step = cong (О» k вҶ’ len {15} m вҲё k) (lcpLen-self-eq m)
  in
  trans step (nвҲёnвүЎ0 (len {15} m))

-- symmetric
lcpLen-symmetric : вҲҖ {n} (x y : Vec Bool n) вҶ’ lcpLen x y вүЎ lcpLen y x
lcpLen-symmetric [] [] = refl
lcpLen-symmetric (x вҲ· xs) (y вҲ· ys) with x | y
... | true | true = cong suc (lcpLen-symmetric xs ys)
... | false | false = cong suc (lcpLen-symmetric xs ys)
... | true | false = refl
... | false | true = refl

len-const : вҲҖ {n} (x : Vec Bool n) вҶ’ len x вүЎ n
len-const [] = refl
len-const (_ вҲ· xs) = cong suc (len-const xs)

dMask-symmetric : вҲҖ {n} (x y : Vec Bool n) вҶ’ dMask {n} x y вүЎ dMask {n} y x
dMask-symmetric {n} x y =
  let
    lenxвүЎn : len {n} x вүЎ n
    lenxвүЎn = len-const x
    lenyвүЎn : len {n} y вүЎ n
    lenyвүЎn = len-const y
  in
  trans (cong (О» k вҶ’ len {n} x вҲё k) (lcpLen-symmetric x y))
        (trans (cong (О» k вҶ’ k вҲё lcpLen y x) lenxвүЎn)
               (cong (О» k вҶ’ k вҲё lcpLen y x) (sym lenyвүЎn)))

symMask : вҲҖ {n} (x y : Vec Bool n) вҶ’ dMask {n} x y вүЎ dMask {n} y x
symMask = dMask-symmetric

-- ultratriangle
lcpLen-ultratriangle :
  вҲҖ {n} (x y z : Vec Bool n) вҶ’
  (lcpLen x y вҠ“ lcpLen y z) вүӨ lcpLen x z
lcpLen-ultratriangle [] [] [] = zвүӨn
lcpLen-ultratriangle (x вҲ· xs) (y вҲ· ys) (z вҲ· zs) with x | y | z
... | true  | true  | true  = sвүӨs (lcpLen-ultratriangle xs ys zs)
... | false | false | false = sвүӨs (lcpLen-ultratriangle xs ys zs)
... | true  | false | _     rewrite вҠ“-zeroЛЎ (lcpLen (y вҲ· ys) (z вҲ· zs)) = zвүӨn
... | false | true  | _     rewrite вҠ“-zeroЛЎ (lcpLen (y вҲ· ys) (z вҲ· zs)) = zвүӨn
... | true  | true  | false rewrite вҠ“-zeroКі (lcpLen (x вҲ· xs) (y вҲ· ys)) = zвүӨn
... | false | false | true  rewrite вҠ“-zeroКі (lcpLen (x вҲ· xs) (y вҲ· ys)) = zвүӨn

ultraMask : вҲҖ x y z вҶ’ dMask {15} x z вүӨ (dMask {15} x y вҠ” dMask {15} y z)
ultraMask x y z =
  let
    a = lcpLen x y
    b = lcpLen y z
    c = lcpLen x z
    lenx = len {15} x
    leny = len {15} y

    lenxвүЎn : lenx вүЎ 15
    lenxвүЎn = len-const x

    lenyвүЎn : leny вүЎ 15
    lenyвүЎn = len-const y

    lenxвүЎleny : lenx вүЎ leny
    lenxвүЎleny = trans lenxвүЎn (sym lenyвүЎn)

    cвүҘmin : (a вҠ“ b) вүӨ c
    cвүҘmin = lcpLen-ultratriangle x y z

    step1 : (lenx вҲё c) вүӨ (lenx вҲё (a вҠ“ b))
    step1 = вҲё-monoКі-вүӨ lenx cвүҘmin

    step2 : (lenx вҲё (a вҠ“ b)) вүЎ (lenx вҲё a) вҠ” (lenx вҲё b)
    step2 = вҲё-distribЛЎ-вҠ“-вҠ” lenx a b

    step2' : (lenx вҲё (a вҠ“ b)) вүЎ (lenx вҲё a) вҠ” (leny вҲё b)
    step2' = trans step2 (cong (О» k вҶ’ (lenx вҲё a) вҠ” (k вҲё b)) lenxвүЎleny)
  in
  NatP.вүӨ-trans step1 (NatP.вүӨ-reflexive step2')

UMask15 : Ultrametric Mask15
UMask15 = record
  { d             = dMask {15}
  ; id-zero       = id-zeroMask
  ; symmetric     = symMask {15}
  ; ultratriangle = ultraMask
  }

projection+invertibleвҶ’identity :
  вҲҖ {S : Set} {K : S вҶ’ S} вҶ’
  Projection K вҶ’ Invertible K вҶ’ (вҲҖ x вҶ’ K x вүЎ x)

    V в„ҡ : Set

    _*в„ҡ_ : в„ҡ вҶ’ в„ҡ вҶ’ в„ҡ

module DASHI.Algebra.MonsterMask15 where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc)
open import Agda.Builtin.Bool using (Bool; true; false)

open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_вүЎ_; refl)

FactorCount : Nat
FactorCount = 15

Mask15 : Set
Mask15 = Vec Bool FactorCount

fullMask : Mask15
fullMask = replicate FactorCount true

emptyMask : Mask15
emptyMask = replicate FactorCount false

-- Pointwise AND (same length, total)
boolAnd : Bool вҶ’ Bool вҶ’ Bool
boolAnd true true = true
boolAnd _    _    = false

_вҲ§_ : вҲҖ {n} вҶ’ Vec Bool n вҶ’ Vec Bool n вҶ’ Vec Bool n
_вҲ§_ {zero} [] [] = []
_вҲ§_ {suc n} (b вҲ· xs) (c вҲ· ys) = boolAnd b c вҲ· (xs вҲ§ ys)

-- Kernel interface (15-fixed)
record Kernel : SetвӮҒ where
  field
    K : Mask15 вҶ’ Mask15

projectTo : Mask15 вҶ’ Kernel
projectTo target = record { K = О» _ вҶ’ target }
module DASHI.Algebra.PhysicsTable where

-- State is literally an enumeration of the witness inputs
data State : Set where
  s0 s1 s2 s3 s4 : State
  -- add as many as your computed witness set needs

-- The witness list you claim coverage on
vectors : List State
vectors = s0 вҲ· s1 вҲ· s2 вҲ· s3 вҲ· s4 вҲ· []

implSig s4 = sig15 true false true  false true  false true  false true  false true  false true  false true

-- If you canвҖҷt define it yet, you can table it too (still honest).
specSig : State вҶ’ Sig15

-- A single-seam bridge: FejГ©r monotonicity plus a convexity/optimality
-- axiom gives closest-point projection.
record FejerClosestAxioms {в„“x в„“s}
  {X : Set в„“x} {P : Preorder {в„“s}}
  (ES : EnergySpace X P) (Pj : Projection X)
  : Set (suc (в„“x вҠ” в„“s)) where
  field
    fejer : FejerMonotone ES Pj
    -- Seam: a single axiom capturing the optimization/convexity step.
    -- If you later prove it, you can replace this with a lemma.

      вҲҖ x y вҶ’ FixP Pj y вҶ’
        Preorder._вүӨ_ P
          (EnergySpace.E ES x (Projection.P Pj x))
          (EnergySpace.E ES x y)

  вҲҖ {в„“x в„“s} {X : Set в„“x} {P : Preorder {в„“s}}

  (Ax : FejerClosestAxioms ES Pj) вҶ’
  ClosestPoint ES Pj

  record { closest = fejerвҮ’closest Ax }

module DASHI.Energy.ClosestPoint where

open import Level using (Level; _вҠ”_; suc; zero)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_вүЎ_)

open import DASHI.Energy.Energy

record Projection {в„“x} (X : Set в„“x) : Set (suc в„“x) where
  field
    P : X вҶ’ X
    idem : вҲҖ x вҶ’ P (P x) вүЎ P x

open Projection public

FixP : вҲҖ {в„“x} {X : Set в„“x} вҶ’ Projection X вҶ’ X вҶ’ Set в„“x
FixP {X = X} Pj x = Projection.P Pj x вүЎ x

-- FejГ©r monotonicity w.r.t. FixP in an energy space.
-- Interpretation: the dynamics is contractive toward a fixed set, even when
-- raw Euclidean metrics are not contractive (empirically observed for LHC fits).
record FejerMonotone {в„“x в„“s}
  {X : Set в„“x} {P : Preorder {в„“s}}
  (ES : EnergySpace X P) (Pj : Projection X)
  : Set (suc (в„“x вҠ” в„“s)) where
  open EnergySpace ES
  open Preorder P
  field
    fejer : вҲҖ x y вҶ’ FixP Pj y вҶ’
      Preorder._вүӨ_ P (EnergySpace.E ES (Projection.P Pj x) y)
                         (EnergySpace.E ES x y)

open FejerMonotone public

-- Closest-point property to FixP.
record ClosestPoint {в„“x в„“s}
  {X : Set в„“x} {P : Preorder {в„“s}}
  (ES : EnergySpace X P) (Pj : Projection X)
  : Set (suc (в„“x вҠ” в„“s)) where
  open EnergySpace ES
  open Preorder P
  field
    closest : вҲҖ x y вҶ’ FixP Pj y вҶ’
      Preorder._вүӨ_ P (EnergySpace.E ES x (Projection.P Pj x))
                         (EnergySpace.E ES x y)

open ClosestPoint public

-- Bridge: FejГ©r + idempotence вҮ’ ClosestPoint.
-- This is the exact hinge lemma youвҖҷll later discharge from your operator facts.
record FejerImpliesClosest {в„“x в„“s}
  {X : Set в„“x} {P : Preorder {в„“s}}
  (ES : EnergySpace X P) (Pj : Projection X)
  (F : FejerMonotone ES Pj)
  : Set (suc (в„“x вҠ” в„“s)) where
  field
    proof : ClosestPoint ES Pj

open FejerImpliesClosest public

-- You likely already have these (or equivalents) in your Prelude:
--   в„•, в„Ө, Bool, ОЈ, вҠҘ, вҠӨ, List, etc.
-- Here we keep it abstract/minimal.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- 0. Primitive carriers

data T : Set where
  neg : T   -- -1
  zer : T   --  0
  pos : T   -- +1

О№ : T вҶ’ T
О№ neg = pos
О№ zer = zer
О№ pos = neg

О№-involutive : вҲҖ x вҶ’ О№ (О№ x) вүЎ x
О№-involutive neg = refl
О№-involutive zer = refl
О№-involutive pos = refl

  field
    _вүә_     : E вҶ’ E вҶ’ Set

    -- you may want antisymmetry if you use вүӨ, or keep it a strict order

-- Local finiteness etc can be added as fields/axioms if used.

-- (e.g. longest chain length and minimal separating antichain size).

  field
    П„ : E вҶ’ E вҶ’ в„•          -- chain depth
    Пғ : E вҶ’ E вҶ’ в„•          -- antichain width / separation width

    -- Axioms you claim proven elsewhere:
    П„-zero : вҲҖ a вҶ’ П„ a a вүЎ 0
    Пғ-zero : вҲҖ a вҶ’ Пғ a a вүЎ 0

    -- Causal direction uniqueness / вҖңone time axisвҖқ property, etc.
    -- (whatever your signature proof uses)
    causal-axis : Set

  open ChainAntichain CA

    c : в„қ  -- you may have your own в„қ
    О”sВІ : E вҶ’ E вҶ’ в„қ

    -- Definition constraint

      О”sВІ a b вүЎ _-_ ((c * c) * (toв„қ (П„ a b) * toв„қ (П„ a b)))
                      (toв„қ (Пғ a b) * toв„қ (Пғ a b))

    -- Theorems you said are proven:

module DASHI.MDL.MDLDescentTradeoff where

open import Level using (Level; _вҠ”_; suc; zero)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_вүЎ_; subst; sym)

-- Minimal ordered commutative monoid interface.
record AddMonoid {в„“} : Set (suc в„“) where
  field
    N   : Set в„“
    _+_ : N вҶ’ N вҶ’ N
    0#  : N

open AddMonoid public

record OrderedMonoid {в„“} : Set (suc в„“) where
  field
    M    : AddMonoid {в„“}
    _вүӨ_  : N M вҶ’ N M вҶ’ Set в„“
    reflвүӨ  : вҲҖ x вҶ’ x вүӨ x
    transвүӨ : вҲҖ x y z вҶ’ x вүӨ y вҶ’ y вүӨ z вҶ’ x вүӨ z
    mono+  : вҲҖ a b c d вҶ’ a вүӨ b вҶ’ c вүӨ d вҶ’
      _вүӨ_ (AddMonoid._+_ M a c) (AddMonoid._+_ M b d)

open OrderedMonoid public

record MDLParts {в„“x в„“n}
  (X : Set в„“x) (O : OrderedMonoid {в„“n})
  : Set (suc (в„“x вҠ” в„“n)) where
  open AddMonoid (M O)
  field
    P D T : X вҶ’ X
    ModelLen ResidLen : X вҶ’ AddMonoid.N (M O)
    MDL : X вҶ’ AddMonoid.N (M O)
    MDL-def : вҲҖ x вҶ’ MDL x вүЎ AddMonoid._+_ (M O) (ModelLen (P x)) (ResidLen (D x))

open MDLParts public

record TradeoffLemma {в„“x в„“n}
  {X : Set в„“x} {O : OrderedMonoid {в„“n}}
  (Parts : MDLParts X O)
  : Set (suc (в„“x вҠ” в„“n)) where
  open OrderedMonoid O
  open AddMonoid (M O)
  field
    model-drop : вҲҖ x вҶ’
      OrderedMonoid._вүӨ_ O
        (ModelLen Parts (P Parts (T Parts x)))
        (ModelLen Parts (P Parts x))
    resid-drop : вҲҖ x вҶ’
      OrderedMonoid._вүӨ_ O
        (ResidLen Parts (D Parts (T Parts x)))
        (ResidLen Parts (D Parts x))

open TradeoffLemma public

-- Descent theorem from the single tradeoff seam.
--
-- Empirical learning (LHC harness): monotone descent holds strongly for
-- L1/MDL-proxy energies even when raw ПҮВІ is non-contractive. This matches
-- the intended geometry: FejГ©r/closest-point descent to a fixed set,
-- not global Euclidean contraction. Keep the seam here; do not assume
-- strict contraction in the raw metric.
MDLDescent :
  вҲҖ {в„“x в„“n} {X : Set в„“x} {O : OrderedMonoid {в„“n}}
  (Parts : MDLParts X O)
  (L : TradeoffLemma Parts)
  вҶ’ вҲҖ x вҶ’ OrderedMonoid._вүӨ_ O (MDL Parts (T Parts x)) (MDL Parts x)
MDLDescent {O = O} Parts L x =
  let
    open OrderedMonoid O
    open AddMonoid (M O)
    open TradeoffLemma L
    mdlt : MDL Parts (T Parts x) вүЎ
      AddMonoid._+_ (M O)
        (ModelLen Parts (P Parts (T Parts x)))
        (ResidLen Parts (D Parts (T Parts x)))
    mdlt = MDL-def Parts (T Parts x)
    mdlx : MDL Parts x вүЎ
      AddMonoid._+_ (M O)
        (ModelLen Parts (P Parts x))
        (ResidLen Parts (D Parts x))
    mdlx = MDL-def Parts x
    step : OrderedMonoid._вүӨ_ O
      (AddMonoid._+_ (M O)
        (ModelLen Parts (P Parts (T Parts x)))
        (ResidLen Parts (D Parts (T Parts x))))
      (AddMonoid._+_ (M O)
        (ModelLen Parts (P Parts x))
        (ResidLen Parts (D Parts x)))
    step = OrderedMonoid.mono+ O
      (ModelLen Parts (P Parts (T Parts x)))
      (ModelLen Parts (P Parts x))
      (ResidLen Parts (D Parts (T Parts x)))
      (ResidLen Parts (D Parts x))
      (TradeoffLemma.model-drop L x)
      (TradeoffLemma.resid-drop L x)
  in
  subst
    (О» v вҶ’ OrderedMonoid._вүӨ_ O v (MDL Parts x))
    (sym mdlt)
    (subst
      (О» v вҶ’ OrderedMonoid._вүӨ_ O
        (AddMonoid._+_ (M O)
          (ModelLen Parts (P Parts (T Parts x)))
          (ResidLen Parts (D Parts (T Parts x))))
        v)
      (sym mdlx)
      step)
