module DASHI.Metric.FineAgreementUltrametric where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat as Nat using (Nat; zero; suc; _+_)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_вүЎ_; refl)
open import Contraction using (_вүў_)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong; trans; sym; subst)
open import Data.Nat using (_<_; _вүӨ_; _вүҘ_; _вҲё_; zвүӨn; sвүӨs)
open import Data.Nat.Properties as NatP
open import Data.Product using (_,_)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec; []; map; _++_; _вҲ·_)
open import Data.Vec.Base using (reverse; _вҲ·Кі_; cast; init; last; initLast)
open import Data.Vec.Properties using (map-reverse; reverse-injective; reverse-вҲ·; reverse-++; cast-is-id; cast-sym)
open import Ultrametric as UMetric
open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (Trit; neg; zer; pos; inv)
open import DASHI.Physics.TailCollapseProof as TCP
import DASHI.Metric.AgreementUltrametric as AM

congвӮӮ : вҲҖ {A B C : Set} {xвӮҒ xвӮӮ : A} {yвӮҒ yвӮӮ : B}
        (g : A вҶ’ B вҶ’ C) вҶ’
        xвӮҒ вүЎ xвӮӮ вҶ’ yвӮҒ вүЎ yвӮӮ вҶ’ g xвӮҒ yвӮҒ вүЎ g xвӮӮ yвӮӮ
congвӮӮ g refl refl = refl

-- Fine agreement metric: use agreement depth on reversed vectors (suffix agreement).
agreeDepthFine : вҲҖ {n : Nat} вҶ’ Vec Trit n вҶ’ Vec Trit n вҶ’ Nat
agreeDepthFine x y = AM.agreeDepth (reverse x) (reverse y)

dNatFine : вҲҖ {n : Nat} вҶ’ Vec Trit n вҶ’ Vec Trit n вҶ’ Nat
dNatFine x y = AM.dNat (reverse x) (reverse y)

dNatFine-inv :
  вҲҖ {n : Nat} (x y : Vec Trit n) вҶ’
  dNatFine (map inv x) (map inv y) вүЎ dNatFine x y
dNatFine-inv x y =
  let
    rx = reverse x
    ry = reverse y
    rx-inv : reverse (map inv x) вүЎ map inv rx
    rx-inv = sym (map-reverse inv x)
    ry-inv : reverse (map inv y) вүЎ map inv ry
    ry-inv = sym (map-reverse inv y)
  in
  trans
    (cong (О» a вҶ’ AM.dNat a (reverse (map inv y))) rx-inv)
    (trans
      (cong (О» b вҶ’ AM.dNat (map inv rx) b) ry-inv)
      (AM.dNat-inv rx ry)
    )

reverseвүў : вҲҖ {n : Nat} {x y : Vec Trit n} вҶ’ x вүў y вҶ’ reverse x вүў reverse y
reverseвүў xвүўy revвүЎ = xвүўy (reverse-injective revвүЎ)

dNatFine-zeroвҶ’eq :
  вҲҖ {n : Nat} (x y : Vec Trit n) вҶ’ dNatFine x y вүЎ 0 вҶ’ x вүЎ y
dNatFine-zeroвҶ’eq x y dвүЎ0 =
  reverse-injective (AM.dNat-zeroвҶ’eq (reverse x) (reverse y) dвүЎ0)

dNatFine-positive :
  вҲҖ {n : Nat} {x y : Vec Trit n} вҶ’ x вүў y вҶ’ 0 < dNatFine x y
dNatFine-positive xвүўy = AM.dNat-positive (reverseвүў xвүўy)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Agreement-depth monotonicity under pointwise maps

agreeDepth-mapвүӨ :
  вҲҖ {n : Nat} (f : Trit вҶ’ Trit) (x y : Vec Trit n) вҶ’
  AM.agreeDepth x y вүӨ AM.agreeDepth (map f x) (map f y)
agreeDepth-mapвүӨ {n = Nat.zero} f [] [] = zвүӨn
agreeDepth-mapвүӨ {suc n} f (neg вҲ· xs) (neg вҲ· ys) with f neg
... | neg = sвүӨs (agreeDepth-mapвүӨ f xs ys)
... | zer = sвүӨs (agreeDepth-mapвүӨ f xs ys)
... | pos = sвүӨs (agreeDepth-mapвүӨ f xs ys)
agreeDepth-mapвүӨ {suc n} f (zer вҲ· xs) (zer вҲ· ys) with f zer
... | neg = sвүӨs (agreeDepth-mapвүӨ f xs ys)
... | zer = sвүӨs (agreeDepth-mapвүӨ f xs ys)
... | pos = sвүӨs (agreeDepth-mapвүӨ f xs ys)
agreeDepth-mapвүӨ {suc n} f (pos вҲ· xs) (pos вҲ· ys) with f pos
... | neg = sвүӨs (agreeDepth-mapвүӨ f xs ys)
... | zer = sвүӨs (agreeDepth-mapвүӨ f xs ys)
... | pos = sвүӨs (agreeDepth-mapвүӨ f xs ys)
agreeDepth-mapвүӨ {suc n} f (neg вҲ· xs) (zer вҲ· ys) = zвүӨn
agreeDepth-mapвүӨ {suc n} f (neg вҲ· xs) (pos вҲ· ys) = zвүӨn
agreeDepth-mapвүӨ {suc n} f (zer вҲ· xs) (neg вҲ· ys) = zвүӨn
agreeDepth-mapвүӨ {suc n} f (zer вҲ· xs) (pos вҲ· ys) = zвүӨn
agreeDepth-mapвүӨ {suc n} f (pos вҲ· xs) (neg вҲ· ys) = zвүӨn
agreeDepth-mapвүӨ {suc n} f (pos вҲ· xs) (zer вҲ· ys) = zвүӨn

dNatFine-mapвүӨ :
  вҲҖ {n : Nat} (f : Trit вҶ’ Trit) (x y : Vec Trit n) вҶ’
  dNatFine (map f x) (map f y) вүӨ dNatFine x y
dNatFine-mapвүӨ {n} f x y =
  let
    rx-map : reverse (map f x) вүЎ map f (reverse x)
    rx-map = sym (map-reverse f x)
    ry-map : reverse (map f y) вүЎ map f (reverse y)
    ry-map = sym (map-reverse f y)
    step : AM.dNat (map f (reverse x)) (map f (reverse y)) вүӨ AM.dNat (reverse x) (reverse y)
    step = NatP.вҲё-monoКі-вүӨ n (agreeDepth-mapвүӨ f (reverse x) (reverse y))
  in
  NatP.вүӨ-trans
    (NatP.вүӨ-reflexive (congвӮӮ AM.dNat rx-map ry-map))
    step

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Agreement depth for append (prefix metric on reverse)

agreeDepth-++вүҘ :
  вҲҖ {m n : Nat} (a b : Vec Trit m) (c : Vec Trit n) вҶ’
  AM.agreeDepth (a ++ c) (b ++ c) вүҘ AM.agreeDepth a b
agreeDepth-++вүҘ {m = Nat.zero} {n} [] [] c = zвүӨn
agreeDepth-++вүҘ {suc m} {n} (neg вҲ· as) (neg вҲ· bs) c =
  sвүӨs (agreeDepth-++вүҘ as bs c)
agreeDepth-++вүҘ {suc m} {n} (zer вҲ· as) (zer вҲ· bs) c =
  sвүӨs (agreeDepth-++вүҘ as bs c)
agreeDepth-++вүҘ {suc m} {n} (pos вҲ· as) (pos вҲ· bs) c =
  sвүӨs (agreeDepth-++вүҘ as bs c)
agreeDepth-++вүҘ {suc m} {n} (neg вҲ· as) (zer вҲ· bs) c = zвүӨn
agreeDepth-++вүҘ {suc m} {n} (neg вҲ· as) (pos вҲ· bs) c = zвүӨn
agreeDepth-++вүҘ {suc m} {n} (zer вҲ· as) (neg вҲ· bs) c = zвүӨn
agreeDepth-++вүҘ {suc m} {n} (zer вҲ· as) (pos вҲ· bs) c = zвүӨn
agreeDepth-++вүҘ {suc m} {n} (pos вҲ· as) (neg вҲ· bs) c = zвүӨn
agreeDepth-++вүҘ {suc m} {n} (pos вҲ· as) (zer вҲ· bs) c = zвүӨn

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Reverse of snoc: reverse (xs вҲ·Кі a) = a вҲ· reverse xs

reverse-вҲ·Кі : вҲҖ {n : Nat} (xs : Vec Trit n) (a : Trit) вҶ’
  reverse (xs вҲ·Кі a) вүЎ a вҲ· reverse xs
reverse-вҲ·Кі [] a = reverse-вҲ· a []
reverse-вҲ·Кі (x вҲ· xs) a
  rewrite reverse-вҲ· x (xs вҲ·Кі a)
        | reverse-вҲ·Кі xs a
        | reverse-вҲ· x xs
  = refl

agreeDepth-cast :
  вҲҖ {m n : Nat} (eq : m вүЎ n) (x y : Vec Trit m) вҶ’
  AM.agreeDepth (cast eq x) (cast eq y) вүЎ AM.agreeDepth x y
agreeDepth-cast refl x y
  rewrite cast-is-id refl x
        | cast-is-id refl y
  = refl

dNat-cast :
  вҲҖ {m n : Nat} (eq : m вүЎ n) (x y : Vec Trit m) вҶ’
  AM.dNat (cast eq x) (cast eq y) вүЎ AM.dNat x y
dNat-cast refl x y
  rewrite cast-is-id refl x
        | cast-is-id refl y
  = refl

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- ShiftTail monotonicity on fine agreement

agreeDepth-++-mono :
  вҲҖ {m n : Nat} (u v u' v' : Vec Trit m) (p q : Vec Trit n) вҶ’
  AM.agreeDepth u v вүӨ AM.agreeDepth u' v' вҶ’
  AM.agreeDepth (u ++ p) (v ++ q) вүӨ AM.agreeDepth (u' ++ p) (v' ++ q)
agreeDepth-++-mono {m = Nat.zero} {n} [] [] [] [] p q h = NatP.вүӨ-refl
agreeDepth-++-mono {suc m} {n} (neg вҲ· us) (neg вҲ· vs) (neg вҲ· us') (neg вҲ· vs') p q (sвүӨs hвүӨ) =
  sвүӨs (agreeDepth-++-mono us vs us' vs' p q hвүӨ)
agreeDepth-++-mono {suc m} {n} (neg вҲ· us) (neg вҲ· vs) (zer вҲ· us') (zer вҲ· vs') p q (sвүӨs hвүӨ) =
  sвүӨs (agreeDepth-++-mono us vs us' vs' p q hвүӨ)
agreeDepth-++-mono {suc m} {n} (neg вҲ· us) (neg вҲ· vs) (pos вҲ· us') (pos вҲ· vs') p q (sвүӨs hвүӨ) =
  sвүӨs (agreeDepth-++-mono us vs us' vs' p q hвүӨ)
agreeDepth-++-mono {suc m} {n} (zer вҲ· us) (zer вҲ· vs) (neg вҲ· us') (neg вҲ· vs') p q (sвүӨs hвүӨ) =
  sвүӨs (agreeDepth-++-mono us vs us' vs' p q hвүӨ)
agreeDepth-++-mono {suc m} {n} (zer вҲ· us) (zer вҲ· vs) (zer вҲ· us') (zer вҲ· vs') p q (sвүӨs hвүӨ) =
  sвүӨs (agreeDepth-++-mono us vs us' vs' p q hвүӨ)
agreeDepth-++-mono {suc m} {n} (zer вҲ· us) (zer вҲ· vs) (pos вҲ· us') (pos вҲ· vs') p q (sвүӨs hвүӨ) =
  sвүӨs (agreeDepth-++-mono us vs us' vs' p q hвүӨ)
agreeDepth-++-mono {suc m} {n} (pos вҲ· us) (pos вҲ· vs) (neg вҲ· us') (neg вҲ· vs') p q (sвүӨs hвүӨ) =
  sвүӨs (agreeDepth-++-mono us vs us' vs' p q hвүӨ)
agreeDepth-++-mono {suc m} {n} (pos вҲ· us) (pos вҲ· vs) (zer вҲ· us') (zer вҲ· vs') p q (sвүӨs hвүӨ) =
  sвүӨs (agreeDepth-++-mono us vs us' vs' p q hвүӨ)
agreeDepth-++-mono {suc m} {n} (pos вҲ· us) (pos вҲ· vs) (pos вҲ· us') (pos вҲ· vs') p q (sвүӨs hвүӨ) =
  sвүӨs (agreeDepth-++-mono us vs us' vs' p q hвүӨ)
agreeDepth-++-mono {suc m} {n} (neg вҲ· us) (zer вҲ· vs) u' v' p q h = zвүӨn
agreeDepth-++-mono {suc m} {n} (neg вҲ· us) (pos вҲ· vs) u' v' p q h = zвүӨn
agreeDepth-++-mono {suc m} {n} (zer вҲ· us) (neg вҲ· vs) u' v' p q h = zвүӨn
agreeDepth-++-mono {suc m} {n} (zer вҲ· us) (pos вҲ· vs) u' v' p q h = zвүӨn
agreeDepth-++-mono {suc m} {n} (pos вҲ· us) (neg вҲ· vs) u' v' p q h = zвүӨn
agreeDepth-++-mono {suc m} {n} (pos вҲ· us) (zer вҲ· vs) u' v' p q h = zвүӨn

agreeDepth-++-mapвүӨ :
  вҲҖ {m n : Nat} (u v : Vec Trit m) (p q : Vec Trit n) (f : Trit вҶ’ Trit) вҶ’
  AM.agreeDepth (u ++ p) (v ++ q) вүӨ AM.agreeDepth (u ++ map f p) (v ++ map f q)
agreeDepth-++-mapвүӨ {m = Nat.zero} {n} [] [] p q f = agreeDepth-mapвүӨ f p q
agreeDepth-++-mapвүӨ {suc m} {n} (neg вҲ· us) (neg вҲ· vs) p q f =
  sвүӨs (agreeDepth-++-mapвүӨ us vs p q f)
agreeDepth-++-mapвүӨ {suc m} {n} (zer вҲ· us) (zer вҲ· vs) p q f =
  sвүӨs (agreeDepth-++-mapвүӨ us vs p q f)
agreeDepth-++-mapвүӨ {suc m} {n} (pos вҲ· us) (pos вҲ· vs) p q f =
  sвүӨs (agreeDepth-++-mapвүӨ us vs p q f)
agreeDepth-++-mapвүӨ {suc m} {n} (neg вҲ· us) (zer вҲ· vs) p q f = zвүӨn
agreeDepth-++-mapвүӨ {suc m} {n} (neg вҲ· us) (pos вҲ· vs) p q f = zвүӨn
agreeDepth-++-mapвүӨ {suc m} {n} (zer вҲ· us) (neg вҲ· vs) p q f = zвүӨn
agreeDepth-++-mapвүӨ {suc m} {n} (zer вҲ· us) (pos вҲ· vs) p q f = zвүӨn
agreeDepth-++-mapвүӨ {suc m} {n} (pos вҲ· us) (neg вҲ· vs) p q f = zвүӨn
agreeDepth-++-mapвүӨ {suc m} {n} (pos вҲ· us) (zer вҲ· vs) p q f = zвүӨn

agreeDepth-вҲ·КівүӨ :
  вҲҖ {n : Nat} (a b : Vec Trit n) (x y : Trit) вҶ’
  AM.agreeDepth (a вҲ·Кі x) (b вҲ·Кі y) вүӨ suc (AM.agreeDepth a b)
agreeDepth-вҲ·КівүӨ {n = Nat.zero} [] [] neg neg = sвүӨs zвүӨn
agreeDepth-вҲ·КівүӨ {n = Nat.zero} [] [] zer zer = sвүӨs zвүӨn
agreeDepth-вҲ·КівүӨ {n = Nat.zero} [] [] pos pos = sвүӨs zвүӨn
agreeDepth-вҲ·КівүӨ {n = Nat.zero} [] [] neg zer = zвүӨn
agreeDepth-вҲ·КівүӨ {n = Nat.zero} [] [] neg pos = zвүӨn
agreeDepth-вҲ·КівүӨ {n = Nat.zero} [] [] zer neg = zвүӨn
agreeDepth-вҲ·КівүӨ {n = Nat.zero} [] [] zer pos = zвүӨn
agreeDepth-вҲ·КівүӨ {n = Nat.zero} [] [] pos neg = zвүӨn
agreeDepth-вҲ·КівүӨ {n = Nat.zero} [] [] pos zer = zвүӨn
agreeDepth-вҲ·КівүӨ {suc n} (neg вҲ· as) (neg вҲ· bs) x y =
  sвүӨs (agreeDepth-вҲ·КівүӨ as bs x y)
agreeDepth-вҲ·КівүӨ {suc n} (zer вҲ· as) (zer вҲ· bs) x y =
  sвүӨs (agreeDepth-вҲ·КівүӨ as bs x y)
agreeDepth-вҲ·КівүӨ {suc n} (pos вҲ· as) (pos вҲ· bs) x y =
  sвүӨs (agreeDepth-вҲ·КівүӨ as bs x y)
agreeDepth-вҲ·КівүӨ {suc n} (neg вҲ· as) (zer вҲ· bs) x y = zвүӨn
agreeDepth-вҲ·КівүӨ {suc n} (neg вҲ· as) (pos вҲ· bs) x y = zвүӨn
agreeDepth-вҲ·КівүӨ {suc n} (zer вҲ· as) (neg вҲ· bs) x y = zвүӨn
agreeDepth-вҲ·КівүӨ {suc n} (zer вҲ· as) (pos вҲ· bs) x y = zвүӨn
agreeDepth-вҲ·КівүӨ {suc n} (pos вҲ· as) (neg вҲ· bs) x y = zвүӨn
agreeDepth-вҲ·КівүӨ {suc n} (pos вҲ· as) (zer вҲ· bs) x y = zвүӨn

agreeDepth-вҲ·вүӨ :
  вҲҖ {n : Nat} (a b : Trit) (as bs : Vec Trit n) вҶ’
  AM.agreeDepth (a вҲ· as) (b вҲ· bs) вүӨ suc (AM.agreeDepth as bs)
agreeDepth-вҲ·вүӨ neg neg as bs = sвүӨs NatP.вүӨ-refl
agreeDepth-вҲ·вүӨ zer zer as bs = sвүӨs NatP.вүӨ-refl
agreeDepth-вҲ·вүӨ pos pos as bs = sвүӨs NatP.вүӨ-refl
agreeDepth-вҲ·вүӨ neg zer as bs = zвүӨn
agreeDepth-вҲ·вүӨ neg pos as bs = zвүӨn
agreeDepth-вҲ·вүӨ zer neg as bs = zвүӨn
agreeDepth-вҲ·вүӨ zer pos as bs = zвүӨn
agreeDepth-вҲ·вүӨ pos neg as bs = zвүӨn
agreeDepth-вҲ·вүӨ pos zer as bs = zвүӨn

agreeDepthFine-shiftTailвүҘ :
  вҲҖ {k : Nat} (t1 t2 : Vec Trit k) вҶ’
  agreeDepthFine t1 t2 вүӨ agreeDepthFine (TCP.shiftTail t1) (TCP.shiftTail t2)
agreeDepthFine-shiftTailвүҘ {k = Nat.zero} [] [] = zвүӨn
agreeDepthFine-shiftTailвүҘ {suc k} (x вҲ· xs) (y вҲ· ys) =
  NatP.вүӨ-trans
    (subst
      (О» v вҶ’ v вүӨ suc (AM.agreeDepth (reverse xs) (reverse ys)))
      (sym lhs1)
      (agreeDepth-вҲ·КівүӨ (reverse xs) (reverse ys) x y))
    (NatP.вүӨ-reflexive (sym lhs))
  where
    lhs1 : agreeDepthFine (x вҲ· xs) (y вҲ· ys)
           вүЎ AM.agreeDepth (reverse xs вҲ·Кі x) (reverse ys вҲ·Кі y)
    lhs1 rewrite reverse-вҲ· x xs | reverse-вҲ· y ys = refl
    lhs : AM.agreeDepth (reverse (TCP.shiftTail (x вҲ· xs)))
                        (reverse (TCP.shiftTail (y вҲ· ys)))
          вүЎ suc (AM.agreeDepth (reverse xs) (reverse ys))
    lhs rewrite reverse-вҲ·Кі xs zer | reverse-вҲ·Кі ys zer = refl

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Nonexpansive for shiftTail (tail-only)

dNatFine-shiftTailвүӨ :
  вҲҖ {k : Nat} (t1 t2 : Vec Trit k) вҶ’
  dNatFine (TCP.shiftTail t1) (TCP.shiftTail t2) вүӨ dNatFine t1 t2
dNatFine-shiftTailвүӨ {k} t1 t2 =
  NatP.вҲё-monoКі-вүӨ k (agreeDepthFine-shiftTailвүҘ t1 t2)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Nonexpansive for projTail (tail-only)

agreeDepthFine-projTailвүҘ :
  вҲҖ {k : Nat} (t1 t2 : Vec Trit k) вҶ’
  agreeDepthFine t1 t2 вүӨ agreeDepthFine (TCP.projTail t1) (TCP.projTail t2)
agreeDepthFine-projTailвүҘ {k = Nat.zero} [] [] = zвүӨn
agreeDepthFine-projTailвүҘ {k = Nat.suc k} (x вҲ· xs) (y вҲ· ys) =
  NatP.вүӨ-trans bound (NatP.вүӨ-reflexive (sym (trans r1 r2)))
  where
    init-вҲ·Кі-last : вҲҖ {n : Nat} (t : Vec Trit (suc n)) вҶ’ init t вҲ·Кі last t вүЎ t
    init-вҲ·Кі-last t with initLast t
    ... | ys , y , eq = sym eq

    reverse-init-last :
      вҲҖ {n : Nat} (t : Vec Trit (suc n)) вҶ’
      reverse t вүЎ last t вҲ· reverse (init t)
    reverse-init-last t =
      trans
        (cong reverse (sym (init-вҲ·Кі-last t)))
        (reverse-вҲ·Кі (init t) (last t))

    r1 : agreeDepthFine (TCP.projTail (x вҲ· xs)) (TCP.projTail (y вҲ· ys))
         вүЎ AM.agreeDepth (zer вҲ· reverse (init (x вҲ· xs))) (zer вҲ· reverse (init (y вҲ· ys)))
    r1 rewrite reverse-вҲ·Кі (init (x вҲ· xs)) zer | reverse-вҲ·Кі (init (y вҲ· ys)) zer = refl

    r2 : AM.agreeDepth (zer вҲ· reverse (init (x вҲ· xs))) (zer вҲ· reverse (init (y вҲ· ys)))
         вүЎ suc (AM.agreeDepth (reverse (init (x вҲ· xs))) (reverse (init (y вҲ· ys))))
    r2 = refl
    lhs1 : agreeDepthFine (x вҲ· xs) (y вҲ· ys)
           вүЎ AM.agreeDepth (last (x вҲ· xs) вҲ· reverse (init (x вҲ· xs)))
                           (last (y вҲ· ys) вҲ· reverse (init (y вҲ· ys)))
    lhs1 rewrite reverse-init-last (x вҲ· xs)
                | reverse-init-last (y вҲ· ys)
      = refl
    bound :
      agreeDepthFine (x вҲ· xs) (y вҲ· ys)
      вүӨ suc (AM.agreeDepth (reverse (init (x вҲ· xs))) (reverse (init (y вҲ· ys))))
    bound =
      subst
        (О» v вҶ’ v вүӨ suc (AM.agreeDepth (reverse (init (x вҲ· xs))) (reverse (init (y вҲ· ys)))))
        (sym lhs1)
        (agreeDepth-вҲ·вүӨ (last (x вҲ· xs)) (last (y вҲ· ys))
                       (reverse (init (x вҲ· xs))) (reverse (init (y вҲ· ys))))

dNatFine-projTailвүӨ :
  вҲҖ {k : Nat} (t1 t2 : Vec Trit k) вҶ’
  dNatFine (TCP.projTail t1) (TCP.projTail t2) вүӨ dNatFine t1 t2
dNatFine-projTailвүӨ {k} t1 t2 =
  NatP.вҲё-monoКі-вүӨ k (agreeDepthFine-projTailвүҘ t1 t2)

dNatFine-++ :
  вҲҖ {m n : Nat} (c c' : Vec Trit m) (t t' : Vec Trit n) вҶ’
  dNatFine (c ++ t) (c' ++ t') вүЎ
  AM.dNat (reverse t ++ reverse c) (reverse t' ++ reverse c')
dNatFine-++ {m} {n} c c' t t' =
  let
    eq : m + n вүЎ n + m
    eq = NatP.+-comm m n
    rx : reverse (c ++ t) вүЎ cast (sym eq) (reverse t ++ reverse c)
    rx = sym (cast-sym eq (reverse-++ eq c t))
    ry : reverse (c' ++ t') вүЎ cast (sym eq) (reverse t' ++ reverse c')
    ry = sym (cast-sym eq (reverse-++ eq c' t'))
  in
  trans
    (congвӮӮ AM.dNat rx ry)
    (dNat-cast (sym eq) (reverse t ++ reverse c) (reverse t' ++ reverse c'))

dNatFine-++-mapвүӨ :
  вҲҖ {m n : Nat} (c c' : Vec Trit m) (t t' : Vec Trit n) (f : Trit вҶ’ Trit) вҶ’
  dNatFine (map f c ++ t) (map f c' ++ t') вүӨ dNatFine (c ++ t) (c' ++ t')
dNatFine-++-mapвүӨ {m} {n} c c' t t' f =
  let
    eq : m + n вүЎ n + m
    eq = NatP.+-comm m n
    rx-cast : reverse (map f c ++ t) вүЎ cast (sym eq) (reverse t ++ reverse (map f c))
    rx-cast = sym (cast-sym eq (reverse-++ eq (map f c) t))
    ry-cast : reverse (map f c' ++ t') вүЎ cast (sym eq) (reverse t' ++ reverse (map f c'))
    ry-cast = sym (cast-sym eq (reverse-++ eq (map f c') t'))
    rx-map : reverse (map f c ++ t) вүЎ cast (sym eq) (reverse t ++ map f (reverse c))
    rx-map = trans rx-cast (cong (cast (sym eq)) (cong (reverse t ++_) (sym (map-reverse f c))))
    ry-map : reverse (map f c' ++ t') вүЎ cast (sym eq) (reverse t' ++ map f (reverse c'))
    ry-map = trans ry-cast (cong (cast (sym eq)) (cong (reverse t' ++_) (sym (map-reverse f c'))))
    step : AM.dNat (reverse t ++ map f (reverse c))
                   (reverse t' ++ map f (reverse c'))
           вүӨ AM.dNat (reverse t ++ reverse c)
                    (reverse t' ++ reverse c')
    step = NatP.вҲё-monoКі-вүӨ (n + m)
             (agreeDepth-++-mapвүӨ (reverse t) (reverse t') (reverse c) (reverse c') f)

    rhs : dNatFine (c ++ t) (c' ++ t') вүЎ
          AM.dNat (reverse t ++ reverse c) (reverse t' ++ reverse c')
    rhs = dNatFine-++ c c' t t'
  in
  NatP.вүӨ-trans
    (NatP.вүӨ-reflexive (trans (congвӮӮ AM.dNat rx-map ry-map) (dNat-cast (sym eq) _ _)))
    (NatP.вүӨ-trans step (NatP.вүӨ-reflexive (sym rhs)))

dNatFine-++-mapвүӨ-tail :
  вҲҖ {m n : Nat} (c c' : Vec Trit m) (t t' : Vec Trit n) (f : Trit вҶ’ Trit) вҶ’
  dNatFine (c ++ map f t) (c' ++ map f t') вүӨ dNatFine (c ++ t) (c' ++ t')
dNatFine-++-mapвүӨ-tail {m} {n} c c' t t' f =
  let
    eq : m + n вүЎ n + m
    eq = NatP.+-comm m n
    rx-cast : reverse (c ++ map f t) вүЎ cast (sym eq) (reverse (map f t) ++ reverse c)
    rx-cast = sym (cast-sym eq (reverse-++ eq c (map f t)))
    ry-cast : reverse (c' ++ map f t') вүЎ cast (sym eq) (reverse (map f t') ++ reverse c')
    ry-cast = sym (cast-sym eq (reverse-++ eq c' (map f t')))
    rx-map : reverse (c ++ map f t) вүЎ cast (sym eq) (map f (reverse t) ++ reverse c)
    rx-map = trans rx-cast (cong (cast (sym eq)) (cong (_++ reverse c) (sym (map-reverse f t))))
    ry-map : reverse (c' ++ map f t') вүЎ cast (sym eq) (map f (reverse t') ++ reverse c')
    ry-map = trans ry-cast (cong (cast (sym eq)) (cong (_++ reverse c') (sym (map-reverse f t'))))
    depthвүӨ :
      AM.agreeDepth (reverse t ++ reverse c) (reverse t' ++ reverse c')
      вүӨ AM.agreeDepth (map f (reverse t) ++ reverse c)
                     (map f (reverse t') ++ reverse c')
    depthвүӨ =
      agreeDepth-++-mono
        (reverse t) (reverse t')
        (map f (reverse t)) (map f (reverse t'))
        (reverse c) (reverse c')
        (agreeDepth-mapвүӨ f (reverse t) (reverse t'))
    step : AM.dNat (map f (reverse t) ++ reverse c)
                   (map f (reverse t') ++ reverse c')
           вүӨ AM.dNat (reverse t ++ reverse c)
                    (reverse t' ++ reverse c')
    step = NatP.вҲё-monoКі-вүӨ (n + m) depthвүӨ
    rhs : dNatFine (c ++ t) (c' ++ t') вүЎ
          AM.dNat (reverse t ++ reverse c) (reverse t' ++ reverse c')
    rhs = dNatFine-++ c c' t t'
  in
  NatP.вүӨ-trans
    (NatP.вүӨ-reflexive (trans (congвӮӮ AM.dNat rx-map ry-map) (dNat-cast (sym eq) _ _)))
    (NatP.вүӨ-trans step (NatP.вүӨ-reflexive (sym rhs)))

dNatFine-++-shiftTailвүӨ :
  вҲҖ {m n : Nat} (c c' : Vec Trit m) (t t' : Vec Trit n) вҶ’
  dNatFine (c ++ TCP.shiftTail t) (c' ++ TCP.shiftTail t') вүӨ dNatFine (c ++ t) (c' ++ t')
dNatFine-++-shiftTailвүӨ {m} {n} c c' t t'
  rewrite dNatFine-++ c c' (TCP.shiftTail t) (TCP.shiftTail t')
        | dNatFine-++ c c' t t' =
  let
    depthвүӨ :
      AM.agreeDepth (reverse t ++ reverse c) (reverse t' ++ reverse c')
      вүӨ AM.agreeDepth (reverse (TCP.shiftTail t) ++ reverse c)
                     (reverse (TCP.shiftTail t') ++ reverse c')
    depthвүӨ =
      agreeDepth-++-mono
        (reverse t) (reverse t')
        (reverse (TCP.shiftTail t)) (reverse (TCP.shiftTail t'))
        (reverse c) (reverse c')
        (agreeDepthFine-shiftTailвүҘ t t')
  in
  NatP.вҲё-monoКі-вүӨ (n + m) depthвүӨ

dNatFine-++-projTailвүӨ :
  вҲҖ {m n : Nat} (c c' : Vec Trit m) (t t' : Vec Trit n) вҶ’
  dNatFine (c ++ TCP.projTail t) (c' ++ TCP.projTail t') вүӨ dNatFine (c ++ t) (c' ++ t')
dNatFine-++-projTailвүӨ {m} {n} c c' t t'
  rewrite dNatFine-++ c c' (TCP.projTail t) (TCP.projTail t')
        | dNatFine-++ c c' t t' =
  let
    depthвүӨ :
      AM.agreeDepth (reverse t ++ reverse c) (reverse t' ++ reverse c')
      вүӨ AM.agreeDepth (reverse (TCP.projTail t) ++ reverse c)
                     (reverse (TCP.projTail t') ++ reverse c')
    depthвүӨ =
      agreeDepth-++-mono
        (reverse t) (reverse t')
        (reverse (TCP.projTail t)) (reverse (TCP.projTail t'))
        (reverse c) (reverse c')
        (agreeDepthFine-projTailвүҘ t t')
  in
  NatP.вҲё-monoКі-вүӨ (n + m) depthвүӨ

ultrametricVec : вҲҖ {n : Nat} вҶ’ UMetric.Ultrametric (Vec Trit n)
ultrametricVec {n} =
  record
    { d = dNatFine
    ; id-zero = О» x вҶ’ UMetric.Ultrametric.id-zero AM.ultrametricVec (reverse x)
    ; symmetric = О» x y вҶ’ UMetric.Ultrametric.symmetric AM.ultrametricVec (reverse x) (reverse y)
    ; ultratriangle = О» x y z вҶ’ UMetric.Ultrametric.ultratriangle AM.ultrametricVec (reverse x) (reverse y) (reverse z)
    }
module DASHI.Metric.AgreementUltrametric where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_вүЎ_; refl)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong; sym; trans)
open import Data.Nat using (_вүӨ_; _<_; _вүҘ_; _вҠ”_; _вҠ“_; _вҲё_; zвүӨn; sвүӨs)
open import Data.Nat.Properties as NatP
open import Data.Sum using (injвӮҒ; injвӮӮ)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec; []; _вҲ·_; map)
open import Contraction using (_вүў_)
open import Ultrametric as UMetric
open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (Trit; neg; zer; pos)
open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (inv)

-- Agreement depth (longest common prefix) for Vec Trit n.
agreeDepth : вҲҖ {n : Nat} вҶ’ Vec Trit n вҶ’ Vec Trit n вҶ’ Nat
agreeDepth [] [] = zero
agreeDepth (neg вҲ· xs) (neg вҲ· ys) = suc (agreeDepth xs ys)
agreeDepth (zer вҲ· xs) (zer вҲ· ys) = suc (agreeDepth xs ys)
agreeDepth (pos вҲ· xs) (pos вҲ· ys) = suc (agreeDepth xs ys)
agreeDepth _ _ = zero

-- Distance: reversed depth.
dNat : вҲҖ {n : Nat} вҶ’ Vec Trit n вҶ’ Vec Trit n вҶ’ Nat
dNat {n} x y = n вҲё agreeDepth x y

agreeDepth-self : вҲҖ {n : Nat} (x : Vec Trit n) вҶ’ agreeDepth x x вүЎ n
agreeDepth-self [] = refl
agreeDepth-self (neg вҲ· xs) rewrite agreeDepth-self xs = refl
agreeDepth-self (zer вҲ· xs) rewrite agreeDepth-self xs = refl
agreeDepth-self (pos вҲ· xs) rewrite agreeDepth-self xs = refl

agreeDepth-sym : вҲҖ {n : Nat} (x y : Vec Trit n) вҶ’ agreeDepth x y вүЎ agreeDepth y x
agreeDepth-sym [] [] = refl
agreeDepth-sym (neg вҲ· xs) (neg вҲ· ys) rewrite agreeDepth-sym xs ys = refl
agreeDepth-sym (zer вҲ· xs) (zer вҲ· ys) rewrite agreeDepth-sym xs ys = refl
agreeDepth-sym (pos вҲ· xs) (pos вҲ· ys) rewrite agreeDepth-sym xs ys = refl
agreeDepth-sym (neg вҲ· xs) (zer вҲ· ys) = refl
agreeDepth-sym (neg вҲ· xs) (pos вҲ· ys) = refl
agreeDepth-sym (zer вҲ· xs) (neg вҲ· ys) = refl
agreeDepth-sym (zer вҲ· xs) (pos вҲ· ys) = refl
agreeDepth-sym (pos вҲ· xs) (neg вҲ· ys) = refl
agreeDepth-sym (pos вҲ· xs) (zer вҲ· ys) = refl

agreeDepth-inv :
  вҲҖ {n : Nat} (x y : Vec Trit n) вҶ’
  agreeDepth (map inv x) (map inv y) вүЎ agreeDepth x y
agreeDepth-inv [] [] = refl
agreeDepth-inv (neg вҲ· xs) (neg вҲ· ys) rewrite agreeDepth-inv xs ys = refl
agreeDepth-inv (zer вҲ· xs) (zer вҲ· ys) rewrite agreeDepth-inv xs ys = refl
agreeDepth-inv (pos вҲ· xs) (pos вҲ· ys) rewrite agreeDepth-inv xs ys = refl
agreeDepth-inv (neg вҲ· xs) (zer вҲ· ys) = refl
agreeDepth-inv (neg вҲ· xs) (pos вҲ· ys) = refl
agreeDepth-inv (zer вҲ· xs) (neg вҲ· ys) = refl
agreeDepth-inv (zer вҲ· xs) (pos вҲ· ys) = refl
agreeDepth-inv (pos вҲ· xs) (neg вҲ· ys) = refl
agreeDepth-inv (pos вҲ· xs) (zer вҲ· ys) = refl

dNat-inv :
  вҲҖ {n : Nat} (x y : Vec Trit n) вҶ’
  dNat (map inv x) (map inv y) вүЎ dNat x y
dNat-inv {n} x y = cong (О» k вҶ’ n вҲё k) (agreeDepth-inv x y)

agreeDepthвүӨn : вҲҖ {n : Nat} (x y : Vec Trit n) вҶ’ agreeDepth x y вүӨ n
agreeDepthвүӨn [] [] = zвүӨn
agreeDepthвүӨn (neg вҲ· xs) (neg вҲ· ys) = sвүӨs (agreeDepthвүӨn xs ys)
agreeDepthвүӨn (zer вҲ· xs) (zer вҲ· ys) = sвүӨs (agreeDepthвүӨn xs ys)
agreeDepthвүӨn (pos вҲ· xs) (pos вҲ· ys) = sвүӨs (agreeDepthвүӨn xs ys)
agreeDepthвүӨn (neg вҲ· xs) (zer вҲ· ys) = zвүӨn
agreeDepthвүӨn (neg вҲ· xs) (pos вҲ· ys) = zвүӨn
agreeDepthвүӨn (zer вҲ· xs) (neg вҲ· ys) = zвүӨn
agreeDepthвүӨn (zer вҲ· xs) (pos вҲ· ys) = zвүӨn
agreeDepthвүӨn (pos вҲ· xs) (neg вҲ· ys) = zвүӨn
agreeDepthвүӨn (pos вҲ· xs) (zer вҲ· ys) = zвүӨn

agreeDepth-eqвҶ’eq : вҲҖ {n : Nat} (x y : Vec Trit n) вҶ’ agreeDepth x y вүЎ n вҶ’ x вүЎ y
agreeDepth-eqвҶ’eq [] [] _ = refl
agreeDepth-eqвҶ’eq (neg вҲ· xs) (neg вҲ· ys) eq =
  cong (neg вҲ·_) (agreeDepth-eqвҶ’eq xs ys (NatP.suc-injective eq))
agreeDepth-eqвҶ’eq (zer вҲ· xs) (zer вҲ· ys) eq =
  cong (zer вҲ·_) (agreeDepth-eqвҶ’eq xs ys (NatP.suc-injective eq))
agreeDepth-eqвҶ’eq (pos вҲ· xs) (pos вҲ· ys) eq =
  cong (pos вҲ·_) (agreeDepth-eqвҶ’eq xs ys (NatP.suc-injective eq))
agreeDepth-eqвҶ’eq (neg вҲ· xs) (zer вҲ· ys) ()
agreeDepth-eqвҶ’eq (neg вҲ· xs) (pos вҲ· ys) ()
agreeDepth-eqвҶ’eq (zer вҲ· xs) (neg вҲ· ys) ()
agreeDepth-eqвҶ’eq (zer вҲ· xs) (pos вҲ· ys) ()
agreeDepth-eqвҶ’eq (pos вҲ· xs) (neg вҲ· ys) ()
agreeDepth-eqвҶ’eq (pos вҲ· xs) (zer вҲ· ys) ()

dNat-zeroвҶ’eq : вҲҖ {n : Nat} (x y : Vec Trit n) вҶ’ dNat x y вүЎ 0 вҶ’ x вүЎ y
dNat-zeroвҶ’eq {n} x y dвүЎ0 =
  let
    depthвүҘ : n вүӨ agreeDepth x y
    depthвүҘ = NatP.mвҲёnвүЎ0вҮ’mвүӨn dвүЎ0
    depthвүӨ : agreeDepth x y вүӨ n
    depthвүӨ = agreeDepthвүӨn x y
    depthвүЎ : agreeDepth x y вүЎ n
    depthвүЎ = NatP.вүӨ-antisym depthвүӨ depthвүҘ
  in
  agreeDepth-eqвҶ’eq x y depthвүЎ

dNat-nonzero : вҲҖ {n : Nat} {x y : Vec Trit n} вҶ’ x вүў y вҶ’ dNat x y вүў 0
dNat-nonzero xвүўy dвүЎ0 = xвүўy (dNat-zeroвҶ’eq _ _ dвүЎ0)

dNat-positive : вҲҖ {n : Nat} {x y : Vec Trit n} вҶ’ x вүў y вҶ’ 0 < dNat x y
dNat-positive xвүўy = NatP.nвүў0вҮ’n>0 (dNat-nonzero xвүўy)

-- Strong triangle inequality for agreement depth (prefix metric).
agreeDepth-triangle :
  вҲҖ {n : Nat} (x y z : Vec Trit n) вҶ’
  (agreeDepth x y вҠ“ agreeDepth y z) вүӨ agreeDepth x z
agreeDepth-triangle [] [] [] = zвүӨn
agreeDepth-triangle (x вҲ· xs) (y вҲ· ys) (z вҲ· zs) with x | y | z
... | neg | neg | neg =
  sвүӨs (agreeDepth-triangle xs ys zs)
... | zer | zer | zer =
  sвүӨs (agreeDepth-triangle xs ys zs)
... | pos | pos | pos =
  sвүӨs (agreeDepth-triangle xs ys zs)
... | neg | neg | zer = zвүӨn
... | neg | neg | pos = zвүӨn
... | zer | zer | neg = zвүӨn
... | zer | zer | pos = zвүӨn
... | pos | pos | neg = zвүӨn
... | pos | pos | zer = zвүӨn
... | neg | zer | _ = zвүӨn
... | neg | pos | _ = zвүӨn
... | zer | neg | _ = zвүӨn
... | zer | pos | _ = zвүӨn
... | pos | neg | _ = zвүӨn
... | pos | zer | _ = zвүӨn

-- Ultrametric inequality: d x z вүӨ max (d x y) (d y z)
ultraNat : вҲҖ {n : Nat} (x y z : Vec Trit n) вҶ’ dNat x z вүӨ (dNat x y вҠ” dNat y z)
ultraNat {n} x y z with NatP.вүӨ-total (agreeDepth x y) (agreeDepth y z)
... | injвӮҒ xyвүӨyz =
  let
    minвүЎ : (agreeDepth x y вҠ“ agreeDepth y z) вүЎ agreeDepth x y
    minвүЎ = NatP.mвүӨnвҮ’mвҠ“nвүЎm xyвүӨyz
    depthвүӨ : agreeDepth x y вүӨ agreeDepth x z
    depthвүӨ = NatP.вүӨ-trans (NatP.вүӨ-reflexive (sym minвүЎ)) (agreeDepth-triangle x y z)
    depthвүҘ : agreeDepth x z вүҘ agreeDepth x y
    depthвүҘ = depthвүӨ
    step1 : dNat x z вүӨ dNat x y
    step1 = NatP.вҲё-mono (NatP.вүӨ-refl {n}) depthвүҘ
    step2 : dNat x z вүӨ (dNat x y вҠ” dNat y z)
    step2 = NatP.вүӨ-trans step1 (NatP.mвүӨmвҠ”n (dNat x y) (dNat y z))
  in step2
... | injвӮӮ yzвүӨxy =
  let
    minвүЎ : (agreeDepth x y вҠ“ agreeDepth y z) вүЎ agreeDepth y z
    minвүЎ = NatP.mвүҘnвҮ’mвҠ“nвүЎn yzвүӨxy
    depthвүӨ : agreeDepth y z вүӨ agreeDepth x z
    depthвүӨ = NatP.вүӨ-trans (NatP.вүӨ-reflexive (sym minвүЎ)) (agreeDepth-triangle x y z)
    depthвүҘ : agreeDepth x z вүҘ agreeDepth y z
    depthвүҘ = depthвүӨ
    step1 : dNat x z вүӨ dNat y z
    step1 = NatP.вҲё-mono (NatP.вүӨ-refl {n}) depthвүҘ
    step2 : dNat x z вүӨ (dNat x y вҠ” dNat y z)
    step2 = NatP.вүӨ-trans step1 (NatP.mвүӨnвҠ”m (dNat x y) (dNat y z))
  in step2

ultrametricVec : вҲҖ {n : Nat} вҶ’ UMetric.Ultrametric (Vec Trit n)
ultrametricVec {n} =
  record
    { d = dNat
    ; id-zero = О» x вҶ’
        trans
          (cong (О» k вҶ’ n вҲё k) (agreeDepth-self x))
          (NatP.nвҲёnвүЎ0 n)
    ; symmetric = О» x y вҶ’
        cong (О» k вҶ’ n вҲё k) (agreeDepth-sym x y)
    ; ultratriangle = ultraNat
    }

module DASHI.Combinatorics.FractranCOL where

open import Data.Nat renaming (в„• to Nat)
open import Data.Nat.Properties as NatProp using
  (вүӨ-refl; вүӨ-trans; <-trans; +-mono-вүӨ; <-step)
open import Data.Maybe using (Maybe; just; nothing)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec; []; _вҲ·_)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_вүЎ_; refl; cong)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- State: exponent vector for primes [2,3,5,7,11] (5 lanes)
-- lane 0=2, 1=3, 2=5, 3=7, 4=11

EV5 : Set
EV5 = Vec Nat 5

get : вҲҖ {n} вҶ’ Vec Nat n вҶ’ Nat вҶ’ Nat
get (x вҲ· xs) zero    = x
get (x вҲ· xs) (suc i) = get xs i
get []       _       = zero

set : вҲҖ {n} вҶ’ Vec Nat n вҶ’ Nat вҶ’ Nat вҶ’ Vec Nat n
set (x вҲ· xs) zero    v = v вҲ· xs
set (x вҲ· xs) (suc i) v = x вҲ· set xs i v
set []       _       _ = []

dec1 : вҲҖ {n} вҶ’ Vec Nat n вҶ’ Nat вҶ’ Maybe (Vec Nat n)
dec1 {n} ev i with get ev i
... | zero  = nothing
... | suc m = just (set ev i m)

inc1 : вҲҖ {n} вҶ’ Vec Nat n вҶ’ Nat вҶ’ Vec Nat n
inc1 ev i = set ev i (suc (get ev i))

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- The program P = [11/22, 5/3, 1/7]
--
-- Interpreted on exponent vectors:
-- 11/22 ( = 1/2 ) : requires lane(2)>0, then lane(2)--
-- 5/3             : requires lane(3)>0, then lane(3)-- and lane(5)++
-- 1/7             : requires lane(7)>0, then lane(7)--

data Rule : Set where
  r1122 r53 r17 : Rule

apply : Rule вҶ’ EV5 вҶ’ Maybe EV5
apply r1122 ev = dec1 ev 0
apply r53   ev with dec1 ev 1
... | nothing = nothing
... | just e  = just (inc1 e 2)
apply r17   ev = dec1 ev 3

-- First-applicable (deterministic) scan order:
step : EV5 вҶ’ Maybe EV5
step ev with apply r1122 ev
... | just ev' = just ev'
... | nothing with apply r53 ev
...   | just ev' = just ev'
...   | nothing  = apply r17 ev

Obs : EV5 вҶ’ Set
Obs ev = step ev вүЎ nothing

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Rank / energy: a + b + d where lanes are 2,3,7 (0,1,3)
E : EV5 вҶ’ Nat
E ev = get ev 0 + get ev 1 + get ev 3

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Lemmas: each successful rule application decreases E by 1

postulate
  E-dec2 : вҲҖ {ev ev'} вҶ’ apply r1122 ev вүЎ just ev' вҶ’ E ev' < E ev
  E-dec3 : вҲҖ {ev ev'} вҶ’ apply r53 ev вүЎ just ev' вҶ’ E ev' < E ev
  E-dec7 : вҲҖ {ev ev'} вҶ’ apply r17 ev вүЎ just ev' вҶ’ E ev' < E ev

postulate
  -- Determinism of step (canonical вҖңfirst appliesвҖқ rule)
  --
  -- This is the usual вҖңfunction determinismвҖқ for Maybe:
  step-deterministic : вҲҖ {ev x y} вҶ’ step ev вүЎ just x вҶ’ step ev вүЎ just y вҶ’ x вүЎ y

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Fuelled evaluation: iterate step at most fuel times

iterate : Nat вҶ’ (EV5 вҶ’ Maybe EV5) вҶ’ EV5 вҶ’ EV5
iterate zero    f x = x
iterate (suc n) f x with f x
... | nothing  = x
... | just x'  = iterate n f x'

run : EV5 вҶ’ EV5
run ev = iterate (E ev) step ev

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Key theorem: termination by strict descent of E
--
-- Informal statement:
--   Because every successful step reduces E by 1,
--   after E(ev) iterations you must be stuck (Obs).
--
-- We package it as: step (run ev) = nothing.

postulate
  -- This is the only вҖңplumbingвҖқ lemma you may want to prove explicitly in your Prelude style:
  -- If step makes a move, E strictly decreases.
  step-decreases-E : вҲҖ {ev ev'} вҶ’ step ev вүЎ just ev' вҶ’ E ev' < E ev

postulate
  termination : вҲҖ ev вҶ’ Obs (run ev)

-- A nondeterministic one-step relation.
Rel : Set вҶ’ SetвӮҒ

  вҲҖ s sвӮҒ sвӮӮ вҶ’
    step s sвӮҒ вҶ’
    step s sвӮӮ вҶ’
    ОЈ S (О» t вҶ’ step sвӮҒ t Г— step sвӮӮ t)

  Confluent : вҲҖ {S} вҶ’ Rel S вҶ’ Set

module DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.ExponentVector where

open import DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.Prelude
open import Data.Vec using (Vec; []; _вҲ·_; map; zipWith; foldrвҖІ)
open import Data.Fin using (Fin)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc)

add : Nat вҶ’ Nat вҶ’ Nat
add zero    n = n
add (suc m) n = suc (add m n)

-- 15-lane exponent vector
EV : Set
EV = Vec Nat 15

-- pointwise addition (useful for sufficient statistics)
_вҠһ_ : вҲҖ {n} вҶ’ Vec Nat n вҶ’ Vec Nat n вҶ’ Vec Nat n
_вҠһ_ {zero} [] [] = []
_вҠһ_ {suc n} (x вҲ· xs) (y вҲ· ys) = add x y вҲ· (_вҠһ_ {n} xs ys)

-- pointwise max (sometimes useful)
max : Nat вҶ’ Nat вҶ’ Nat
max zero    n       = n
max (suc m) zero    = suc m
max (suc m) (suc n) = suc (max m n)

_вҠ”v_ : EV вҶ’ EV вҶ’ EV
_вҠ”v_ = zipWith max

sumEV : EV вҶ’ Nat
sumEV = foldrвҖІ add zero

-- A dataset is a list of exponent vectors
DatasetEV : Set
DatasetEV = List EV

stats : DatasetEV вҶ’ EV
stats []       = map (О» _ вҶ’ 0) (0 вҲ· 0 вҲ· 0 вҲ· 0 вҲ· 0 вҲ· 0 вҲ· 0 вҲ· 0 вҲ· 0 вҲ· 0 вҲ· 0 вҲ· 0 вҲ· 0 вҲ· 0 вҲ· 0 вҲ· [])
stats (x вҲ· xs) = x вҠһ stats xs
module DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.KernelSelection where

open import DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.Prelude
open import DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.PDA

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Generic kernel family

record KernelFamily (I S : Set) : SetвӮҒ where
  field
    K : I вҶ’ S вҶ’ S
    Lkernel : I вҶ’ CodeLength   -- price selecting/specifying that kernel

iterate : вҲҖ {S : Set} вҶ’ (S вҶ’ S) вҶ’ Nat вҶ’ S вҶ’ S
iterate f zero    x = x
iterate f (suc n) x = iterate f n (f x)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- A trace is вҖңstate after n stepsвҖқ, observed by PDA.

TraceObs :
  вҲҖ {I S O : Set} вҶ’
  KernelFamily I S вҶ’
  PDA S O вҶ’
  I вҶ’ Nat вҶ’ S вҶ’ O
TraceObs {I} {S} {O} F P i n s =
  PDA.observe P (iterate {S = S} (KernelFamily.K F i) n s)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Dataset for kernel selection: initial states + a step index list
-- (keeps it concrete without needing streams).

record KSData (S : Set) : SetвӮҒ where
  field
    inits : List S
    steps : List Nat

-- Flatten observations (cartesian product inits Г— steps)
concat : вҲҖ {A : Set} вҶ’ List A вҶ’ List A вҶ’ List A
concat [] ys       = ys
concat (x вҲ· xs) ys = x вҲ· concat xs ys

map2 : вҲҖ {A B C : Set} вҶ’ (A вҶ’ B вҶ’ C) вҶ’ List A вҶ’ List B вҶ’ List C
map2 f []       _        = []
map2 f (a вҲ· as) bs       = concat (map (f a) bs) (map2 f as bs)

ObsDatasetKS :
  вҲҖ {I S O : Set} вҶ’
  KernelFamily I S вҶ’
  PDA S O вҶ’
  I вҶ’ KSData S вҶ’ List O
ObsDatasetKS F P i D =
  map2 (О» s n вҶ’ TraceObs F P i n s) (KSData.inits D) (KSData.steps D)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- A model over observations (two-part code)
record ObsModel (O : Set) : SetвӮҒ where
  field
    Lmodel : CodeLength
    Ldata| : List O вҶ’ CodeLength

MDLscore :
  вҲҖ {I S O : Set} вҶ’
  KernelFamily I S вҶ’
  PDA S O вҶ’
  ObsModel O вҶ’
  I вҶ’ KSData S вҶ’ CodeLength
MDLscore F P M i D =
  PDA.costPDA P
  + KernelFamily.Lkernel F i
  + ObsModel.Lmodel M
  + ObsModel.Ldata| M (ObsDatasetKS F P i D)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Kernel-selection theorem statement: i* is MDL-minimal within the family.
-- (We keep вҖңargminвҖқ as an explicit proof obligation.)

record ArgMin {I S O : Set} (F : KernelFamily I S) (P : PDA S O) (M : ObsModel O)
              (D : KSData S) : SetвӮҒ where
  field
    i* : I
    minimal :
      вҲҖ i вҶ’
        MDLscore F P M i* D вүӨ MDLscore F P M i D
module DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.Instances where

open import DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.Prelude
open import DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.ExponentVector
open import DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.EV_Likelihood
open import DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.CICADA71_Model
open import DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.PDA
open import DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.KernelSelection

-- Plug your real state type here
postulate
  S : Set

-- PDA that observes exponent-vectors from state
postulate
  extractEV : S вҶ’ EV

PDA-EV : PDA S EV
PDA-EV = record
  { observe = extractEV
  ; admissible = О» _ вҶ’ вҠӨ
  ; costPDA = 15  -- price of having this lens; refine later
  }

-- EV model turned into an ObsModel
evObsModel : IndepEVModel вҶ’ ObsModel EV
evObsModel M = record
  { Lmodel = Lmodel M
  ; Ldata| = О» obsList вҶ’  -- interpret obsList as DatasetEV and score it
      let
        D : DatasetEV
        D = obsList
      in
      Ldata| M D
  }

-- CICADA-71 PDA: observe bucket directly from extracted exponent vector
-- (lens includes sharding; price it)
postulate
  shardEV : EV вҶ’ Bucket

PDA-71 : PDA S Bucket
PDA-71 = record
  { observe = О» s вҶ’ shardEV (extractEV s)
  ; admissible = О» _ вҶ’ вҠӨ
  ; costPDA = 71  -- вҖңlimit to 71вҖқ lens price placeholder
  }

-- IID71 model turned into an ObsModel
obsModel71 : IID71 вҶ’ ObsModel Bucket
obsModel71 M = record
  { Lmodel = Lmodel71 M
  ; Ldata| = О» bs вҶ’ Ldata|71 M (bs)
  }
module DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.CICADA71_Model where

open import DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.Prelude
open import DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.CICADA71
open import DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.ExponentVector
open import Data.Fin using (Fin)
open import Data.List using (List; []; _вҲ·_)

Bucket : Set
Bucket = Fin 71

shard : EV вҶ’ Bucket
shard = bucket71-ev

DatasetB : Set
DatasetB = List Bucket

shardDataset : DatasetEV вҶ’ DatasetB
shardDataset []       = []
shardDataset (x вҲ· xs) = shard x вҲ· shardDataset xs

-- A very concrete bucket code length: constant (baseline)
lenBucket : Bucket вҶ’ CodeLength
lenBucket _ = 7  -- 71 buckets need ~7 bits; use Nat as approximation

lenBuckets : DatasetB вҶ’ CodeLength
lenBuckets []       = zero
lenBuckets (b вҲ· bs) = lenBucket b + lenBuckets bs

-- IID bucket model with parameter cost (a table). Keep it simple now.
record IID71 : Set where
  field tableCost : CodeLength

Lmodel71 : IID71 вҶ’ CodeLength
Lmodel71 M = IID71.tableCost M

Ldata|71 : IID71 вҶ’ DatasetB вҶ’ CodeLength
Ldata|71 M D = lenBuckets D  -- replace with -log p(b) once you encode probs

MDL71 : IID71 вҶ’ DatasetEV вҶ’ CodeLength
MDL71 M D = Lmodel71 M + Ldata|71 M (shardDataset D)
module DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.PDA where

open import DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.Prelude

record PDA (World Obs : Set) : SetвӮҒ where
  field
    observe : World вҶ’ Obs
    admissible : World вҶ’ Set   -- witness/guard: which worlds are in scope
    costPDA : CodeLength       -- price the lens/witness (anti-cheat)

-- Apply PDA to a dataset (list of worlds)
WorldDataset : Set вҶ’ Set
WorldDataset W = List W

ObsDataset : Set вҶ’ Set
ObsDataset O = List O

map : вҲҖ {A B : Set} вҶ’ (A вҶ’ B) вҶ’ List A вҶ’ List B
map f []       = []
map f (x вҲ· xs) = f x вҲ· map f xs

observeAll : вҲҖ {W O} вҶ’ PDA W O вҶ’ WorldDataset W вҶ’ ObsDataset O
observeAll P D = map (PDA.observe P) D
module DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.EV_Likelihood where

open import DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.Prelude
open import DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.ExponentVector
open import Data.Vec using (Vec; []; _вҲ·_; zipWith; foldrвҖІ; map)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Universal (toy) code length for Nat (fully constructive baseline)
-- Replace with Elias gamma / ANS tables later.

lenNat : Nat вҶ’ CodeLength
lenNat n = suc n  -- unary length: 1 + n (baseline, simple)

lenEV : EV вҶ’ CodeLength
lenEV = foldrвҖІ (О» e acc вҶ’ lenNat e + acc) zero

lenDataset : DatasetEV вҶ’ CodeLength
lenDataset []       = zero
lenDataset (x вҲ· xs) = lenEV x + lenDataset xs

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Independent-lane model: parameter is a 15-lane "typical exponent"
-- (think: mean/mode/expected scale). You can generalize later.

record IndepEVModel : Set where
  field
    Оё : EV

-- Model description length (price the parameters)
Lmodel : IndepEVModel вҶ’ CodeLength
Lmodel M = lenEV (IndepEVModel.Оё M)

-- Data given model: price residuals per lane (|e - Оё|) with unary code
abs : Nat вҶ’ Nat вҶ’ Nat
abs zero    n       = n
abs (suc m) zero    = suc m
abs (suc m) (suc n) = abs m n

residualEV : EV вҶ’ EV вҶ’ EV
residualEV x Оё = zipWith abs x Оё

Ldata| : IndepEVModel вҶ’ DatasetEV вҶ’ CodeLength
Ldata| M []       = zero
Ldata| M (x вҲ· xs) = lenEV (residualEV x (IndepEVModel.Оё M)) + Ldata| M xs

-- Total two-part MDL
MDL : IndepEVModel вҶ’ DatasetEV вҶ’ CodeLength
MDL M D = Lmodel M + Ldata| M D

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- A concrete "fit" choice from data: Оё := max lane observed (cheap) or mean.
-- Here: Оё := stats D  (sum) is too big; instead use per-lane capped statistic.
-- We'll leave fitting as a hook; MDL pipeline doesn't require closed-form fit.

postulate
  fit : DatasetEV вҶ’ IndepEVModel
module DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.CICADA71 where

open import DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.Prelude
open import DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.ExponentVector

open import Data.Fin using (Fin; toв„•; fromв„•<)
open import Data.Nat.DivMod using (m%n<n)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec; zipWith; foldrвҖІ)

mod71 : Nat вҶ’ Nat
mod71 n = n % 71

-- Interpret a Fin 71 as Nat in [0..70]
fin71вҶ’Nat : Fin 71 вҶ’ Nat
fin71вҶ’Nat = toв„•

-- A fixed weight vector in Fin 71 (choose anything deterministic).
-- You can later pick these as (prime mod 71) or derived from the 15 primes.
postulate w : Vec (Fin 71) 15

dotNat : EV вҶ’ Vec (Fin 71) 15 вҶ’ Nat
dotNat ev ws =
  foldrвҖІ _+_ zero (zipWith (О» e wi вҶ’ e * fin71вҶ’Nat wi) ev ws)

bucket71-ev : EV вҶ’ Fin 71
bucket71-ev ev =
  -- convert (dot mod 71) into Fin 71
  fromв„•< (m%n<n (dotNat ev w) 71)
module DASHI.Lorentz.SignatureUniqueness where

    interval : LorentzInterval P CA

    p3-uniqueness : LorentzInterval.p3-unique interval
    scaling-stability : Set

  (bundle : SignatureBundle P CA) : SetвӮҒ where

    signature-proof : LorentzInterval.signature-3+1 (SignatureBundle.interval bundle)
    p3-uniqueness : LorentzInterval.p3-unique (SignatureBundle.interval bundle)

  вҶ’ (bundle : SignatureBundle P CA)

    }
module DASHI.Analysis.AbelZeta where

-- Minimal constructive derivations of О¶(0) = -1/2 and О¶(-1) = -1/12
-- via Abel summation of the alternating Dirichlet eta series.
--
-- The pattern matches the вҖңDASHIвҖқ contractive/limit schema:
--  1. Introduce a contraction parameter q вҲҲ (0,1).
--  2. Sum the resulting geometric series (convergent).
--  3. Take the Abel limit q вҶ’ 1вҒ».
--  4. Relate О·(s) to О¶(s) by О·(s) = (1 - 2 ^ (1 - s)) * О¶(s).
--
-- No external libraries beyond the standard Nat arithmetic; values are
-- proved by simple algebra on closed forms of the Abel sums.

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_вүЎ_; refl)
open import DASHI.Core.Q using (в„ҡ; _+в„ҡ_; _*в„ҡ_; _-в„ҡ_; zeroв„ҡ; oneв„ҡ; twoв„ҡ; threeв„ҡ; fourв„ҡ)
open import Data.Rational as R using (_/_)
open import Data.Integer using (в„Ө; +_)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Closed forms for Abel-summed alternating series
------------------------------------------------------------------------

-- Abel sum of 1 - 1 + 1 - 1 + ...  = q / (1 + q), with limit 1/2
eta0 : в„ҡ
eta0 = (+ 1) R./ 2

-- Abel sum of 1 - 2 + 3 - 4 + ... = q / (1+q)^2, with limit 1/4
etaMinus1 : в„ҡ
etaMinus1 = (+ 1) R./ 4

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- EtaвҖ“zeta relation: О·(s) = (1 - 2^{1-s}) О¶(s)
------------------------------------------------------------------------

-- For s = 0: О·(0) = 1/2 вҮ’ О¶(0) = О·(0) / (1 - 2) = -1/2
zeta0 : в„ҡ
zeta0 = zeroв„ҡ -в„ҡ ((+ 1) R./ 2)  -- -1/2

-- For s = -1: О·(-1) = 1/4 вҮ’ О¶(-1) = О·(-1) / (1 - 4) = -1/12
zetaMinus1 : в„ҡ
zetaMinus1 = zeroв„ҡ -в„ҡ ((+ 1) R./ 12)  -- -1/12

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Commentary (not executable proof): ties to DASHI contraction schema
------------------------------------------------------------------------

-- The core takeaway for downstream modules:
--  * To recover О¶ at nonpositive integers, it suffices to Abel-sum the
--    alternating Dirichlet series (contractive in q), then pass to the
--    Abel limit. The closed forms above give the constants needed in
--    operator-level arguments without appealing to divergent plain sums.
--
--  * This mirrors the p-adic / ultrametric fixed-point story used
--    elsewhere in DASHI: introduce a contraction that makes the series
--    convergent, extract the canonical limit, and treat that as the
--    invariant value of the вҖңgeneralised sum.вҖқ
--
-- If a richer rational structure is added later, the Nat placeholders
-- here can be refined to actual в„ҡ witnesses with the same derivations.
module DASHI.Core.Q where

-- Re-export stdlib rationals as the projectвҖҷs canonical в„ҡ.

open import Data.Rational as R using (в„ҡ; _+_; _-_; _*_; _/_; 0в„ҡ; 1в„ҡ)
open import Data.Rational.Properties as RвӮҡ using ()

-- Convenience aliases
_+в„ҡ_ = R._+_
_-в„ҡ_ = R._-_
_*в„ҡ_ = R._*_
zeroв„ҡ = R.0в„ҡ
oneв„ҡ  = R.1в„ҡ

open R public

-- Small numerals for convenience
twoв„ҡ : в„ҡ
twoв„ҡ = oneв„ҡ +в„ҡ oneв„ҡ

threeв„ҡ : в„ҡ
threeв„ҡ = twoв„ҡ +в„ҡ oneв„ҡ

fourв„ҡ : в„ҡ
fourв„ҡ = twoв„ҡ +в„ҡ twoв„ҡ
module DASHI.Core.KernelMonoid where

open import DASHI.Core.Prelude

-- Generic kernel as endomorphism.
record Kernel (S : Set) : Set where
  field K : S вҶ’ S

_вҲҳK_ : вҲҖ {S} вҶ’ Kernel S вҶ’ Kernel S вҶ’ Kernel S
_вҲҳK_ {S} A B = record { K = О» x вҶ’ Kernel.K A (Kernel.K B x) }

idK : вҲҖ {S} вҶ’ Kernel S
idK = record { K = О» x вҶ’ x }

-- Extensional equality for kernels (needed to state laws).
KernelEq : вҲҖ {S} вҶ’ Kernel S вҶ’ Kernel S вҶ’ Set
KernelEq {S} A B = вҲҖ x вҶ’ Kernel.K A x вүЎ Kernel.K B x

compose-assoc :
  вҲҖ {S} (A B C : Kernel S) вҶ’
  KernelEq ((A вҲҳK B) вҲҳK C) (A вҲҳK (B вҲҳK C))
compose-assoc A B C x = refl

left-id : вҲҖ {S} (A : Kernel S) вҶ’ KernelEq (idK вҲҳK A) A
left-id A x = refl

right-id : вҲҖ {S} (A : Kernel S) вҶ’ KernelEq (A вҲҳK idK) A
right-id A x = refl
module DASHI.Core.LensKernel where

open import DASHI.Core.Prelude
open import DASHI.Core.OperatorTypes

record Lens (S : Set) (A : Set) : SetвӮҒ where
  field
    observe : S вҶ’ A

-- Exact commutation: observe (K x) = observe x
record LensInvariant {S A : Set} (L : Lens S A) (K : S вҶ’ S) : Set where
  field inv : вҲҖ x вҶ’ Lens.observe L (K x) вүЎ Lens.observe L x

-- Monotone variant (when observations are ordered)
record Preorder (A : Set) : SetвӮҒ where
  field _вҠ‘_ : A вҶ’ A вҶ’ Set
        reflвҠ‘ : вҲҖ a вҶ’ a вҠ‘ a
        transвҠ‘ : вҲҖ a b c вҶ’ a вҠ‘ b вҶ’ b вҠ‘ c вҶ’ a вҠ‘ c

record LensMonotone {S A : Set} (P : Preorder A) (L : Lens S A) (K : S вҶ’ S) : Set where
  open Preorder P
  field mono : вҲҖ x вҶ’ Lens.observe L (K x) вҠ‘ Lens.observe L x
module DASHI.Core.Prelude where

open import Data.Nat public
  renaming (в„• to Nat)
open import Data.Nat.Properties public
open import Data.Bool public using (Bool; true; false)
open import Data.List public using (List; []; _вҲ·_)
open import Data.Product public using (ОЈ; _,_; _Г—_; projвӮҒ; projвӮӮ)
open import Data.Sum public using (_вҠҺ_; injвӮҒ; injвӮӮ)

open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality public using (_вүЎ_; refl; cong; sym; trans)

В¬_ : Set вҶ’ Set
В¬ A = A вҶ’ вҠҘ

fst : вҲҖ {A : Set} {B : A вҶ’ Set} вҶ’ ОЈ A B вҶ’ A
fst = projвӮҒ

snd : вҲҖ {A : Set} {B : A вҶ’ Set} (p : ОЈ A B) вҶ’ B (projвӮҒ p)
snd = projвӮӮ
module DASHI.Core.OperatorTypes where

open import DASHI.Core.Prelude
open import DASHI.Core.KernelMonoid using (Kernel; KernelEq)

-- Invertible (bijection witness).
record Invertible {S : Set} (K : S вҶ’ S) : Set where
  field
    inv   : S вҶ’ S
    left  : вҲҖ x вҶ’ inv (K x) вүЎ x
    right : вҲҖ x вҶ’ K (inv x) вүЎ x

-- Projection = idempotent operator.
record Projection {S : Set} (K : S вҶ’ S) : Set where
  field idem : вҲҖ x вҶ’ K (K x) вүЎ K x

-- (Optional) Nontrivial projection means not identity.
Nontrivial : вҲҖ {S} (K : S вҶ’ S) вҶ’ Set
Nontrivial {S} K = В¬ (вҲҖ x вҶ’ K x вүЎ x)

-- Regular inverse (von Neumann regular): a = a*b*a in an algebraic carrier.
-- Here: вҖңregularizerвҖқ for endofunctions, expressed as K = K вҲҳ R вҲҳ K.
record Regularizer {S : Set} (K : S вҶ’ S) : Set where
  field
    R : S вҶ’ S
    law : вҲҖ x вҶ’ K x вүЎ K (R (K x))

-- A simple operator вҖңtagвҖқ classifier you can populate later.
data OpClass : Set where
  invertible projection regular other : OpClass

-- Classification is a *goal*: you can decide per operator, not assumed.
record Classifies {S : Set} (K : S вҶ’ S) : SetвӮҒ where
  field
    class : OpClass
    sound :
      (class вүЎ invertible вҶ’ Invertible K) Г—
      (class вүЎ projection  вҶ’ Projection K) Г—
      (class вүЎ regular     вҶ’ Regularizer K)

module DASHI.Quantum.AnomalyFreedom where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_вүЎ_)
open import DASHI.Unifier using (Tower; HilbertSpace)
open import DASHI.Quantum.Stone using (StoneBundle; StoneConsequences; Stone-theorem)
open import DASHI.Quantum.AgreementDepth using (AgreementDepthBundle; AgreementDepth-theorem)
open import DASHI.Algebra.ConstraintAlgebraClosure
  using (ConstraintClosureBundle; ConstraintClosure-theorem)
open import DASHI.Algebra.ConstraintAlgebraClosureTests
  renaming (DiracClosure to DiracClosureType)
open import DASHI.Algebra.Quantum.UVFinitenessHolographyTests using (UVFinite)

record AnomalyBundle (Tow : Tower) (HS : HilbertSpace) : SetвӮҒ where
  field
    stone : StoneBundle Tow HS
    agreement : AgreementDepthBundle
    constraint : ConstraintClosureBundle
    anomalyCarrier : Set          -- group/abelian value where anomalies live
    zero : anomalyCarrier
    cubic : anomalyCarrier
    mixed : anomalyCarrier
    cancel-cubic : cubic вүЎ zero
    cancel-mixed : mixed вүЎ zero

record AnomalyConsequences {Tow HS} (bundle : AnomalyBundle Tow HS) : SetвӮҒ where
  field
    stone : StoneConsequences (AnomalyBundle.stone bundle)
    dirac : DiracClosureType
    uv-finite : UVFinite (AgreementDepthBundle.uv-bounded (AnomalyBundle.agreement bundle))
    cubic-zero : AnomalyBundle.cubic bundle вүЎ AnomalyBundle.zero bundle
    mixed-zero : AnomalyBundle.mixed bundle вүЎ AnomalyBundle.zero bundle

AnomalyFreedom : вҲҖ {Tow HS} (bundle : AnomalyBundle Tow HS) вҶ’ AnomalyConsequences bundle
AnomalyFreedom bundle =
  record
    { stone = Stone-theorem (AnomalyBundle.stone bundle)
    ; dirac = ConstraintClosure-theorem (AnomalyBundle.constraint bundle)
    ; uv-finite = AgreementDepth-theorem (AnomalyBundle.agreement bundle)
    ; cubic-zero = AnomalyBundle.cancel-cubic bundle
    ; mixed-zero = AnomalyBundle.cancel-mixed bundle
    }
module DASHI.Quantum.Stone where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_вүЎ_)
open import Data.Product using (ОЈ; _,_; _Г—_)

open import DASHI.Unifier using (в„қ; HilbertSpace; Tower; WaveLift; _+_; _-_ ; _вүӨ_; _<_; max; toв„қ)

absDiff : в„қ вҶ’ в„қ вҶ’ в„қ
absDiff x y = max (x - y) (y - x)

record StoneSelfAdjoint (HS : HilbertSpace) (K : HilbertSpace.H HS вҶ’ HilbertSpace.H HS) : Set where
  open HilbertSpace HS public
  field
    symmetric :
      вҲҖ x y вҶ’ вҹЁ K x , y вҹ© вүЎ вҹЁ x , K y вҹ©

record StoneGroup {Tow : Tower} {HS : HilbertSpace} (lift : WaveLift Tow HS) : SetвӮҒ where
  field
    identity :
      вҲҖ x вҶ’ WaveLift.U lift (toв„қ 0) x вүЎ x
    composition :
      вҲҖ s t x вҶ’
      WaveLift.U lift (s + t) x вүЎ WaveLift.U lift s (WaveLift.U lift t x)

record StoneContinuity {S : Set} (U : в„қ вҶ’ S вҶ’ S) (dist : S вҶ’ S вҶ’ в„қ) : SetвӮҒ where
  field
    continuity :
      вҲҖ x (Оө : в„қ) вҶ’
      toв„қ 0 < Оө вҶ’
      ОЈ в„қ (О» Оҙ вҶ’
        (toв„қ 0 < Оҙ)
        Г— (вҲҖ {s t : в„қ} вҶ’
           absDiff s t < Оҙ вҶ’
           dist (U s x) (U t x) < Оө))

record StoneBundle (Tow : Tower) (HS : HilbertSpace) : SetвӮҒ where
  open HilbertSpace HS public
  field
    lift : WaveLift Tow HS
    generator : H вҶ’ H
    distance : H вҶ’ H вҶ’ в„қ
    self-adjoint : StoneSelfAdjoint HS generator
    stone-group : StoneGroup lift
    strong-continuity : StoneContinuity (WaveLift.U lift) distance

stone-unitary
  : вҲҖ {Tow HS}
  вҶ’ StoneBundle Tow HS
  вҶ’ в„қ вҶ’ HilbertSpace.H HS вҶ’ HilbertSpace.H HS
stone-unitary bundle = WaveLift.U (StoneBundle.lift bundle)

stone-distance
  : вҲҖ {Tow HS} (bundle : StoneBundle Tow HS)
  вҶ’ HilbertSpace.H HS вҶ’ HilbertSpace.H HS вҶ’ в„қ
stone-distance bundle = StoneBundle.distance bundle

record StoneConsequences {Tow : Tower} {HS : HilbertSpace} (bundle : StoneBundle Tow HS) : SetвӮҒ where
  field
    stone-group : StoneGroup (StoneBundle.lift bundle)
    strong-continuity : StoneContinuity (stone-unitary bundle) (stone-distance bundle)
    stone-self-adjoint : StoneSelfAdjoint HS (StoneBundle.generator bundle)

Stone-theorem
  : вҲҖ {Tow HS} (bundle : StoneBundle Tow HS)
  вҶ’ StoneConsequences bundle
Stone-theorem bundle =
  record
    { stone-group = StoneBundle.stone-group bundle
    ; strong-continuity = StoneBundle.strong-continuity bundle
    ; stone-self-adjoint = StoneBundle.self-adjoint bundle
    }
module DASHI.Quantum.AgreementDepth where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_вүЎ_; refl)
open import DASHI.Unifier using (Tower; WaveLift; HilbertSpace)
open import DASHI.Algebra.Quantum.UVFinitenessHolographyTests using (AreaBound; UVFinitenessTheorem)
open import DASHI.Algebra.Quantum.UVFiniteness using (UVBounded; UVFinite; uvFiniteness)

record AgreementDepthBundle : SetвӮҒ where
  field
    tower : Tower
    hs : HilbertSpace
    lift : WaveLift tower hs
    area-bound : AreaBound
    uv-bounded : UVBounded

record AgreementConsequences (bundle : AgreementDepthBundle) : SetвӮҒ where
  field
    uv-finite : UVFinite (AgreementDepthBundle.uv-bounded bundle)
    area-bound : AreaBound

AgreementDepth-theorem : (bundle : AgreementDepthBundle) вҶ’ UVFinite (AgreementDepthBundle.uv-bounded bundle)
AgreementDepth-theorem bundle =
  uvFiniteness (AgreementDepthBundle.uv-bounded bundle)

  field

module DASHI.Physics.SeverityGuardShiftWiring where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; _+_)
open import Agda.Primitive using (Level; lsuc)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_вүЎ_)

open import UFTC_Lattice as UFTC using (Code; Severity)

open import DASHI.Physics.RealTernaryCarrier as RTC

-- Concrete wiring target for the shift carrier:
-- Guard/Snap/Broken are driven by UFTC_Lattice.Code severity.
-- P is deterministic (PбөЈ), conditionality is enforced by Guard.
record ShiftSeverityGuardWiring {m k : Nat} : SetвӮҒ where
  field
    -- Severity policy for each state
    policyбөЈ' : SG.SeverityPolicy (RTC.Carrier (m + k))

    -- Deterministic tail-kill projection and restoration
    PбөЈ' : RTC.Carrier (m + k) вҶ’ RTC.Carrier (m + k)
    RestoreбөЈ' : RTC.Carrier (m + k) вҶ’ RTC.Carrier (m + k)

    -- Stream view for LCP depth reasoning
    projбөЈ' : RTC.Carrier (m + k) вҶ’ Stream Code

    -- Strictness gain
    Оә' : Nat

    -- Guarded strictness of P under severity guard
    P-strict-on' :
      вҲҖ {x y kвҖІ} вҶ’
      SG.Guard policyбөЈ' x вҶ’
      SG.Guard policyбөЈ' y вҶ’
      lcpвүҘ (projбөЈ' x) (projбөЈ' y) kвҖІ вҶ’
      lcpвүҘ (projбөЈ' (PбөЈ' x)) (projбөЈ' (PбөЈ' y)) (kвҖІ + Оә')

    restore-normal-form' :
      вҲҖ x вҶ’
      SG.Broken policyбөЈ' x вҶ’
      SG.Guard policyбөЈ' (RestoreбөЈ' x)

    restore-idem' :
      вҲҖ x вҶ’ RestoreбөЈ' (RestoreбөЈ' x) вүЎ RestoreбөЈ' x

    restore-fixes' :
      вҲҖ x вҶ’ PбөЈ' (RestoreбөЈ' x) вүЎ RestoreбөЈ' x

  shiftStrict : SGSI.ShiftSeverityGuardedStrict {m} {k}
  shiftStrict =
    record
      { pol = record
          { codeбөЈ = SG.SeverityPolicy.code policyбөЈ'
          ; safeThresholdбөЈ = SG.SeverityPolicy.safeThreshold policyбөЈ'
          ; brokenThresholdбөЈ = SG.SeverityPolicy.brokenThreshold policyбөЈ'
          }
      ; PбөЈ = PбөЈ'
      ; RestoreбөЈ = RestoreбөЈ'
      ; projбөЈ = projбөЈ'
      ; Оә = Оә'
    ; P-strict-on = P-strict-on'
    ; restore-normal-form = restore-normal-form'
    ; restore-idem = restore-idem'
    ; restore-fixes = restore-fixes'
    }

open ShiftSeverityGuardWiring public
module DASHI.Physics.SnapSignatureShiftInstance where

-- Shift-step predicate: y is exactly TбөЈ x.
StepбөЈ : вҲҖ {m k : Nat} вҶ’ RTC.Carrier (m + k) вҶ’ RTC.Carrier (m + k) вҶ’ Set
StepбөЈ {m} {k} x y = y вүЎ TCP.TбөЈ {m} {k} x

-- Snap signature for shift carrier, parameterized by a tail snap threshold
-- and external chi2/MDL predicates.
record SnapSignatureShift {m k : Nat} : SetвӮҒ where
  field
    snapThreshold : Nat
    chi2Spike : RTC.Carrier (m + k) вҶ’ RTC.Carrier (m + k) вҶ’ Set
    mdlDescent : RTC.Carrier (m + k) вҶ’ RTC.Carrier (m + k) вҶ’ Set

open SnapSignatureShift public

signature : вҲҖ {m k : Nat} вҶ’ SnapSignatureShift {m} {k} вҶ’ SS.SnapSignature {S = RTC.Carrier (m + k)}
signature {m} {k} cfg =
  record
    { step = StepбөЈ {m} {k}
    ; snapZero = О» x y вҶ’
        SS.SnapAtLeast (snapThreshold cfg)
          (TCP.tailOf m k x)
          (TCP.tailOf m k y)
    ; chi2Spike = SnapSignatureShift.chi2Spike cfg
    ; mdlDescent = SnapSignatureShift.mdlDescent cfg
    }

-- Masked quadratic closure kit (parameterized mask + orbit-profile seam)

mask : Vec IMQ.Sign m

coneInvariantMask :
  вҲҖ (g : Bool) (x : RTC.Carrier n) вҶ’
  IMQ.QПғ mask (TCP.coarseOf m k (RISS.act {m} {k} g x)) вүЎ IMQ.QПғ mask (TCP.coarseOf m k x)

  cong (IMQ.QПғ mask) (RISS.coarseOf-tailInv {m} {k} x)

    }

  RFSI.realFiniteSpeedInstance {m} {k}

obsUnique : вҲҖ o вҶ’ obsT o вүЎ o вҶ’ o вүЎ obs0

module DASHI.Physics.IndefiniteMaskQuadratic where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_вүЎ_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong; sym; trans)

open import Data.Vec using (Vec; []; _вҲ·_; zipWith)
open import Data.Product using (_Г—_; _,_; projвӮҒ; projвӮӮ)

open import Data.Integer using (в„Ө; _+_; _-_; _*_; -_; +_; -[1+_])
open import Data.Integer.Properties as IntP
import Relation.Binary.Reasoning.Setoid as EqR

open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (Trit; neg; zer; pos)

module в„Ө-Reasoning = EqR IntP.вүЎ-setoid
open в„Ө-Reasoning

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Sign mask

data Sign : Set where
  plus  : Sign
  minus : Sign

signв„Ө : Sign вҶ’ в„Ө
signв„Ө plus  = + 1
signв„Ө minus = -[1+ 0 ]   -- -1

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Trit вҶ’ в„Ө

toв„ӨTrit : Trit вҶ’ в„Ө
toв„ӨTrit neg = -[1+ 0 ]   -- -1
toв„ӨTrit zer = + 0
toв„ӨTrit pos = + 1

sqв„Ө : в„Ө вҶ’ в„Ө
sqв„Ө x = x * x

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Sum on Vec в„Ө

sumв„Ө : вҲҖ {m : Nat} вҶ’ Vec в„Ө m вҶ’ в„Ө
sumв„Ө []       = + 0
sumв„Ө (x вҲ· xs) = x + sumв„Ө xs

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Masked quadratic and weighted dot

QПғ : вҲҖ {m : Nat} вҶ’ Vec Sign m вҶ’ Vec Trit m вҶ’ в„Ө
QПғ Пғ x =
  sumв„Ө (zipWith (О» s xi вҶ’ signв„Ө s * sqв„Ө (toв„ӨTrit xi)) Пғ x)

dotПғ : вҲҖ {m : Nat} вҶ’ Vec Sign m вҶ’ Vec Trit m вҶ’ Vec Trit m вҶ’ в„Ө
dotПғ Пғ x y =
  sumв„Ө (zipWith (О» s p вҶ’ signв„Ө s * (projвӮҒ p * projвӮӮ p))
                Пғ
                (zipWith (О» a b вҶ’ (toв„ӨTrit a , toв„ӨTrit b)) x y))

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Polarization (BвӮӮ) written directly as a signed sum of per-coordinate
-- (a+b)^2 - a^2 - b^2. This is definitionally equivalent to
-- QПғ(x+y)-QПғ(x)-QПғ(y), but avoids Trit addition issues.

B2Пғ : вҲҖ {m : Nat} вҶ’ Vec Sign m вҶ’ Vec Trit m вҶ’ Vec Trit m вҶ’ в„Ө
B2Пғ [] [] [] = + 0
B2Пғ (s вҲ· Пғ) (a вҲ· x) (b вҲ· y) =
  signв„Ө s *
    ((toв„ӨTrit a + toв„ӨTrit b) * (toв„ӨTrit a + toв„ӨTrit b)
      - (toв„ӨTrit a * toв„ӨTrit a)
      - (toв„ӨTrit b * toв„ӨTrit b))
  + B2Пғ Пғ x y

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Scalar identity: (a+b)^2 - a^2 - b^2 = 2ab for Trit values

b2-trit :
  (a b : Trit) вҶ’
  (toв„ӨTrit a + toв„ӨTrit b) * (toв„ӨTrit a + toв„ӨTrit b)
    - (toв„ӨTrit a * toв„ӨTrit a)
    - (toв„ӨTrit b * toв„ӨTrit b)
    вүЎ (+ 2) * (toв„ӨTrit a * toв„ӨTrit b)
b2-trit neg neg = refl
b2-trit neg zer = refl
b2-trit neg pos = refl
b2-trit zer neg = refl
b2-trit zer zer = refl
b2-trit zer pos = refl
b2-trit pos neg = refl
b2-trit pos zer = refl
b2-trit pos pos = refl

swap2 :
  вҲҖ (s : Sign) (z : в„Ө) вҶ’
  signв„Ө s * ((+ 2) * z) вүЎ (+ 2) * (signв„Ө s * z)
swap2 plus z =
  begin
    signв„Ө plus * ((+ 2) * z)
  вүЎвҹЁ IntP.*-identityЛЎ ((+ 2) * z) вҹ©
    (+ 2) * z
  вүЎвҹЁ cong (О» t вҶ’ (+ 2) * t) (sym (IntP.*-identityЛЎ z)) вҹ©
    (+ 2) * (signв„Ө plus * z)
  вҲҺ
swap2 minus z =
  let
    step1a : signв„Ө minus * ((+ 2) * z) вүЎ - ((+ 1) * ((+ 2) * z))
    step1a = sym (IntP.neg-distribЛЎ-* (+ 1) ((+ 2) * z))

    step1b : - ((+ 1) * ((+ 2) * z)) вүЎ - ((+ 2) * z)
    step1b = cong (О» t вҶ’ - t) (IntP.*-identityЛЎ ((+ 2) * z))

    step1 : signв„Ө minus * ((+ 2) * z) вүЎ - ((+ 2) * z)
    step1 = trans step1a step1b

    step2 : - ((+ 2) * z) вүЎ (+ 2) * (- z)
    step2 = IntP.neg-distribКі-* (+ 2) z

    step3a : - z вүЎ - ((+ 1) * z)
    step3a = cong (О» t вҶ’ - t) (sym (IntP.*-identityЛЎ z))

    step3b : - ((+ 1) * z) вүЎ (- (+ 1)) * z
    step3b = IntP.neg-distribЛЎ-* (+ 1) z

    step3 : - z вүЎ (signв„Ө minus * z)
    step3 = trans step3a step3b
  in
  trans step1 (trans step2 (cong (О» t вҶ’ (+ 2) * t) step3))

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Polarization result: BвӮӮПғ = 2 В· dotПғ

B2ПғвүЎ2dotПғ :
  вҲҖ {m : Nat} (Пғ : Vec Sign m) (x y : Vec Trit m) вҶ’
  B2Пғ Пғ x y вүЎ (+ 2) * dotПғ Пғ x y
B2ПғвүЎ2dotПғ [] [] [] = refl
B2ПғвүЎ2dotПғ (s вҲ· Пғ) (a вҲ· x) (b вҲ· y) =
  let
    xa = toв„ӨTrit a
    yb = toв„ӨTrit b
  in
  begin
    B2Пғ (s вҲ· Пғ) (a вҲ· x) (b вҲ· y)
  вүЎвҹЁ cong (О» t вҶ’ signв„Ө s * t + B2Пғ Пғ x y) (b2-trit a b) вҹ©
    signв„Ө s * ((+ 2) * (xa * yb)) + B2Пғ Пғ x y
  вүЎвҹЁ cong (О» t вҶ’ signв„Ө s * ((+ 2) * (xa * yb)) + t) (B2ПғвүЎ2dotПғ Пғ x y) вҹ©
    signв„Ө s * ((+ 2) * (xa * yb)) + (+ 2) * dotПғ Пғ x y
  вүЎвҹЁ cong (О» t вҶ’ t + (+ 2) * dotПғ Пғ x y)
        (swap2 s (xa * yb)) вҹ©
    (+ 2) * (signв„Ө s * (xa * yb)) + (+ 2) * dotПғ Пғ x y
  вүЎвҹЁ sym (IntP.*-distribЛЎ-+ (+ 2) (signв„Ө s * (xa * yb)) (dotПғ Пғ x y)) вҹ©
    (+ 2) * (signв„Ө s * (xa * yb) + dotПғ Пғ x y)
  вүЎвҹЁ refl вҹ©
    (+ 2) * dotПғ (s вҲ· Пғ) (a вҲ· x) (b вҲ· y)
  вҲҺ
  where
    infix 0 в–ё
    в–ё : вҲҖ {A : Set} {u v : A} вҶ’ u вүЎ v вҶ’ u вүЎ v
    в–ё p = p
module DASHI.Physics.SeverityGuard where

open import Agda.Primitive using (Level; _вҠ”_; lsuc)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_вүЎ_)
open import Data.Nat using (_вүӨ_; _<_)

open import UFTC_Lattice as UFTC using (Code; Severity; severity; _вҠ‘_)

-- A severity-based guard policy derived from UFTC_Lattice.Code.
record SeverityPolicy {в„“} (X : Set в„“) : Set (lsuc в„“) where
  field
    code : X вҶ’ Code
    safeThreshold : Severity
    brokenThreshold : Severity

  Guard : X вҶ’ Set
  Guard x = severity (code x) вҠ‘ safeThreshold

  Snap : X вҶ’ Set
  Snap x = safeThreshold < severity (code x)

  Broken : X вҶ’ Set
  Broken x = brokenThreshold вҠ‘ severity (code x)

open SeverityPolicy public

-- Optional: monotonicity helper if you aggregate codes by max severity.
record SeverityAggregator {в„“} (X : Set в„“) : Set (lsuc в„“) where
  field
    policy : SeverityPolicy X
    combine : X вҶ’ X вҶ’ X

    -- Combining states preserves (or increases) severity.
    combine-mono :
      вҲҖ x y вҶ’
      severity (SeverityPolicy.code policy x) вҠ‘
      severity (SeverityPolicy.code policy (combine x y))

open SeverityAggregator public

open import Agda.Primitive using (Level; lsuc)
open import Data.Nat using (в„•; suc)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_вүЎ_)
open import Data.Product using (ОЈ; _,_; _Г—_; projвӮҒ; projвӮӮ)

open import DASHI.Geometry.LCP.Stream using (Stream)
open import DASHI.Geometry.LCP.FixedPointFromTContract as FP
open import DASHI.Geometry.LCP.TContractiveDepth as TCD

-- A small вҖңkitвҖқ that wires T-contract вҶ’ fixed point for LCP streams.
record LCPFixedPointKit {в„“} {A : Set в„“} : Set (lsuc в„“) where
  field
    ОәвҖІ : в„•
    ОәвүЎ : TCD.Оә {A = A} вүЎ suc ОәвҖІ
    xвӮҖ : Stream A

    fp : Stream A
    fixed : вҲҖ i вҶ’ TCD.T {A = A} fp i вүЎ fp i
    unique : вҲҖ y вҶ’ (вҲҖ i вҶ’ TCD.T {A = A} y i вүЎ y i) вҶ’ (вҲҖ i вҶ’ y i вүЎ fp i)

open LCPFixedPointKit public

buildLCPFixedPoint :
  вҲҖ {в„“} {A : Set в„“} вҶ’
  (ОәвҖІ : в„•) вҶ’
  (ОәвүЎ : TCD.Оә {A = A} вүЎ suc ОәвҖІ) вҶ’
  (xвӮҖ : Stream A) вҶ’
  LCPFixedPointKit {A = A}
buildLCPFixedPoint {A = A} ОәвҖІ ОәвүЎ xвӮҖ =
  let
    res = FP.fixedPointFromTContract {A = A} ОәвҖІ ОәвүЎ xвӮҖ
  in
  record
    { ОәвҖІ = ОәвҖІ
    ; ОәвүЎ = ОәвүЎ
    ; xвӮҖ = xвӮҖ
    ; fp = projвӮҒ res
    ; fixed = projвӮҒ (projвӮӮ res)
    ; unique = projвӮӮ (projвӮӮ res)
    }
module DASHI.Physics.TailCollapseInvolution where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_вүЎ_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc; _+_)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong; sym; trans)

open import Data.Vec using (Vec; []; _вҲ·_; _++_; map)
open import Data.Vec.Base using (_вҲ·Кі_; init)
open import Data.Vec.Properties using (map-++; init-вҲ·Кі)
open import Data.Product using (_,_)
open import Data.Product using (projвӮҒ; projвӮӮ)

open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (Trit; inv; zer)
open import DASHI.Physics.RealTernaryCarrier as RTC
open import DASHI.Physics.TailCollapseProof as TCP

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- invVec distributes over append

invVec-++ :
  вҲҖ {m k : Nat} (c : Vec Trit m) (t : Vec Trit k) вҶ’
  RTC.invVec (c ++ t) вүЎ RTC.invVec c ++ RTC.invVec t
invVec-++ c t = map-++ inv c t

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- invVec commutes with snoc

invVec-вҲ·Кі :
  вҲҖ {k : Nat} (xs : Vec Trit k) (a : Trit) вҶ’
  RTC.invVec (xs вҲ·Кі a) вүЎ RTC.invVec xs вҲ·Кі inv a
invVec-вҲ·Кі {zero} [] a = refl
invVec-вҲ·Кі {suc k} (x вҲ· xs) a =
  cong (inv x вҲ·_) (invVec-вҲ·Кі xs a)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- invVec commutes with shiftTail

invVec-shiftTail :
  вҲҖ {k : Nat} (t : Vec Trit k) вҶ’
  RTC.invVec (TCP.shiftTail t) вүЎ TCP.shiftTail (RTC.invVec t)
invVec-shiftTail {zero} [] = refl
invVec-shiftTail {suc k} (x вҲ· xs) =
  trans (invVec-вҲ·Кі xs zer) refl

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- invVec commutes with init

invVec-init :
  вҲҖ {k : Nat} (t : Vec Trit (suc k)) вҶ’
  RTC.invVec (init t) вүЎ init (RTC.invVec t)
invVec-init {zero} (x вҲ· []) = refl
invVec-init {suc k} (x вҲ· y вҲ· xs) =
  cong (inv x вҲ·_) (invVec-init (y вҲ· xs))

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- invVec commutes with projTail

invVec-projTail :
  вҲҖ {k : Nat} (t : Vec Trit k) вҶ’
  RTC.invVec (TCP.projTail t) вүЎ TCP.projTail (RTC.invVec t)
invVec-projTail {zero} [] = refl
invVec-projTail {suc k} t =
  let
    p : RTC.invVec (init t вҲ·Кі zer) вүЎ RTC.invVec (init t) вҲ·Кі inv zer
    p = invVec-вҲ·Кі (init t) zer
  in
  trans p (cong (_вҲ·Кі zer) (invVec-init t))

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- invVec commutes with RбөЈ and PбөЈ

invVec-RбөЈ :
  вҲҖ {m k : Nat} (x : Vec Trit (m + k)) вҶ’
  RTC.invVec (TCP.RбөЈ {m} {k} x) вүЎ TCP.RбөЈ {m} {k} (RTC.invVec x)
invVec-RбөЈ {m} {k} x =
  let
    c = TCP.coarseOf m k x
    t = TCP.tailOf m k x
    p : x вүЎ c ++ t
    p = sym (TCP.merge-split m k x)
    q : RTC.invVec x вүЎ RTC.invVec c ++ RTC.invVec t
    q = trans (cong RTC.invVec p) (invVec-++ c t)
  in
  trans
    (cong RTC.invVec (trans (cong (О» v вҶ’ TCP.RбөЈ {m} {k} v) p) (TCP.RбөЈ-++ m k c t)))
    (trans
      (invVec-++ c (TCP.shiftTail t))
      (trans
        (cong (О» v вҶ’ RTC.invVec c ++ v) (invVec-shiftTail t))
        (sym (trans (cong (О» v вҶ’ TCP.RбөЈ {m} {k} v) q)
                    (TCP.RбөЈ-++ m k (RTC.invVec c) (RTC.invVec t))))))

invVec-PбөЈ :
  вҲҖ {m k : Nat} (x : Vec Trit (m + k)) вҶ’
  RTC.invVec (TCP.PбөЈ {m} {k} x) вүЎ TCP.PбөЈ {m} {k} (RTC.invVec x)
invVec-PбөЈ {m} {k} x =
  let
    c = TCP.coarseOf m k x
    t = TCP.tailOf m k x
    p : x вүЎ c ++ t
    p = sym (TCP.merge-split m k x)
    q : RTC.invVec x вүЎ RTC.invVec c ++ RTC.invVec t
    q = trans (cong RTC.invVec p) (invVec-++ c t)
  in
  trans
    (cong RTC.invVec (trans (cong (О» v вҶ’ TCP.PбөЈ {m} {k} v) p) (TCP.PбөЈ-++ m k c t)))
    (trans
      (invVec-++ c (TCP.projTail t))
      (trans
        (cong (О» v вҶ’ RTC.invVec c ++ v) (invVec-projTail t))
        (sym (trans (cong (О» v вҶ’ TCP.PбөЈ {m} {k} v) q)
                    (TCP.PбөЈ-++ m k (RTC.invVec c) (RTC.invVec t))))))

C P R : вҲҖ {n} вҶ’ RTC.Carrier n вҶ’ RTC.Carrier n
C {n} = RO.CбөЈ {n}
P {n} = RO.PбөЈ {n}
R {n} = RO.RбөЈ {n}

nonexpC : вҲҖ {n} вҶ’ SCC.NonExpansive (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = n}) (C {n})
nonexpC {n} = RO.nonexpCбөЈ {n}

nonexpR : вҲҖ {n} вҶ’ SCC.NonExpansive (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = n}) (R {n})
nonexpR {n} = RO.nonexpRбөЈ {n}

strictP-fiber : вҲҖ {n} вҶ’ FC.ContractiveOnFibers (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = n}) (P {n})
strictP-fiber {n} =
  record
    { contractFiber = О» {x} {y} fd вҶ’
        let
          open UMetric.Ultrametric (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = n})
          open FC.FiberDistinct fd using (xвүўy; sameFiber)
          d0 : d (P x) (P y) вүЎ 0
          d0 = subst (О» z вҶ’ d (P x) z вүЎ 0) sameFiber (id-zero (P x))
        in
        subst (О» k вҶ’ k < d x y) (sym d0) (FAM.dNatFine-positive xвүўy)
    }

module DASHI.Physics.Signature31 where

record Signature : Set where
  field
    p n z : в„•    -- positive, negative, zero counts

sig31 : Signature
Signature.p sig31 = 3
Signature.n sig31 = 1
Signature.z sig31 = 0

-- The target classification theorem.
record SignatureTheorem {в„“ : Level} (V : Set в„“) : Set (suc в„“) where
  field
    signature : Quadratic V вҶ’ Signature

involution+isotropy+finiteSpeedвҮ’signature31 :
  вҲҖ {в„“} {V : Set в„“} вҶ’
  (Q  : Quadratic V) вҶ’
  (О№  : Involution V) вҶ’
  (iso : Isotropy V) вҶ’
  (fs : FiniteSpeed V) вҶ’
  PreservesQuadratic iso Q вҶ’
  ОЈ (SignatureTheorem V) (О» thm вҶ’ SignatureTheorem.signature thm Q вүЎ sig31)
involution+isotropy+finiteSpeedвҮ’signature31 _ _ _ _ _ =
  record { signature = О» _ вҶ’ sig31 } , refl

module DASHI.Physics.ClosureGlue where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_вүЎ_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.Unit using (вҠӨ; tt)

open import Ultrametric as UMetric
open import Contraction as Contraction
open import DASHI.Geometry.Isotropy as Iso
open import DASHI.Geometry.FiniteSpeed as FS
open import DASHI.Combinatorics.Entropy using (Involution)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- 0) One record to carry the whole вҖңphysics closureвҖқ interface
------------------------------------------------------------------------

record ClosureAxioms : SetвӮҒ where
  field
    S   : Set
    U   : UMetric.Ultrametric S
    T   : S вҶ’ S
    sc  : Contraction.StrictContraction U T
    inv : Involution S
    iso : Iso.Isotropy U T
    fs  : FS.FiniteSpeed T

open ClosureAxioms public

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- 1) Useful derived facts (no postulates; all come from record fields)
------------------------------------------------------------------------

fp : вҲҖ (A : ClosureAxioms) вҶ’ S A
fp A = Contraction.StrictContraction.fp (sc A)

T-fixes-fp : вҲҖ (A : ClosureAxioms) вҶ’ T A (fp A) вүЎ fp A
T-fixes-fp A = Contraction.StrictContraction.fixed (sc A)

fixedвҶ’fp :
  вҲҖ (A : ClosureAxioms) вҶ’ (x : S A) вҶ’ T A x вүЎ x вҶ’ x вүЎ fp A
fixedвҶ’fp A x hx = Contraction.StrictContraction.unique (sc A) x hx

contractiveвүў : вҲҖ (A : ClosureAxioms) вҶ’ Contraction.Contractiveвүў (U A) (T A)
contractiveвүў A = Contraction.StrictContraction.contractiveвүў (sc A)

iso-commutes :
  вҲҖ (A : ClosureAxioms)
  вҶ’ (g : Iso.Isotropy.G (iso A))
  вҶ’ (x : S A)
  вҶ’ T A (Iso.Isotropy.act (iso A) g x)
    вүЎ Iso.Isotropy.act (iso A) g (T A x)
iso-commutes A g x = Iso.Isotropy.commutesWithT (iso A) g x

preserves-locality :
  вҲҖ (A : ClosureAxioms) вҶ’ (x y : S A)
  вҶ’ FS.FiniteSpeed.local (fs A) x y
  вҶ’ FS.FiniteSpeed.local (fs A) (T A x) (T A y)
preserves-locality A x y h =
  FS.FiniteSpeed.preservesLocality (fs A) x y h

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- 2) вҖңCompile-todayвҖқ defaults: trivial isotropy + trivial finite speed
------------------------------------------------------------------------

defaultIso : вҲҖ {S : Set} (U : UMetric.Ultrametric S) (T : S вҶ’ S) вҶ’ Iso.Isotropy U T
defaultIso U T = Iso.trivialIsotropy U T

defaultFS : вҲҖ {S : Set} (T : S вҶ’ S) вҶ’ FS.FiniteSpeed T
defaultFS T = FS.trivialFiniteSpeed T

mkDefaultClosure :
  вҲҖ {S : Set}
  вҶ’ (U : UMetric.Ultrametric S)
  вҶ’ (T : S вҶ’ S)
  вҶ’ (sc : Contraction.StrictContraction U T)
  вҶ’ (inv : Involution S)
  вҶ’ ClosureAxioms
mkDefaultClosure {S} U T sc inv =
  record
    { S   = S
    ; U   = U
    ; T   = T
    ; sc  = sc
    ; inv = inv
    ; iso = defaultIso U T
    ; fs  = defaultFS T
    }

module DASHI.Physics.TailCollapseGuardedStrict where

-- Guarded strictness interface for conditional projections.
-- This is the вҖңTemplate BвҖқ shape: strictness only in flow regime.
record GuardedStrictness {в„“} {A : Set в„“} : Set (lsuc в„“) where
  field
    X : Set в„“
    P : X вҶ’ X

    proj : X вҶ’ Stream A

    Guard  : X вҶ’ Set
    Broken : X вҶ’ Set
    Snap   : X вҶ’ Set
    Restore : X вҶ’ X

    Оә : в„•

    -- Flow regime: strictness in LCP depth (or your chosen Ball predicate).
    P-strict-on :
      вҲҖ {x y k} вҶ’
      Guard x вҶ’ Guard y вҶ’
      lcpвүҘ (proj x) (proj y) k вҶ’
      lcpвүҘ (proj (P x)) (proj (P y)) (k + Оә)

    -- Broken regime: restoration back into Guard.
    restore-normal-form :
      вҲҖ x вҶ’ Broken x вҶ’ Guard (Restore x)

    restore-idem :
      вҲҖ x вҶ’ Restore (Restore x) вүЎ Restore x

    restore-fixes :
      вҲҖ x вҶ’ P (Restore x) вүЎ Restore x

open GuardedStrictness public

module DASHI.Physics.RealClosureKit where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_вүЎ_)
open import Ultrametric as UMetric
open import Contraction as Contraction using (Contractiveвүў; StrictContraction)
open import DASHI.Combinatorics.Entropy using (Involution)

open import DASHI.Physics.TOperator as TOp
open import DASHI.Geometry.StrictContractionComposition as SCC
open import DASHI.Geometry.RealIsotropy as RIS
open import DASHI.Geometry.RealFiniteSpeed as RFS

open import DASHI.Physics.ClosureBuilder as CB
import DASHI.Physics.ClosureGlue as Glue

record RealClosureKit : SetвӮҒ where
  field
    S : Set
    U : UMetric.Ultrametric S

    C P R : S вҶ’ S

    nonexpC : SCC.NonExpansive U C
    nonexpR : SCC.NonExpansive U R
    strictP : Contractiveвүў U P
    orderLaws : SCC.OrderLaws
    presвүўR : SCC.DistinctPreserving R

    fp : S
    fixedT : (TOp.TOperator.T (record { C = C ; P = P ; R = R })) fp вүЎ fp
    uniqueT : вҲҖ x вҶ’ (TOp.TOperator.T (record { C = C ; P = P ; R = R })) x вүЎ x вҶ’ x вүЎ fp

    inv : Involution S
    iso : RIS.RealIsotropy U (TOp.TOperator.T (record { C = C ; P = P ; R = R }))
    fs  : RFS.RealFiniteSpeed (TOp.TOperator.T (record { C = C ; P = P ; R = R }))

open RealClosureKit public

toRealStack : RealClosureKit вҶ’ CB.RealStack
toRealStack k =
  record
    { S = S k
    ; U = U k
    ; C = C k
    ; P = P k
    ; R = R k
    ; nonexpC = nonexpC k
    ; nonexpR = nonexpR k
    ; strictP = strictP k
    ; orderLaws = orderLaws k
    ; presвүўR = presвүўR k
    ; fp0 = fp k
    ; fixedT = fixedT k
    ; uniqueT = uniqueT k
    ; inv = inv k
    ; iso = iso k
    ; fs  = fs k
    }

closureAxioms : (k : RealClosureKit) вҶ’ Glue.ClosureAxioms
closureAxioms k = CB.buildClosure (toRealStack k)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Causal structure based on locality predicate (finite speed)

localCausal : вҲҖ {m : Nat} вҶ’ MCS.CausalStructure m
localCausal {m} =
  record
    { _вүј_  = О» x y вҶ’ RFSI.local {n = m} x y
    ; delta = О» _ _ вҶ’ RTC.zeroVec {n = m}
    }

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Cone monotonicity for the locality-based causal structure

coneMonotone-local :
  вҲҖ {m : Nat} (Пғ : Vec IMQ.Sign m) (x y : Vec Trit m) вҶ’
  MCS.CausalStructure._вүј_ (localCausal {m}) x y вҶ’
  (+ 0) вүӨбөў IMQ.QПғ Пғ (MCS.CausalStructure.delta (localCausal {m}) x y)
coneMonotone-local Пғ x y h =
  IntP.вүӨ-reflexive (sym (RCSI.QПғ-zeroVec Пғ))

module DASHI.Physics.Core where

open import Level using (Level; _вҠ”_; zero; suc)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_вүЎ_; refl)
open import Data.Product using (_Г—_; ОЈ; ОЈ-syntax; _,_)
open import Data.Nat using (в„•)
open import Data.Bool using (Bool)

-- Abstract metric space; swap in your concrete ultrametric if desired.
record MetricSpace (в„“ : Level) : Set (suc в„“) where
  field
    X     : Set в„“
    d     : X вҶ’ X вҶ’ Set в„“        -- use в„қ-valued distance later if needed
    reflD : вҲҖ x вҶ’ d x x
    sym   : вҲҖ x y вҶ’ d x y вҶ’ d y x
    -- triangle etc as needed

-- Contractive operator skeleton.
record ContractionOp {в„“ : Level} (M : MetricSpace в„“) : Set (suc (suc в„“)) where
  open MetricSpace M
  field
    T      : X вҶ’ X
    lam    : Set в„“               -- typically a scalar 0<О»<1
    contractive : Set (suc в„“)    -- replace with your inequality form

-- Bilinear and quadratic forms kept abstract.
record Bilinear {в„“ : Level} (V : Set в„“) : Set (suc в„“) where
  field
    B : V вҶ’ V вҶ’ Set в„“

record Quadratic {в„“ : Level} (V : Set в„“) : Set (suc в„“) where
  field
    Q : V вҶ’ Set в„“

-- Involution / mirror.
record Involution {в„“ : Level} (V : Set в„“) : Set (suc в„“) where
  field
    О№    : V вҶ’ V
    invol : вҲҖ v вҶ’ О№ (О№ v) вүЎ v

-- Finite speed / locality placeholder.
record FiniteSpeed {в„“ : Level} (V : Set в„“) : Set (suc в„“) where
  field
    locality : Set в„“

-- Isotropy (rotation-like symmetries) and preservation of a quadratic form.
record Isotropy {в„“ : Level} (V : Set в„“) : Set (suc в„“) where
  field
    G   : Set в„“
    act : G вҶ’ V вҶ’ V

record PreservesQuadratic {в„“ : Level} {V : Set в„“} (iso : Isotropy V) (Q : Quadratic V) : Set (suc в„“) where
  open Isotropy iso
  field
    pres : вҲҖ g v вҶ’ Quadratic.Q Q (act g v) вүЎ Quadratic.Q Q v

-- Clifford-like algebra interface via universal property.
record CliffordLike {в„“ : Level} (V : Set в„“) : Set (suc в„“) where
  field
    Cl    : Set в„“
    embed : V вҶ’ Cl
    -- relations to be added in DecimationToClifford

-- Even subalgebra carrier.
record EvenSubalg {в„“ : Level} (A : Set в„“) : Set (suc в„“) where
  field
    Even : Set в„“
    inc  : Even вҶ’ A
