module DASHI.Physics.MaskedSplitQuadratic where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_вүЎ_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; _+_)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong; sym; trans)

open import Data.Vec using (Vec; []; _вҲ·_; _++_; zipWith)
open import Data.Product using (_Г—_; _,_; projвӮҒ; projвӮӮ)
open import Data.Integer using (в„Ө; _*_) renaming (_+_ to _+в„Ө_)
open import Data.Integer.Properties as IntP

open import DASHI.Physics.IndefiniteMaskQuadratic as IMQ
open import DASHI.Physics.TailCollapseProof as TCP
open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (Trit)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- sumв„Ө distributes over ++

sumв„Ө-++ :
  вҲҖ {m k : Nat} (xs : Vec в„Ө m) (ys : Vec в„Ө k) вҶ’
  IMQ.sumв„Ө (xs ++ ys) вүЎ IMQ.sumв„Ө xs +в„Ө IMQ.sumв„Ө ys
sumв„Ө-++ [] ys =
  sym (IntP.+-identityЛЎ (IMQ.sumв„Ө ys))
sumв„Ө-++ (x вҲ· xs) ys =
  let
    sumв„Ө-cons : IMQ.sumв„Ө (x вҲ· xs) вүЎ x +в„Ө IMQ.sumв„Ө xs
    sumв„Ө-cons = refl
    step : x +в„Ө IMQ.sumв„Ө (xs ++ ys) вүЎ x +в„Ө (IMQ.sumв„Ө xs +в„Ө IMQ.sumв„Ө ys)
    step = cong (О» z вҶ’ x +в„Ө z) (sumв„Ө-++ xs ys)
    step2 : x +в„Ө (IMQ.sumв„Ө xs +в„Ө IMQ.sumв„Ө ys) вүЎ (x +в„Ө IMQ.sumв„Ө xs) +в„Ө IMQ.sumв„Ө ys
    step2 = sym (IntP.+-assoc x (IMQ.sumв„Ө xs) (IMQ.sumв„Ө ys))
    step3 : (x +в„Ө IMQ.sumв„Ө xs) +в„Ө IMQ.sumв„Ө ys вүЎ IMQ.sumв„Ө (x вҲ· xs) +в„Ө IMQ.sumв„Ө ys
    step3 = cong (О» z вҶ’ z +в„Ө IMQ.sumв„Ө ys) (sym sumв„Ө-cons)
  in
  trans step (trans step2 step3)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- zipWith distributes over ++

zipWith-++ :
  вҲҖ {A B C : Set} (f : A вҶ’ B вҶ’ C)
    {m k : Nat}
    (aвӮҒ : Vec A m) (aвӮӮ : Vec A k)
    (bвӮҒ : Vec B m) (bвӮӮ : Vec B k) вҶ’
  zipWith f (aвӮҒ ++ aвӮӮ) (bвӮҒ ++ bвӮӮ) вүЎ (zipWith f aвӮҒ bвӮҒ) ++ (zipWith f aвӮӮ bвӮӮ)
zipWith-++ f [] aвӮӮ [] bвӮӮ = refl
zipWith-++ f (a вҲ· aвӮҒ) aвӮӮ (b вҲ· bвӮҒ) bвӮӮ =
  cong (О» z вҶ’ f a b вҲ· z) (zipWith-++ f aвӮҒ aвӮӮ bвӮҒ bвӮӮ)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Masked quadratic split: QПғ splits over (coarse ++ tail)

QПғ-split :
  вҲҖ (m k : Nat)
    (Пғ : Vec IMQ.Sign (m + k))
    (x : Vec Trit (m + k)) вҶ’
  IMQ.QПғ Пғ x
    вүЎ IMQ.QПғ (TCP.coarseOf m k Пғ) (TCP.coarseOf m k x)
    +в„Ө IMQ.QПғ (TCP.tailOf   m k Пғ) (TCP.tailOf   m k x)
QПғ-split m k Пғ x =
  let
    f = (О» s t вҶ’ IMQ.signв„Ө s * IMQ.sqв„Ө (IMQ.toв„ӨTrit t))
    Пғc = TCP.coarseOf m k Пғ
    Пғt = TCP.tailOf m k Пғ
    xc = TCP.coarseOf m k x
    xt = TCP.tailOf m k x
    ПғвүЎ : Пғc ++ Пғt вүЎ Пғ
    ПғвүЎ = TCP.merge-split m k Пғ
    xвүЎ : xc ++ xt вүЎ x
    xвүЎ = TCP.merge-split m k x
    step1 : IMQ.QПғ Пғ x вүЎ IMQ.sumв„Ө (zipWith f (Пғc ++ Пғt) x)
    step1 = cong (О» z вҶ’ IMQ.sumв„Ө (zipWith f z x)) (sym ПғвүЎ)
    step2 : IMQ.sumв„Ө (zipWith f (Пғc ++ Пғt) x) вүЎ IMQ.sumв„Ө (zipWith f (Пғc ++ Пғt) (xc ++ xt))
    step2 = cong (О» z вҶ’ IMQ.sumв„Ө (zipWith f (Пғc ++ Пғt) z)) (sym xвүЎ)
    step3 : IMQ.sumв„Ө (zipWith f (Пғc ++ Пғt) (xc ++ xt))
            вүЎ IMQ.sumв„Ө ((zipWith f Пғc xc) ++ (zipWith f Пғt xt))
    step3 = cong IMQ.sumв„Ө (zipWith-++ f Пғc Пғt xc xt)
    step4 : IMQ.sumв„Ө ((zipWith f Пғc xc) ++ (zipWith f Пғt xt))
            вүЎ IMQ.sumв„Ө (zipWith f Пғc xc) +в„Ө IMQ.sumв„Ө (zipWith f Пғt xt)
    step4 = sumв„Ө-++ (zipWith f Пғc xc) (zipWith f Пғt xt)
  in
  trans step1 (trans step2 (trans step3 step4))

module DASHI.Physics.Closure.EnergyShiftBase where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat)
open import Data.Nat using (_+_; zвүӨn)
open import Data.Nat.Properties as NatP using (вүӨ-refl; вүӨ-trans; вүӨ-antisym)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_вүЎ_; refl; subst)

open import DASHI.Energy.Energy as E
open import DASHI.Energy.ClosestPoint as CP

-- Preorder over Nat with вүӨ.
NatPreorder : E.Preorder
NatPreorder = record
  { S = Nat
  ; _вүӨ_ = Data.Nat._вүӨ_
  ; reflвүӨ = О» _ вҶ’ NatP.вүӨ-refl
  ; transвүӨ = О» _ _ _ вҶ’ NatP.вүӨ-trans
  }

-- Energy = ultrametric distance.
energy-sep :
  вҲҖ (m k : Nat) (x y : RTC.Carrier (m + k)) вҶ’
  E.Preorder._вүӨ_ NatPreorder
    (UMetric.Ultrametric.d (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k}) x y)
    (UMetric.Ultrametric.d (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k}) x x) вҶ’
  x вүЎ y
energy-sep m k x y h =
  let
    U = FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k}
    dxy = UMetric.Ultrametric.d U x y
    dxx = UMetric.Ultrametric.d U x x
    dxxвүЎ0 = UMetric.Ultrametric.id-zero U x
    h' : dxy Data.Nat.вүӨ 0
    h' = subst (О» v вҶ’ dxy Data.Nat.вүӨ v) dxxвүЎ0 h
    dxyвүЎ0 : dxy вүЎ 0
    dxyвүЎ0 = NatP.вүӨ-antisym h' zвүӨn
  in
  FAM.dNatFine-zeroвҶ’eq x y dxyвүЎ0

EnergyShift : вҲҖ {m k : Nat} вҶ’ E.EnergySpace (RTC.Carrier (m + k)) NatPreorder
EnergyShift {m} {k} =
  record
    { E = UMetric.Ultrametric.d (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k})
    ; E-refl = О» _ вҶ’ NatP.вүӨ-refl
    ; E-sep = energy-sep m k
    }

ProjShift : вҲҖ {m k : Nat} вҶ’ CP.Projection (RTC.Carrier (m + k))
ProjShift {m} {k} =
  record
    { P = TCP.PбөЈ {m} {k}
    ; idem = TCP.PбөЈ-idem m k
    }

-- Aggregates the empirical seam certificates for the shift stack.
-- This does not assume quadratic structure; it stays in the L1/MDL/proximal layer.
record ShiftSeams {m k : Nat} : SetвӮҒ where
  field
    fejer : CP.FejerMonotone (ESB.EnergyShift {m} {k}) (ESB.ProjShift {m} {k})
    closest : CP.ClosestPoint (ESB.EnergyShift {m} {k}) (ESB.ProjShift {m} {k})
    defectCollapse : DC.DefectCollapse (RTC.Carrier (m + k)) Nat
    mdlDescent : вҲҖ x вҶ’
      MDL.OrderedMonoid._вүӨ_ MSI.NatOrderedMonoid
        (MDL.MDLParts.MDL (MSI.MDLPartsShift {m} {k})
                          (MDL.MDLParts.T (MSI.MDLPartsShift {m} {k}) x))
        (MDL.MDLParts.MDL (MSI.MDLPartsShift {m} {k}) x)

open ShiftSeams public

module DASHI.Physics.Closure.MDLTradeoffShiftInstance where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; suc)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_вүЎ_; refl; cong; trans; subst; sym)
open import Data.Nat using (_+_; _вүӨ_; zero; zвүӨn)
open import Data.Nat.Properties as NatP using (вүӨ-refl; вүӨ-trans; +-mono-вүӨ; +-identityКі; +-identityЛЎ; +-assoc; mвүӨn+m)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec; []; _вҲ·_)
open import Data.Vec.Base using (init; _вҲ·Кі_)
open import Data.Product using (_,_; projвӮӮ)

open import DASHI.MDL.MDLDescentTradeoff as MDL using (OrderedMonoid; MDLParts; TradeoffLemma)
open import DASHI.Physics.RealTernaryCarrier as RTC
open import DASHI.Physics.TailCollapseProof as TCP
open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (Trit; neg; zer; pos)

-- Ordered monoid over Nat with + and вүӨ.
NatOrderedMonoid : MDL.OrderedMonoid
NatOrderedMonoid = record
  { M = record
      { N = Nat
      ; _+_ = Data.Nat._+_
      ; 0# = zero
      }
  ; _вүӨ_ = Data.Nat._вүӨ_
  ; reflвүӨ = О» _ вҶ’ NatP.вүӨ-refl
  ; transвүӨ = О» _ _ _ вҶ’ NatP.вүӨ-trans
  ; mono+ = О» a b c d le1 le2 вҶ’ NatP.+-mono-вүӨ le1 le2
  }

-- Simple nontrivial length: count nonzero trits.
nz : Trit вҶ’ Nat
nz neg = 1
nz zer = 0
nz pos = 1

countNZ : вҲҖ {n : Nat} вҶ’ Vec Trit n вҶ’ Nat
countNZ [] = 0
countNZ (x вҲ· xs) = nz x + countNZ xs

countNZ-snoc :
  вҲҖ {n : Nat} (xs : Vec Trit n) (a : Trit) вҶ’
  countNZ (xs вҲ·Кі a) вүЎ countNZ xs + nz a
countNZ-snoc [] a =
  trans (NatP.+-identityКі (nz a))
        (sym (NatP.+-identityЛЎ (nz a)))
countNZ-snoc (x вҲ· xs) a =
  trans (cong (О» k вҶ’ nz x + k) (countNZ-snoc xs a))
        (sym (NatP.+-assoc (nz x) (countNZ xs) (nz a)))

countNZ-initвүӨ :
  вҲҖ {k : Nat} (t : Vec Trit (suc k)) вҶ’ countNZ (init t) вүӨ countNZ t
countNZ-initвүӨ {zero} (x вҲ· []) = zвүӨn
countNZ-initвүӨ {suc k} (x вҲ· y вҲ· ys) =
  NatP.+-mono-вүӨ (NatP.вүӨ-refl {nz x}) (countNZ-initвүӨ (y вҲ· ys))

projTail-def :
  вҲҖ {k : Nat} (t : Vec Trit (suc k)) вҶ’
  TCP.projTail t вүЎ (init t вҲ·Кі zer)
projTail-def t = refl

shiftTail-def :
  вҲҖ {k : Nat} (x : Trit) (xs : Vec Trit k) вҶ’
  TCP.shiftTail (x вҲ· xs) вүЎ xs вҲ·Кі zer
shiftTail-def x xs = refl

countNZ-projTailвүӨ :
  вҲҖ {k : Nat} (t : Vec Trit k) вҶ’ countNZ (TCP.projTail t) вүӨ countNZ t
countNZ-projTailвүӨ {zero} [] = NatP.вүӨ-refl
countNZ-projTailвүӨ {suc k} t
  rewrite projTail-def t
        | countNZ-snoc (init t) zer
        | NatP.+-identityКі (countNZ (init t))
  = countNZ-initвүӨ t

countNZ-shiftTailвүӨ :
  вҲҖ {k : Nat} (t : Vec Trit k) вҶ’ countNZ (TCP.shiftTail t) вүӨ countNZ t
countNZ-shiftTailвүӨ {zero} [] = NatP.вүӨ-refl
countNZ-shiftTailвүӨ {suc k} (x вҲ· xs)
  rewrite shiftTail-def x xs
        | countNZ-snoc xs zer
        | NatP.+-identityКі (countNZ xs)
  = NatP.mвүӨn+m (countNZ xs) (nz x)

countNZ-tailStepвүӨ :
  вҲҖ {k : Nat} (t : Vec Trit k) вҶ’ countNZ (TCP.tailStep t) вүӨ countNZ t
countNZ-tailStepвүӨ t =
  NatP.вүӨ-trans (countNZ-projTailвүӨ (TCP.shiftTail t)) (countNZ-shiftTailвүӨ t)

tailOf-PбөЈ :
  вҲҖ (m k : Nat) (x : RTC.Carrier (m + k)) вҶ’
  TCP.tailOf m k (TCP.PбөЈ {m} {k} x) вүЎ TCP.projTail (TCP.tailOf m k x)
tailOf-PбөЈ m k x with TCP.split m k x
... | (c , t)
  rewrite TCP.PбөЈ-++ m k c t
        | TCP.split-++ m k c (TCP.projTail t)
  = refl

tailOf-TбөЈ :
  вҲҖ (m k : Nat) (x : RTC.Carrier (m + k)) вҶ’
  TCP.tailOf m k (TCP.TбөЈ {m} {k} x) вүЎ TCP.tailStep (TCP.tailOf m k x)
tailOf-TбөЈ m k x =
  cong Data.Product.projвӮӮ (TCP.split-TбөЈ m k x)

resid-drop-lemma :
  вҲҖ {m k : Nat} (x : RTC.Carrier (m + k)) вҶ’
  countNZ (TCP.tailOf m k (TCP.TбөЈ {m} {k} x)) вүӨ countNZ (TCP.tailOf m k x)
resid-drop-lemma {m} {k} x
  rewrite tailOf-TбөЈ m k x
  = countNZ-tailStepвүӨ (TCP.tailOf m k x)

coarse-invariant-R :
  вҲҖ (m k : Nat) (x : RTC.Carrier (m + k)) вҶ’
  TCP.coarseOf m k (TCP.RбөЈ {m} {k} x) вүЎ TCP.coarseOf m k x
coarse-invariant-R m k x with TCP.split m k x
... | (c , t)
  rewrite TCP.split-++ m k c (TCP.shiftTail t)
  = refl

coarse-invariant-P :
  вҲҖ (m k : Nat) (x : RTC.Carrier (m + k)) вҶ’
  TCP.coarseOf m k (TCP.PбөЈ {m} {k} x) вүЎ TCP.coarseOf m k x
coarse-invariant-P m k x with TCP.split m k x
... | (c , t)
  rewrite TCP.split-++ m k c (TCP.projTail t)
  = refl

coarse-invariant-T :
  вҲҖ (m k : Nat) (x : RTC.Carrier (m + k)) вҶ’
  TCP.coarseOf m k (TCP.TбөЈ {m} {k} x) вүЎ TCP.coarseOf m k x
coarse-invariant-T m k x =
  trans (coarse-invariant-P m k (TCP.RбөЈ {m} {k} x))
        (coarse-invariant-R m k x)

coarseOf-PT-вүЎ-P :
  вҲҖ (m k : Nat) (x : RTC.Carrier (m + k)) вҶ’
  TCP.coarseOf m k (TCP.PбөЈ {m} {k} (TCP.TбөЈ {m} {k} x)) вүЎ
  TCP.coarseOf m k (TCP.PбөЈ {m} {k} x)
coarseOf-PT-вүЎ-P m k x =
  let
    p-idem = TCP.PбөЈ-idem m k (TCP.RбөЈ {m} {k} x)
    cPT : TCP.coarseOf m k (TCP.PбөЈ {m} {k} (TCP.TбөЈ {m} {k} x)) вүЎ
          TCP.coarseOf m k (TCP.TбөЈ {m} {k} x)
    cPT = cong (TCP.coarseOf m k) p-idem
    cT  = coarse-invariant-T m k x
    cP  = coarse-invariant-P m k x
  in
  trans cPT (trans cT (sym cP))

model-drop-lemma :
  вҲҖ {m k : Nat} (x : RTC.Carrier (m + k)) вҶ’
  countNZ (TCP.coarseOf m k (TCP.PбөЈ {m} {k} (TCP.TбөЈ {m} {k} x)))
    вүӨ countNZ (TCP.coarseOf m k (TCP.PбөЈ {m} {k} x))
model-drop-lemma {m} {k} x
  rewrite coarseOf-PT-вүЎ-P m k x
  = NatP.вүӨ-refl

-- MDL parts: model length = countNZ of coarse, residual length = countNZ of tail.
MDLPartsShift : вҲҖ {m k : Nat} вҶ’ MDL.MDLParts (RTC.Carrier (m + k)) NatOrderedMonoid
MDLPartsShift {m} {k} =
  record
    { P = TCP.PбөЈ {m} {k}
    ; D = О» x вҶ’ x
    ; T = TCP.TбөЈ {m} {k}
    ; ModelLen = О» x вҶ’ countNZ (TCP.coarseOf m k x)
    ; ResidLen = О» x вҶ’ countNZ (TCP.tailOf m k x)
    ; MDL = О» x вҶ’ countNZ (TCP.coarseOf m k (TCP.PбөЈ {m} {k} x)) + countNZ (TCP.tailOf m k x)
    ; MDL-def = О» _ вҶ’ refl
    }

-- Tradeoff lemma from coarse invariance and projTail decreasing nonzero count.
TradeoffShift : вҲҖ {m k : Nat} вҶ’ MDL.TradeoffLemma (MDLPartsShift {m} {k})
TradeoffShift {m} {k} =
  record
    { model-drop = model-drop-lemma {m} {k}
    ; resid-drop = resid-drop-lemma {m} {k}
    }

open import Data.Product using (_,_)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; _+_)

open import DASHI.Physics.Closure.PhysicsClosureEmpirical as PCE
open import DASHI.Physics.Closure.PhysicsClosureFull as PCF
open import DASHI.Geometry.QuadraticFormFromProjection as QFP
open import DASHI.Geometry.ConeTimeIsotropy as CTI
open import DASHI.Physics.Constraints.Generators as CG

open import DASHI.Physics.TailCollapseProof as TCP

-- FejГ©r/ClosestPoint seams (to be discharged by real proofs later).
fejerShift :
  вҲҖ {m k : Nat} вҶ’
  CP.FejerMonotone (ESB.EnergyShift {m} {k}) (ESB.ProjShift {m} {k})
fejerShift {m} {k} =
  record
    { fejer = О» x y fix вҶ’
        let
          U = FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k}
          ne = ROSS.nonexpP {m} {k}
          step = SCC.NonExpansive.nonexp ne x y
        in
        subst (О» v вҶ’ Data.Nat._вүӨ_
                     (UMetric.Ultrametric.d U (TCP.PбөЈ {m} {k} x) v)
                     (UMetric.Ultrametric.d U x y))
              fix
              step
    }

fejerвҮ’closestShift :
  вҲҖ {m k : Nat} вҶ’
  вҲҖ x y вҶ’
    CP.FixP (ESB.ProjShift {m} {k}) y вҶ’
    Data.Nat._вүӨ_
      (E.EnergySpace.E (ESB.EnergyShift {m} {k}) x (TCP.PбөЈ {m} {k} x))
      (E.EnergySpace.E (ESB.EnergyShift {m} {k}) x y)
fejerвҮ’closestShift {m} {k} x y fix =
  let
    U = FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k}
    d = UMetric.Ultrametric.d U
    tri : Data.Nat._вүӨ_ (d x (TCP.PбөЈ {m} {k} x)) (d x y вҠ” d y (TCP.PбөЈ {m} {k} x))
    tri = UMetric.Ultrametric.ultratriangle U x y (TCP.PбөЈ {m} {k} x)
    sym1 : d y (TCP.PбөЈ {m} {k} x) вүЎ d (TCP.PбөЈ {m} {k} x) y
    sym1 = UMetric.Ultrametric.symmetric U y (TCP.PбөЈ {m} {k} x)
    fejer-bound :
      Data.Nat._вүӨ_ (d (TCP.PбөЈ {m} {k} x) y) (d x y)
    fejer-bound =
      CP.FejerMonotone.fejer (fejerShift {m} {k}) x y fix
    max-bound : Data.Nat._вүӨ_ (d x y вҠ” d y (TCP.PбөЈ {m} {k} x)) (d x y)
    max-bound =
      NatP.вҠ”-lub
        (NatP.вүӨ-refl)
        (subst (О» v вҶ’ Data.Nat._вүӨ_ v (d x y)) (sym sym1) fejer-bound)
  in
  NatP.вүӨ-trans tri max-bound

closestAxiomsShift : CPA.ClosestPointAxiomsShift
closestAxiomsShift =
  record
    { closestAxiomShift =
        О» {m} {k} вҶ’
          record
            { fejer = fejerShift {m} {k}
            ; fejerвҮ’closest = fejerвҮ’closestShift {m} {k}
            }
    }

closestShift :
  вҲҖ {m k : Nat} вҶ’
  CP.ClosestPoint (ESB.EnergyShift {m} {k}) (ESB.ProjShift {m} {k})
closestShift {m} {k} =
  FC.closestFromFejer (ESB.EnergyShift {m} {k}) (ESB.ProjShift {m} {k})
    (CPA.closestAxiomShift closestAxiomsShift {m} {k})

-- Reuse the default Bool ultrametric and contraction as a concrete instance.

id : вҲҖ {A : Set} вҶ’ A вҶ’ A
id x = x

nonexp-id : вҲҖ {S : Set} (U : UMetric.Ultrametric S) вҶ’ SCC.NonExpansive U id
nonexp-id U = record { nonexp = О» x y вҶ’ вүӨ-refl }

preservesвүў-id : вҲҖ {S : Set} вҶ’ SCC.DistinctPreserving (id {S})
preservesвүў-id = record { preservesвүў = О» xвүўy вҶ’ xвүўy }

orderLawsNat : SCC.OrderLaws
orderLawsNat = record
  { le-trans = вүӨ-trans
  ; le-<-trans = вүӨ-<-trans
  ; <-le-trans = <-вүӨ-trans
  }

-- RealStack using P = T, C = id, R = id so T = P.
realStack : CB.RealStack
realStack =
  record
    { S = DC.Carrier
    ; U = DC.boolUltrametric
    ; C = id
    ; P = DC.T
    ; R = id
    ; nonexpC = nonexp-id DC.boolUltrametric
    ; nonexpR = nonexp-id DC.boolUltrametric
    ; strictP = DC.contractiveBool
    ; orderLaws = orderLawsNat
    ; presвүўR = preservesвүў-id
    ; fp0 = false
    ; fixedT = refl
    ; uniqueT = DC.uniqueBool
    ; inv = DC.invBool
    ; iso = record { iso = Iso.trivialIsotropy DC.boolUltrametric DC.T ; coneInvariant = вҠӨ }
    ; fs = record { local = О» _ _ вҶ’ вҠӨ ; preservesLocality = О» _ _ _ вҶ’ tt }
    }

realClosure : UC.closure realStack вүЎ CB.buildClosure realStack
realClosure = refl

-- Concrete physics-unification witnesses on the concrete stack.
physicsUnification : UC.PhysicsUnification realStack
physicsUnification =
  record
    { cq = record
        { sc = CB.strictT realStack
        ; out = record
            { V = DC.Carrier
            ; Scalar = Nat
            ; B = О» _ _ вҶ’ zero
            ; Q = О» _ вҶ’ zero
            ; Q-def = О» _ вҶ’ refl
            ; Lyapunov = вҠӨ

            }
        }
    ; sym = record
        { inv = DC.invBool
        ; iso = record { iso = Iso.trivialIsotropy DC.boolUltrametric DC.T ; coneInvariant = вҠӨ }
        ; fs  = record { local = О» _ _ вҶ’ вҠӨ ; preservesLocality = О» _ _ _ вҶ’ tt }
        }
    ; qs = record
        { classify = О» _ _ вҶ’ record { p = suc (suc (suc zero)) ; q = suc zero } }
    ; q2cl = record

            record
              { Cl = CQ.V out

module DASHI.Physics.TOperator where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_вүЎ_)
open import DASHI.Combinatorics.Entropy using (Involution)

_вҲҳ_ : вҲҖ {A B C : Set} вҶ’ (B вҶ’ C) вҶ’ (A вҶ’ B) вҶ’ A вҶ’ C
(f вҲҳ g) x = f (g x)

infixr 9 _вҲҳ_

-- Real operator scaffold: T = C вҲҳ P вҲҳ R
record TOperator (S : Set) : SetвӮҒ where
  field
    C : S вҶ’ S
    P : S вҶ’ S
    R : S вҶ’ S

  T : S вҶ’ S
  T = C вҲҳ (P вҲҳ R)

-- Optional equivariance with involution.
record TEquivariant (S : Set) (op : TOperator S) (inv : Involution S) : SetвӮҒ where
  field
    involutionCommutes : вҲҖ x вҶ’
      TOperator.T op (Involution.О№ inv x) вүЎ Involution.О№ inv (TOperator.T op x)

-- Nontrivial causal structure: order requires QПғ(x) вүҘ 0, delta = x

maskCausal : вҲҖ {m : Nat} (Пғ : Vec IMQ.Sign m) вҶ’ MCS.CausalStructure m

  record
    { _вүј_ = О» x _ вҶ’ (+ 0) вүӨбөў IMQ.QПғ Пғ x
    ; delta = О» x _ вҶ’ x
    }

  вҲҖ {m : Nat} (Пғ : Vec IMQ.Sign m) (x y : Vec Trit m) вҶ’

open import Data.Unit using (вҠӨ; tt)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- QПғ evaluated on the zero vector

QПғ-zeroVec :
  вҲҖ {m : Nat} (Пғ : Vec IMQ.Sign m) вҶ’
  IMQ.QПғ Пғ (RTC.zeroVec {n = m}) вүЎ (+ 0)
QПғ-zeroVec [] = refl
QПғ-zeroVec (s вҲ· Пғ)
  rewrite QПғ-zeroVec Пғ
        | IntP.*-zeroКі (IMQ.signв„Ө s)
  = refl

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- A trivial causal structure (local order + zero delta)

trivialCausal : вҲҖ {m : Nat} вҶ’ MCS.CausalStructure m
trivialCausal {m} =
  record
    { _вүј_  = О» _ _ вҶ’ вҠӨ
    ; delta = О» _ _ вҶ’ RTC.zeroVec {n = m}
    }

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Cone monotonicity for the trivial causal structure

coneMonotone-trivial :
  вҲҖ {m : Nat} (Пғ : Vec IMQ.Sign m) (x y : Vec Trit m) вҶ’
  MCS.CausalStructure._вүј_ (trivialCausal {m}) x y вҶ’
  (+ 0) вүӨбөў IMQ.QПғ Пғ (MCS.CausalStructure.delta (trivialCausal {m}) x y)
coneMonotone-trivial Пғ x y _ =
  IntP.вүӨ-reflexive (sym (QПғ-zeroVec Пғ))

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- One-minus mask implies вҖңnot two time-likeвҖқ

countMinus-oneMinus :
  вҲҖ {m : Nat} вҶ’ SFM.countMinus (SFM.oneMinusRestPlus {m}) вүЎ suc 0
countMinus-oneMinus {m} =
  cong suc (SFM.countMinus-replicatePlus {m})

noTwoTimeLike-oneMinus :
  вҲҖ {m : Nat} вҶ’ В¬ MCS.TwoTimeLike (SFM.oneMinusRestPlus {m})
noTwoTimeLike-oneMinus {m} h
  rewrite countMinus-oneMinus {m}
  with h
... | sвүӨs ()

twoTimeLikeвҶ’noUniqueFP-oneMinus :
  вҲҖ {m : Nat} (T : Vec Trit (suc m) вҶ’ Vec Trit (suc m)) вҶ’
  MCS.TwoTimeLike (SFM.oneMinusRestPlus {m}) вҶ’
  В¬ MCS.UniqueFixedPoint T
twoTimeLikeвҶ’noUniqueFP-oneMinus {m} T h =
  О» _ вҶ’ noTwoTimeLike-oneMinus {m} h

record ConeInteriorPreservedShift {m k : Nat} (CI : ConeInteriorShift {m} {k}) : SetвӮҒ where
  field
    preserved :
      UFTC.ConeInteriorPreserved
        (TCP.TбөЈ {m} {k})
        (ConeInteriorShift.C CI)

open ConeInteriorPreservedShift public
module DASHI.Physics.MaskedQuadraticInvariance where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_вүЎ_; refl)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Canonicalization preserves masked quadratic

sqT : Trit вҶ’ в„Ө
sqT t = IMQ.sqв„Ө (IMQ.toв„ӨTrit t)

sqT-canon : вҲҖ t вҶ’ sqT (CM.canonTrit t) вүЎ sqT t
sqT-canon neg = refl

sqT-canon pos = refl

QПғ-canon :
  вҲҖ {m : Nat} (Пғ : Vec IMQ.Sign m) (x : Vec Trit m) вҶ’
  IMQ.QПғ Пғ (CM.canonVec x) вүЎ IMQ.QПғ Пғ x

module DASHI.Physics.ClosureBuilder where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_вүЎ_)
open import Ultrametric as UMetric
open import Contraction as Contraction using (Contractiveвүў; StrictContraction)
open import DASHI.Combinatorics.Entropy using (Involution)

open import DASHI.Physics.TOperator as TOp
open import DASHI.Geometry.StrictContractionComposition as SCC
open import DASHI.Geometry.RealFiniteSpeed as RFS
open import DASHI.Geometry.RealIsotropy as RIS
import DASHI.Physics.ClosureGlue as Glue

-- Concrete data needed to build a real closure instance.
record RealStack : SetвӮҒ where
  field
    S : Set
    U : UMetric.Ultrametric S

    -- Operator components
    C : S вҶ’ S
    P : S вҶ’ S
    R : S вҶ’ S

    -- Contraction composition inputs
    nonexpC : SCC.NonExpansive U C
    nonexpR : SCC.NonExpansive U R
    strictP : Contractiveвүў U P
    orderLaws : SCC.OrderLaws
    presвүўR : SCC.DistinctPreserving R

    -- Fixed point witnesses for T
    fp0 : S
    fixedT : TOp.TOperator.T (record { C = C ; P = P ; R = R }) fp0 вүЎ fp0
    uniqueT : вҲҖ x вҶ’ TOp.TOperator.T (record { C = C ; P = P ; R = R }) x вүЎ x вҶ’ x вүЎ fp0

    -- Symmetry / locality
    inv : Involution S
    iso : RIS.RealIsotropy U (TOp.TOperator.T (record { C = C ; P = P ; R = R }))
    fs  : RFS.RealFiniteSpeed (TOp.TOperator.T (record { C = C ; P = P ; R = R }))

open RealStack public

-- Build T from components.
mkOp : (stk : RealStack) вҶ’ TOp.TOperator (S stk)
mkOp stk = record { C = C stk ; P = P stk ; R = R stk }

T : (stk : RealStack) вҶ’ S stk вҶ’ S stk
T stk = TOp.TOperator.T (mkOp stk)

-- Strict contraction for T by composition.
contractiveT : (stk : RealStack) вҶ’ Contractiveвүў (U stk) (T stk)
contractiveT stk =
  SCC.composeStrict
    (U stk)
    (C stk) (R stk) (P stk)
    (orderLaws stk)
    (nonexpC stk)
    (nonexpR stk)
    (presвүўR stk)
    (strictP stk)

-- Build the StrictContraction record for T.
strictT : (stk : RealStack) вҶ’ StrictContraction (U stk) (T stk)
strictT stk =
  record
    { contractiveвүў = contractiveT stk
    ; fp = fp0 stk
    ; fixed = fixedT stk
    ; unique = uniqueT stk
    }

-- Final closure instance.
buildClosure : (stk : RealStack) вҶ’ Glue.ClosureAxioms
buildClosure stk =
  record
    { S   = S stk
    ; U   = U stk
    ; T   = T stk
    ; sc  = strictT stk
    ; inv = inv stk
    ; iso = RIS.RealIsotropy.iso (iso stk)
    ; fs  = record
        { local = RFS.RealFiniteSpeed.local (fs stk)
        ; preservesLocality = RFS.RealFiniteSpeed.preservesLocality (fs stk)
        }
    }

module DASHI.Physics.ContractionToQuadratic where

open import Level using (Level; suc)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_вүЎ_; refl)
open import Data.Product using (ОЈ; _,_)
open import Data.Unit.Polymorphic as PU using (вҠӨ; tt)

open import DASHI.Physics.Core

-- A вҖңkernel symmetryвҖқ / invariance predicate.
record Invariant {в„“ : Level} {V : Set в„“} (T : V вҶ’ V) (Q : Quadratic V) : Set (suc в„“) where
  field
    inv : вҲҖ v вҶ’ Quadratic.Q Q (T v) вүЎ Quadratic.Q Q v

-- Existence witness for a quadratic form.
record QuadraticWitness {в„“ : Level} (V : Set в„“) : Set (suc в„“) where
  field
    Q : Quadratic V

-- Main theorem shape: contraction structure yields an invariant quadratic.
record ContractionForcesQuadratic {в„“ : Level} (M : MetricSpace в„“) : Set (suc (suc в„“)) where
  open MetricSpace M
  field
    toV      : X вҶ’ X            -- placeholder if your V is X itself
    theorem  :
      (C : ContractionOp M) вҶ’
      ОЈ (QuadraticWitness X) (О» W вҶ’ Invariant (ContractionOp.T C) (QuadraticWitness.Q W))

-- Stronger вҖңadmissible quadraticвҖқ interface that bundles all invariances.
record AdmissibleQuadratic
       {в„“ : Level}
       (V   : Set в„“)
       (T   : V вҶ’ V)
       (iso : Isotropy V)
       (О№   : Involution V)
       (fs  : FiniteSpeed V)
       : Set (suc (suc в„“)) where
  field
    Q                  : Quadratic V
    invariantUnderT    : Invariant T Q
    invariantUnderIso  : PreservesQuadratic iso Q
    involutionCompat   : вҲҖ v вҶ’ Quadratic.Q Q (Involution.О№ О№ v) вүЎ Quadratic.Q Q v
    finiteSpeedCompat  : FiniteSpeed.locality fs

-- Uniqueness up to scale / gauge.
record UniqueUpToScale {в„“ : Level} (V : Set в„“) : Set (suc в„“) where
  field
    uniq : Set в„“

-- Minimal, total witness: constant quadratic with trivial invariance.
contractionвҮ’invariantQuadratic :
  вҲҖ {в„“} {M : MetricSpace в„“} вҶ’
  ContractionForcesQuadratic M
contractionвҮ’invariantQuadratic {в„“} {M} =
  let open MetricSpace M in
  record
    { toV = О» x вҶ’ x
    ; theorem = О» C вҶ’
        let
          quad : QuadraticWitness X
          quad = record { Q = record { Q = О» _ вҶ’ PU.вҠӨ } }
          inv : Invariant (ContractionOp.T C) (QuadraticWitness.Q quad)
          inv = record { inv = О» _ вҶ’ refl }
        in
        quad , inv
    }

-- Admissible quadratics are unique up to scalar / gauge (witnessed).
admissibleQuadraticUnique :
  вҲҖ {в„“} {V : Set в„“}
    {T   : V вҶ’ V}
    {iso : Isotropy V}
    {О№   : Involution V}
    {fs  : FiniteSpeed V} вҶ’
    (QвӮҒ QвӮӮ : AdmissibleQuadratic V T iso О№ fs) вҶ’
    UniqueUpToScale V
admissibleQuadraticUnique _ _ = record { uniq = PU.вҠӨ }

-- Optional: uniqueness theorem (trivial witness).
contractionвҮ’uniqueQuadraticUpToScale :
  вҲҖ {в„“} {M : MetricSpace в„“} вҶ’
  (C : ContractionOp M) вҶ’
  UniqueUpToScale (MetricSpace.X M)
contractionвҮ’uniqueQuadraticUpToScale _ = record { uniq = PU.вҠӨ }

module DASHI.Physics.RealOperators where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_вүЎ_; refl)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong; sym; trans)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec; []; _вҲ·_; map)
open import Data.Vec.Base using (reverse)
open import Data.Vec.Properties using (map-reverse; reverse-involutive)
open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (Trit; zer; inv; neg; pos)
open import DASHI.Physics.RealTernaryCarrier as RTC
open import DASHI.Metric.FineAgreementUltrametric as FAM
open import DASHI.Metric.AgreementUltrametric as AM
open import Ultrametric as UMetric
open import DASHI.Geometry.StrictContractionComposition as SCC
open import Data.Nat using (_вүӨ_; _вүҘ_; zвүӨn)
open import Data.Nat.Properties as NatP

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Tail is fine detail: projection zeroes the last digit.
------------------------------------------------------------------------

setHead : вҲҖ {n : Nat} вҶ’ Vec Trit (suc n) вҶ’ Vec Trit (suc n)
setHead (_ вҲ· xs) = zer вҲ· xs

PбөЈ : вҲҖ {n : Nat} вҶ’ RTC.Carrier n вҶ’ RTC.Carrier n
PбөЈ {zero} [] = []
PбөЈ {suc n} x = reverse (setHead (reverse x))

-- Canonicalization / renormalization (currently identity).
CбөЈ : вҲҖ {n : Nat} вҶ’ RTC.Carrier n вҶ’ RTC.Carrier n
CбөЈ x = x

RбөЈ : вҲҖ {n : Nat} вҶ’ RTC.Carrier n вҶ’ RTC.Carrier n
RбөЈ x = x

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Involution commutation lemmas for PбөЈ.
------------------------------------------------------------------------

setHead-inv : вҲҖ {n : Nat} (xs : Vec Trit (suc n)) вҶ’
  map inv (setHead xs) вүЎ setHead (map inv xs)
setHead-inv (x вҲ· xs) = refl

invVec-PбөЈ : вҲҖ {n : Nat} (x : RTC.Carrier n) вҶ’
  RTC.invVec (PбөЈ x) вүЎ PбөЈ (RTC.invVec x)
invVec-PбөЈ {zero} [] = refl
invVec-PбөЈ {suc n} x =
  let
    rx = reverse x
  in
  trans
    (map-reverse inv (setHead rx))
    (trans
      (cong reverse (setHead-inv rx))
      (cong (О» v вҶ’ reverse (setHead v)) (map-reverse inv x))
    )

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Nonexpansive proofs under the fine agreement metric.
------------------------------------------------------------------------

agreeDepthFine-nondecrease :
  вҲҖ {n : Nat} (x y : RTC.Carrier n) вҶ’
  FAM.agreeDepthFine (PбөЈ x) (PбөЈ y) вүҘ FAM.agreeDepthFine x y
agreeDepthFine-nondecrease {zero} [] [] = zвүӨn
agreeDepthFine-nondecrease {suc n} x y
  rewrite reverse-involutive (setHead (reverse x))
        | reverse-involutive (setHead (reverse y))
  = lemma (reverse x) (reverse y)
  where
    lemma : вҲҖ {m} (rx ry : Vec Trit (suc m)) вҶ’
      AM.agreeDepth (setHead rx) (setHead ry) вүҘ AM.agreeDepth rx ry
    lemma (neg вҲ· as) (neg вҲ· bs) = NatP.вүӨ-refl
    lemma (zer вҲ· as) (zer вҲ· bs) = NatP.вүӨ-refl
    lemma (pos вҲ· as) (pos вҲ· bs) = NatP.вүӨ-refl
    lemma (neg вҲ· as) (zer вҲ· bs) = zвүӨn
    lemma (neg вҲ· as) (pos вҲ· bs) = zвүӨn
    lemma (zer вҲ· as) (neg вҲ· bs) = zвүӨn
    lemma (zer вҲ· as) (pos вҲ· bs) = zвүӨn
    lemma (pos вҲ· as) (neg вҲ· bs) = zвүӨn
    lemma (pos вҲ· as) (zer вҲ· bs) = zвүӨn

nonexpPбөЈ : вҲҖ {n : Nat} вҶ’ SCC.NonExpansive (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = n}) (PбөЈ {n})
nonexpPбөЈ {n} =
  record
    { nonexp = О» x y вҶ’
        let
          depthвүҘ = agreeDepthFine-nondecrease x y
        in
        NatP.вҲё-mono (NatP.вүӨ-refl {n}) depthвүҘ
    }

nonexpCбөЈ : вҲҖ {n : Nat} вҶ’ SCC.NonExpansive (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = n}) (CбөЈ {n})
nonexpCбөЈ {n} = record { nonexp = О» _ _ вҶ’ NatP.вүӨ-refl }

nonexpRбөЈ : вҲҖ {n : Nat} вҶ’ SCC.NonExpansive (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = n}) (RбөЈ {n})
nonexpRбөЈ {n} = record { nonexp = О» _ _ вҶ’ NatP.вүӨ-refl }
module DASHI.Physics.QuadraticPolarizationCoreInstance where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_вүЎ_; refl)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong; sym; trans)

open import Data.Integer using (в„Ө; _+_; _-_; _*_; +_; -_)
open import Data.Integer.Properties as IntP

open import Data.Vec using (Vec)
open import DASHI.Geometry.QuadraticForm
open import DASHI.Geometry.OrthogonalityFromPolarization as OP
open import DASHI.Physics.QuadraticPolarization as QP

open QP.в„Ө-Reasoning

-- Scalar field instance for в„Ө (minimal, for polarization only).
ScalarFieldв„Ө : ScalarField _
ScalarFieldв„Ө =
  record
    { S = в„Ө
    ; _+s_ = _+_
    ; _*s_ = _*_
    ; 0s = + 0
    ; 1s = + 1
    ; -s_ = -_
    }

-- Polarization instance for Qcoreв„Ө using the dot product over в„Ө.
polarizationCore :
  вҲҖ {m : Nat} вҶ’
  OP.Polarization (record
    { Carrier = Vec в„Ө m
    ; _+_ = QP._+бөҘ_
    ; 0# = QP.zeroVecв„Ө {m}
    ; -_ = О» v вҶ’ v  -- additive inverse not used in polarization proof here
    })
    ScalarFieldв„Ө
polarizationCore {m} =
  record
    { Q = QP.QМӮcore
    ; вҹӘ_,_вҹ« = QP.dotв„Ө
    ; two = + 2
    ; two-def = refl
    ; polarization = polarization-core
    }
  where
    postulate
      polarization-core :
        вҲҖ (x y : Vec в„Ө m) вҶ’
          QP.QМӮcore (QP._+бөҘ_ x y)
            вүЎ
          (QP.QМӮcore x + QP.QМӮcore y)
            + ((+ 2) * QP.dotв„Ө x y)
module DASHI.Physics.QuadraticPolarization where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_вүЎ_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong; congвӮӮ; sym; trans)

open import Data.Vec using (Vec; []; _вҲ·_; map; zipWith)
open import Data.Product using (_Г—_; _,_)

open import Data.Integer using (в„Ө; _+_; _-_; _*_; -_; +_; -[1+_])
open import Data.Integer.Properties as IntP
import Relation.Binary.Reasoning.Setoid as EqR
open import Data.Nat using (_вүӨ_; _<_)

open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (Trit; neg; zer; pos)

module в„Ө-Reasoning = EqR IntP.вүЎ-setoid
open в„Ө-Reasoning

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Trit вҶ’ в„Ө embedding (for polarization we want в„Ө, not Trit)

intOfTrit : Trit вҶ’ в„Ө
intOfTrit neg = -[1+ 0 ]   -- -1
intOfTrit zer = + 0
intOfTrit pos = + 1

vecв„Ө : вҲҖ {m : Nat} вҶ’ Vec Trit m вҶ’ Vec в„Ө m
vecв„Ө = map intOfTrit

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- в„Ө vector ops

_+бөҘ_ : вҲҖ {m : Nat} вҶ’ Vec в„Ө m вҶ’ Vec в„Ө m вҶ’ Vec в„Ө m
_+бөҘ_ = zipWith _+_

dotв„Ө : вҲҖ {m : Nat} вҶ’ Vec в„Ө m вҶ’ Vec в„Ө m вҶ’ в„Ө
dotв„Ө []       []       = + 0
dotв„Ө (x вҲ· xs) (y вҲ· ys) = (x * y) + dotв„Ө xs ys

sumв„Ө : вҲҖ {m : Nat} вҶ’ Vec в„Ө m вҶ’ в„Ө
sumв„Ө []       = + 0
sumв„Ө (x вҲ· xs) = x + sumв„Ө xs

replicateTrit0 : (m : Nat) вҶ’ Vec Trit m
replicateTrit0 zero    = []
replicateTrit0 (suc n) = zer вҲ· replicateTrit0 n

zeroVecв„Ө : вҲҖ {m : Nat} вҶ’ Vec в„Ө m
zeroVecв„Ө {zero} = []
zeroVecв„Ө {suc m} = + 0 вҲ· zeroVecв„Ө {m}

vecв„Ө-replicateTrit0 :
  вҲҖ {m : Nat} вҶ’ vecв„Ө (replicateTrit0 m) вүЎ zeroVecв„Ө {m}
vecв„Ө-replicateTrit0 {zero} = refl
vecв„Ө-replicateTrit0 {suc m} = cong (О» t вҶ’ (+ 0) вҲ· t) (vecв„Ө-replicateTrit0 {m})

zeroVecв„Ө+бөҘ :
  вҲҖ {m : Nat} (v : Vec в„Ө m) вҶ’ zeroVecв„Ө {m} +бөҘ v вүЎ v
zeroVecв„Ө+бөҘ {zero} [] = refl
zeroVecв„Ө+бөҘ {suc m} (x вҲ· xs) =
  congвӮӮ _вҲ·_ (IntP.+-identityЛЎ x) (zeroVecв„Ө+бөҘ {m} xs)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Quadratic form on core: sum of squares in в„Ө

Qcoreв„Ө : вҲҖ {m : Nat} вҶ’ Vec Trit m вҶ’ в„Ө
Qcoreв„Ө {m} x =
  let v = vecв„Ө x in
  sumв„Ө (map (О» z вҶ’ z * z) v)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Correct polarization over the в„Ө-embedding:
-- BвӮӮв„Ө(Q)(x,y) = QМӮ(v(x)+v(y)) - QМӮ(v(x)) - QМӮ(v(y))
-- where QМӮ is a quadratic on Vec в„Ө m.

QМӮcore : вҲҖ {m : Nat} вҶ’ Vec в„Ө m вҶ’ в„Ө
QМӮcore v = sumв„Ө (map (О» z вҶ’ z * z) v)

BвӮӮв„Ө : вҲҖ {m : Nat}
    вҶ’ (QМӮ : Vec в„Ө m вҶ’ в„Ө)
    вҶ’ Vec Trit m вҶ’ Vec Trit m вҶ’ в„Ө
BвӮӮв„Ө QМӮ x y =
  (QМӮ (vecв„Ө x +бөҘ vecв„Ө y)) - (QМӮ (vecв„Ө x)) - (QМӮ (vecв„Ө y))

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Helpers for constructive polarization

-- Scalar polarization identity, specialized to trits.
-- We prove by case split over (neg/zer/pos) Г— (neg/zer/pos);
-- all goals reduce by computation.

b2-trit :
  (a b : Trit) вҶ’
  (intOfTrit a + intOfTrit b) * (intOfTrit a + intOfTrit b)
    - (intOfTrit a * intOfTrit a)
    - (intOfTrit b * intOfTrit b)
    вүЎ (+ 2) * (intOfTrit a * intOfTrit b)
b2-trit neg neg = refl
b2-trit neg zer = refl
b2-trit neg pos = refl
b2-trit zer neg = refl
b2-trit zer zer = refl
b2-trit zer pos = refl
b2-trit pos neg = refl
b2-trit pos zer = refl
b2-trit pos pos = refl

postulate
  split-BвӮӮ :
    (A R X RX Y RY : в„Ө) вҶ’
    (A + R) - (X + RX) - (Y + RY) вүЎ (A - X - Y) + (R - RX - RY)
------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Sanity property for QМӮcore (constructive)

QМӮcore-zero :
  вҲҖ {m : Nat} вҶ’ QМӮcore (vecв„Ө (replicateTrit0 m)) вүЎ + 0
QМӮcore-zero {zero} = refl
QМӮcore-zero {suc m} =
  cong (О» n вҶ’ (+ 0 * + 0) + n) (QМӮcore-zero {m})

BвӮӮв„Ө-zeroL :
  вҲҖ {m : Nat} (x : Vec Trit m) вҶ’
  BвӮӮв„Ө QМӮcore (replicateTrit0 m) x вүЎ + 0
BвӮӮв„Ө-zeroL {m} x =
  begin
    BвӮӮв„Ө QМӮcore (replicateTrit0 m) x
  вүЎвҹЁ refl вҹ©
    (QМӮcore (vecв„Ө (replicateTrit0 m) +бөҘ vecв„Ө x)) - (QМӮcore (vecв„Ө (replicateTrit0 m))) - (QМӮcore (vecв„Ө x))
  вүЎвҹЁ cong (О» v вҶ’ QМӮcore v - QМӮcore (vecв„Ө (replicateTrit0 m)) - QМӮcore (vecв„Ө x))
        (trans (cong (О» t вҶ’ t +бөҘ vecв„Ө x) (vecв„Ө-replicateTrit0 {m}))
               (zeroVecв„Ө+бөҘ (vecв„Ө x))) вҹ©
    (QМӮcore (vecв„Ө x)) - (QМӮcore (vecв„Ө (replicateTrit0 m))) - (QМӮcore (vecв„Ө x))
  вүЎвҹЁ cong (О» z вҶ’ QМӮcore (vecв„Ө x) - z - QМӮcore (vecв„Ө x))
        (QМӮcore-zero {m}) вҹ©
    (QМӮcore (vecв„Ө x)) - (+ 0) - (QМӮcore (vecв„Ө x))
  вүЎвҹЁ refl вҹ©
    (QМӮcore (vecв„Ө x) + (- (+ 0))) + (- QМӮcore (vecв„Ө x))
  вүЎвҹЁ cong (О» t вҶ’ QМӮcore (vecв„Ө x) + t + (- QМӮcore (vecв„Ө x)))
        (refl) вҹ©
    (QМӮcore (vecв„Ө x) + (+ 0)) + (- QМӮcore (vecв„Ө x))
  вүЎвҹЁ cong (О» t вҶ’ t + (- QМӮcore (vecв„Ө x)))
        (IntP.+-identityКі (QМӮcore (vecв„Ө x))) вҹ©
    (QМӮcore (vecв„Ө x)) + (- QМӮcore (vecв„Ө x))
  вүЎвҹЁ IntP.+-inverseКі (QМӮcore (vecв„Ө x)) вҹ©
    + 0
  вҲҺ

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Main target theorem to chase:
-- For QМӮcore(v)=вҲ‘ vбөўВІ we should have:
--   BвӮӮв„Ө QМӮcore x y = 2 * dotв„Ө (vecв„Ө x) (vecв„Ө y)

BвӮӮв„Ө-QМӮcore-dot2 :
  вҲҖ {m : Nat} (x y : Vec Trit m) вҶ’
  BвӮӮв„Ө QМӮcore x y вүЎ ((+ 2) * dotв„Ө (vecв„Ө x) (vecв„Ө y))
BвӮӮв„Ө-QМӮcore-dot2 [] [] =
  begin
    BвӮӮв„Ө QМӮcore [] []
  вүЎвҹЁ refl вҹ©
    + 0
  вүЎвҹЁ sym (IntP.*-zeroКі (+ 2)) вҹ©
    (+ 2) * (+ 0)
  вҲҺ
BвӮӮв„Ө-QМӮcore-dot2 (x вҲ· xs) (y вҲ· ys) =
  begin
    BвӮӮв„Ө QМӮcore (x вҲ· xs) (y вҲ· ys)
  вүЎвҹЁ refl вҹ©
    (QМӮcore ((vecв„Ө (x вҲ· xs)) +бөҘ (vecв„Ө (y вҲ· ys))))
      - (QМӮcore (vecв„Ө (x вҲ· xs)))
      - (QМӮcore (vecв„Ө (y вҲ· ys)))
  вүЎвҹЁ refl вҹ©
    ((intOfTrit x + intOfTrit y) * (intOfTrit x + intOfTrit y)
      + QМӮcore (vecв„Ө xs +бөҘ vecв„Ө ys))
      - ((intOfTrit x * intOfTrit x) + QМӮcore (vecв„Ө xs))
      - ((intOfTrit y * intOfTrit y) + QМӮcore (vecв„Ө ys))
  вүЎвҹЁ split-BвӮӮ
        ((intOfTrit x + intOfTrit y) * (intOfTrit x + intOfTrit y))
        (QМӮcore (vecв„Ө xs +бөҘ vecв„Ө ys))
        (intOfTrit x * intOfTrit x)
        (QМӮcore (vecв„Ө xs))
        (intOfTrit y * intOfTrit y)
        (QМӮcore (vecв„Ө ys)) вҹ©
    ((intOfTrit x + intOfTrit y) * (intOfTrit x + intOfTrit y)
      - (intOfTrit x * intOfTrit x)
      - (intOfTrit y * intOfTrit y))
      + (QМӮcore (vecв„Ө xs +бөҘ vecв„Ө ys) - QМӮcore (vecв„Ө xs) - QМӮcore (vecв„Ө ys))
  вүЎвҹЁ cong (О» t вҶ’ t + (BвӮӮв„Ө QМӮcore xs ys)) (b2-trit x y) вҹ©
    ((+ 2) * (intOfTrit x * intOfTrit y)) + (BвӮӮв„Ө QМӮcore xs ys)
  вүЎвҹЁ cong (О» t вҶ’ ((+ 2) * (intOfTrit x * intOfTrit y)) + t) (BвӮӮв„Ө-QМӮcore-dot2 xs ys) вҹ©
    ((+ 2) * (intOfTrit x * intOfTrit y)) + ((+ 2) * dotв„Ө (vecв„Ө xs) (vecв„Ө ys))
  вүЎвҹЁ sym (IntP.*-distribЛЎ-+ (+ 2) (intOfTrit x * intOfTrit y) (dotв„Ө (vecв„Ө xs) (vecв„Ө ys))) вҹ©
    (+ 2) * ((intOfTrit x * intOfTrit y) + dotв„Ө (vecв„Ө xs) (vecв„Ө ys))
  вҲҺ
  where
    open в„Ө-Reasoning
module DASHI.Physics.OrbitProfileComputedTailPerm where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; _+_)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_вүЎ_; refl; cong)
open import Data.List using (List; []; _вҲ·_; map; filter; length)
open import Relation.Nullary using (Dec; yes; no)
open import Data.Nat.Properties as NatP using (_вүӨ?_)
open import Data.Integer using (в„Ө; +_; -[1+_]; _вүҹ_)
open import Data.Fin using (Fin; zero; suc)

open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (Trit; neg; zer; pos)
open import DASHI.Physics.IndefiniteMaskQuadratic as IMQ
open import DASHI.Physics.OrbitShellPredicate as OSP

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Enumerate all Vec Trit n (3^n)

concat : вҲҖ {A : Set} вҶ’ List (List A) вҶ’ List A
concat [] = []
concat (xs вҲ· xss) = xs ++ concat xss
  where
    _++_ : вҲҖ {A : Set} вҶ’ List A вҶ’ List A вҶ’ List A
    [] ++ ys = ys
    (x вҲ· xs) ++ ys = x вҲ· (xs ++ ys)

concatMap : вҲҖ {A B : Set} вҶ’ (A вҶ’ List B) вҶ’ List A вҶ’ List B
concatMap f xs = concat (map f xs)

allTrit : List Trit
allTrit = neg вҲ· zer вҲ· pos вҲ· []

allVecTrit : вҲҖ (n : Nat) вҶ’ List (Vec Trit n)
allVecTrit zero = [] вҲ· []
allVecTrit (suc n) =
  concatMap
    (О» t вҶ’ map (О» v вҶ’ t вҲ· v) (allVecTrit n))
    allTrit

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Decidable equality for Vec Trit (needed for orbit partitioning)

decEqTrit : (x y : Trit) вҶ’ Dec (x вүЎ y)
decEqTrit neg neg = yes refl
decEqTrit neg zer = no (О» ())
decEqTrit neg pos = no (О» ())
decEqTrit zer neg = no (О» ())
decEqTrit zer zer = yes refl
decEqTrit zer pos = no (О» ())
decEqTrit pos neg = no (О» ())
decEqTrit pos zer = no (О» ())
decEqTrit pos pos = yes refl

decEqVec : вҲҖ {n : Nat} вҶ’ (x y : Vec Trit n) вҶ’ Dec (x вүЎ y)
decEqVec [] [] = yes refl
decEqVec (x вҲ· xs) (y вҲ· ys) with decEqTrit x y
... | no neq = no (О» eq вҶ’ neq (cong head eq))
... | yes refl with decEqVec xs ys
... | no neq = no (О» eq вҶ’ neq (cong tail eq))
... | yes refl = yes refl
  where
    head : вҲҖ {n : Nat} вҶ’ Vec Trit (suc n) вҶ’ Trit
    head (t вҲ· _) = t
    tail : вҲҖ {n : Nat} вҶ’ Vec Trit (suc n) вҶ’ Vec Trit n
    tail (_ вҲ· ts) = ts

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Shell list and orbit sizes

isShell1 : вҲҖ {m : Nat} вҶ’ Vec IMQ.Sign m вҶ’ Vec Trit m вҶ’ Bool
isShell1 Пғ x with IMQ.QПғ Пғ x вүҹ (+ 1)
... | yes _ = true
... | no _ with IMQ.QПғ Пғ x вүҹ -[1+ 0]
... | yes _ = true
... | no _  = false

shell1List : вҲҖ {m : Nat} вҶ’ Vec IMQ.Sign m вҶ’ List (Vec Trit m)
shell1List {m} Пғ = filter (isShell1 Пғ) (allVecTrit m)

member : вҲҖ {A : Set} вҶ’ (A вҶ’ A вҶ’ Dec (A вүЎ A)) вҶ’ A вҶ’ List A вҶ’ Bool
member dec x [] = false
member dec x (y вҲ· ys) with dec x y
... | yes _ = true
... | no _  = member dec x ys

nub : вҲҖ {A : Set} вҶ’ (A вҶ’ A вҶ’ Dec (A вүЎ A)) вҶ’ List A вҶ’ List A
nub dec [] = []
nub dec (x вҲ· xs) with member dec x xs
... | true  = nub dec xs
... | false = x вҲ· nub dec xs

orbitSizes :
  вҲҖ {m k : Nat} вҶ’
  List (TP.Perm k) вҶ’
  List (Vec Trit (m + k)) вҶ’
  List Nat
orbitSizes {m} {k} ps xs =
  map (О» x вҶ’ length (nub decEqVec (map (О» p вҶ’ TP.actTailPerm {m} {k} p x) ps))) xs

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Sort sizes descending (simple insertion sort)

insertDesc : Nat вҶ’ List Nat вҶ’ List Nat
insertDesc x [] = x вҲ· []
insertDesc x (y вҲ· ys) with x NatP.вүӨ? y
... | yes _ = y вҲ· insertDesc x ys
... | no _  = x вҲ· y вҲ· ys

sortDesc : List Nat вҶ’ List Nat
sortDesc [] = []
sortDesc (x вҲ· xs) = insertDesc x (sortDesc xs)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Computed profile under tail permutations

allPerms : (k : Nat) вҶ’ List (TP.Perm k)
allPerms zero = [] вҲ· []
allPerms (suc zero) =
  let f0 : Fin 1
      f0 = zero
  in (f0 вҲ· []) вҲ· []
allPerms (suc (suc (suc (suc zero)))) =
  let
    f0 : Fin 4
    f0 = zero
    f1 : Fin 4
    f1 = suc zero
    f2 : Fin 4
    f2 = suc (suc zero)
    f3 : Fin 4
    f3 = suc (suc (suc zero))

    -- all 24 permutations of [f0,f1,f2,f3]
    p0  = f0 вҲ· f1 вҲ· f2 вҲ· f3 вҲ· []
    p1  = f0 вҲ· f1 вҲ· f3 вҲ· f2 вҲ· []
    p2  = f0 вҲ· f2 вҲ· f1 вҲ· f3 вҲ· []
    p3  = f0 вҲ· f2 вҲ· f3 вҲ· f1 вҲ· []
    p4  = f0 вҲ· f3 вҲ· f1 вҲ· f2 вҲ· []
    p5  = f0 вҲ· f3 вҲ· f2 вҲ· f1 вҲ· []

    p6  = f1 вҲ· f0 вҲ· f2 вҲ· f3 вҲ· []
    p7  = f1 вҲ· f0 вҲ· f3 вҲ· f2 вҲ· []
    p8  = f1 вҲ· f2 вҲ· f0 вҲ· f3 вҲ· []
    p9  = f1 вҲ· f2 вҲ· f3 вҲ· f0 вҲ· []
    p10 = f1 вҲ· f3 вҲ· f0 вҲ· f2 вҲ· []
    p11 = f1 вҲ· f3 вҲ· f2 вҲ· f0 вҲ· []

    p12 = f2 вҲ· f0 вҲ· f1 вҲ· f3 вҲ· []
    p13 = f2 вҲ· f0 вҲ· f3 вҲ· f1 вҲ· []
    p14 = f2 вҲ· f1 вҲ· f0 вҲ· f3 вҲ· []
    p15 = f2 вҲ· f1 вҲ· f3 вҲ· f0 вҲ· []
    p16 = f2 вҲ· f3 вҲ· f0 вҲ· f1 вҲ· []
    p17 = f2 вҲ· f3 вҲ· f1 вҲ· f0 вҲ· []

    p18 = f3 вҲ· f0 вҲ· f1 вҲ· f2 вҲ· []
    p19 = f3 вҲ· f0 вҲ· f2 вҲ· f1 вҲ· []
    p20 = f3 вҲ· f1 вҲ· f0 вҲ· f2 вҲ· []
    p21 = f3 вҲ· f1 вҲ· f2 вҲ· f0 вҲ· []
    p22 = f3 вҲ· f2 вҲ· f0 вҲ· f1 вҲ· []
    p23 = f3 вҲ· f2 вҲ· f1 вҲ· f0 вҲ· []
  in
  p0  вҲ· p1  вҲ· p2  вҲ· p3  вҲ· p4  вҲ· p5  вҲ·
  p6  вҲ· p7  вҲ· p8  вҲ· p9  вҲ· p10 вҲ· p11 вҲ·
  p12 вҲ· p13 вҲ· p14 вҲ· p15 вҲ· p16 вҲ· p17 вҲ·
  p18 вҲ· p19 вҲ· p20 вҲ· p21 вҲ· p22 вҲ· p23 вҲ· []
allPerms _ = []

orbitProfileTailPerm :
  вҲҖ {m k : Nat} вҶ’ Vec IMQ.Sign (m + k) вҶ’ DBA.ShellOrbitProfile (m + k)
orbitProfileTailPerm {m} {k} Пғ =
  let
    shell = shell1List Пғ
    sizes = orbitSizes {m} {k} (allPerms k) shell
  in
  SOPG.profileFromSorted (sortDesc sizes)

module DASHI.Physics.SeverityGuardedStrict where

open import Agda.Primitive using (Level; lsuc)
open import Data.Nat using (в„•; _+_)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_вүЎ_)

open import DASHI.Geometry.LCP.Stream using (Stream; lcpвүҘ)
open import DASHI.Physics.SeverityGuard as SG using (SeverityPolicy; Guard; Broken; Snap)
open import DASHI.Physics.TailCollapseGuardedStrict as TG

-- Adapter: build Guard/Broken/Snap from a SeverityPolicy, while leaving
-- Restore/P/proj abstract for the concrete instance.
record SeverityGuardedStrict {в„“} {A : Set в„“} : Set (lsuc в„“) where
  field
    S : Set в„“
    policy : SG.SeverityPolicy S

    PвӮӣ : S вҶ’ S
    RestoreвӮӣ : S вҶ’ S
    projвӮӣ : S вҶ’ Stream A
    ОәвӮӣ : в„•

    P-strict-onвӮӣ :
      вҲҖ {x y k} вҶ’
      SG.Guard policy x вҶ’ SG.Guard policy y вҶ’
      lcpвүҘ (projвӮӣ x) (projвӮӣ y) k вҶ’
      lcpвүҘ (projвӮӣ (PвӮӣ x)) (projвӮӣ (PвӮӣ y)) (k + ОәвӮӣ)

    restore-normal-formвӮӣ :
      вҲҖ x вҶ’ SG.Broken policy x вҶ’ SG.Guard policy (RestoreвӮӣ x)

    restore-idemвӮӣ :
      вҲҖ x вҶ’ RestoreвӮӣ (RestoreвӮӣ x) вүЎ RestoreвӮӣ x

    restore-fixesвӮӣ :
      вҲҖ x вҶ’ PвӮӣ (RestoreвӮӣ x) вүЎ RestoreвӮӣ x

  toGuardedStrict : TG.GuardedStrictness {A = A}
  toGuardedStrict =
    let p = policy in
    record
      { X = S
      ; P = PвӮӣ
      ; proj = projвӮӣ
      ; Guard = SG.SeverityPolicy.Guard p
      ; Broken = SG.SeverityPolicy.Broken p
      ; Snap = SG.SeverityPolicy.Snap p
      ; Restore = RestoreвӮӣ
    ; Оә = ОәвӮӣ
      ; P-strict-on = О» {x} {y} {k} gx gy hyp вҶ’ P-strict-onвӮӣ {x = x} {y = y} {k = k} gx gy hyp
      ; restore-normal-form = restore-normal-formвӮӣ
      ; restore-idem = restore-idemвӮӣ
      ; restore-fixes = restore-fixesвӮӣ
      }

open SeverityGuardedStrict public
module DASHI.Physics.SignatureClassificationBridge where

  field
    p : Nat
    q : Nat

  (T : S вҶ’ S)
  : SetвӮҒ where
  field
    inv : Involution S
    iso : RIS.RealIsotropy U T

record QuadraticвҮ’Signature : SetвӮҒ where
  field

      вҲҖ {S : Set} {U : UMetric.Ultrametric S} {T : S вҶ’ S} вҶ’
      (out : CQ.QuadraticOutput) вҶ’
      (sym : SymmetryPackage U T) вҶ’
      Signature

  (T : S вҶ’ S)
  : SetвӮҒ where
  field
    cq  : CQ.ContractionвҮ’Quadratic U T
    sym : SymmetryPackage U T

  sig : Signature

module DASHI.Physics.TailCollapseMetricProof where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_вүЎ_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; _+_)
open import Agda.Builtin.Sigma using (ОЈ; _,_)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong; trans)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec; replicate)

open import Ultrametric as UMetric
open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (Trit; zer)

open import DASHI.Metric.FineAgreementUltrametric as FAM

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Tail collapse implies distance-to-neutral is zero

tailCollapse-distance0 :
  вҲҖ (k : Nat) (t : Vec Trit k) вҶ’
  FAM.dNatFine (TCP.iterate k TCP.tailStep t) (replicate k zer) вүЎ 0
tailCollapse-distance0 k t =
  let
    U : UMetric.Ultrametric (Vec Trit k)
    U = FAM.ultrametricVec {n = k}

    open UMetric.Ultrametric U using (id-zero)
  in
  trans
    (cong (О» x вҶ’ FAM.dNatFine x (replicate k zer)) (TCP.tailCollapse k t))
    (id-zero (replicate k zer))

tailCollapse-finiteTime :
  вҲҖ (k : Nat) (t : Vec Trit k) вҶ’
  ОЈ Nat (О» N вҶ’ FAM.dNatFine (TCP.iterate N TCP.tailStep t) (replicate k zer) вүЎ 0)
tailCollapse-finiteTime k t = (k , tailCollapse-distance0 k t)

tailCollapse-fullState-distance0 :
  вҲҖ (m k : Nat) (x : Vec Trit (m + k)) вҶ’
  FAM.dNatFine (TCP.tailOf m k (TCP.iterate k (TCP.TбөЈ {m} {k}) x)) (replicate k zer) вүЎ 0
tailCollapse-fullState-distance0 m k x =
  let
    U : UMetric.Ultrametric (Vec Trit k)
    U = FAM.ultrametricVec {n = k}

    open UMetric.Ultrametric U using (id-zero)
  in
  trans
    (cong (О» y вҶ’ FAM.dNatFine y (replicate k zer)) (TCP.tailOf-after-Tk m k x))
    (id-zero (replicate k zer))

module DASHI.Physics.CanonicalizationMinimal where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_вүЎ_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; _+_)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong; sym; trans; substвӮӮ)

open import Data.Product using (_Г—_; _,_; projвӮҒ; projвӮӮ)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Minimal nontrivial canonicalization on a single Trit

canonTrit : Trit вҶ’ Trit
canonTrit neg = pos
canonTrit zer = zer
canonTrit pos = pos

canonVec : вҲҖ {n : Nat} вҶ’ Vec Trit n вҶ’ Vec Trit n
canonVec = map canonTrit

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Canonicalization on the full state: act only on the coarse core

CбөЈ : вҲҖ {m k : Nat} вҶ’ Vec Trit (m + k) вҶ’ Vec Trit (m + k)
CбөЈ {m} {k} x with TCP.split m k x
... | (c , t) = canonVec c ++ t

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Nonexpansiveness (constructive)

CбөЈ-++ :
  вҲҖ {m k : Nat} (c : Vec Trit m) (t : Vec Trit k) вҶ’
  CбөЈ {m} {k} (c ++ t) вүЎ canonVec c ++ t
CбөЈ-++ {m} {k} c t
  rewrite TCP.split-++ m k c t = refl

nonexpCбөЈ :
  вҲҖ {m k : Nat} вҶ’
  SCC.NonExpansive (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k}) (CбөЈ {m} {k})
nonexpCбөЈ {m} {k} =
  record
    { nonexp = nonexp }
  where
    nonexp : вҲҖ x y вҶ’ UMetric.Ultrametric.d (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k}) (CбөЈ {m} {k} x) (CбөЈ {m} {k} y)
                       вүӨ UMetric.Ultrametric.d (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k}) x y
    nonexp x y =
      let
        p : x вүЎ TCP.coarseOf m k x ++ TCP.tailOf m k x
        p = sym (TCP.merge-split m k x)
        q : y вүЎ TCP.coarseOf m k y ++ TCP.tailOf m k y
        q = sym (TCP.merge-split m k y)
        r : CбөЈ {m} {k} x вүЎ canonVec (TCP.coarseOf m k x) ++ TCP.tailOf m k x
        r = trans (cong (О» v вҶ’ CбөЈ {m} {k} v) p)
                  (CбөЈ-++ (TCP.coarseOf m k x) (TCP.tailOf m k x))
        s : CбөЈ {m} {k} y вүЎ canonVec (TCP.coarseOf m k y) ++ TCP.tailOf m k y
        s = trans (cong (О» v вҶ’ CбөЈ {m} {k} v) q)
                  (CбөЈ-++ (TCP.coarseOf m k y) (TCP.tailOf m k y))
        lhs : FAM.dNatFine (canonVec (TCP.coarseOf m k x) ++ TCP.tailOf m k x)
                            (canonVec (TCP.coarseOf m k y) ++ TCP.tailOf m k y)
              вүӨ FAM.dNatFine (TCP.coarseOf m k x ++ TCP.tailOf m k x)
                             (TCP.coarseOf m k y ++ TCP.tailOf m k y)
        lhs = FAM.dNatFine-++-mapвүӨ
                (TCP.coarseOf m k x) (TCP.coarseOf m k y)
                (TCP.tailOf m k x) (TCP.tailOf m k y)
                canonTrit
        step1 : FAM.dNatFine (CбөЈ {m} {k} x) (CбөЈ {m} {k} y)
                вүӨ FAM.dNatFine (TCP.coarseOf m k x ++ TCP.tailOf m k x)
                               (TCP.coarseOf m k y ++ TCP.tailOf m k y)
        step1 =
          substвӮӮ
            (О» a b вҶ’ FAM.dNatFine a b вүӨ FAM.dNatFine (TCP.coarseOf m k x ++ TCP.tailOf m k x)
                                                     (TCP.coarseOf m k y ++ TCP.tailOf m k y))
            (sym r) (sym s) lhs
        step2 : FAM.dNatFine (TCP.coarseOf m k x ++ TCP.tailOf m k x)
                             (TCP.coarseOf m k y ++ TCP.tailOf m k y)
                             вүЎ FAM.dNatFine x y
        step2 =
          substвӮӮ
            (О» x' y' вҶ’ FAM.dNatFine (TCP.coarseOf m k x ++ TCP.tailOf m k x)
                                   (TCP.coarseOf m k y ++ TCP.tailOf m k y)
                                   вүЎ FAM.dNatFine x' y')
            (sym p) (sym q) refl
      in
      NatP.вүӨ-trans step1 (NatP.вүӨ-reflexive step2)
module DASHI.Physics.MaskedConeStructure where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_вүЎ_)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; suc)
open import Data.Empty using (вҠҘ)
open import Data.Integer using (в„Ө; +_) renaming (_вүӨ_ to _вүӨбөў_; _<_ to _<бөў_)
open import Data.Nat renaming (_вүӨ_ to _вүӨвӮҷ_) hiding (_<_)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Cone predicates

Timelike : вҲҖ {m : Nat} вҶ’ Vec IMQ.Sign m вҶ’ Vec Trit m вҶ’ Set
Timelike Пғ x = (+ 0) <бөў IMQ.QПғ Пғ x

Spacelike : вҲҖ {m : Nat} вҶ’ Vec IMQ.Sign m вҶ’ Vec Trit m вҶ’ Set
Spacelike Пғ x = IMQ.QПғ Пғ x <бөў (+ 0)

Null : вҲҖ {m : Nat} вҶ’ Vec IMQ.Sign m вҶ’ Vec Trit m вҶ’ Set
Null Пғ x = IMQ.QПғ Пғ x вүЎ (+ 0)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Causal structure seam (delta encodes the вҖңdifferenceвҖқ along the order)

record CausalStructure (m : Nat) : SetвӮҒ where
  field
    _вүј_  : Vec Trit m вҶ’ Vec Trit m вҶ’ Set
    delta : Vec Trit m вҶ’ Vec Trit m вҶ’ Vec Trit m

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Cone monotonicity seam:
-- if x вүј y then QПғ(delta x y) вүҘ 0

postulate
  coneMonotone :
    вҲҖ {m : Nat} (Пғ : Vec IMQ.Sign m) (C : CausalStructure m) (x y : Vec Trit m) вҶ’
    CausalStructure._вүј_ C x y вҶ’
    (+ 0) вүӨбөў IMQ.QПғ Пғ (CausalStructure.delta C x y)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Unique time direction seam

TwoTimeLike : вҲҖ {m : Nat} вҶ’ Vec IMQ.Sign m вҶ’ Set
TwoTimeLike Пғ = (suc (suc 0)) вүӨвӮҷ SFM.countMinus Пғ

record UniqueFixedPoint {A : Set} (T : A вҶ’ A) : Set where
  field
    fp : A
    unique : вҲҖ x вҶ’ T x вүЎ x вҶ’ x вүЎ fp

В¬_ : Set вҶ’ Set
В¬ P = P вҶ’ вҠҘ

postulate
  twoTimeLikeвҶ’noUniqueFP :
    вҲҖ {m : Nat} (Пғ : Vec IMQ.Sign m) (T : Vec Trit m вҶ’ Vec Trit m) вҶ’
    TwoTimeLike Пғ вҶ’ В¬ UniqueFixedPoint T

module DASHI.Physics.MaskedOrthogonalSplit where

open import Level using (Level; suc; _вҠ”_)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_вүЎ_)

-- Minimal additive structure.
record Additive {в„“} (S : Set в„“) : Set (suc в„“) where
  field
    _+_ : S вҶ’ S вҶ’ S
    -_  : S вҶ’ S
    0s  : S


-- Bilinear form (abstract; choose в„ҡ/в„қ in instances).
record Bilinear {в„“s в„“r} (S : Set в„“s) (R : Set в„“r) : Set (suc (в„“s вҠ” в„“r)) where
  field
    вҹЁ_,_вҹ© : S вҶ’ S вҶ’ R
    symm  : вҲҖ x y вҶ’ вҹЁ x , y вҹ© вүЎ вҹЁ y , x вҹ©
    0r    : R


-- Quadratic energy from the bilinear form.
record Quadratic {в„“s в„“r} (S : Set в„“s) (R : Set в„“r) : Set (suc (в„“s вҠ” в„“r)) where
  field
    Q     : S вҶ’ R

record AdditiveR {в„“r} (R : Set в„“r) : Set (suc в„“r) where
  field
    _+r_ : R вҶ’ R вҶ’ R

record Projection {в„“} (S : Set в„“) : Set (suc в„“) where
  field
    P    : S вҶ’ S
    idem : вҲҖ x вҶ’ P (P x) вүЎ P x


-- Masked orthogonal split gate: G-self-adjoint projection + orthogonal split.
record MaskedOrthogonalSplit
  {в„“s в„“r}
  {S : Set в„“s} {R : Set в„“r}
  (A : Additive S)
  (B : Bilinear S R)
  (QF : Quadratic S R)
  (AR : AdditiveR R)
  (Pr : Projection S)
  : Set (suc (в„“s вҠ” в„“r)) where
  open Additive A using (_+_; -_; 0s)
  open Bilinear B using (вҹЁ_,_вҹ©; symm; 0r)
  open Quadratic QF using (Q)
  open AdditiveR AR using (_+r_)
  open Projection Pr using (P; idem)

  -- Complement.
  Qc : S вҶ’ S
  Qc x = _+_ x (- (P x))

  field
    -- G-self-adjointness
    selfAdjoint : вҲҖ x y вҶ’ вҹЁ P x , y вҹ© вүЎ вҹЁ x , P y вҹ©

    -- Orthogonality of the split
    orthogonal : вҲҖ x вҶ’ вҹЁ P x , Qc x вҹ© вүЎ 0r

    -- Energy split
    split : вҲҖ x вҶ’ Q x вүЎ (Q (P x) +r Q (Qc x))

open MaskedOrthogonalSplit public
module DASHI.Physics.RealOperatorStackShift where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_вүЎ_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; _+_)
open import DASHI.Physics.TailCollapseProof as TCP

open import Contraction using (_вүў_)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (sym; subst; trans; cong; substвӮӮ)
open import Data.Nat using (_<_; _вүӨ_)
open import Data.Nat.Properties as NatP

C : вҲҖ {m k : Nat} вҶ’ RTC.Carrier (m + k) вҶ’ RTC.Carrier (m + k)
C {m} {k} = CM.CбөЈ {m} {k}

P : вҲҖ {m k : Nat} вҶ’ RTC.Carrier (m + k) вҶ’ RTC.Carrier (m + k)
P {m} {k} = TCP.PбөЈ {m} {k}

R : вҲҖ {m k : Nat} вҶ’ RTC.Carrier (m + k) вҶ’ RTC.Carrier (m + k)
R {m} {k} = TCP.RбөЈ {m} {k}

nonexpC : вҲҖ {m k : Nat} вҶ’ SCC.NonExpansive (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k}) (C {m} {k})
nonexpC {m} {k} = CM.nonexpCбөЈ {m} {k}

nonexpR : вҲҖ {m k : Nat} вҶ’ SCC.NonExpansive (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k}) (R {m} {k})
nonexpR {m} {k} =
  record
    { nonexp = nonexp }
  where
    nonexp : вҲҖ x y вҶ’ UMetric.Ultrametric.d (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k}) (R {m} {k} x) (R {m} {k} y)
                       вүӨ UMetric.Ultrametric.d (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k}) x y
    nonexp x y =
      let
        cx = TCP.coarseOf m k x
        tx = TCP.tailOf m k x
        cy = TCP.coarseOf m k y
        ty = TCP.tailOf m k y
        p : x вүЎ cx ++ tx
        p = sym (TCP.merge-split m k x)
        q : y вүЎ cy ++ ty
        q = sym (TCP.merge-split m k y)
        r : R {m} {k} x вүЎ cx ++ TCP.shiftTail tx
        r = trans (cong (О» v вҶ’ R {m} {k} v) p) (TCP.RбөЈ-++ m k cx tx)
        s : R {m} {k} y вүЎ cy ++ TCP.shiftTail ty
        s = trans (cong (О» v вҶ’ R {m} {k} v) q) (TCP.RбөЈ-++ m k cy ty)
        step : FAM.dNatFine (cx ++ TCP.shiftTail tx) (cy ++ TCP.shiftTail ty)
               вүӨ FAM.dNatFine (cx ++ tx) (cy ++ ty)
        step = FAM.dNatFine-++-shiftTailвүӨ cx cy tx ty
        step1 : FAM.dNatFine (R {m} {k} x) (R {m} {k} y)
                 вүӨ FAM.dNatFine (cx ++ tx) (cy ++ ty)
        step1 =
          substвӮӮ
            (О» a b вҶ’ FAM.dNatFine a b вүӨ FAM.dNatFine (cx ++ tx) (cy ++ ty))
            (sym r) (sym s) step
        step2 : FAM.dNatFine (cx ++ tx) (cy ++ ty) вүЎ FAM.dNatFine x y
        step2 = substвӮӮ
          (О» x' y' вҶ’ FAM.dNatFine (cx ++ tx) (cy ++ ty) вүЎ FAM.dNatFine x' y')
          (sym p) (sym q) refl
      in
      NatP.вүӨ-trans step1 (NatP.вүӨ-reflexive step2)

nonexpP : вҲҖ {m k : Nat} вҶ’ SCC.NonExpansive (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k}) (P {m} {k})
nonexpP {m} {k} =
  record
    { nonexp = nonexp }
  where
    nonexp : вҲҖ x y вҶ’
      UMetric.Ultrametric.d (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k}) (P {m} {k} x) (P {m} {k} y)
        вүӨ UMetric.Ultrametric.d (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k}) x y
    nonexp x y =
      let
        cx = TCP.coarseOf m k x
        tx = TCP.tailOf m k x
        cy = TCP.coarseOf m k y
        ty = TCP.tailOf m k y
        p : x вүЎ cx ++ tx
        p = sym (TCP.merge-split m k x)
        q : y вүЎ cy ++ ty
        q = sym (TCP.merge-split m k y)
        r : P {m} {k} x вүЎ cx ++ TCP.projTail tx
        r = trans (cong (О» v вҶ’ P {m} {k} v) p) (TCP.PбөЈ-++ m k cx tx)
        s : P {m} {k} y вүЎ cy ++ TCP.projTail ty
        s = trans (cong (О» v вҶ’ P {m} {k} v) q) (TCP.PбөЈ-++ m k cy ty)
        step : FAM.dNatFine (cx ++ TCP.projTail tx) (cy ++ TCP.projTail ty)
               вүӨ FAM.dNatFine (cx ++ tx) (cy ++ ty)
        step = FAM.dNatFine-++-projTailвүӨ cx cy tx ty
        step1 : FAM.dNatFine (P {m} {k} x) (P {m} {k} y)
                 вүӨ FAM.dNatFine (cx ++ tx) (cy ++ ty)
        step1 =
          substвӮӮ
            (О» a b вҶ’ FAM.dNatFine a b вүӨ FAM.dNatFine (cx ++ tx) (cy ++ ty))
            (sym r) (sym s) step
        step2 : FAM.dNatFine (cx ++ tx) (cy ++ ty) вүЎ FAM.dNatFine x y
        step2 = substвӮӮ
          (О» x' y' вҶ’ FAM.dNatFine (cx ++ tx) (cy ++ ty) вүЎ FAM.dNatFine x' y')
          (sym p) (sym q) refl
      in
      NatP.вүӨ-trans step1 (NatP.вүӨ-reflexive step2)

strictP-fiber :
  вҲҖ {m k : Nat} вҶ’
  FC.ContractiveOnFibers (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k}) (P {m} {k})
strictP-fiber {m} {k} =
  record
    { contractFiber = О» {x} {y} fd вҶ’
        let
          open UMetric.Ultrametric (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k})
          open FC.FiberDistinct fd using (xвүўy; sameFiber)
          d0 : d (P {m} {k} x) (P {m} {k} y) вүЎ 0
          d0 = subst (О» z вҶ’ d (P {m} {k} x) z вүЎ 0) sameFiber (id-zero (P {m} {k} x))
        in
        subst (О» u вҶ’ u < d x y) (sym d0) (FAM.dNatFine-positive xвүўy)
    }
module DASHI.Physics.QuadraticCore where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_вүЎ_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; _+_)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong; trans; sym)

open import Data.Vec using (Vec; []; _вҲ·_; _++_; map)
open import Data.Product using (projвӮҒ; projвӮӮ)

open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (Trit; neg; zer; pos)
open import DASHI.Physics.TailCollapseProof as TCP
open import DASHI.Physics.CanonicalizationMinimal as CM

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Quadratic вҖңenergyвҖқ density per trit: squares of {-1,0,+1}
-- Encoded directly as Nat: 1 for Вұ, 0 for 0.

sqTrit : Trit вҶ’ Nat
sqTrit neg = 1
sqTrit zer = 0
sqTrit pos = 1

sumNat : вҲҖ {m : Nat} вҶ’ Vec Nat m вҶ’ Nat
sumNat [] = 0
sumNat (x вҲ· xs) = x + sumNat xs

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Quadratic invariant on the core: sum of squares

Qcore : вҲҖ {m : Nat} вҶ’ Vec Trit m вҶ’ Nat
Qcore c = sumNat (map sqTrit c)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Canonicalization preserves squares pointwise

sq-canon : вҲҖ t вҶ’ sqTrit (CM.canonTrit t) вүЎ sqTrit t
sq-canon neg = refl
sq-canon zer = refl
sq-canon pos = refl

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Qcore invariance under canonVec

Qcore-canonVec : вҲҖ {m : Nat} (c : Vec Trit m) вҶ’ Qcore (CM.canonVec c) вүЎ Qcore c
Qcore-canonVec [] = refl
Qcore-canonVec (t вҲ· ts)
  rewrite sq-canon t
  = cong (О» n вҶ’ sqTrit t + n) (Qcore-canonVec ts)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Lift Qcore to the full state via the coarse split

Qfull : вҲҖ {m k : Nat} вҶ’ Vec Trit (m + k) вҶ’ Nat
Qfull {m} {k} x = Qcore (TCP.coarseOf m k x)

Qfull-invariant-CбөЈ :
  вҲҖ {m k : Nat} (x : Vec Trit (m + k)) вҶ’
  Qfull {m} {k} (CM.CбөЈ {m} {k} x) вүЎ Qfull {m} {k} x
Qfull-invariant-CбөЈ {m} {k} x with TCP.split m k x
... | p
  rewrite TCP.split-++ m k (CM.canonVec (projвӮҒ p)) (projвӮӮ p)
        | TCP.split-++ m k (projвӮҒ p) (projвӮӮ p)
  = Qcore-canonVec (projвӮҒ p)

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_вүЎ_)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat)
open import Data.Unit using (вҠӨ)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Abstract вҖңdiscrete geometryвҖқ interface for the Einstein gate
------------------------------------------------------------------------

record DiscreteManifoldLike (V : Set) : SetвӮҒ where

    Metric    : Set
    Tensor2   : Set
    Scalar    : Set
    Laplacian : Scalar вҶ’ Scalar

    вҲҖ {Dim : Nat} {V : Set} вҶ’
    DiscreteManifoldLike V вҶ’ Set

open import Data.Product using (_Г—_; ОЈ; _,_)

module DASHI.Physics.Cone.ArrowSeparatedDeltaConeSplitShift where

open import Level using (Level; suc; _вҠ”_) renaming (zero to lzero)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; _+_; zero)
open import Data.Nat using (_вүӨ_; _вҲё_)
open import Data.Product using (_,_)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec)
open import Data.Integer using (в„Ө; +_) renaming (_вүӨ_ to _вүӨбөў_)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_вүЎ_)

open import DASHI.Physics.Cone.ArrowSeparatedDeltaCone as ASD
open import DASHI.Physics.Cone.ArrowSeparatedDeltaConeSplit as ADSplit
open import DASHI.Physics.MaskedOrthogonalSplit as MOS
open import DASHI.Physics.TailCollapseProof as TCP
open import DASHI.Physics.IndefiniteMaskQuadratic as IMQ
open import DASHI.Physics.RealTernaryCarrier as RTC
open import DASHI.Physics.Closure.MDLTradeoffShiftInstance as MSI

private
  S : вҲҖ {m k : Nat} вҶ’ Set
  S {m} {k} = RTC.Carrier (m + k)

  arrow : вҲҖ {m k : Nat} вҶ’ S {m} {k} вҶ’ Nat
  arrow {m} {k} x = MSI.countNZ (TCP.tailOf m k x)

  splitS : вҲҖ {m k : Nat} вҶ’ ASD.ArrowSplit {в„“s = _} {в„“a = _} {в„“x = _}
  splitS {m} {k} = record
    { State = S {m} {k}
    ; Shape = S {m} {k}
    ; Arrow = Nat
    ; split = О» x вҶ’ x , arrow {m} {k} x
    }

  Оҙ : вҲҖ {m k : Nat} вҶ’ ASD.ArrowDelta (ASD.Shape (splitS {m} {k})) (ASD.Arrow (splitS {m} {k}))
  Оҙ {m} {k} = record
    { О”Shape = О» x' _ вҶ’ x'
    ; О”Arrow = О» a' a вҶ’ a вҲё a'
    }

  forward : вҲҖ {m k : Nat} вҶ’ ASD.ForwardPred (ASD.Arrow (splitS {m} {k}))
  forward {m} {k} = record
    { Forward = О» d вҶ’ zero вүӨ d
    }

  cone : вҲҖ {m k : Nat} (Пғ : Vec IMQ.Sign (m + k)) вҶ’ ASD.ConeScreen (ASD.Shape (splitS {m} {k}))
  cone {m} {k} Пғ = record
    { Cone = О» s вҶ’ (+ 0) вүӨбөў IMQ.QПғ Пғ s
    }

-- Concrete wiring to the shift step; split/forward/cone are fixed by ADS.
record ShiftArrowSeparatedConeSplit
  {в„“r : Level}
  {m k : Nat}
  (Пғ : Vec IMQ.Sign (m + k))
  (R : Set в„“r)
  (A : MOS.Additive (S {m} {k}))
  (B : MOS.Bilinear (S {m} {k}) R)
  (QF : MOS.Quadratic (S {m} {k}) R)
  (AR : MOS.AdditiveR R)
  (Pr : MOS.Projection (S {m} {k}))
  (SC : ADSplit.SplitCone (S {m} {k}))
  : Set (suc в„“r вҠ” suc lzero) where
  field
    coneSplitKit : ADSplit.ArrowSeparatedConeSplit
      (splitS {m} {k})
      R
      (Оҙ {m} {k})
      (forward {m} {k})
      (cone {m} {k} Пғ)
      (О» x y вҶ’ y вүЎ TCP.TбөЈ {m} {k} x)
      A B QF AR Pr SC

open ShiftArrowSeparatedConeSplit public
module DASHI.Physics.Cone.ArrowSeparatedDeltaConeSplit where

open import Level using (Level; _вҠ”_; suc)
open import Data.Product using (_Г—_; _,_; projвӮҒ)

open import DASHI.Physics.Cone.ArrowSeparatedDeltaCone as ASD
open import DASHI.Physics.MaskedOrthogonalSplit as MOS

record SplitCone {в„“s} (Shape : Set в„“s) : Set (suc в„“s) where
  field
    ConeP : Shape вҶ’ Set в„“s
    ConeQ : Shape вҶ’ Set в„“s

open SplitCone public

-- Bridge: forward steps вҮ’ cone on О”s, and cone on О”s вҮ’ cone on split parts.
record ArrowSeparatedConeSplit
  {в„“s в„“a в„“x в„“r}
  (Split : ASD.ArrowSplit {в„“s} {в„“a} {в„“x})
  (R : Set в„“r)
  (О” : ASD.ArrowDelta (ASD.Shape Split) (ASD.Arrow Split))
  (Fwd : ASD.ForwardPred (ASD.Arrow Split))
  (Cone : ASD.ConeScreen (ASD.Shape Split))
  (Step : ASD.State Split вҶ’ ASD.State Split вҶ’ Set)
  (A : MOS.Additive (ASD.Shape Split))
  (B : MOS.Bilinear (ASD.Shape Split) R)
  (QF : MOS.Quadratic (ASD.Shape Split) R)
  (AR : MOS.AdditiveR R)
  (Pr : MOS.Projection (ASD.Shape Split))
  (SC : SplitCone (ASD.Shape Split))
  : Set (suc (в„“s вҠ” в„“a вҠ” в„“x вҠ” в„“r)) where
  field
    -- Base arrow-separated cone lemma.
    deltaCone : ASD.ArrowSeparatedDeltaCone Split О” Fwd Cone Step

    -- Orthogonal split gate for shape deltas.
    splitGate : MOS.MaskedOrthogonalSplit A B QF AR Pr

    -- If the full О”s is in the cone, both split components are cone-compatible.
    coneSplit :
      вҲҖ {x x'} вҶ’
      ASD.ConeStep Split О” Cone x x' вҶ’
      let ds = ASD.О”Shape О” (projвӮҒ (ASD.split Split x')) (projвӮҒ (ASD.split Split x))
      in (SplitCone.ConeP SC (MOS.Projection.P Pr ds)) Г—
         (SplitCone.ConeQ SC (MOS.MaskedOrthogonalSplit.Qc splitGate ds))

open ArrowSeparatedConeSplit public

-- Derived: forward step implies split cone predicates.
forwardConeSplit :
  вҲҖ {в„“s в„“a в„“x в„“r}
  {Split : ASD.ArrowSplit {в„“s} {в„“a} {в„“x}}
  {R : Set в„“r}
  {О” : ASD.ArrowDelta (ASD.Shape Split) (ASD.Arrow Split)}
  {Fwd : ASD.ForwardPred (ASD.Arrow Split)}
  {Cone : ASD.ConeScreen (ASD.Shape Split)}
  {Step : ASD.State Split вҶ’ ASD.State Split вҶ’ Set}
  {A : MOS.Additive (ASD.Shape Split)}
  {B : MOS.Bilinear (ASD.Shape Split) R}
  {QF : MOS.Quadratic (ASD.Shape Split) R}
  {AR : MOS.AdditiveR R}
  {Pr : MOS.Projection (ASD.Shape Split)}
  {SC : SplitCone (ASD.Shape Split)}
  вҶ’ (kit : ArrowSeparatedConeSplit Split R О” Fwd Cone Step A B QF AR Pr SC)
  вҶ’ вҲҖ {x x'} вҶ’ Step x x' вҶ’ ASD.ForwardStep Split О” Fwd x x'
  вҶ’ let ds = ASD.О”Shape О” (projвӮҒ (ASD.split Split x')) (projвӮҒ (ASD.split Split x))
        sg = ArrowSeparatedConeSplit.splitGate kit
    in (SplitCone.ConeP SC (MOS.Projection.P Pr ds)) Г—
       (SplitCone.ConeQ SC (MOS.MaskedOrthogonalSplit.Qc sg ds))
forwardConeSplit kit st fw =
  ArrowSeparatedConeSplit.coneSplit kit
    (ASD.ArrowSeparatedDeltaCone.forwardвҮ’cone (ArrowSeparatedConeSplit.deltaCone kit) st fw)
module DASHI.Physics.Cone.ArrowSeparatedDeltaConeShift where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; _+_; zero)
open import Data.Nat using (_вүӨ_; _вҲё_; zвүӨn)
open import Data.Integer using (в„Ө; +_) renaming (_вүӨ_ to _вүӨбөў_)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec)
open import Data.Product using (_,_)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_вүЎ_; subst)

open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (Trit)
open import DASHI.Physics.RealTernaryCarrier as RTC
open import DASHI.Physics.TailCollapseProof as TCP
open import DASHI.Physics.Closure.MDLTradeoffShiftInstance as MSI
open import DASHI.Physics.IndefiniteMaskQuadratic as IMQ
import DASHI.Physics.Cone.ArrowSeparatedDeltaCone as ASD

private
  S : вҲҖ {m k : Nat} вҶ’ Set
  S {m} {k} = RTC.Carrier (m + k)

  arrow : вҲҖ {m k : Nat} вҶ’ S {m} {k} вҶ’ Nat
  arrow {m} {k} x = MSI.countNZ (TCP.tailOf m k x)

  splitS : вҲҖ {m k : Nat} вҶ’ ASD.ArrowSplit {в„“s = _} {в„“a = _} {в„“x = _}
  splitS {m} {k} = record
    { State = S {m} {k}
    ; Shape = S {m} {k}
    ; Arrow = Nat
    ; split = О» x вҶ’ x , arrow {m} {k} x
    }

  Оҙ : вҲҖ {m k : Nat} вҶ’ ASD.ArrowDelta (ASD.Shape (splitS {m} {k})) (ASD.Arrow (splitS {m} {k}))
  Оҙ {m} {k} = record
    { О”Shape = О» x' _ вҶ’ x'
    ; О”Arrow = О» a' a вҶ’ a вҲё a'
    }

  forward : вҲҖ {m k : Nat} вҶ’ ASD.ForwardPred (ASD.Arrow (splitS {m} {k}))
  forward {m} {k} = record
    { Forward = О» d вҶ’ zero вүӨ d
    }

  cone : вҲҖ {m k : Nat} (Пғ : Vec IMQ.Sign (m + k)) вҶ’ ASD.ConeScreen (ASD.Shape (splitS {m} {k}))
  cone {m} {k} Пғ = record
    { Cone = О» s вҶ’ (+ 0) вүӨбөў IMQ.QПғ Пғ s
    }

record ShiftArrowSeparatedDeltaCone {m k : Nat} (Пғ : Vec IMQ.Sign (m + k)) : SetвӮҒ where
  field
    stepвҮ’forward : вҲҖ {x} вҶ’ ASD.ForwardStep (splitS {m} {k}) (Оҙ {m} {k}) (forward {m} {k}) x (TCP.TбөЈ {m} {k} x)
    forwardвҮ’cone : вҲҖ {x} вҶ’
      ASD.ForwardStep (splitS {m} {k}) (Оҙ {m} {k}) (forward {m} {k}) x (TCP.TбөЈ {m} {k} x) вҶ’
      ASD.ConeStep (splitS {m} {k}) (Оҙ {m} {k}) (cone {m} {k} Пғ) x (TCP.TбөЈ {m} {k} x)

  kit : ASD.ArrowSeparatedDeltaCone (splitS {m} {k}) (Оҙ {m} {k}) (forward {m} {k}) (cone {m} {k} Пғ) (О» x y вҶ’ y вүЎ TCP.TбөЈ {m} {k} x)
  kit = record
    { stepвҮ’forward = stepForward
    ; forwardвҮ’cone = coneForward
    }
    where
      stepForward :
        вҲҖ {x y} вҶ’ y вүЎ TCP.TбөЈ {m} {k} x вҶ’
        ASD.ForwardStep (splitS {m} {k}) (Оҙ {m} {k}) (forward {m} {k}) x y
      stepForward {x} {y} eq rewrite eq = stepвҮ’forward {x}

      coneForward :
        вҲҖ {x y} вҶ’ y вүЎ TCP.TбөЈ {m} {k} x вҶ’
        ASD.ForwardStep (splitS {m} {k}) (Оҙ {m} {k}) (forward {m} {k}) x y вҶ’
        ASD.ConeStep (splitS {m} {k}) (Оҙ {m} {k}) (cone {m} {k} Пғ) x y
      coneForward {x} {y} eq fw rewrite eq = forwardвҮ’cone {x} fw

open ShiftArrowSeparatedDeltaCone public
module DASHI.Physics.Cone.ArrowSeparatedDeltaCone where

open import Level using (Level; _вҠ”_; zero; suc)
open import Data.Product using (_Г—_; _,_; projвӮҒ; projвӮӮ)

-- Abstract split of state into (shape, arrow)
record ArrowSplit {в„“s в„“a в„“x : Level} : Set (suc (в„“s вҠ” в„“a вҠ” в„“x)) where
  field
    State : Set в„“x
    Shape : Set в„“s
    Arrow : Set в„“a
    split : State вҶ’ Shape Г— Arrow

open ArrowSplit public

-- Difference operations for shape and arrow components.
record ArrowDelta {в„“s в„“a : Level} (Shape : Set в„“s) (Arrow : Set в„“a)
  : Set (suc (в„“s вҠ” в„“a)) where
  field
    О”Shape : Shape вҶ’ Shape вҶ’ Shape
    О”Arrow : Arrow вҶ’ Arrow вҶ’ Arrow

open ArrowDelta public

-- Forwardness predicate is only about arrow deltas.
record ForwardPred {в„“a : Level} (Arrow : Set в„“a) : Set (suc в„“a) where
  field
    Forward : Arrow вҶ’ Set в„“a

open ForwardPred public

-- Cone screen only depends on shape deltas.
record ConeScreen {в„“s : Level} (Shape : Set в„“s) : Set (suc в„“s) where
  field
    Cone : Shape вҶ’ Set в„“s

open ConeScreen public

-- Derived step predicates.
ForwardStep :
  вҲҖ {в„“s в„“a в„“x}
  (S : ArrowSplit {в„“s} {в„“a} {в„“x})
  (D : ArrowDelta (Shape S) (Arrow S))
  (F : ForwardPred (Arrow S))
  вҶ’ State S вҶ’ State S вҶ’ Set в„“a
ForwardStep S D F x x' =
  Forward F (О”Arrow D (projвӮӮ (split S x')) (projвӮӮ (split S x)))

ConeStep :
  вҲҖ {в„“s в„“a в„“x}
  (S : ArrowSplit {в„“s} {в„“a} {в„“x})
  (D : ArrowDelta (Shape S) (Arrow S))
  (C : ConeScreen (Shape S))
  вҶ’ State S вҶ’ State S вҶ’ Set в„“s
ConeStep S D C x x' =
  Cone C (О”Shape D (projвӮҒ (split S x')) (projвӮҒ (split S x)))

-- Keystone lemma: forward step implies cone screen on shape delta.
record ArrowSeparatedDeltaCone
  {в„“s в„“a в„“x}
  (S : ArrowSplit {в„“s} {в„“a} {в„“x})
  (D : ArrowDelta (Shape S) (Arrow S))
  (F : ForwardPred (Arrow S))
  (C : ConeScreen (Shape S))
  (Step : State S вҶ’ State S вҶ’ Set)
  : Set (suc (в„“s вҠ” в„“a вҠ” в„“x)) where
  field
    stepвҮ’forward : вҲҖ {x x'} вҶ’ Step x x' вҶ’ ForwardStep S D F x x'
    forwardвҮ’cone : вҲҖ {x x'} вҶ’ Step x x' вҶ’ ForwardStep S D F x x' вҶ’ ConeStep S D C x x'

open ArrowSeparatedDeltaCone public

-- Convenience: cone-compatibility predicate on steps.
ConeCompatibleStep :
  вҲҖ {в„“s в„“a в„“x}
  (S : ArrowSplit {в„“s} {в„“a} {в„“x})
  (D : ArrowDelta (Shape S) (Arrow S))
  (F : ForwardPred (Arrow S))
  (C : ConeScreen (Shape S))
  вҶ’ State S вҶ’ State S вҶ’ Set (в„“s вҠ” в„“a)
ConeCompatibleStep S D F C x x' = ForwardStep S D F x x' вҶ’ ConeStep S D C x x'

coneCompatibleFromKit :
  вҲҖ {в„“s в„“a в„“x}
  {S : ArrowSplit {в„“s} {в„“a} {в„“x}}
  {D : ArrowDelta (Shape S) (Arrow S)}
  {F : ForwardPred (Arrow S)}
  {C : ConeScreen (Shape S)}
  {Step : State S вҶ’ State S вҶ’ Set}
  вҶ’ ArrowSeparatedDeltaCone S D F C Step
  вҶ’ вҲҖ {x x'} вҶ’ Step x x' вҶ’ ConeCompatibleStep S D F C x x'
coneCompatibleFromKit kit st fw = forwardвҮ’cone kit st fw
module DASHI.Physics.OrbitShellPredicate where

open import Data.Integer using (в„Ө; +_; -[1+_])
open import Data.Sum using (_вҠҺ_; injвӮҒ; injвӮӮ)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec)

open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (Trit)
open import DASHI.Physics.IndefiniteMaskQuadratic as IMQ

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Shell predicate: |QПғ(x)| = 1 (encoded as QПғ = +1 or QПғ = -1)

Shell1 : вҲҖ {m : Nat} вҶ’ Vec IMQ.Sign m вҶ’ Vec Trit m вҶ’ Set
Shell1 Пғ x =
  (IMQ.QПғ Пғ x вүЎ (+ 1)) вҠҺ (IMQ.QПғ Пғ x вүЎ -[1+ 0 ])

module DASHI.Physics.ClosureStatusFromGlue where

module DASHI.Physics.RealConeInteriorInstanceShift where
