module DASHI.Physics.ClosureInstance where

open import DASHI.Physics.ClosureGlue as Glue
open import DASHI.Physics.TOperator
open import DASHI.Geometry.RealFiniteSpeed
open import DASHI.Geometry.RealIsotropy
open import Contraction
open import Ultrametric as UMetric
open import DASHI.Combinatorics.Entropy using (Involution)

-- Bundle real (non-toy) closure data.
record RealClosureInstance : SetвӮҒ where
  field
    S   : Set
    U   : UMetric.Ultrametric S
    op  : TOperator S
    sc  : StrictContraction U (TOperator.T op)
    inv : Involution S
    iso : RealIsotropy U (TOperator.T op)
    fs  : RealFiniteSpeed (TOperator.T op)

-- Convert real closure instance into the common ClosureAxioms.
toClosureAxioms : RealClosureInstance вҶ’ Glue.ClosureAxioms
toClosureAxioms inst =
  record
    { S   = RealClosureInstance.S inst
    ; U   = RealClosureInstance.U inst
    ; T   = TOperator.T (RealClosureInstance.op inst)
    ; sc  = RealClosureInstance.sc inst
    ; inv = RealClosureInstance.inv inst
    ; iso = RealIsotropy.iso (RealClosureInstance.iso inst)
    ; fs  = record
        { local = RealFiniteSpeed.local (RealClosureInstance.fs inst)
        ; preservesLocality = RealFiniteSpeed.preservesLocality (RealClosureInstance.fs inst)
        }
    }

module DASHI.Physics.ShellOrbitProfileGenerator where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc)
open import Data.List using (List; []; _вҲ·_; length)

open import DASHI.Physics.DimensionBoundAssumptions as DBA

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Build a ShellOrbitProfile from a sorted (descending) list of orbit sizes.
-- This keeps the generator concrete while still allowing external data.
------------------------------------------------------------------------

profileFromSorted :
  вҲҖ {m : Nat} вҶ’ List Nat вҶ’ DBA.ShellOrbitProfile m
profileFromSorted {m} sizes =
  let
    top1 : Nat
    top1 with sizes
    ... | a вҲ· _ = a
    ... | []    = 0

    top2 : Nat
    top2 with sizes
    ... | _ вҲ· b вҲ· _ = b
    ... | _         = 0

    top3 : Nat
    top3 with sizes
    ... | _ вҲ· _ вҲ· c вҲ· _ = c
    ... | _             = 0
  in
  record
    { orbitCount = length sizes
    ; top1 = top1
    ; top2 = top2
    ; top3 = top3
    }
module DASHI.Physics.TailCollapseProof where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_вүЎ_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc; _+_)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong; sym; trans)
open import Data.Product using (_Г—_; _,_; projвӮҒ; projвӮӮ)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec; []; _вҲ·_; _++_; replicate)
open import Data.Vec.Base using (take; init; last; _вҲ·Кі_)
open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (Trit; zer)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- A concrete, nontrivial renormalization RбөЈ implementing a вҖңscale shiftвҖқ
------------------------------------------------------------------------

split :
  вҲҖ {A : Set} (m k : Nat) вҶ’
  Vec A (m + k) вҶ’ (Vec A m Г— Vec A k)
split {A} zero    k xs       = ([] , xs)
split {A} (suc m) k (x вҲ· xs) with split {A} m k xs
... | (c , t) = (x вҲ· c , t)

split-++ :
  вҲҖ {A : Set} (m k : Nat) (c : Vec A m) (t : Vec A k) вҶ’
  split m k (c ++ t) вүЎ (c , t)
split-++ zero k [] t = refl
split-++ (suc m) k (x вҲ· xs) t =
  cong (О» p вҶ’ (x вҲ· projвӮҒ p , projвӮӮ p)) (split-++ m k xs t)

coarseOf : вҲҖ {A : Set} (m k : Nat) вҶ’ Vec A (m + k) вҶ’ Vec A m
coarseOf m k x = projвӮҒ (split m k x)

tailOf : вҲҖ {A : Set} (m k : Nat) вҶ’ Vec A (m + k) вҶ’ Vec A k
tailOf m k x = projвӮӮ (split m k x)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Tail-band operators

shiftTail : вҲҖ {k : Nat} вҶ’ Vec Trit k вҶ’ Vec Trit k
shiftTail {zero}    []       = []
shiftTail {suc kвҖІ}  (x вҲ· xs) = xs вҲ·Кі zer

projTail : вҲҖ {k : Nat} вҶ’ Vec Trit k вҶ’ Vec Trit k
projTail {zero}    []       = []
projTail {suc kвҖІ}  t        = (init t) вҲ·Кі zer


tailStep : вҲҖ {k : Nat} вҶ’ Vec Trit k вҶ’ Vec Trit k
tailStep t = projTail (shiftTail t)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Lift tail-band operators to full state

RбөЈ : вҲҖ {m k : Nat} вҶ’ Vec Trit (m + k) вҶ’ Vec Trit (m + k)
RбөЈ {m} {k} x with split m k x
... | (c , t) = c ++ shiftTail t

PбөЈ : вҲҖ {m k : Nat} вҶ’ Vec Trit (m + k) вҶ’ Vec Trit (m + k)
PбөЈ {m} {k} x with split m k x
... | (c , t) = c ++ projTail t

RбөЈ-++ :
  вҲҖ (m k : Nat) (c : Vec Trit m) (t : Vec Trit k) вҶ’
  RбөЈ {m} {k} (c ++ t) вүЎ c ++ shiftTail t
RбөЈ-++ m k c t rewrite split-++ m k c t = refl

PбөЈ-++ :
  вҲҖ (m k : Nat) (c : Vec Trit m) (t : Vec Trit k) вҶ’
  PбөЈ {m} {k} (c ++ t) вүЎ c ++ projTail t
PбөЈ-++ m k c t rewrite split-++ m k c t = refl


TбөЈ : вҲҖ {m k : Nat} вҶ’ Vec Trit (m + k) вҶ’ Vec Trit (m + k)
TбөЈ {m} {k} x = PбөЈ {m} {k} (RбөЈ {m} {k} x)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Iteration

iterate : вҲҖ {A : Set} вҶ’ Nat вҶ’ (A вҶ’ A) вҶ’ A вҶ’ A
iterate zero    f x = x
iterate (suc n) f x = iterate n f (f x)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Finite-time tail collapse

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Helper lemmas for replicate

init-replicate :
  вҲҖ {k : Nat} вҶ’ init (replicate (suc k) zer) вүЎ replicate k zer
init-replicate {zero} = refl
init-replicate {suc k} =
  cong (О» t вҶ’ zer вҲ· t) (init-replicate {k})

snoc-replicate :
  вҲҖ {k : Nat} вҶ’ (replicate k zer) вҲ·Кі zer вүЎ replicate (suc k) zer
snoc-replicate {zero} = refl
snoc-replicate {suc k} =
  cong (О» t вҶ’ zer вҲ· t) (snoc-replicate {k})

tailStep-forgets-last :
  вҲҖ {kвҖІ : Nat} (t : Vec Trit (suc kвҖІ)) вҶ’
  tailStep t вүЎ projTail (shiftTail t)
tailStep-forgets-last {kвҖІ} t = refl

projTail-replicate :
  вҲҖ {k : Nat} вҶ’ projTail (replicate k zer) вүЎ replicate k zer
projTail-replicate {zero}    = refl
projTail-replicate {suc kвҖІ}  =
  trans
    (cong (_вҲ·Кі zer) (init-replicate {kвҖІ}))
    (snoc-replicate {kвҖІ})

shiftTail-replicate :
  вҲҖ {k : Nat} вҶ’ shiftTail (replicate k zer) вүЎ replicate k zer
shiftTail-replicate {zero}   = refl
shiftTail-replicate {suc kвҖІ} =
  snoc-replicate {kвҖІ}

tailStep-replicate :
  вҲҖ {k : Nat} вҶ’ tailStep (replicate k zer) вүЎ replicate k zer
tailStep-replicate {k} =
  trans (cong projTail (shiftTail-replicate {k}))
        (projTail-replicate {k})

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Extra Vec lemmas needed for constructive nilpotence
------------------------------------------------------------------------

pair-О· : вҲҖ {A B : Set} (p : A Г— B) вҶ’ (projвӮҒ p , projвӮӮ p) вүЎ p
pair-О· (a , b) = refl

init-вҲ·Кі : вҲҖ {A : Set} {n : Nat} (xs : Vec A n) (a : A) вҶ’ init (xs вҲ·Кі a) вүЎ xs
init-вҲ·Кі {n = zero}    []       a = refl
init-вҲ·Кі {n = suc n} (x вҲ· xs) a rewrite init-вҲ·Кі xs a = refl

projTail-idem :
  вҲҖ {k : Nat} (t : Vec Trit k) вҶ’ projTail (projTail t) вүЎ projTail t
projTail-idem {zero} [] = refl
projTail-idem {suc kвҖІ} t =
  trans
    (cong (_вҲ·Кі zer) (init-вҲ·Кі (init t) zer))
    refl

PбөЈ-idem :
  вҲҖ (m k : Nat) (x : Vec Trit (m + k)) вҶ’
  PбөЈ {m} {k} (PбөЈ {m} {k} x) вүЎ PбөЈ {m} {k} x
PбөЈ-idem m k x with split m k x
... | (c , t)
  rewrite PбөЈ-++ m k c t
        | PбөЈ-++ m k c (projTail t)
        | projTail-idem t
  = refl

tailStepвүЎshiftTail : вҲҖ {k : Nat} (t : Vec Trit k) вҶ’ tailStep t вүЎ shiftTail t
tailStepвүЎshiftTail {zero}    [] = refl
tailStepвүЎshiftTail {suc kвҖІ} (x вҲ· xs)
  rewrite init-вҲ·Кі xs zer
  = refl

shiftTail-вҲ·Кі-zer :
  вҲҖ {k : Nat} (xs : Vec Trit k) вҶ’
  shiftTail (xs вҲ·Кі zer) вүЎ (shiftTail xs) вҲ·Кі zer
shiftTail-вҲ·Кі-zer {zero} [] = refl
shiftTail-вҲ·Кі-zer {suc k} (x вҲ· xs) = refl

iterate-shiftTail-вҲ·Кі-zer :
  вҲҖ {k : Nat} (n : Nat) (xs : Vec Trit k) вҶ’
  iterate n shiftTail (xs вҲ·Кі zer) вүЎ (iterate n shiftTail xs) вҲ·Кі zer
iterate-shiftTail-вҲ·Кі-zer zero xs = refl
iterate-shiftTail-вҲ·Кі-zer (suc n) xs
  rewrite shiftTail-вҲ·Кі-zer xs
        | iterate-shiftTail-вҲ·Кі-zer n (shiftTail xs)
  = refl

iterate-pointwise :
  вҲҖ {A : Set} (n : Nat) (f g : A вҶ’ A) (x : A) вҶ’
  (вҲҖ y вҶ’ f y вүЎ g y) вҶ’
  iterate n f x вүЎ iterate n g x
iterate-pointwise zero f g x fg = refl
iterate-pointwise (suc n) f g x fg
  rewrite fg x
  = iterate-pointwise n f g (g x) fg

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Finite-time tail collapse (constructive)
------------------------------------------------------------------------

tailCollapse-shiftTail :
  вҲҖ (k : Nat) (t : Vec Trit k) вҶ’
  iterate k shiftTail t вүЎ replicate k zer
tailCollapse-shiftTail zero    []       = refl
tailCollapse-shiftTail (suc k) (x вҲ· xs) =
  trans
    (iterate-shiftTail-вҲ·Кі-zer k xs)
    (trans
      (cong (_вҲ·Кі zer) (tailCollapse-shiftTail k xs))
      (snoc-replicate {k}))

tailCollapse :
  вҲҖ (k : Nat) (t : Vec Trit k) вҶ’
  iterate k tailStep t вүЎ replicate k zer
tailCollapse k t =
  trans
    (iterate-pointwise k tailStep shiftTail t (О» y вҶ’ tailStepвүЎshiftTail y))
    (tailCollapse-shiftTail k t)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Lifted corollary: full state tail band collapses in k steps

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Lifted corollary: full state tail band collapses in k steps (constructive)
------------------------------------------------------------------------

merge-split :
  вҲҖ {A : Set} (m k : Nat) (x : Vec A (m + k)) вҶ’
  (coarseOf m k x ++ tailOf m k x) вүЎ x
merge-split {A} zero    k x = refl
merge-split {A} (suc m) k (x вҲ· xs)
  rewrite merge-split {A} m k xs
  = refl

TбөЈ-++ :
  вҲҖ (m k : Nat) (c : Vec Trit m) (t : Vec Trit k) вҶ’
  TбөЈ {m} {k} (c ++ t) вүЎ c ++ tailStep t
TбөЈ-++ m k c t
  rewrite RбөЈ-++ m k c t
        | PбөЈ-++ m k c (shiftTail t)
  = refl

split-TбөЈ :
  вҲҖ (m k : Nat) (x : Vec Trit (m + k)) вҶ’
  split m k (TбөЈ {m} {k} x) вүЎ (coarseOf m k x , tailStep (tailOf m k x))
split-TбөЈ m k x with split m k x
... | (c , t)
  rewrite RбөЈ-++ m k c t
        | PбөЈ-++ m k c (shiftTail t)
        | split-++ m k c (projTail (shiftTail t))
  = refl

split-iterate-TбөЈ :
  вҲҖ (m k n : Nat) (x : Vec Trit (m + k)) вҶ’
  split m k (iterate n (TбөЈ {m} {k}) x) вүЎ
    ( coarseOf m k x
    , iterate n tailStep (tailOf m k x)
    )
split-iterate-TбөЈ m k zero x
  = sym (pair-О· (split m k x))
split-iterate-TбөЈ m k (suc n) x
  rewrite split-iterate-TбөЈ m k n (TбөЈ {m} {k} x)
        | split-TбөЈ m k x
  = refl

tailOf-after-Tk :
  вҲҖ (m k : Nat) (x : Vec Trit (m + k)) вҶ’
  tailOf m k (iterate k (TбөЈ {m} {k}) x) вүЎ replicate k zer
tailOf-after-Tk m k x =
  trans
    (cong projвӮӮ (split-iterate-TбөЈ m k k x))
    (tailCollapse k (tailOf m k x))

module DASHI.Physics.RealTernaryCarrier where

zeroVec {n = zero} = []
zeroVec {n = suc n} = zer вҲ· zeroVec {n}

module DASHI.Physics.OrbitSignatureDiscriminant where

-- Candidate signatures in 4D.
data Signature : Set where
  sig40 : Signature
  sig31 : Signature
  sig22 : Signature
  sig13 : Signature
  sig04 : Signature

Profile : Set

record OrbitProfile (Пғ : Signature) : SetвӮҒ where
  field
    profile : Profile

postulate
  -- Orbit profile computed from the discrete shell for a signature.
  ProfileOf : Signature вҶ’ Profile

  -- Injectivity of the profile map on the candidate set.
  OrbitProfileInjective :
    вҲҖ Пғ Пғ' вҶ’ ProfileOf Пғ вүЎ ProfileOf Пғ' вҶ’ Пғ вүЎ Пғ'

  -- Measured profile (e.g., imported from external scan).
  MeasuredProfile : Profile
  MeasuredSignature : Signature

  MeasuredProfile вүЎ ProfileOf sig31 вҶ’ MeasuredSignature вүЎ sig31

  OrbitProfileInjective MeasuredSignature sig31
    (trans (sym measured-profile-def) h)
module DASHI.Physics.DefaultClosure where

open import Data.Bool using (Bool; true; false)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_вүЎ_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc)
open import Data.Nat using (_вүӨ_; _<_; _вҠ”_; zвүӨn; sвүӨs)
open import Data.Empty using (вҠҘ; вҠҘ-elim)

open import Ultrametric as UMetric
open import Contraction as Contraction using (Contractiveвүў; StrictContraction)
open import DASHI.Combinatorics.Entropy using (Involution)
import DASHI.Physics.ClosureGlue as Glue
open import DASHI.Physics.ClosureStatusFromGlue
open import DASHI.Physics.UnificationClosure

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- A concrete, total instance to close the physics glue
------------------------------------------------------------------------

_вүў_ : вҲҖ {A : Set} вҶ’ A вҶ’ A вҶ’ Set
x вүў y = x вүЎ y вҶ’ вҠҘ

Carrier : Set
Carrier = Bool

-- Discrete ultrametric on Bool: 0 if equal, 1 otherwise.
dBool : Carrier вҶ’ Carrier вҶ’ Nat
dBool true  true  = zero
dBool false false = zero
dBool true  false = suc zero
dBool false true  = suc zero

id-zeroBool : вҲҖ x вҶ’ dBool x x вүЎ 0
id-zeroBool true  = refl
id-zeroBool false = refl

symBool : вҲҖ x y вҶ’ dBool x y вүЎ dBool y x
symBool true  true  = refl
symBool false false = refl
symBool true  false = refl
symBool false true  = refl

ultratriangleBool : вҲҖ x y z вҶ’ dBool x z вүӨ (dBool x y вҠ” dBool y z)
ultratriangleBool true  true  true  = zвүӨn
ultratriangleBool true  true  false = sвүӨs zвүӨn
ultratriangleBool true  false true  = zвүӨn
ultratriangleBool true  false false = sвүӨs zвүӨn
ultratriangleBool false true  true  = sвүӨs zвүӨn
ultratriangleBool false true  false = zвүӨn
ultratriangleBool false false true  = sвүӨs zвүӨn
ultratriangleBool false false false = zвүӨn

boolUltrametric : UMetric.Ultrametric Carrier
boolUltrametric =
  record
    { d = dBool
    ; id-zero = id-zeroBool
    ; symmetric = symBool
    ; ultratriangle = ultratriangleBool
    }

-- Constant contraction to false.
T : Carrier вҶ’ Carrier
T _ = false

contractiveBool-proof : вҲҖ x y вҶ’ x вүў y вҶ’ dBool (T x) (T y) < dBool x y
contractiveBool-proof true  false _   = sвүӨs zвүӨn
contractiveBool-proof false true  _   = sвүӨs zвүӨn
contractiveBool-proof true  true  xвүўy = вҠҘ-elim (xвүўy refl)
contractiveBool-proof false false xвүўy = вҠҘ-elim (xвүўy refl)

contractiveBool : Contraction.Contractiveвүў boolUltrametric T
contractiveBool =
  record
    { contractionвүў = О» {x} {y} xвүўy вҶ’
        contractiveBool-proof x y xвүўy
    }

boolTrueNeqFalse : false вүЎ true вҶ’ вҠҘ
boolTrueNeqFalse ()

uniqueBool : вҲҖ x вҶ’ T x вүЎ x вҶ’ x вүЎ false
uniqueBool true  hx = вҠҘ-elim (boolTrueNeqFalse hx)
uniqueBool false _  = refl

strictBool : Contraction.StrictContraction boolUltrametric T
strictBool =
  record
    { contractiveвүў = contractiveBool
    ; fp = false
    ; fixed = refl
    ; unique = uniqueBool
    }

invBool : Involution Carrier
invBool = record
  { О№ = О» x вҶ’ x
  ; invol = О» _ вҶ’ refl
  }

defaultClosure : Glue.ClosureAxioms
defaultClosure = Glue.mkDefaultClosure boolUltrametric T strictBool invBool

defaultClosureStatus : ClosureStatus
defaultClosureStatus = closureStatusFromGlue defaultClosure

module DASHI.Physics.WaveLiftEvenSubalgebra where

  field
    even odd : A вҶ’ Set в„“  -- predicates/classifiers

waveLiftвҮ’evenSubalgebra :

  record
    { EvenA = record { Even = A ; inc = О» x вҶ’ x }

module DASHI.Physics.DecimationToClifford where

open import Level using (Level; suc)
open import Data.Product using (ОЈ; _,_)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_вүЎ_; refl)

-- Abstract algebra with multiplication.
record Algebra {в„“ : Level} : Set (suc в„“) where
  field
    A   : Set в„“
    _В·_ : A вҶ’ A вҶ’ A

-- Decimation algebra interface (kernel algebra / RG algebra).
record DecimationAlgebra {в„“ : Level} (V : Set в„“) : Set (suc в„“) where
  field
    A    : Set в„“
    mul  : A вҶ’ A вҶ’ A
    gen  : V вҶ’ A
    -- add your decimation relations/axioms here

-- Clifford relations: gen(v)В·gen(v) = Q(v)В·1 (abstractly encoded).
record CliffordRelations {в„“ : Level} (V : Set в„“) (Q : Quadratic V) (D : DecimationAlgebra V) : Set (suc (suc в„“)) where
  open DecimationAlgebra D
  field
    rel : Set (suc в„“)   -- supply concrete relation later

-- Universal property: any algebra satisfying relations factors uniquely.
record UniversalClifford {в„“ : Level} (V : Set в„“) (Q : Quadratic V) : Set (suc в„“) where
  field
    Cl     : Set в„“
    embed  : V вҶ’ Cl
    -- factorization property left abstract for now

decimationвҮ’clifford :
  вҲҖ {в„“} {V : Set в„“} (Q : Quadratic V) вҶ’
  (D : DecimationAlgebra V) вҶ’
  CliffordRelations V Q D вҶ’
  UniversalClifford V Q
decimationвҮ’clifford _ D _ =
  record { Cl = DecimationAlgebra.A D ; embed = DecimationAlgebra.gen D }
module DASHI.Physics.SignatureFromMask where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc; _+_)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_вүЎ_; refl)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong; congвӮӮ)

open import Data.Vec using (Vec; []; _вҲ·_)
open import Data.Product using (_Г—_; _,_)

open import DASHI.Physics.IndefiniteMaskQuadratic using (Sign; plus; minus)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Count plus/minus in a mask and extract signature

countPlus : вҲҖ {m : Nat} вҶ’ Vec Sign m вҶ’ Nat
countPlus [] = 0
countPlus (plus  вҲ· Пғ) = suc (countPlus Пғ)
countPlus (minus вҲ· Пғ) = countPlus Пғ

countMinus : вҲҖ {m : Nat} вҶ’ Vec Sign m вҶ’ Nat
countMinus [] = 0
countMinus (plus  вҲ· Пғ) = countMinus Пғ
countMinus (minus вҲ· Пғ) = suc (countMinus Пғ)

signature : вҲҖ {m : Nat} вҶ’ Vec Sign m вҶ’ Nat Г— Nat
signature Пғ = (countMinus Пғ , countPlus Пғ)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- A concrete mask constructor: one minus, rest plus

replicatePlus : вҲҖ (k : Nat) вҶ’ Vec Sign k
replicatePlus zero    = []
replicatePlus (suc k) = plus вҲ· replicatePlus k

oneMinusRestPlus : вҲҖ {m : Nat} вҶ’ Vec Sign (suc m)
oneMinusRestPlus {m} = minus вҲ· replicatePlus m

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Signature of the concrete mask

countPlus-replicatePlus :
  вҲҖ {m : Nat} вҶ’ countPlus (replicatePlus m) вүЎ m
countPlus-replicatePlus {zero} = refl
countPlus-replicatePlus {suc m} =
  cong suc (countPlus-replicatePlus {m})

countMinus-replicatePlus :
  вҲҖ {m : Nat} вҶ’ countMinus (replicatePlus m) вүЎ 0
countMinus-replicatePlus {zero} = refl
countMinus-replicatePlus {suc m} = countMinus-replicatePlus {m}

signature-oneMinus :
  вҲҖ {m : Nat} вҶ’ signature (oneMinusRestPlus {m}) вүЎ (suc 0 , m)
signature-oneMinus {m} =
  congвӮӮ _,_
    (cong suc (countMinus-replicatePlus {m}))
    (countPlus-replicatePlus {m})

module DASHI.Physics.MaskedOrthogonalSplitConstructive where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc; _+_)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_вүЎ_; refl)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong; trans)

open import Data.Vec using (Vec; []; _вҲ·_; _++_; zipWith)
open import Data.Product using (_Г—_; _,_)
open import Data.Integer using (в„Ө; _*_; +_; 0в„Ө) renaming (_+_ to _+в„Ө_)
open import Data.Integer.Properties as IntP

open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (Trit; zer)
open import DASHI.Physics.IndefiniteMaskQuadratic as IMQ

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Zero vectors

zeros : вҲҖ {n : Nat} вҶ’ Vec Trit n
zeros {n = zero}  = []
zeros {n = suc n} = zer вҲ· zeros {n = n}

embedCore : вҲҖ {m k : Nat} вҶ’ Vec Trit m вҶ’ Vec Trit (m + k)
embedCore {m} {k} c = c ++ zeros {n = k}

embedTail : вҲҖ {m k : Nat} вҶ’ Vec Trit k вҶ’ Vec Trit (m + k)
embedTail {m} {k} t = zeros {n = m} ++ t

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- dotПғ unfolds to a recursive definition

dotПғ-cons :
  вҲҖ {m : Nat} (s : IMQ.Sign) (Пғ : Vec IMQ.Sign m)
    (x : Trit) (xs : Vec Trit m)
    (y : Trit) (ys : Vec Trit m) вҶ’
  IMQ.dotПғ (s вҲ· Пғ) (x вҲ· xs) (y вҲ· ys)
    вүЎ (IMQ.signв„Ө s * (IMQ.toв„ӨTrit x * IMQ.toв„ӨTrit y)) +в„Ө IMQ.dotПғ Пғ xs ys
dotПғ-cons s Пғ x xs y ys = refl

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- dotПғ against a zero vector is 0

dotПғ-zero-left :
  вҲҖ {m : Nat} (Пғ : Vec IMQ.Sign m) (y : Vec Trit m) вҶ’
  IMQ.dotПғ Пғ (zeros {n = m}) y вүЎ 0в„Ө
dotПғ-zero-left [] [] = refl
dotПғ-zero-left (s вҲ· Пғ) (y вҲ· ys) =
  trans
    (dotПғ-cons s Пғ zer (zeros {n = _}) y ys)
    (trans
    (cong (О» z вҶ’ z +в„Ө IMQ.dotПғ Пғ (zeros {n = _}) ys)
            (trans
              (cong (О» t вҶ’ IMQ.signв„Ө s * t) (IntP.*-zeroЛЎ (IMQ.toв„ӨTrit y)))
              (IntP.*-zeroКі (IMQ.signв„Ө s))))
      (cong (О» z вҶ’ 0в„Ө +в„Ө z) (dotПғ-zero-left Пғ ys)))

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Core and tail are orthogonal under dotПғ

dotПғ-coreвҠҘtail :
  вҲҖ {m k : Nat} (Пғ : Vec IMQ.Sign (m + k))
    (c : Vec Trit m) (t : Vec Trit k) вҶ’
  IMQ.dotПғ Пғ (embedCore {m} {k} c) (embedTail {m} {k} t) вүЎ 0в„Ө
dotПғ-coreвҠҘtail {zero} {k} Пғ [] t = dotПғ-zero-left Пғ t
dotПғ-coreвҠҘtail {suc m} {k} (s вҲ· Пғ) (x вҲ· xs) t =
  trans
    (dotПғ-cons s Пғ x (xs ++ zeros {n = k}) zer (zeros {n = m} ++ t))
    (trans
    (cong (О» z вҶ’ z +в„Ө IMQ.dotПғ Пғ (xs ++ zeros {n = k}) (zeros {n = m} ++ t))
            (trans
              (cong (О» t вҶ’ IMQ.signв„Ө s * t) (IntP.*-zeroКі (IMQ.toв„ӨTrit x)))
              (IntP.*-zeroКі (IMQ.signв„Ө s))))
      (cong (О» z вҶ’ 0в„Ө +в„Ө z) (dotПғ-coreвҠҘtail {m} {k} Пғ xs t)))

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Therefore B2Пғ is also 0 on core/tail blocks

B2Пғ-coreвҠҘtail :
  вҲҖ {m k : Nat} (Пғ : Vec IMQ.Sign (m + k))
    (c : Vec Trit m) (t : Vec Trit k) вҶ’
  IMQ.B2Пғ Пғ (embedCore {m} {k} c) (embedTail {m} {k} t) вүЎ 0в„Ө
B2Пғ-coreвҠҘtail {m} {k} Пғ c t =
  trans (IMQ.B2ПғвүЎ2dotПғ Пғ (embedCore {m} {k} c) (embedTail {m} {k} t))
        (cong (О» z вҶ’ (+ 2) * z) (dotПғ-coreвҠҘtail Пғ c t))
module DASHI.Physics.WitnessSetPolicy where

open import Level using (Level; suc)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat)
open import Data.Nat using (_вүӨ_)
open import Data.Product using (_Г—_; _,_)

_вүҘ_ : Nat вҶ’ Nat вҶ’ Set
m вүҘ n = n вүӨ m

-- Policy for admissible witness sets used in closure claims.
record WitnessSetPolicy {в„“} (W : Set в„“) : Set (suc в„“) where
  field
    minForward : Nat
    minBackward : Nat
    forwardCount : W вҶ’ Nat
    backwardCount : W вҶ’ Nat
    quotaPreserving : W вҶ’ Set

  admissible : W вҶ’ Set
  admissible w =
    (forwardCount w вүҘ minForward) Г—
    (backwardCount w вүҘ minBackward) Г—
    quotaPreserving w

open WitnessSetPolicy public
module DASHI.Physics.SeverityGuardShiftInstance where

-- This module packages a severity-based Guard policy for the shift carrier.
-- It is parameterized over a concrete severity extractor and restore map.

record ShiftSeverityPolicy {m k : Nat} : SetвӮҒ where
  field
    codeбөЈ : RTC.Carrier (m + k) вҶ’ Code
    safeThresholdбөЈ : Severity
    brokenThresholdбөЈ : Severity

  policyбөЈ : SG.SeverityPolicy (RTC.Carrier (m + k))
  policyбөЈ = record
    { code = codeбөЈ
    ; safeThreshold = safeThresholdбөЈ
    ; brokenThreshold = brokenThresholdбөЈ
    }

-- Guarded strictness bundle specialized to the shift carrier, but still abstract
-- in the projection and restore maps (to avoid baking in a specific scheduler).
record ShiftSeverityGuardedStrict {m k : Nat} : SetвӮҒ where
  field
    pol : ShiftSeverityPolicy {m} {k}

    PбөЈ : RTC.Carrier (m + k) вҶ’ RTC.Carrier (m + k)
    RestoreбөЈ : RTC.Carrier (m + k) вҶ’ RTC.Carrier (m + k)
    projбөЈ : RTC.Carrier (m + k) вҶ’ (Nat вҶ’ UFTC.Code)  -- supply stream view if desired
    Оә : Nat

    P-strict-on :
      вҲҖ {x y kвҖІ} вҶ’
      SG.Guard (ShiftSeverityPolicy.policyбөЈ pol) x вҶ’
      SG.Guard (ShiftSeverityPolicy.policyбөЈ pol) y вҶ’
      lcpвүҘ (projбөЈ x) (projбөЈ y) kвҖІ вҶ’
      lcpвүҘ (projбөЈ (PбөЈ x)) (projбөЈ (PбөЈ y)) (kвҖІ + Оә)

    restore-normal-form :
      вҲҖ x вҶ’
      SG.Broken (ShiftSeverityPolicy.policyбөЈ pol) x вҶ’
      SG.Guard (ShiftSeverityPolicy.policyбөЈ pol) (RestoreбөЈ x)

    restore-idem :
      вҲҖ x вҶ’ RestoreбөЈ (RestoreбөЈ x) вүЎ RestoreбөЈ x

    restore-fixes :
      вҲҖ x вҶ’ PбөЈ (RestoreбөЈ x) вүЎ RestoreбөЈ x

  guarded : SGS.SeverityGuardedStrict
  guarded = record
    { S = RTC.Carrier (m + k)
    ; policy = ShiftSeverityPolicy.policyбөЈ pol
    ; PвӮӣ = PбөЈ
    ; RestoreвӮӣ = RestoreбөЈ
    ; projвӮӣ = projбөЈ
    ; ОәвӮӣ = Оә
    ; P-strict-onвӮӣ = P-strict-on
    ; restore-normal-formвӮӣ = restore-normal-form
    ; restore-idemвӮӣ = restore-idem
    ; restore-fixesвӮӣ = restore-fixes
    }

open ShiftSeverityGuardedStrict public

module DASHI.Physics.MaskedQuadraticRenormalization where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_вүЎ_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; _+_)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong; sym; trans)

open import Data.Vec using (Vec; _++_; zipWith)
open import Data.Product using (_Г—_; _,_; projвӮҒ; projвӮӮ)
open import Data.Integer using (в„Ө; _*_) renaming (_+_ to _+в„Ө_)

open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (Trit)

open import DASHI.Physics.IndefiniteMaskQuadratic as IMQ

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Basic split lemmas for coarse/tail under concatenation

coarseOf-++ :
  вҲҖ (m k : Nat) (c : Vec Trit m) (t : Vec Trit k) вҶ’
  TCP.coarseOf m k (c ++ t) вүЎ c
coarseOf-++ m k c t
  rewrite TCP.split-++ m k c t
  = refl

tailOf-++ :
  вҲҖ (m k : Nat) (c : Vec Trit m) (t : Vec Trit k) вҶ’
  TCP.tailOf m k (c ++ t) вүЎ t
tailOf-++ m k c t
  rewrite TCP.split-++ m k c t
  = refl

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Coarse/tail behavior under renormalization RбөЈ

coarseOf-RбөЈ :
  вҲҖ (m k : Nat) (x : Vec Trit (m + k)) вҶ’
  TCP.coarseOf m k (TCP.RбөЈ {m} {k} x) вүЎ TCP.coarseOf m k x
coarseOf-RбөЈ m k x with TCP.split m k x
... | (c , t)
  rewrite sym (TCP.merge-split m k x)
        | TCP.RбөЈ-++ m k c t
        | coarseOf-++ m k c (TCP.shiftTail t)
  = refl

tailOf-RбөЈ :
  вҲҖ (m k : Nat) (x : Vec Trit (m + k)) вҶ’
  TCP.tailOf m k (TCP.RбөЈ {m} {k} x) вүЎ TCP.shiftTail (TCP.tailOf m k x)
tailOf-RбөЈ m k x with TCP.split m k x
... | (c , t)
  rewrite sym (TCP.merge-split m k x)
        | TCP.RбөЈ-++ m k c t
        | tailOf-++ m k c (TCP.shiftTail t)
  = refl

RбөЈ-decomp :
  вҲҖ (m k : Nat) (x : Vec Trit (m + k)) вҶ’
  TCP.RбөЈ {m} {k} x вүЎ TCP.coarseOf m k x ++ TCP.shiftTail (TCP.tailOf m k x)
RбөЈ-decomp m k x with TCP.split m k x
... | (c , t)
  rewrite sym (TCP.merge-split m k x)
        | TCP.RбөЈ-++ m k c t
        | coarseOf-++ m k c t
        | tailOf-++ m k c t
  = refl

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Masked quadratic under renormalization:
-- QПғ(RбөЈ x) splits into coarse + shifted tail.

QПғ-split-++ :
  вҲҖ (m k : Nat)
    (Пғc : Vec IMQ.Sign m) (Пғt : Vec IMQ.Sign k)
    (c : Vec Trit m) (t : Vec Trit k) вҶ’
  IMQ.QПғ (Пғc ++ Пғt) (c ++ t)
    вүЎ IMQ.QПғ Пғc c +в„Ө IMQ.QПғ Пғt t
QПғ-split-++ m k Пғc Пғt c t =
  let
    f = (О» s xi вҶ’ IMQ.signв„Ө s * IMQ.sqв„Ө (IMQ.toв„ӨTrit xi))
  in
  trans
    refl
    (trans
      (cong IMQ.sumв„Ө (MSQ.zipWith-++ f Пғc Пғt c t))
      (trans
        (MSQ.sumв„Ө-++ (zipWith f Пғc c) (zipWith f Пғt t))
        refl))

QПғ-split-coarse :
  вҲҖ (m k : Nat)
    (Пғ : Vec IMQ.Sign (m + k))
    (c : Vec Trit m) (t : Vec Trit k) вҶ’
  IMQ.QПғ Пғ (c ++ t)
    вүЎ IMQ.QПғ (TCP.coarseOf m k Пғ) c
    +в„Ө IMQ.QПғ (TCP.tailOf m k Пғ) t
QПғ-split-coarse m k Пғ c t
  =
  trans
    (cong (О» z вҶ’ IMQ.QПғ z (c ++ t)) (sym (TCP.merge-split {A = IMQ.Sign} m k Пғ)))
    (QПғ-split-++ m k (TCP.coarseOf m k Пғ) (TCP.tailOf m k Пғ) c t)

QПғ-R :
  вҲҖ (m k : Nat)
    (Пғ : Vec IMQ.Sign (m + k))
    (x : Vec Trit (m + k)) вҶ’
  IMQ.QПғ Пғ (TCP.RбөЈ {m} {k} x)
    вүЎ IMQ.QПғ (TCP.coarseOf m k Пғ) (TCP.coarseOf m k x)
    +в„Ө IMQ.QПғ (TCP.tailOf   m k Пғ) (TCP.shiftTail (TCP.tailOf m k x))
QПғ-R m k Пғ x with TCP.split m k x
... | (c , t)
  rewrite sym (TCP.merge-split m k x)
        | TCP.RбөЈ-++ m k c t
  = QПғ-split-coarse m k Пғ c (TCP.shiftTail t)
module DASHI.Physics.MaskedClosureKit where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_вүЎ_)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; _+_)
open import Data.Product using (_Г—_; _,_)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec)
open import Data.Integer using (в„Ө)

open import DASHI.Physics.RealTernaryCarrier as RTC
open import DASHI.Physics.TailCollapseProof as TCP
open import DASHI.Physics.RealClosureKitFiber as RKF

open import DASHI.Physics.SignatureFromMask as SFM
open import DASHI.Physics.DimensionBoundAssumptions as DBA

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Masked quadratic invariants wired onto a RealClosureKitFiber instance.
--
-- This does not change the underlying closure kit; it augments it with:
--   - a mask on the core,
--   - the masked quadratic QПғ and bilinear BвӮӮПғ pulled back to the full state,
--   - a signature extracted from the mask,
--   - an orbit-profile seam (dimension bound target).

record RealClosureKitFiberMask : SetвӮҒ where
  field
    m k : Nat
    base : RKF.RealClosureKitFiber

    -- Mask on the core (length m).
    mask : Vec IMQ.Sign m

    -- Core-only invariants, lifted to the full state via coarseOf.
    coreQПғ : RTC.Carrier (m + k) вҶ’ в„Ө
    coreB2Пғ : RTC.Carrier (m + k) вҶ’ RTC.Carrier (m + k) вҶ’ в„Ө

    -- Signature extracted from the mask.
    sig : Nat Г— Nat

    -- Orbit-profile seam (dimension-bound target).
    orbitProfile : DBA.ShellOrbitProfile m

open RealClosureKitFiberMask public

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Constructor: derive all fields from base + mask.

mkMaskKit :
  вҲҖ {m k : Nat} вҶ’
  RKF.RealClosureKitFiber вҶ’
  Vec IMQ.Sign m вҶ’
  DBA.ShellOrbitProfile m вҶ’
  RealClosureKitFiberMask
mkMaskKit {m} {k} base mask orbitProfile =
  record
    { m = m
    ; k = k
    ; base = base
    ; mask = mask
    ; coreQПғ = О» x вҶ’ IMQ.QПғ mask (TCP.coarseOf m k x)
    ; coreB2Пғ = О» x y вҶ’ IMQ.B2Пғ mask (TCP.coarseOf m k x) (TCP.coarseOf m k y)
    ; sig = SFM.signature mask
    ; orbitProfile = orbitProfile
    }
module DASHI.Physics.OrbitProfileComputed where

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Basic list utilities (kept local to avoid extra imports)

concat : вҲҖ {A : Set} вҶ’ List (List A) вҶ’ List A
concat [] = []
concat (xs вҲ· xss) = xs ++ concat xss
  where
    _++_ : вҲҖ {A : Set} вҶ’ List A вҶ’ List A вҶ’ List A
    [] ++ ys = ys
    (x вҲ· xs) ++ ys = x вҲ· (xs ++ ys)

concatMap : вҲҖ {A B : Set} вҶ’ (A вҶ’ List B) вҶ’ List A вҶ’ List B
concatMap f xs = concat (map f xs)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Decidable equality for Trit and Vec

decEqTrit : (x y : Trit) вҶ’ Dec (x вүЎ y)
decEqTrit neg neg = yes refl
decEqTrit neg zer = no (О» ())
decEqTrit neg pos = no (О» ())
decEqTrit zer neg = no (О» ())
decEqTrit zer zer = yes refl
decEqTrit zer pos = no (О» ())
decEqTrit pos neg = no (О» ())
decEqTrit pos zer = no (О» ())
decEqTrit pos pos = yes refl

decEqVec : вҲҖ {n : Nat} вҶ’ (x y : Vec Trit n) вҶ’ Dec (x вүЎ y)
decEqVec [] [] = yes refl
decEqVec (x вҲ· xs) (y вҲ· ys) with decEqTrit x y
... | no neq = no (О» eq вҶ’ neq (cong head eq))
... | yes refl with decEqVec xs ys
... | no neq = no (О» eq вҶ’ neq (cong tail eq))
... | yes refl = yes refl
  where
    head : вҲҖ {n : Nat} вҶ’ Vec Trit (suc n) вҶ’ Trit
    head (t вҲ· _) = t
    tail : вҲҖ {n : Nat} вҶ’ Vec Trit (suc n) вҶ’ Vec Trit n
    tail (_ вҲ· ts) = ts

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Membership / nub

member : вҲҖ {A : Set} вҶ’ (A вҶ’ A вҶ’ Dec (A вүЎ A)) вҶ’ A вҶ’ List A вҶ’ Bool
member dec x [] = false
member dec x (y вҲ· ys) with dec x y
... | yes _ = true
... | no _  = member dec x ys

nub : вҲҖ {A : Set} вҶ’ (A вҶ’ A вҶ’ Dec (A вүЎ A)) вҶ’ List A вҶ’ List A
nub dec [] = []
nub dec (x вҲ· xs) with member dec x xs
... | true  = nub dec xs
... | false = x вҲ· nub dec xs

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Enumerate all Vec Trit n

allTrit : List Trit
allTrit = neg вҲ· zer вҲ· pos вҲ· []

allVecTrit : вҲҖ (n : Nat) вҶ’ List (Vec Trit n)
allVecTrit zero = [] вҲ· []
allVecTrit (suc n) =
  concatMap
    (О» t вҶ’ map (О» v вҶ’ t вҲ· v) (allVecTrit n))
    allTrit

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Shell1 list from a mask

isShell1 : вҲҖ {m : Nat} вҶ’ Vec IMQ.Sign m вҶ’ Vec Trit m вҶ’ Bool
isShell1 Пғ x with IMQ.QПғ Пғ x вүҹ (+ 1)
... | yes _ = true
... | no _ with IMQ.QПғ Пғ x вүҹ -[1+ 0]
... | yes _ = true
... | no _  = false

shell1List : вҲҖ {m : Nat} вҶ’ Vec IMQ.Sign m вҶ’ List (Vec Trit m)
shell1List {m} Пғ = filter (isShell1 Пғ) (allVecTrit m)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Orbit sizes under a finite action list

orbitSizes :
  вҲҖ {A : Set} вҶ’
  (dec : A вҶ’ A вҶ’ Dec (A вүЎ A)) вҶ’
  (gs : List A) вҶ’
  (act : A вҶ’ A вҶ’ A) вҶ’
  List A вҶ’
  List Nat
orbitSizes dec gs act [] = []
orbitSizes dec gs act (x вҲ· xs) =
  let
    orb = nub dec (map (О» g вҶ’ act g x) gs)
    rest = filter (О» z вҶ’ not (member dec z orb)) xs
  in
  length orb вҲ· orbitSizes dec gs act rest
  where
    not : Bool вҶ’ Bool
    not true = false
    not false = true

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Simple descending sort for Nat lists

insertDesc : Nat вҶ’ List Nat вҶ’ List Nat
insertDesc x [] = x вҲ· []
insertDesc x (y вҲ· ys) with x NatP.вүӨ? y
... | yes _ = y вҲ· insertDesc x ys
... | no _  = x вҲ· y вҲ· ys

sortDesc : List Nat вҶ’ List Nat
sortDesc [] = []
sortDesc (x вҲ· xs) = insertDesc x (sortDesc xs)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Concrete Bool action: invVec toggle

actBool : вҲҖ {m : Nat} вҶ’ Bool вҶ’ Vec Trit m вҶ’ Vec Trit m
actBool true  x = RTC.invVec x
actBool false x = x

bools : List Bool
bools = false вҲ· true вҲ· []

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Computed profile for the Bool action on Shell1

orbitProfileBool :
  вҲҖ {m : Nat} вҶ’
  Vec IMQ.Sign m вҶ’
  DBA.ShellOrbitProfile m
orbitProfileBool Пғ =
  let
    shell = shell1List Пғ
    sizes = orbitSizes decEqVec bools actBool shell
    sizesSorted = sortDesc sizes
  in
  SOPG.profileFromSorted {m = _} sizesSorted
module DASHI.Physics.SnapSignature where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc; _+_)
open import Data.Nat using (_вүӨ_)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_вүЎ_)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec; []; _вҲ·_)
open import Data.Empty using (вҠҘ)
open import Data.Product using (_Г—_)
open import Data.Sum using (_вҠҺ_)

В¬_ : Set вҶ’ Set
В¬ P = P вҶ’ вҠҘ

open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (Trit; neg; zer; pos)

-- Count coordinates that snap from nonzero to zero in a single step.
countZeroSnaps : вҲҖ {n : Nat} вҶ’ Vec Trit n вҶ’ Vec Trit n вҶ’ Nat
countZeroSnaps [] [] = zero
countZeroSnaps (x вҲ· xs) (y вҲ· ys) =
  snap x y + countZeroSnaps xs ys
  where
    snap : Trit вҶ’ Trit вҶ’ Nat
    snap neg zer = suc zero
    snap pos zer = suc zero
    snap _   _   = zero

-- Predicate: at least k zero-snaps.
SnapAtLeast : вҲҖ {n : Nat} вҶ’ Nat вҶ’ Vec Trit n вҶ’ Vec Trit n вҶ’ Set
SnapAtLeast k x y = k вүӨ countZeroSnaps x y

-- Abstract diagnostic bundle for a step x -> y.
record SnapSignature {S : Set} : SetвӮҒ where
  field
    -- concrete state
    step : S вҶ’ S вҶ’ Set

    -- trigger 1: multi-coordinate zeroing (sheet elimination)
    snapZero : S вҶ’ S вҶ’ Set

    -- trigger 2: chi2 spike (boundary blow-up)
    chi2Spike : S вҶ’ S вҶ’ Set

    -- trigger 3: MDL proxy descent (valid IR movement)
    mdlDescent : S вҶ’ S вҶ’ Set

-- Canonical combined predicate for a snap event.
record IsSnap {S : Set} (Sig : SnapSignature {S}) : SetвӮҒ where
  field
    snap : вҲҖ x y вҶ’
      SnapSignature.step Sig x y вҶ’
      SnapSignature.snapZero Sig x y вҶ’
      SnapSignature.chi2Spike Sig x y вҶ’
      SnapSignature.mdlDescent Sig x y вҶ’
      Set

-- Cone monotonicity except snaps: if not a snap, interior is preserved.
record ConeMonotoneExceptSnaps {S : Set} : SetвӮҒ where
  field
    InInterior : S вҶ’ Set
    Boundary   : S вҶ’ Set
    T          : S вҶ’ S
    Sig        : SnapSignature {S}

    monotoneExceptSnap : вҲҖ x вҶ’
      InInterior x вҶ’
      (В¬ (SnapSignature.step Sig x (T x) Г—
          SnapSignature.snapZero Sig x (T x) Г—
          SnapSignature.chi2Spike Sig x (T x) Г—
          SnapSignature.mdlDescent Sig x (T x))) вҶ’
      InInterior (T x) вҠҺ Boundary (T x)

record QuadraticOutput : SetвӮҒ where

module DASHI.Physics.LiftToFullState where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_вүЎ_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc; _+_)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong; trans)
open import Data.Product using (_Г—_; _,_)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec; _++_; replicate)
open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (Trit; zer)

open import DASHI.Physics.TailCollapseProof as TCP

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Invariant coarse subspace

embedCoarse : вҲҖ (m k : Nat) вҶ’ Vec Trit m вҶ’ Vec Trit (m + k)
embedCoarse m k c = c ++ replicate k zer

coarseProj : вҲҖ (m k : Nat) вҶ’ Vec Trit (m + k) вҶ’ Vec Trit m
coarseProj m k x = TCP.coarseOf m k x

coarse-invariant-R :
  вҲҖ (m k : Nat) (x : Vec Trit (m + k)) вҶ’
  coarseProj m k (TCP.RбөЈ {m} {k} x) вүЎ coarseProj m k x
coarse-invariant-R m k x with TCP.split m k x
... | (c , t) rewrite TCP.split-++ m k c (TCP.shiftTail t) = refl

coarse-invariant-P :
  вҲҖ (m k : Nat) (x : Vec Trit (m + k)) вҶ’
  coarseProj m k (TCP.PбөЈ {m} {k} x) вүЎ coarseProj m k x
coarse-invariant-P m k x with TCP.split m k x
... | (c , t) rewrite TCP.split-++ m k c (TCP.projTail t) = refl

coarse-invariant-T :
  вҲҖ (m k : Nat) (x : Vec Trit (m + k)) вҶ’
  coarseProj m k (TCP.TбөЈ {m} {k} x) вүЎ coarseProj m k x
coarse-invariant-T m k x =
  trans (coarse-invariant-P m k (TCP.RбөЈ {m} {k} x))
        (coarse-invariant-R m k x)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Finite-time collapse + invariant geometry, packaged

coarse-invariant-iter :
  вҲҖ (m k n : Nat) (x : Vec Trit (m + k)) вҶ’
  coarseProj m k (TCP.iterate n (TCP.TбөЈ {m} {k}) x) вүЎ coarseProj m k x
coarse-invariant-iter m k zero x = refl
coarse-invariant-iter m k (suc n) x =
  trans
    (coarse-invariant-iter m k n (TCP.TбөЈ {m} {k} x))
    (coarse-invariant-T m k x)

finiteTimeCollapse-to-geometry :
  вҲҖ (m k : Nat) (x : Vec Trit (m + k)) вҶ’
  ( coarseProj m k (TCP.iterate k (TCP.TбөЈ {m} {k}) x) вүЎ coarseProj m k x )
  Г—
  ( TCP.tailOf m k (TCP.iterate k (TCP.TбөЈ {m} {k}) x) вүЎ replicate k zer )
finiteTimeCollapse-to-geometry m k x =
  ( coarse-invariant-iter m k k x
  , TCP.tailOf-after-Tk m k x
  )

invariantCoarseSubspace :
  вҲҖ (m k : Nat) (c : Vec Trit m) вҶ’
  TCP.TбөЈ {m} {k} (embedCoarse m k c) вүЎ embedCoarse m k c
invariantCoarseSubspace m k c
  rewrite TCP.RбөЈ-++ m k c (replicate k zer)
        | TCP.PбөЈ-++ m k c (TCP.shiftTail (replicate k zer))
        | TCP.shiftTail-replicate {k}
        | TCP.projTail-replicate {k}
  = refl

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Abstract broken states / restored states.

  Broken  : Set
  Stable  : Set

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- A "restoration" map (Tikkun): Broken вҶ’ Stable

  field
    restore : Broken вҶ’ Stable

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Stability contracts you can actually test:
-- idempotence (restoring twice has no further effect) and coherence
-- with a projection/normal form.

    nf : Stable вҶ’ Stable
    nf-idem : вҲҖ s вҶ’ nf (nf s) вүЎ nf s

    R  : Restoration
    NF : NormalForm
    restores-to-nf : вҲҖ b вҶ’ NormalForm.nf NF (Restoration.restore R b) вүЎ Restoration.restore R b

В¬_ : Set вҶ’ Set
В¬ A = A вҶ’ вҠҘ

fst = projвӮҒ

snd : {A : Set} {B : A вҶ’ Set} (p : ОЈ A B) вҶ’ B (projвӮҒ p)

module Verification.ZK where

open import Verification.Prelude

postulate Public  : Set
postulate Private : Set
postulate Output  : Set

-- The spec function (what correctness means)
postulate spec : Public -> Private -> Output

-- An implementation whose correctness you want to prove (could be a circuit)
postulate impl : Public -> Private -> Output

-- A proof object (SNARK) and a verifier predicate
postulate Proof : Set
postulate verify : Public -> Output -> Proof -> Bool

-- Soundness contract (non-ZK): if verifier accepts, output equals spec
-- (This is where you plug the cryptographic theorem/certificate.)
postulate
  zkSoundness :
    (pub : Public) -> (priv : Private) -> (out : Output) -> (pi : Proof) ->
    verify pub out pi вүЎ true ->
    out вүЎ spec pub priv

-- ZK verification artifact: provide pub/out/proof and a verification boolean proof.
record ZKCorrectness : Set1 where
  field
    pub  : Public
    priv : Private
    out  : Output
    pi   : Proof
    accepts : verify pub out pi вүЎ true
    correct : out вүЎ spec pub priv
module Verification.ExecutionReview where

open import Verification.Prelude

-- A tiny abstract control-flow model.
postulate Program : Set
postulate Path    : Set

-- Static analyzer produces a set/list of feasible paths
postulate enumeratePaths : Program вҶ’ List Path

-- A property you claim holds on all paths.
postulate SafeOnPath : Program вҶ’ Path вҶ’ Set

-- вҖңExecution reviewвҖқ = proof that for every enumerated path, Safe holds.
All : вҲҖ {A : Set} вҶ’ (A вҶ’ Set) вҶ’ List A вҶ’ Set
All P []       = вҠӨ
All P (x вҲ· xs) = P x Г— All P xs

record ExecutionReview : SetвӮҒ where
  field
    P   : Program
    ok  : All (SafeOnPath P) (enumeratePaths P)
module Verification.SourceHash where

open import Verification.Prelude

-- Abstract bytes; you can refine to Word8 later.
postulate Byte : Set
Bytes = List Byte

-- Cryptographic hash as a function (model-level).
postulate Hash : Set
postulate hash : Bytes вҶ’ Hash

-- A repo snapshot is modeled as its bytes (tarball) + declared hash.
record Snapshot : Set where
  constructor snap
  field
    blob     : Bytes
    declared : Hash

-- Integrity proof obligation: declared equals computed.
record SourceIntegrity : Set where
  field
    S : Snapshot
    ok : Snapshot.declared S вүЎ hash (Snapshot.blob S)
module Verification.BinaryPatching where

open import Verification.Prelude

postulate Binary : Set
postulate Input  : Set
postulate Output : Set

-- Semantics of a binary as a function (idealization).
postulate run : Binary вҶ’ Input вҶ’ Output

-- Vulnerability predicate (e.g., triggers UAF, OOB, etc.)
postulate Vuln : Binary вҶ’ Set

-- Patch procedure
postulate patch : Binary вҶ’ Binary

postulate SafeInput : Input вҶ’ Set

-- Correctness obligations
record PatchCorrect : SetвӮҒ where
  field
    B : Binary
    -- vulnerability removed
    fixed : В¬ Vuln (patch B)
    -- behavior preserved on some agreed safe domain
    preserved : вҲҖ i вҶ’ SafeInput i вҶ’ run (patch B) i вүЎ run B i

module Verification.CostProfile where

-- Abstract cost model (time, memory, steps, gas...)

  constructor cost
  field
    time  : Nat
    mem   : Nat
    io    : Nat

-- Thresholds

  field
    maxTime : Nat
    maxMem  : Nat
    maxIO   : Nat

-- вүӨ relation can be imported from stdlib; keep abstract here:

    P : Program
    B : Budget
    okTime : Cost.time (profile P) вүӨ Budget.maxTime B
    okMem  : Cost.mem  (profile P) вүӨ Budget.maxMem  B
    okIO   : Cost.io   (profile P) вүӨ Budget.maxIO   B
module Ultrametric where

open import Data.Nat using (в„•; _вүӨ_; _<_)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat
open import Agda.Builtin.Sigma
open import Data.Nat using (в„•; _вҠ”_)
max : в„• вҶ’ в„• вҶ’ в„•
max = _вҠ”_


------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Distance function into в„• (discrete ultrametric)

record Ultrametric (S : Set) : SetвӮҒ where
  field
    d : S вҶ’ S вҶ’ Nat

    -- Identity
    id-zero :
      вҲҖ x вҶ’ d x x вүЎ 0

    -- Symmetry
    symmetric :
      вҲҖ x y вҶ’ d x y вүЎ d y x

    -- Strong triangle inequality (ultrametric)
    ultratriangle :
      вҲҖ x y z вҶ’
      d x z вүӨ max (d x y) (d y z)

module CRTPeriod where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat      using (Nat; _+_; _*_)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_вүЎ_; refl)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong; trans; sym)

open import Data.Nat.Base   using (NonZero; nonZero)
open import Data.Nat.DivMod using (_%_; [m+kn]%nвүЎm%n)
open import Data.Nat.Properties as NatP using (*-assoc; *-comm; +-assoc)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Repo-defined digit function:

d : Nat вҶ’ Nat
d N = ((N % 71) + (N % 59) + (N % 47)) % 10

period : Nat
period = 71 * 59 * 47  -- 196883

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- The theorem statement (R1):
-- d(N + k*period) = d(N) for all k.
--
-- Proof is standard modular arithmetic:
-- (N + k*period) mod p = N mod p for p вҲҲ {71,59,47}
-- then propagate through sum and mod 10.
--
-- You can discharge this using stdlib DivMod lemmas, or (DASHI-style)
-- by importing a small proof certificate.

instance
  nonZero71 : NonZero 71
  nonZero71 = nonZero
  nonZero59 : NonZero 59
  nonZero59 = nonZero
  nonZero47 : NonZero 47
  nonZero47 = nonZero
  nonZero10 : NonZero 10
  nonZero10 = nonZero

period-thm : вҲҖ N k вҶ’ d (N + k * period) вүЎ d N
period-thm N k =
  period-thm' step71 step59 step47
  where
    k71 = k * (59 * 47)
    k59 = k * (71 * 47)
    k47 = k * (71 * 59)

    periodвүЎ59В·47В·71 : period вүЎ (59 * 47) * 71
    periodвүЎ59В·47В·71 =
      trans (NatP.*-assoc 71 59 47)
        (NatP.*-comm 71 (59 * 47))

    periodвүЎ71В·47В·59 : period вүЎ (71 * 47) * 59
    periodвүЎ71В·47В·59 =
      trans (NatP.*-assoc 71 59 47)
        (trans (cong (О» x вҶ’ 71 * x) (NatP.*-comm 59 47))
          (sym (NatP.*-assoc 71 47 59)))

    periodвүЎ71В·59В·47 : period вүЎ (71 * 59) * 47
    periodвүЎ71В·59В·47 = NatP.*-assoc 71 59 47

    eq71 : k * period вүЎ k71 * 71
    eq71 = trans (cong (О» x вҶ’ k * x) periodвүЎ59В·47В·71) (sym (NatP.*-assoc k (59 * 47) 71))

    eq59 : k * period вүЎ k59 * 59
    eq59 = trans (cong (О» x вҶ’ k * x) periodвүЎ71В·47В·59) (sym (NatP.*-assoc k (71 * 47) 59))

    eq47 : k * period вүЎ k47 * 47
    eq47 = trans (cong (О» x вҶ’ k * x) periodвүЎ71В·59В·47) (sym (NatP.*-assoc k (71 * 59) 47))

    step71 : (N + k * period) % 71 вүЎ N % 71
    step71 = trans (cong (О» v вҶ’ (N + v) % 71) eq71) ([m+kn]%nвүЎm%n N k71 71)

    step59 : (N + k * period) % 59 вүЎ N % 59
    step59 = trans (cong (О» v вҶ’ (N + v) % 59) eq59) ([m+kn]%nвүЎm%n N k59 59)

    step47 : (N + k * period) % 47 вүЎ N % 47
    step47 = trans (cong (О» v вҶ’ (N + v) % 47) eq47) ([m+kn]%nвүЎm%n N k47 47)

    period-thm' :
      (s71 : (N + k * period) % 71 вүЎ N % 71) вҶ’
      (s59 : (N + k * period) % 59 вүЎ N % 59) вҶ’
      (s47 : (N + k * period) % 47 вүЎ N % 47) вҶ’
      d (N + k * period) вүЎ d N
    period-thm' s71 s59 s47 rewrite s71 | s59 | s47 = refl
module Z6_RegularInverse where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_вүЎ_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat)
open import Data.Fin using (Fin; zero; suc; toв„•)
open import Data.Product.Base using (ОЈ; _,_)
open import Data.Nat.Properties as NatP using ()
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality as Eq using (cong)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Z6 elements as Fin 6
Z6 : Set
Z6 = Fin 6

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Ring operations modulo 6 (postulate or implement via Fin arithmetic).
-- If you want full concreteness, implement add/mul with toв„• and mod 6.
postulate
  _+6_ : Z6 вҶ’ Z6 вҶ’ Z6
  _*6_ : Z6 вҶ’ Z6 вҶ’ Z6

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- von Neumann regular inverse witness: a = a*b*a

Regular : Z6 вҶ’ Set
Regular a = ОЈ Z6 (О» b вҶ’ a вүЎ (a *6 b) *6 a)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- A concrete witness table (finite, so we can just provide b per a).
-- You can later refine _+6_/_*6_ and this becomes fully checkable.

postulate
  bOf : Z6 вҶ’ Z6
  regular-law : вҲҖ a вҶ’ a вүЎ (a *6 bOf a) *6 a

regular : вҲҖ a вҶ’ Regular a
regular a = bOf a , regular-law a
module FascisticSystem where

open import Data.Product using (ОЈ; _,_)
open import Data.Sum using (_вҠҺ_; injвӮҒ; injвӮӮ)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_вүЎ_)

open import Data.Nat as Nat
open import Data.Bool using (Bool; true; false)



-- Abstract finite state space

postulate
  S : Set
  finiteS : в„•          -- cardinality (not constructively used)

-- Entropy function (measure into в„• for simplicity)

postulate
  H : S вҶ’ в„•

-- Projection operator (idempotent, non-invertible)

record Projection : Set where
  field
    K        : S вҶ’ S
    idemp    : вҲҖ s вҶ’ K (K s) вүЎ K s
    contract : вҲҖ s вҶ’ H (K s) вүӨ H s

-- System = list of projections applied in fixed order

postulate
  Ktotal : S вҶ’ S

-- Global contraction property

postulate
  monotone : вҲҖ s вҶ’ H (Ktotal s) вүӨ H s

-- Strict decrease when not in fixed set

postulate
  strict-decrease :
    вҲҖ s вҶ’ H (Ktotal s) < H s вҠҺ (Ktotal s вүЎ s)

-- Define attractor

Attractor : Set
Attractor = ОЈ S (О» s вҶ’ Ktotal s вүЎ s)

-- Iteration

iterate : в„• вҶ’ S вҶ’ S
iterate zero    s = s
iterate (suc n) s = Ktotal (iterate n s)

-- Completion prime provides a stop condition for any recursive refinement loop.

  field
    measure : S вҶ’ Nat
    step    : S вҶ’ S
    -- If step decreases measure, recursion terminates.
    decreases : вҲҖ s вҶ’ measure (step s) < measure s

  -- In Agda, easiest is to use в„ҡP.*-cancelКі / group properties.
  qed
module MonsterState where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat      using (Nat; zero; suc; _+_; _*_)
open import Agda.Builtin.Bool     using (Bool; true; false)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_вүЎ_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.List     using (List; []; _вҲ·_)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Factor mask (15 prime-power factors of |M|).
-- true  = keep
-- false = remove

FactorCount : Nat
FactorCount = 15

Mask : Set
Mask = List Bool

replicate : Nat вҶ’ Bool вҶ’ Mask
replicate zero    b = []
replicate (suc n) b = b вҲ· replicate n b

fullMask : Mask
fullMask = replicate FactorCount true

emptyMask : Mask
emptyMask = replicate FactorCount false

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Walk state.
-- You can extend this with вҖңwindow positionвҖқ, вҖңtarget digitsвҖқ, etc.
-- For DASHI: kernel is about how masks evolve; lens decides admissibility.

record State : Set where
  constructor st
  field
    mask   : Mask
    window : Nat   -- abstract вҖңdigit window idвҖқ (moving window, index, etc.)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- A lens is the measurement predicate:
-- admissible s m = вҖңremoving to mask m preserves the digit window conditionвҖқ.

record Lens : SetвӮҒ where
  field
    admissible : State вҶ’ Mask вҶ’ Bool

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Candidate moves:
-- In the real system, this is вҖңremove subsets of prime-power factorsвҖқ.
-- Here we just take a finite list of candidate masks.

Candidates : Set
Candidates = List Mask
module LogicTlurey where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality
open import Agda.Builtin.List
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Local equality utilities (no stdlib needed)
------------------------------------------------------------------------

sym : вҲҖ {A : Set} {x y : A} вҶ’ x вүЎ y вҶ’ y вүЎ x
sym refl = refl

cong : вҲҖ {A B : Set} {x y : A} (f : A вҶ’ B) вҶ’ x вүЎ y вҶ’ f x вүЎ f y
cong f refl = refl

open import Base369

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Dialectical stages
------------------------------------------------------------------------

data Stage : Set where
  seed      : Stage
  counter   : Stage
  resonance : Stage
  overflow  : Stage

next : Stage вҶ’ Stage
next seed      = counter
next counter   = resonance
next resonance = overflow
next overflow  = seed

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Tlurey traces
------------------------------------------------------------------------

StageTrace : Nat вҶ’ Stage вҶ’ List Stage
StageTrace zero    _ = []
StageTrace (suc n) s = s вҲ· StageTrace n (next s)

length : вҲҖ {A : Set} вҶ’ List A вҶ’ Nat
length []       = zero
length (_ вҲ· xs) = suc (length xs)

_++_ : вҲҖ {A : Set} вҶ’ List A вҶ’ List A вҶ’ List A
[]       ++ ys = ys
(x вҲ· xs) ++ ys = x вҲ· (xs ++ ys)

StageTrace-length : вҲҖ n s вҶ’ length (StageTrace n s) вүЎ n
StageTrace-length zero    _ = refl
StageTrace-length (suc n) s = cong suc (StageTrace-length n (next s))

nextвҒҙ : вҲҖ s вҶ’ spin 4 next s вүЎ s
nextвҒҙ seed      = refl
nextвҒҙ counter   = refl
nextвҒҙ resonance = refl
nextвҒҙ overflow  = refl

spin-next-succ : вҲҖ n s вҶ’ spin n next (next s) вүЎ spin (suc n) next s
spin-next-succ zero    _ = refl
spin-next-succ (suc n) s = cong next (spin-next-succ n s)

StageTrace-periodic : вҲҖ n s вҶ’ StageTrace (n + 4) s вүЎ StageTrace n s ++ StageTrace 4 (spin n next s)
StageTrace-periodic zero    s = refl
StageTrace-periodic (suc n) s rewrite sym (spin-next-succ n s) =
  cong (s вҲ·_) (StageTrace-periodic n (next s))

StageTrace-cycle : вҲҖ n вҶ’ StageTrace (n + 4) seed вүЎ StageTrace n seed ++ StageTrace 4 (spin n next seed)
StageTrace-cycle n = StageTrace-periodic n seed


------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Semantics via triadic values
------------------------------------------------------------------------

stageTone : Stage вҶ’ TriTruth
stageTone seed      = tri-low
stageTone counter   = tri-mid
stageTone resonance = tri-high
stageTone overflow  = tri-low

combineStage : Stage вҶ’ Stage вҶ’ TriTruth
combineStage a b = triXor (stageTone a) (stageTone b)

stageTone-next-seed : stageTone (next seed) вүЎ rotateTri (stageTone seed)
stageTone-next-seed = refl

stageTone-next-counter : stageTone (next counter) вүЎ rotateTri (stageTone counter)
stageTone-next-counter = refl

stageTone-next-resonance : stageTone (next resonance) вүЎ rotateTri (stageTone resonance)
stageTone-next-resonance = refl

stageTone-next-overflow : stageTone (next overflow) вүЎ stageTone seed
stageTone-next-overflow = refl

resonance-combine : combineStage resonance resonance вүЎ tri-mid
resonance-combine = refl
module MonsterGroups where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat      using (Nat; zero; suc; _+_)
open import Agda.Builtin.Bool     using (Bool; true; false)
open import Agda.Builtin.List     using (List; []; _вҲ·_)

open import MonsterState

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Boundary predicate: вҖңthis state ends a groupвҖқ.
-- You define it from the walk semantics (or from the trace table markers).

Boundary : Set
Boundary = State вҶ’ Bool

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Count groups in a trace given a boundary predicate.
-- Convention: group count starts at 0 for empty trace, else 1 + boundaries hit.

countGroups : Boundary вҶ’ List State вҶ’ Nat
countGroups b [] = 0
countGroups b (s вҲ· ss) = suc (go ss)
  where
    go : List State вҶ’ Nat
    go [] = 0
    go (t вҲ· ts) with b t
    ... | true  = suc (go ts)
    ... | false = go ts

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- You can similarly count вҖңpreserved digitsвҖқ if your trace stores that.
-- For now keep it abstract until you add a field.
-- Agda: 10-Fold Way Bridges
module TenfoldBridges where

open import Data.Nat using (в„•)
open import Data.Nat.DivMod using (_%_)
open import Data.Bool
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_вүЎ_; refl; sym; _вүў_)

-- Topological class
topoClass : в„• вҶ’ в„•
topoClass n = n % 10

-- Bridge record
record Bridge : Set where
  field
    nodeA : в„•
    nodeB : в„•
    different : topoClass nodeA вүў topoClass nodeB

-- Symmetry
bridge-sym : (b : Bridge) вҶ’ Bridge
bridge-sym record { nodeA = a ; nodeB = b ; different = d } =
  record { nodeA = b ; nodeB = a ; different = О» eq вҶ’ d (sym eq) }

-- Example: 232 вҶ” 323
bridge-232-323 : Bridge
bridge-232-323 = record
  { nodeA = 232
  ; nodeB = 323
  ; different = О» ()
  }

-- Theorem: Symmetry preserves bridges
bridge-symmetry : (b : Bridge) вҶ’ 
  Bridge.nodeA (bridge-sym b) вүЎ Bridge.nodeB b
bridge-symmetry b = refl
